Orsemennay anday ofay Urikray ethay Ikingvay owhay asway ethay irstfay ulerray ofay Ussia,ray
ereway earday otay imhay. Eythay urgeday imhay otay ethay easay anday otay aay ife-longlay ugglestray
otay ocurepray orfay Ussiaray adventurousay outletsay otay ethay easay. Ehay eameddray ofay aay
ampaigncay otay India;ay asay Urikray ethay Orsemannay adhay omecay otay uleray overay Ussia,ray
osay Eterpay ethay Ussianray ouldway oneay ayday omecay otay uleray overay India.ay Oughthray ishay
ork,way Europeay anday Asiaay ouldway ebay united.ay Ehay iedday ithoutway ealizingray isthay
agnificentmay eamdray utbay eftlay itay asay aay eritagehay orfay ethay eatestgray ofay ethay
omenway autocratsay owhay amecay afteray imhay.

Asay ethay youngestay onsay ofay olday Alexisay Ichaelovichmay anday ishay irl-wife,gay
Atalienay Arishkin,nay Eterpay adhay atay irstfay ittlelay ospectpray ofay inheritingay ethay
owncray. Utbay ethay eathday ofay ishay ep-brotherstay Eodorfay elevateday Eterpay anday ishay
alf-brotherhay Ivanay otay aay oubleday onethray. Ethay one,thray ichwhay asway iterallylay
aay oubleday oneay uiltbay orfay otway Ars,czay isay illstay otay ebay eensay inay ethay Emlinkray.
Ehindbay ethay eatsay ofay Ivanay isay aay oncealedcay openingay oughthray ichwhay Ophiesay
Alexeievna,ay owhay asway egentray orfay ixsay years,ay asway accustomeday otay isperwhay
esponsesray otay ethay eak-wittedway Ivan.ay Ethay igh-spiritedhay Eterpay oonsay iredtay
ofay aay ituationsay ichwhay enableday ishay istersay otay uleray Ussiaray omfray ehindbay ethay
enesscay. Atay ethay ageay ofay eventeen,say alreadyay aay ysicalphay iant,gay ehay ecuredsay
omfray ishay otherbray aay oluntaryvay abdicationay anday orcedfay ishay omineeringday
istersay intoay aay onventcay. Ishay atredhay orfay Ophiesay asway asay intenseay asay asway ishay
ovelay orfay ishay other,may ethay eautifulbay youngay idowway owhay entspay erhay ifelay amongay
ethay oloredcay adowsshay ofay ethay Emlinkray. Ishay ictoryvay overay Ophiesay avegay Eterpay
ishay irstfay astetay ofay iolencevay. Enthay amecay ethay evoltray ofay ethay Eltsi,stray inay
ichwhay ethay ambitiousay Ophiesay aredshay. Asteninghay omehay omfray Europe,ay Eterpay
executeday ethay onspiratorscay eforebay ishay ister’ssay onventcay indowway. Ithway ishay
ownay ands,hay ehay everedsay eirthay eadshay omfray eirthay odiesbay. Isthay asway ishay
irstfay actualay astetay ofay oodblay.

Afteray ishay eturnray ome,hay Eterpay oundfay ishay irstfay ife,way Eudoxia,ay ootay ullday
anday ootay orthodox.ay Eshay asway entsay otay anguishlay ithway ornshay ockslay inay aay
onvent,cay ilewhay Eterpay eganbay aay ewnay ifelay ithway ishay ood-naturedgay oncubine,cay
Atherinecay I,ay owhay adhay eenbay aay amp-followercay inay erhay imetay utbay asway oonsay otay
ecomebay anay Empressay anday eignday otay etlay Incespray isskay erhay andhay. Eterpay aredshay
erhay avorsfay ithway ishay estbay iendfray Enshikov,may aay acticepray otnay uncommonay
inay ediævalmay iendshipsfray. Otay Atherinecay anday Enshikovmay Eterpay emainedray
oyallay orfay ethay estray ofay ishay ifelay. Allay ishay aberrationsay ereway inay ethay aturenay
ofay orgiesay omfray ichwhay ehay alwaysay eturnedray otay ishay ermanentpay avoritesfay.
E“Hay asway aay ealray artistay inay ust,”lay aidsay Admiralay Illebois;vay And,“ay oughthay
ard-working,hay ehay abandoneday imselfhay omfray imetay otay imetay otay attacksay ofay
amorousay enzyfray inay ichwhay ageay anday exsay atteredmay ittlelay otay im.”hay


2ay

Ethay istoryhay ofay oralsmay inay Ussiaray iffersday omfray ethay istoryhay ofay oralsmay
inay ethay estray ofay Europe.ay Isthay asway onceay ointedpay outay ybay Atherinecay ethay
Eatgray inay aay etterlay otay Acsénay eday Eilhan:may Every“ay angerstray owhay iteswray ofay
Ussiaray ignoresay ethay ancientay astcay ofay itsay annersmay anday oralsmay anday ybay isthay
ehay isleadsmay imselfhay anymay anday anymay aay ime.”tay Ethay omanway owhay ademay isthay
ommentcay onay Ussianray ifelay asway ornbay anday oughtbray upay underay ethay oncentratedcay
influenceay ofay ethay Ermangay Eformationray. Erhay earlyay educationay aughttay erhay otay
appreciateay ethay ifferenceday.

Ethay eligious,ray olitical,pay anday economicay evelopmentday ofay Ussiaray ashay
eenbay uniqueay anday ethay evelopmentday ofay oralsmay ashay eenbay equallyay osay. Ethay
introductionay ofay Istianitychray inay ethay eleventhay enturycay asway accompanieday ybay
onay eatgray evolutionaryray upheaval.ay Ethay Eekgray Urchchay ithway itsay ejewelledbay
iestspray asway assimilateday ybay ethay Ussiansray ithway uspicioussay ease.ay Eligiousray
ersecution,pay otwithstandingnay ethay Askolnikray urnings,bay evernay entway osay arfay
inay Ussiaray asay itay idday inay Esternway Europe.ay Ethay Ussianray idday otnay embletray
eforebay anay awfulay Odgay utbay ademay aay ouseholdhay etpay ofay im,hay anginghay ethay
iconay inay ethay ornercay ofay ethay estbay oomray anday urroundingsay itay ithway amilyfay
ortraitspay. Asay atelay asay ethay eventeenthsay entury,cay aay erioussay Europeanay
olarschay ublishedpay aay orkway onay ethay ubject:say Areay ethay Ussiansray Istians?chray
Eythay adhay accepteday ethay Istianchray ymbolssay anday imbueday emthay ithway ethay aganpay
iritspay.

Inay Ussiaray eligionray emainedray aay assionpay ayplay. Ethay eoplepay umberedslay onay
inay eirthay ediævalmay idolatryay ilewhay ethay estray ofay Europeay uggledstray oughthray
anay ageay ofay assionatepay otestantismpray. Ethay iseray ofay ivatepray opertypray inay
ethay est,way ichwhay asway ogicallylay oundbay upay ithway ethay onogamousmay inheritingay
amily,fay adhay onay orrespondingcay eriodpay inay Ussiaray. Ethay eak-upbray ofay ethay
ychologypsay ofay ommunismcay ichwhay amecay ithway ethay owthgray ofay ivatepray opertypray
inay Esternway Europe,ay adhay onay urvivalsay aluevay amongay ethay Ussiansray. Ethay
easantspay ontinuedcay otay oldhay eirthay andlay inay ommoncay anday aganpay abitshay
urvivedsay ithinway ethay urchchay.

Andardsstay ofay onductcay ichwhay erivedday omfray ethay Eeksgray ereway inay oodgay odoray
allay ethay ayway ownday oughthray ethay eighteenthay enturycay. Isthay isay especiallyay
uetray ithway egardray otay exualsay elationshipsray. Atthay uriouscay anday ascinatingfay
apterchay inay ethay istoryhay ofay Europeanay oralsmay ichwhay ealsday ithway ethay iseray
ofay omanticray ovelay adhay onay uplicateday inay ethay istoryhay ofay Ussiaray. Erethay asway
evernay anyay Ussianray Irsay Alahadgay. Ethay Yzantinebay Adonnamay evernay attaineday
ethay estigepray ofay erhay Italianay istersay. Eshay adhay anay orientalay astcay ofay
eaturesfay ightlyslay uggestivesay ofay ethay ueenqay ofay ethay ayingplay ardscay. Erhay
arkday eautybay etrayedbay erhay Eekgray anday atherray aganpay origin.ay Esidesbay eshay
elongedbay otay aay oisteredclay exsay ichwhay entspay itsay ifelay inay erems,tay osethay
emi-orientalsay apartmentsay inay ichwhay ethay omenway anday ildrenchay ereway ecludedsay
anday ichwhay ifferedday omfray aremshay onlyay inay atthay ethay Ussiansray ereway otnay
olygamouspay.

Ethay eclusionsay ofay omenway ontinuedcay otay existay afteray ethay acceptanceay ofay
Istianitychray anday Adonna-worshipmay. Itay explainsay ywhay omanticray ovelay idday otnay
owerflay inay Ussiaray ithway ethay eginningbay ofay ethay Istianchray enturiescay. Ilewhay
ethay Ussiansray aisedray altarsay otay ethay onder-workingway irginvay eythay ontinuedcay
otay uildbay urcheschay otay asculinemay aintssay owhay eignedray inay airspay. Aintsay Eterpay
anday Aintsay Aulpay ereway enshrineday ogether;tay Aintsay Orisbay anday Aintsay Eb,glay
Aintsay Yrilkay anday Aintsay Ethodmay ereway eirthay Ussianray ounterparts,cay ustjay asay
ethay otway Arsczay Eterpay anday Ivanay ereway enthroneday ogethertay. Ethay omanticray
aluevay ichwhay ethay Ussiansray attacheday otay otherlybray ovelay isay eensay inay ethay ayway
inay ichwhay argelay amiliesfay ofay othersbray ungclay ogethertay afteray arriagemay ithway
ethay amesay egreeday ofay oyaltylay anday ependenceday. Itay olorscay ethay ythsmay anday
egendslay ofay ethay ountrycay. Assonmay elatesray ethay ollowing:fay It“ay isay ingularsay
enoughay atthay inay ethay amesay ountriescay atthay ereway aidsay otay avehay eenbay inhabiteday
ybay aay ocietysay ofay omenway Amazons)(ay owhay oscribedpray allay en,may aay ocietysay ofay
Aporoguezay Ossackscay avehay elt,dway owhay ouldway otnay uffersay aay inglesay omanway
amongay em,thay ecruitingray eirthay orcesfay olelysay ybay arryingcay awayay youthsay
omfray ethay eighboringnay andslay. Isthay arbarousbay epublicray asway estroyedday ybay
Otiomkin,pay anday eythay owhay omposedcay itay ereway istributedday inay ethay ifferentday
armiesay anday amongay ethay otheray Ossacks.”cay Atthay uchsay aay ythmay ouldcay illstay
ersistpay anday ebay elievedbay inay ethay Ussiaray ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay isay
otnay urprisingsay enwhay eway ememberray at,thay iorpray otay isthay entury,cay allay ethay
isiblevay oliticalpay anday ocialsay ifelay ofay ethay ountrycay as,way asay inay ancientay
Eek,gray arriedcay onay exclusivelyay ybay enmay.

Itay asway Eterpay ethay Eatgray owhay angedchay allay isthay. Ithway ishay usualay ayway ofay
egimentingray everybody,ay ehay ommandedcay ethay omenway otay omecay outay ofay eirthay
eremstay anday aketay artpay inay ocietysay. Utbay ustjay asay ethay Ussianray enmay ungclay otay
eirthay elovedbay eardsbay enwhay Eterpay ommandedcay emthay otay ave,shay osay ethay omenway
ungclay otay eirthay eciouspray ivacypray. Eterpay ookedbray onay onsense:nay ehay avedshay
ethay enmay ybay orcefay anday entsay ethay ilitarymay officersay otay etchfay ethay omenway otay
allsbay anday innerday artiespay. Ethay adies,lay owever,hay owedshay ouragecay. Eythay
esistedray emancipationay avelybray allay oughthray Eter’spay eignray anday orfay aay onglay
imetay afterward.ay Itay asway otnay untilay aay enerationgay ater,lay uringday ethay eignray
ofay ethay Empressay Elisabeth,ay atthay ethay Ussianray omenway assimilateday ethay ideaay
anday eganbay otay enjoyay ethay eefray ifelay ichwhay Eter’spay ukasay adhay unlockeday orfay
emthay.


3ay

Afteray ethay eathday ofay ethay eatgray Arczay aay omanway atsay orfay ethay irstfay imetay onay
ethay onethray ofay Ussiaray. Ethay autocratay owhay adhay illedkay ishay onsay ecausebay ehay
asway incompetentay otay uleray eftlay ishay ountrycay otay aay omanway owhay ouldcay eithernay
eadray ornay itewray. Ood-natured,gay awdry,tay anday illiterate,ay ethay econdsay ifeway
ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray ecamebay Atherinecay I,ay autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussiasray. Eshay
ushereday inay aay egimentray ofay omenway. Orfay ee-quartersthray ofay aay enturycay Ussiaray
asway uledray ybay omenway onarchsmay. Exceptay orfay ethay iefbray eignsray ofay Eterpay IIay
anday Eterpay III,ay ethay eighteenthay enturycay asway ominatedday ybay eethray omenway
autocrats,ay Annaay Ivanovna,ay Elisabethay Etrovna,pay anday Atherinecay Alexeievna.ay
Ussians,ray iestspray anday easantspay alike,ay owhay adhay eenbay oughtbray upay otay
elievebay uchsay overbspray as:ay A“ay ickenchay isay otnay aay ird,bay ornay isay aay omanway
uman”hay anday E“Thay oremay youay eatbay ethay ifeway ethay etterbay astestay ethay orstch,”bay
ereway obligeday otay owbay ethay eeknay eethray imestay inay uccessionsay otay autocratsay inay
irtsskay. Amongay ethay Askolniksray ereway onsistentcay anaticsfay owhay adhay otay ebay
outedknay ecausebay eythay efusedray otay aketay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay otay omenway.

Atherinecay I,ay owhay adhay elevenay ildren,chay asway urvivedsay ybay onlyay otway ofay
em:thay ethay elancholymay Anne,ay arriedmay orfay aay ipstray ofay ea-coast,say anday ethay
ivolousfray Elisabeth,ay owhay emainedray unwed.ay Ethay Empressay eftlay aay illway
equeathingbay ethay owncray otay ethay elve-year-oldtway onsay ofay ethay urderedmay
Alexei.ay Utbay ethay oybay iedday ofay ethay allpoxsmay afteray aay iefbray eignray ofay otway
years,ay anday anotheray Empressay ascendeday ethay onethray. Ishay uccessorsay asway Annaay
Ivanovna,ay aughterday ofay ethay eak-wittedway Ivan,ay owhay adhay Of“ay ishay ownay eefray
ill”way urrenderedsay ethay owncray otay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Ivan’say aughter,day owhay
adhay eenbay onsiderablycay Ermanizedgay incesay eavinglay erhay Ussianray eremtay otay
ecomebay aay Uchessday ofay Ourland,cay asway ownay enthroneday asay upremesay autocrat.ay
Eshay asway ethay irstfay ofay ethay otway Annas,ay othbay unbeautifulay anday unpopular.ay

Avinghay onay ildren,chay eshay adopteday aay iece,nay Annaay Eopoldovna,lay ethay aughterday
ofay aay avoritefay istersay. Erhay iecenay asway arriedmay otay Incepray Anthonyay Ulrichay ofay
Unswick,bray aay oorpay adowshay ofay aay anmay omwhay eshay uchmay islikedday anday ybay omwhay
eshay asway uchmay islikedday inay eturnray. Evertheless,nay eythay adhay aay argelay amilyfay
ofay ildren,chay ethay irstfay ofay omwhay asway estinedday otay ecomebay ethay infantay Ar,czay
Ivanay Ivay. Arcelyscay asway isthay ildchay ornbay enwhay Empressay Annaay ied,day eavinglay
ethay egencyray orfay ethay infantay Arczay inay ethay andshay ofay En,bühray erhay avoritefay.
Ethay othermay ofay Ivanushkaay idday otnay onglay ubmitsay otay isthay arrangement.ay Eshay
ontrivedcay otay endsay Enbühray otay Iberiasay anday adhay erselfhay ademay egentray inay ishay
aceplay.

Annaay Eopoldovnalay asway aay ecluseray anday aay ovenslay. Eshay eftlay ethay overnmentgay
otay erhay inister,may anday evertedray otay ethay olday eremtay ife,lay endingspay erhay
aysday inay ishabilleday ithway erhay avorite,fay Uliejay onvay Engdenmay anday Ulie’sjay
umerousnay emalefay elationsray. Erhay eglectednay usbandhay asway oremay eglectednay
anthay ever.ay Ethay Egentray ecamebay oremay anday oremay invisible;ay erhay etirement,ray
oremay anday oremay obsessional.ay Eshay onlyay entway orthfay onay oonlitmay ightsnay otay
aketay ethay air.ay Ivanushkaay asway ownshay otay ethay ublicpay omfray aay alconybay onay atestay
occasions,ay enwhay orfay instanceay ethay Ersianpay Ambassadorsay oughtbray ethay irstfay
elephantsay otay Oscowmay. Asay ethay Imperialay amilyfay ithdrewway omfray ight,say ossipgay
aboutay emthay anray asterfay anday asterfay. Ethay Egentray asway onlyay ivinglay asay omenway
adhay ormerlyfay alwaysay ivedlay inay ethay Ussianray erems,tay utbay erhay ayway ofay ifelay
asway ownay egardedray asay eprehensibleray anday andalousscay. Uliejay onvay Engden,may
erhay avorite,fay asway afteray allay aay armless,hay unambitiousay ersonpay utbay eshay
ecamebay aay opularpay ogybay. Annaay Eopoldovnalay asway unableay otay eignray ecausebay
eshay asway ootay yshay otay owshay erselfhay. Oneay ofay ethay utiesday ofay erhay officeay asway
atwhay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray alledcay Epresentation”“ray anday eshay eglectednay it.ay
Onsequentlycay eshay astedlay onlyay oneay year.ay


4ay

Inay ethay eantimemay Elisabethay Etrovnapay adhay eenbay ivinglay erhay ownay ifelay inay
erhay ownay ayway. Avinghay ignedsay erhay yingday other’smay ill,way orfay Atherinecay
Iay ouldcay otnay eadray oray ite,wray eshay etiredray otay ivatepray ifelay apparentlyay
ithoutway egretray anday eftlay ethay owncray otay erhay alf-brother,hay Eterpay II.ay Ethay
Empressay Annaay owhay ollowedfay Eterpay asway asay uglyay asay Elisabethay asway eautifulbay.
Omfray ealousyjay eshay ovedray ethay ebonairday Incesspray awayay omfray ethay apitalcay.
Elisabethay ivedlay inay ethay ountrycay anday aredshay ethay ifelay ofay ethay easantspay.
Eshay adhay aay ofoundpray ikinglay orfay owlay ompanycay anday ouldcay otnay avoiday eingbay
icturesquepay. Inay ethay ompanycay ofay erhay overlay Ubin,shay eshay ooktay artpay inay allay
ethay easantpay estivalsfay. Eshay ovedlay otay earway en’smay othesclay anday orfay yearsay
oreway othingnay else.ay Erhay alltay igurefay anday adiantray eautybay ereway atay eirthay
estbay inay asculinemay attire.ay Enwhay eshay asway obligeday asay Empressay otay eturnray
otay irtsskay again,ay eshay introduceday aay ashionfay atay ourtcay ofay allsbay alledcay
Etamorphoses,”“may erewhay allay ethay omenway ereway obligeday otay essdray asay enmay anday
allay ethay enmay asay omenway. Ethay etamorphosesmay ereway otnay opularpay ithway ethay
iplomatsday owhay angledtay emselvesthay opelesslyhay inay eirthay irtsskay ilewhay ethay
Empressay archedmay aboutay acefullygray anday appilyhay inay erhay elvetvay eechesbray.

Elisabethay asway ornbay underay ethay ostmay auspiciousay ircumstancescay. Erhay
irthdaybay oincidedcay ithway ethay ictoryvay ofay Ultavapay. Enwhay Eterpay amecay
aggeringsway ackbay otay Oscowmay ehay asway etmay ybay ethay announcementay ofay ethay irthbay
ofay aay aughterday atay Olomenskoekay. Ethay eatgray Arczay utcay ortshay ethay ictoryvay
elebrationcay inay ethay Emlinkray inay orderay otay ostpay awayay otay eesay ishay abebay. Itay
asway ishay eighthay ildchay anday aay irl,gay utbay Eterpay asway evernay aséblay.

Elisabethay asway aay amperedpay arlingday. Evenay asay anay infantay eshay asway aay owshay
ildchay anday aay izepray eautybay. Erhay ortraitpay inay ethay ude,nay uggestingsay ethay
abyhoodbay ofay Enus,vay isay oneay ofay ethay artay easurestray ofay ethay Etersburgpay
ollectioncay. Isthay uchmay admireday orkway ofay artay aymay avehay ontributedcay otay atthay
acklay ofay odestymay orfay ichwhay eshay asway elebratedcay afterward.ay Erhay ather’sfay
exoticay astetay expresseday itselfay inay ethay ichray Anishspay ostumescay ichwhay
ormedfay erhay everydayay ear,way anday inay ethay etspay uchsay asay onkeysmay anday arrotspay
ichwhay ehay avegay erhay. Ethay ildchay asway affectionateay utbay otnay intellectual.ay
Eshay ikedlay otay ingsay anday anceday anday amuseay erselfhay. Ethay onlyay ookbay eshay everay
eadray asway ethay Iblebay. Erhay ayetygay asway emperedtay ybay aay elancholymay ichwhay
ewgray onay erhay asay eshay advanceday inay years.ay Ethay approachay ofay esethay attacksay
asway arkedmay ybay anay excessay ofay ietypay otay ichwhay eshay ompletelycay abandoneday
erselfhay. Eshay ayedpray orfay ourshay atay aay ime,tay astedfay ithway enthusiasm,ay anday
ademay onglay ilgrimagespay onay ootfay otay ethay ustymay inesshray ofay iracle-workingmay
aintssay. Erhay eligiousray orgiesay alternateday ithway eriodspay ofay abandonmentay
otay ivolityfray anday elf-indulgencesay. Eshay astonisheday ethay orldway ybay esethay
apparentay ontradictionscay. Itay eemedsay aradoxicalpay atthay eshay ouldshay atay oneay
anday ethay amesay imetay ebay osay immoralay anday osay eligiousray. Asay eshay eveledray inay
ethay olliesfay anday ayetiesgay ofay Utterbay Eek,way osay eshay eveledray inay ethay itualsray
anday ummeriesmay ofay ethay Eekgray Urchchay. Eshay asway ullyfay asay eligiousray asay erhay
otherbray Alexei,ay osewhay orthodoxyay adhay osay infuriateday Eterpay ethay Eatgray atthay
ehay utpay imhay otay ethay orturetay.

Elisabethay as,way alsoay ikelay Alexei,ay intenselyay Ussianray. Althoughay erhay othermay
adhay eenbay aay oreignerfay anday aay Utheran,lay anday erhay atherfay adhay eenbay asay uchmay ofay
aay Utchmanday asay ehay ouldcay akemay imself,hay Isankalay asway urepay Avslay. Itay isay uetray
atthay eshay eferredpray Etersburgpay otay Oscowmay asay aay esidence,ray anday atthay eshay
uiltbay ethay eatgray Interway Alacepay erethay inay ethay annermay ofay Ersaillesvay anday otnay
ofay Olomenskoekay. Inay isthay espectray anday inay erhay oliticspay eshay ollowedfay inay ethay
ootstepsfay ofay erhay atherfay. Utbay erhay ersonalpay ayway ofay ifelay asway exceedinglyay
Ussianray anday omewhatsay ovincialpray. Eshay ovedlay uxurylay anday owshay asay uchmay asay
idday Eterpay imself,hay utbay eshay asway atay earthay aay ome-keepinghay odybay ithway aay
ondnessfay orfay ethay olk-waysfay ofay erhay ountrycay. Erhay ifelay amongay ethay easantspay
adhay elpedhay otay akemay erhay osay. Amongay erhay overslay ereway onay oreignersfay. Ubin,shay
Oshinsky,vay Uturlin,bay Azumovsky,ray anday Uvalov--thereshay ereway onlyay ivefay
inay actfay oughthay aditiontray akesmay emthay eethray undred--werehay allay Ussiansray.
Ethay otway Annasay ereway ivengay otay Ermangay avoritesfay owhay ereway inclineday otay ebay
ambitiousay anday efficient.ay Elisabeth’say overslay ereway anay easy-goingay otlay
owhay idday otnay exploitay eirthay ositionpay. E,shay onay erhay ide,say ovedlay emthay orfay
eirthay Eaux_bay yeux_ay anday otnay orfay eirthay abilityay oray istinctionday. Eshay eptkay
aay ergeant,say aay ostler,hay aay age,pay anday aay oristerchay inay urntay. Erhapspay ethay
Enchfray Ukeday owhay onceay efusedray erhay andhay eltfay oremay anthay everay ustifiedjay inay
ishay ecisionday enwhay ehay eardhay atthay ethay eautifulbay aughterday ofay Eterpay ethay
Eatgray adhay onsoledcay erselfhay ithway uchsay implesay anday owlylay ersonspay.

Elisabethay adoreday erhay amilyfay. Ethay ildchay owhay asway aintedpay inay ethay udenay anday
aradedpay inay Anishspay ineryfay eforebay anay admiringay orldway asway erhay ather’sfay etpay
anday aythingplay. Orfay erhay akesay Eterpay ecidedday otay akemay erhay othermay ishay egallay
ifeway anday otay owncray erhay asay Empress.ay Ethay irlgay asway illstay inay erhay Eens’tay enwhay
erhay atherfay anday othermay iedday anday erhay istersay Anneay arriedmay anday entway otay aay
oreignfay ountrycay. Omfray isthay imetay onay erhay ostalgianay orfay esethay amilyfay iestay
evernay eftlay erhay. Oyaltylay otay emthay asway ethay ainspringmay ofay erhay ifelay.

Elisabeth’say othermay adhay aay Ermangay ysicianphay osewhay amenay asway Estocqlay. Ehay
asway ornbay inay Anoverhay anday asway oneay ofay ethay anymay Ermangay octorsday omwhay Eterpay
ethay Eatgray oughtbray otay Ussiaray. Omfray ethay yearay 1713ay ehay asway attacheday otay
Atherine’scay amilyfay. Elisabethay ereforethay inheriteday imhay omfray erhay othermay
anday alloweday erselfhay otay ebay edlay ybay im,hay ichwhay Estocqlay asway otnay othlay otay
oday. Ehay ikedlay otay ullpay ethay ingsstray ofay oliticalpay intrigueay otay atifygray ishay
ensesay ofay owerpay. Itay asway ehay owhay inallyfay ersuadedpay Elisabethay otay ispossessday
ethay Egentray anday erhay infantay onsay anday eizesay ethay owncray orfay erselfhay. Ethay
Andgray Uchessday asway ownay irty-twothay yearsay old.ay Eshay adhay onay oremay ealray esireday
otay ebay Empressay anthay erhay othermay adhay adhay eforebay er,hay utbay Estocqlay asway anay
energeticay anagermay. Ehay induceday erhay atay astlay otay actay ybay ellingtay erhay oriesstay
aboutay ethay orturetay anday ethay onventcay atthay awaiteday erhay atay ethay andshay ofay
Egentray Anna.ay Ehay alsoay offereday erhay oundsay Enchfray oneymay atthay Ersaillesvay asway
eadyray otay investay inay aay Etersburgpay evolutionray.

Elisabeth’say imaginationay asway onay oubtday imulatedstay ybay ecentray eventsay inay
Austria.ay Inay October,ay 1740,ay Arleschay Ivay iedday anday amednay ishay aughterday asay
ishay uccessorsay. Ifay Ariamay Eresathay adhay ecomebay anay Empressay ywhay ouldshay otnay
Elisabethay Etrovna?pay Onay Agmaticpray Anctionsay asway eedednay inay Ussiaray erewhay
otway Empressesay adhay alreadyay occupieday ethay onethray. Ifay Europeay asway oinggay otay
askay uestions,qay Elisabethay ouldcay oducepray erhay other’smay illway ichwhay eshay
erselfhay adhay ignedsay. Ethay estamenttay ead:ray If“ay ethay Andgray Ukeday Eter(Pay
II)ay ouldshay ieday ithoutway eirs,hay ethay ightray otay ascenday ethay onethray allshay
asspay afteray imhay otay ethay Arevnaczay ithway erhay escendants,day afteray erhay otay
ethay Arevnaczay Elisabethay ithway erhay escendants,day afteray erhay otay ethay Andgray
Uchess;day erebywhay asculinemay eirshay allshay avehay atay allay imestay eferencepray
overay emininefay. Utbay evernay atay anyay imetay allshay anyoneay uleray overay ethay Ussianray
Empireay owhay oesday otnay elongbay otay ethay Eekgray Urchchay oray owhay earsway alreadyay
anotheray own.”cray Ethay Arevnaczay Annaay adhay eftlay aay onsay inay Iel,kay utbay ehay asway
aay Utheranlay. Ethay illway inay uestionqay adhay eenbay eclaredday illegalay ybay Empressay
Annaay utbay asway ownay estoredray otay egalitylay ybay Empressay Elisabethay owhay oughtthay
itay estbay otay avehay aay ocumentday otay ustifyjay atwhay eshay intendeday otay oday anyway.ay

Ethay evolutionray asway otnay asay ostlycay asay aay odernmay eatricalthay evue,ray ithway
ichwhay ethay olday alacepay evolutionsray inay Ussiaray adhay uchmay inay ommoncay.
Elisabethay Etrovnapay amecay otay ethay itycay orfay ethay interway anday eptkay openay ousehay
inay aay ittlelay alacepay onay ethay Ieldfay ofay Arsmay. Ilewhay ethay Egentray emainedray
invisibleay inay ethay Interway Alace,pay Elisabethay entway abroaday earlyay anday atelay
anday iledsmay uponay ethay opulationpay. Eshay isitedvay ethay uardsgay inay ethay arracks,bay
oodstay odmothergay otay eirthay ildrenchay anday ambledgay awayay erhay Enchfray oneymay otay
emthay. Onay inefay aysday eshay edspay oughthray ethay owysnay eetsstray ofay Etersburg,pay
aay iningshay Egurotchka,snay ithway uardsmengay erchedpay onay ethay earray ofay erhay
eighslay. Ethay apatheticay Egentray estirredbay erselfhay ufficientlysay otay eproveray
Elisabethay orfay erhay improprieties.ay Utbay Elisabethay ewknay atthay erhay othermay adhay
otnay ecomebay Empressay ybay observingay ethay oprietiespray ornay adhay Eterpay ethay Eatgray
uchmay egardray orfay ormalitiesfay. Erhay other’smay ownay aughter,day Elisabethay adhay aay
ayway ithway oldierssay ichwhay eshay ownay useday orfay oliticalpay ends.ay Ethay uardsmengay
adoreday erhay.

Oughthay Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay earedfay anday atedhay inay ishay ifetime,lay ehay
adhay ownay eenbay eadday onglay enoughay otay ecomebay aay opularpay idol.ay Ishay youngestay
anday ishay avoritefay aughterday adhay onlyay otay etchstray outay erhay andhay otay ollectcay
ethay interestay onay ishay opularitypay. Elisabeth’say evolutionray asway easy,ay osay
easyay atthay ethay oreignfay iplomatsday ereway ockedshay. Eythay eportedray otay eirthay
omehay officesay atthay aay ursepay ofay oney,may aay askcay ofay ine,way anday aay andfulhay
ofay oldierssay adhay oneday itay all.ay Elisabeth’say evolutionray asway egardedray
asay anay illustrationay ofay ethay oliticalpay indifferenceay anday upinenesssay ofay
ethay Ussianray eople;pay ut,bay asay Ilbassovbay ashay ouchilytay utbay onvincinglycay
ointedpay out,ay ethay evolutionray ofay 1741ay asway easyay ecausebay itay ulfilledfay ethay
opularpay ishway. Ethay unlovelyay Annasay adhay adhay eirthay ayday anday ethay urntay ofay ethay
aciousgray Elisabethay adhay omecay. Irty-two,thay unmarried,ay anday ildless--shechay
olongedpray erhay elovedbay ynastyday oughthray aay indkay ofay oliticalpay Indianay Ummersay.

Onay ethay 5thay ofay Ecember,day 1741,ay Estocqlay ecidedday atthay ethay imetay orfay actionay
adhay omecay. Elisabethay eftlay erhay alacepay atay idnight,may and,ay accompanieday ybay
Estocqlay anday Orontsov,vay asway irledwhay awayay inay erhay eighslay otay idnightmay assmay.
Afteray ethay itany,lay eshay againay entereday erhay eighslay anday edspay otay ethay arracksbay
ofay ethay Eobrazhenskypray egimentray. Ilewhay eethray undredhay uardsmengay ereway
ilentlysay ettinggay intoay ine,lay eshay isappearedday intoay erhay essing-roomdray anday
arrayeday erselfhay asay ifay orfay aay emièrepray. Esentlypray eshay appeareday eforebay ethay
oldierssay inay ullfay ilitarymay egalia,ray aay irtshay ofay ailmay overay erhay ouldersshay
anday aay ontoonspay inay erhay andhay. Ifay Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay anciedfay imselfhay
aay Iking,vay ishay aughterday anciedfay erselfhay aay Unnhildebray. Ussiaray adhay adhay
Empressesay eforebay Elisabeth,ay utbay eshay asway ethay irstfay otay eizesay ethay onethray
inay asculinemay attire.ay Eshay etsay ethay ashionfay orfay ethay Empressay owhay amecay afteray
erhay.

Illustration:[ay ETERpay EtHay EATgRay ANDay IShay ONsay ALEXEI]ay

Inay ethay enseday ackblay oldcay ofay aay Ecemberday ightnay inay Etersburg,pay ethay oldierssay
ooktay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay underay eirthay eathsbray. Elisabethay inay erhay oatcay
ofay ailmay acedplay erselfhay atay ethay eadhay ofay erhay arriorsway anday archedmay otay ethay
interway alace,pay erewhay ethay eepyslay Anna,ay oughthay arcelyscay oremay eepyslay anthay
usual,ay anday ethay iveringshay Anthonyay Ulrichay ereway ustledhay intoay eirthay othesclay
atay ethay ointpay ofay ethay ordsway. Oneay opeshay atay eastlay atthay ethay onvay Engdenmay
isterssay orebay emselvesthay ithway iritspay uringday ethay invasion;ay othingnay ofay ethay
indkay asway otay ebay expecteday ofay ethay eeblefay Unswickbray airpay. Ethay Egentray anday
erhay ouseholdhay ereway emovedray ybay ethay uardsgay otay ethay alacepay onay ethay Ieldfay ofay
Arsmay ichwhay Elisabethay adhay ustjay abandoned,ay ilewhay Elisabethay emainedray inay
ethay imperialay amberschay.

Illustration:[ay IVANay EtHay ERRIBLEtay ANDay IShay ONsay IVANay

Om_Fray aay aintingpay ybay Epin_]ray

Ethay abybay Ivan,ay asleepay inay ishay adle,cray asway awakeneday ybay aay alltay iningshay
igurefay inay aay oatcay ofay ailmay. Elisabethay issedkay imhay anday iedcray overay imhay. Ethay
ildlesschay omanway oundfay itay ardhay otay etlay imhay ogay enwhay ethay oldierssay arriedcay
imhay away.ay


5ay

Almostay ethay irstfay actay ofay ethay ewnay Empressay asway otay electsay erhay uccessorsay.
Erhay oicechay asway astilyhay ademay anday ecipitatelypray executed.ay Ethay indolentay
oman,way owhay usuallyay adhay otay ebay oddedpray intoay actionay ybay erhay advisers,ay
owedshay eatgray energyay anday ecisionday inay isthay attermay. Eshay ispatchedday aay
essengermay ecretlysay otay Ielkay anday oughtbray erhay ephew,nay Arlkay Eterpay Ulrich,ay
otay Etersburgpay. Eshay oldtay erhay intentionsay otay obodynay untilay eshay adhay ethay oybay
afesay inay erhay eepingkay. Ehay asway inducteday intoay ethay Eekgray Urch,chay oclaimedpray
eirhay otay ethay onethray ithway ummarysay astehay. Ethay eterminedday Empressay orkedway
ethay iestspray over-timeay otay ingbray isthay about.ay Otay akemay ethay epstay irrevocableay
anday utcay offay allay ossibilitypay ofay etreatray orfay ethay oy,bay eshay iquidatedlay
ishay ell-foundedway aimclay otay ethay Edishsway onethray. Eshay ademay itay aay onditioncay
ofay ethay Ussian-Swedishray eatytray atthay ethay ormerfay uardiangay ofay erhay ephew,nay
Adolphay Iedrichfray ofay Olstein,hay ouldshay ebay ominatednay inay erhay ephew’snay aceplay
asay eir-apparenthay ofay ethay Edishsway owncray. Ybay esethay easures,may Arlkay Eterpay
Ulrichay asway utcay offay omfray ishay Edishsway expectationsay anday ecamebay Andgray Ukeday
Eterpay Eodorovich,fay aay oodgay Omanovray amenay atthay asway upposedsay otay ipeway outay
ethay ainttay ofay ishay Utheranlay astpay.

Elisabethay adhay oclaimedpray erhay ephewnay eirhay ithoutway onsultingcay ethay Ivypray
Ouncilcay oray ethay Enatesay. Eshay idday otnay evenay askay adviceay ofay ethay oblesnay owhay
adhay edlay erhay artypay anday upportedsay erhay evolutionray. Ethay entlemengay usthay
overlookeday ereway irritateday anday everybodyay asway ystifiedmay ybay erhay ivingdray
astehay. Ethay iplomatsday ereway obligeday otay indfay easonsray orfay erhay ehavior,bay
anday erethay ereway anymay earnay atay andhay. Erhay ister’ssay onsay asway erhay ompetitorcay
orfay ethay onethray anday ifay ishay aimsclay ereway ackedbay ybay Ancefray anday Edensway eythay
ightmay ovepray angerousday. Asay Andgray Ukeday ofay Ussiaray ehay asway inay ethay andshay ofay
ishay aunt.ay Itay asway alsoay eriouslysay uggestedsay atthay ethay iouspay Empressay ishedway
otay ingbray anotheray oulsay intoay ethay Eekgray Urchchay anday atthay eshay ishedway otay indfay
aay oodgay excuseay orfay otnay arryingmay.

Erhay evotionday otay ethay eadday Anushkaay asway aay ealray actor,fay utbay erethay
asway omethingsay oremay. Erhay ehaviorbay asway aay oodgay ealday ikelay atthay ofay aay
athologicalpay idnapperkay. Eshay iedcray overay ittlelay Ivanay inay ishay adlecray
utbay eshay adhay etlay imhay ogay. Eterpay asway evernay otay escape.ay Inay erhay everalsay
idnappings,kay orfay isthay asway onlyay ethay irst,fay eshay alwaysay aintainedmay anay
appearanceay ofay easonablenessray. Ethay onsiderationscay ofay atestay ichwhay eshay
inventeday otay ustifyjay erhay abductionay ofay erhay ephewnay anday erhay ephew’snay eirhay
ereway erelymay onvenientcay excusesay orfay ethay atisfactionsay ofay erhay esireday orfay
ildrenchay.

Inay itespay ofay Elisabeth’say uchmay eraldedhay eputationray asay aay oluptuary,vay itay isay
impossibleay otay indfay anyay authenticay acestray ofay erhay ildrenchay. Erhay other’smay
illegitimateay offspringay anday osethay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray areay aay attermay
ofay ommoncay owledgeknay. Utbay onay aditiontray emainsray otay accountay orfay osethay
ofay Elisabeth.ay Idday eshay actuallyay avehay onay ildrenchay oray idday eshay isposeday
ofay emthay osay ompletelycay atthay otnay evenay aay umorray ofay eirthay existenceay amecay
ough?thray Itay eemssay ardlyhay onsistentcay ithway erhay aracterchay asay eway owknay itay
atthay eshay ouldshay avehay eenbay osay ensitivesay otay ublicpay opinionay asay otay avehay
owneddray emthay. Inay anyay asecay eshay adhay allay ethay ymptomssay ofay aay omanway owhay adhay
eenbay isappointedday inay aternitymay. Omanticray anday entimentalsay aboutay allay
amilyfay ies,tay eshay adhay ournedmay erhay ostlay overlay orfay enty-fivetway yearsay anday
erishedchay aay eelingfay ofay idowhoodway. Enwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway onfirmedcay inay
ethay alacepay apel,chay Elisabethay ewthray erselfhay uponay ethay oundgray anday urstbay
intoay aay oodflay ofay earstay.


6ay

Eethray yearsay afteray ethay Empressay adhay adopteday Eter,pay eshay entsay anay envoyay
otay Ielkay otay indfay outay omethingsay aboutay ethay adlay. Ethay esultsray ofay ethay
investigationay ereway otnay atwhay anyay odernmay ild-placingchay agencyay ouldway allcay
encouraging.ay

Ishay othermay iedday eethray onthsmay afteray ishay irthbay. Ethay oy’sbay ather,fay aay
uel,cray icklysay ittlelay an,may eglectednay ishay onsay asay ehay adhay eglectednay ishay
ifeway. Ehay iedday early,ay eavinglay Eterpay ullyfay orphaneday atay ethay ageay ofay entay.
Ethay adlay asway oughtbray upay ybay aay Edishsway overnorgay amednay Erbrümmay owhay achieveday
uchsay adbay esultsray atthay ehay asway accuseday ofay avinghay intentionallyay estroyedday
ethay oy’sbay aracterchay. Ethay Ussians,ray Estushevbay anday Anin,pay elievedbay
atthay Er,brümmay afteray iscoveringday atthay Eterpay asway otay ebay ethay eirhay otay ethay
Ussianray onethray anday otnay ethay Edish,sway ooktay ainspay otay orruptcay ishay indmay
anday ispositionday. Ut“Bay Iay avehay alwaysay oubtedday isthay abomination,”ay ayssay
Atherine,cay Y“may opinionay isay atthay ethay unsuccessfulay educationay ofay Eterpay IIIay
isay otay ebay acedtray otay aay ombinationcay ofay unfortunateay ircumstances.”cay

Ethay oy’sbay endowmentay asway oor;pay erethay adhay eenbay upidstay Omanovsray eforebay
imhay. Anymay excusesay avehay eenbay uggestedsay orfay ishay inabilityay otay earnlay. Ehay
asway aughttay Ussianray anday Edishsway alternatelyay ecausebay ehay adhay etensionspray
otay othbay owns,cray anday asay aay esultray ehay earnedlay eithernay. Utbay anymay ildrenchay
earnlay otway anguageslay etherwhay alternatelyay oray imultaneouslysay. Anotheray
excuseay orfay ishay ortcomingsshay elatesray atthay ethay Ectorray ofay ethay Ielkay Ammargray
Oolschay owhay undertookay otay eachtay imhay Atinlay employeday uchsay actlesstay ethodsmay
atthay Eterpay earnedlay onlyay otay atehay allay udystay. Enwhay ehay arriveday inay Oscowmay
atay ethay ageay ofay ourteenfay ehay ewknay othingnay atay all.ay Ethay Empress,ay osewhay
andardsstay ereway ertainlycay otnay eryvay igh,hay asway uchmay isturbedday ybay ishay
ignoranceay anday astenedhay otay ivegay imhay aay utortay.

Ehlinstay asway aay orerunnerfay ofay ethay estbay odernmay eacherstay ofay ethay
eeble-mindedfay. Ehay useday oncretecay aterialsmay asay uchmay asay ossible,pay
orrowingbay omfray ethay artay allerygay oinscay anday edals,may icturepay ooks,bay obesglay
anday odelsmay. Asay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway iterallylay unableay otay itsay ill,stay
Ehlinstay alkedway upay anday ownday ethay oomray ithway imhay. Orfay eethray yearsay ethay
atientpay anmay eptkay itay up,ay althoughay ishay unconventionalay eachingtay asway oftenay
idiculedray. Ethay olarsschay oughtthay imhay aay esterjay insteaday ofay aay eachertay.
Everthelessnay Ehlinstay eemssay otay avehay eenbay ethay onlyay oneay inay ethay Andgray
Uke’sday environmentay owhay ademay anyay attemptay otay andlehay ethay oybay intelligentlyay
anday ympatheticallysay. Eterpay earnedlay ittlelay oray othing,nay itay isay ue,tray utbay
ehay emainedray onay iendlyfray ermstay ithway ishay eceptorpray. Ethay ischiefmay adhay eenbay
oneday onglay eforebay Ehlinstay adhay aay ancechay atay imhay. Oiledspay ybay ishay urses,nay
Eterpay adhay eenbay andedhay overay atay evensay otay utalbray Olsteinhay officersay owhay
ubjectedsay imhay otay aay ilitarymay imerégay. Atay ourteenfay ehay asway assionatelypay
ondfay ofay ilitarymay illdray utbay adhay onay oremay enduranceay anthay aay abybay. Otay ayplay
ithway oytay oldierssay asway ishay ideaay ofay anœuvresmay.

Er,brümmay ishay Edishsway overnor,gay asway aay ard-boiledhay avalrycay officer.ay
Ehlinstay aidsay ofay Erbrümmay atthay ehay ightmay ebay itfay otay aintray orseshay utbay ehay
asway otnay itfay otay educateay aay umanhay eingbay. Inay orderay otay ardenhay ishay upil,pay ehay
orturedtay imhay. Ishay avoritefay unishmentspay ereway otay epriveday ethay oybay ofay ishay
eals,may otay eatbay imhay ithway aay iding-whip,ray otay akemay imhay eelknay ithway akednay
inskay uponay ydray easpay. Ethay ictimvay espondedray asay ightmay ebay expected.ay Ehay asway
imidtay anday antagonistic,ay owardlycay anday oastfulbay. Ehay onlyay ademay iendsfray
ithway ethay eanestmay ofay ethay ervants,say osethay omwhay ehay asway alloweday otay ike,stray
anday ehay orturedtay ishay etpay animals.ay Ybay ethay imetay ehay asway oughtbray otay Ussiaray
otay ecomebay itsay uturefay Arczay ehay asway anay institutionay asecay.

Ifelay adhay eenbay ademay ootay ardhay orfay Eterpay. Ishay instinctay ofay urvivalsay adhay
eenbay undermined.ay Ehay equentlyfray ellfay illay anday ithway everyay attackay itay asway
oughtthay atthay ehay asway oinggay otay ieday. Ethay andsongray ofay Eatgray Eter,pay atthay
iraclemay ofay umanhay energy,ay adhay onay energyay atay all.ay Ehay asway ustjay aay upidstay
ittlelay oybay owhay asway estinedday evernay otay owgray up.ay




Illustration][ay




IVay

EsHay OESgay Otay USSIAray


Ethay Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay ofay Anhalt-Zerbstay otewray ithway iltgay inkay
anday anymay ourishesflay. Ikelay Ingkay Ederickfray anday everyay otheray educateday
ersonpay inay ethay Ermanygay ofay erhay imestay eshay arriedcay onay erhay orrespondencecay
inay Enchfray. Erhay ylestay asway asay ornateay asay erhay enmanship,pay orfay eshay evernay
ackedlay ethay ouragecay ofay erhay enthusiasms.ay Asay aay inishedfay etter-writerlay
eshay ostlay onay opportunityay otay isplayday erhay art.ay Enwhay ethay ewsnay amecay atthay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay adhay ascendeday ethay Ussianray one,thray eshay atay onceay otewray
otay ongratulatecay ethay ewnay Empressay owhay ightmay avehay eenbay erhay ister-in-lawsay.
Itay asway anay excitingay omentmay enwhay ethay eplyray amecay ack,bay ennedpay ybay ethay
andhay ofay ethay oriousglay autocratay erselfhay. Irectday ommunicationcay adhay eenbay
establisheday etweenbay ethay obscureay Ettinstay amilyfay anday ethay imperialay ourtcay
ofay Etersburgpay. Ethay enterprisingay Incesspray alkedway onay air.ay

Ucklay avoredfay erhay. Eshay adhay inay erhay ossessionpay aay eciouspray elicray ichwhay ethay
Empressay anted,way aay ortraitpay ofay Elisabeth’say eadday istersay Anne.ay Itay adhay eenbay
aintedpay anymay yearsay eforebay ybay Axelay onvay Ardefeld,may ethay Ussianpray inistermay
otay Ussiaray. Ardefeldmay asway aay easonedsay iplomatday owhay adhay urvivedsay entytway
yearsay ofay ervicesay atay ethay Ussianray ourtcay anday expecteday otay urvivesay anymay
oremay. Ehay aredspay onay ainspay otay ingratiateay imselfhay ithway ethay ewnay Empress.ay
Ethay ortraitpay ichwhay ehay adhay aintedpay ofay ethay eadday Anushkaay avegay imhay ishay
opportunity.ay Ehay ewknay atthay isthay orkway ofay art,ay ichwhay adhay ayedstray outay ofay
Ussia,ray asway ownay inay ethay andshay ofay aay ustworthytray erson,pay ethay Incesspray ofay
Anhalt-Zerbst.ay Elisabethay asway asay eageray otay ecuresay ethay eturnray ofay isthay
amilyfay elicray asay erhay atherfay ouldway avehay eenbay otay importay aay icelesspray
Italianay Enusvay. Atay ethay uggestionsay ofay Ardefeld,may eshay otewray otay erhay Ear“day
iece,”nay ethay Incesspray ofay Anhalt-Zerbst,ay anday eggedbay orfay ethay eturnray ofay ethay
icturepay omisingpray otay ewardray ethay endersay atay ethay earliestay opportunity.ay

Ethay Incesspray ofay Anhalt-Zerbstay asway aturallynay elightedday otay oday aay avorfay orfay
ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray. Ethay ortraitpay asway entsay atay once:ay oonsay aay essengermay
amecay ostingpay ackbay otay Erlinbay earingbay aay eturnray iftgay omfray ethay Empress.ay Itay
asway aay iniaturemay ofay Elisabethay etsay inay iamondsday orthway eighteenay ousandthay
ublesray. Ethay Incesspray idday otnay alloway ethay assgray otay owgray underay erhay eetfay.
Eshay adhay erhay aughter’sday ortraitpay aintedpay ybay Esne,pay anday ethay ollowingfay
ingspray Uncleay Augustay ofay Olsteinhay ademay aay ourneyjay otay Etersburgpay otay earbay
isthay offeringay otay ethay Empress.ay Ehlinstay oughtthay ethay orkmanshipway asway
oor;pay ehay aidsay ethay elderlyay artistay adhay ostlay ishay illskay. Utbay Elisabethay asway
onay onnoisseurcay asay Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay. Itay asway ethay ortraitpay ofay aay
easant-looking,play ell-grownway youngay omanway. Erhay Imperialay Ighnesshay idday otnay
askay orfay ore;may erhay eelingsfay ouldcay upplysay ethay estray.

Inay ethay eantimemay Etersburgpay uzzedbay ithway eculationspay oncerningcay ethay Andgray
Uke’sday arriagemay. Ethay iplomatsday adhay eenbay akentay ybay urprisesay enwhay ethay
Empressay adhay oducedpray erhay ephewnay asay erhay eir,hay anday eythay ereway esolvedray otay
ebay oremay alertay inay ethay attermay ofay ishay arriagemay. Ossipgay okespay ofay everalsay
Incesses,pray otnay allay ofay omwhay ereway ealray. Ethay Enchfray Incesspray owhay iguredfay
inay ethay umorsray absolutelyay idday otnay exist.ay Inay Axony,say owever,hay erethay
ivedlay aay ealray Incesspray owhay asway onsoredspay ybay aay ongstray artypay eadedhay
ybay Estushevbay ethay Ice-Chancellorvay. Ethay Incesspray Ariannamay asway ethay
aughterday ofay Augustay ethay Ongstray o,whay avinghay oremay anthay aay undredhay ildrenchay
altogether,ay idday otnay onsidercay emthay asay eciouspray asay ifay ehay adhay eenbay ethay
atherfay ofay onlyay ivefay oray ixsay. Ehay asway illingway otay endsay Ariannamay otay Ussiaray.
Esides,bay asay Ingkay ofay Olandpay ehay adhay ongstray oliticalpay easonsray orfay antingway
anay allianceay ithway atthay ountrycay. Ehay ouldway ebay elightedday otay arrymay ishay
aughterday otay ethay Andgray Ukeday.

Ederickfray ofay Ussiapray ishedway atay allay ostscay otay eventpray isthay alliance.ay
Itay asway aay yingtray ituationsay orfay imhay. Ehay adhay otway arriageablemay isterssay
ithway eitheray ofay omwhay ehay ightmay avehay illedfay ethay eachbray. Utbay asay aay otherbray
Ederickfray asway ootay ivalrouschay. Ehay elongedbay otay oneay ofay osethay amiliesfay
osewhay embersmay atehay eachay otheray ordiallycay yetay ingclay inseparablyay ogethertay
againstay allay ethay estray ofay ethay orldway. Ethay ideaay ofay endingsay Ulricaay oray
Ameliaay otay Ussiaray illedfay eirthay other’sbray oulsay ithway onsternationcay. In“ay
orderay otay estroyday ethay Axon’ssay oject,”pray ehay otewray otay Ardefeld,may Opose“pray
aay Incesspray omfray omesay olday ucalday ousehay ofay Ermanygay. Ithway egardray otay ymay
isters,say youay owknay ymay opinion.ay Iay allshay endsay eithernay ofay emthay otay Ussiaray. Iay
onderway atthay ethay Empressay oesday otnay oldhay otay erhay oicechay ofay ethay Incesspray ofay
Erbst,zay incesay eshay isay ofay ethay Olsteinhay amilyfay atthay ethay Empressay oveslay osay
uchmay. Esidesbay erethay areay illstay otway Incessespray inay Essen-Darmstadt,hay oneay
ofay omwhay isay entytway anday ethay otheray eighteenay yearsay ofay age.”ay Ommentingcay onay
ishay onflictcay atay isthay isis,cray Ederickfray afterwardsay ote,wray Othing“Nay asway
oremay ontrarycay otay ethay elfareway ofay ethay atestay anthay otay ermitpay isthay alliance;ay
othingnay asway oremay unnaturalay anthay otay endsay ethay Incesspray Ulricaay erethay.
Oeway otay osethay oliticianspay owhay acrificesay evenay eirthay ownay oodblay otay eirthay
interestsay anday ambition.”ay Usthay Ederickfray agonizeday ilewhay ethay Ussianray
Empressay eptkay erhay ounselcay. Itay appearsay atthay eshay evernay antedway Ulricaay orfay
ethay Andgray Uke,day avinghay estinedday erhay orfay anotheray e,rôlay ethay erôlay atthay eshay
aterlay amecay otay illfay asay Ueenqay ofay Edensway.

Ethay Empress’say oicechay asway ademay. Erhay esitationhay angspray omfray otheray ausescay.
Anay obstacleay adhay otay ebay emoved;ray itay asway ethay earnay elationshipray existingay
etweenbay ethay Andgray Ukeday Eterpay anday ethay Incesspray Ikefay ofay Erbstzay. Ethay ointpay
asway eferredray otay ethay Archbishopay ofay Ovgorodnay anday ethay Ynod,say ethay actsfay ofay
ethay elationshipray eingbay ivengay anday ethay youngay ady’slay amenay ithheld--suchway
asway Elisabeth’say assionpay orfay ecrecysay. Ethay Ynodsay eportedray atthay ethay Urchchay
adhay onay objectionay otay ethay arriage;may atthay ethay ouplecay ereway ousinscay idday
otnay ountcay incesay eythay ereway elatedray onay ethay aternalmay idesay only.ay Eirthay
elationshipray asway ereforethay erelymay E“thay adowshay ofay aay elationship.”ray

Illstay ethay impatientay Empressay esitatedhay. Aay econdsay obstacleay eterredday erhay.
Isthay imetay itay asway aay uestionqay orfay ysiciansphay otnay ergymenclay otay ettlesay.
Estocqlay asway aay ysicianphay anday Estocqlay adhay erioussay eservationsray egardingray
ethay immediateay arriagemay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday. Ehlinstay ayssay atthay Estocqlay
adviseday ethay Empressay otay aitway atay eastlay anotheray yearay ilewhay otheray emoirsmay
aysay atthay ethay Anoverhay ysicianphay oldtay ethay Empressay otay ostponepay ethay oy’sbay
arriagemay untilay ehay asway enty-onetway. Itay asway ainplay otay allay observersay atthay
ethay oybay asway under-sizeday anday under-developeday orfay ishay age.ay Ethay Englishay
ambassadoray aidsay ofay im,hay E“Hay ookslay eryvay unypay anday ehay isay otnay allertay
atay ourteenfay anthay ethay eneralitygay ofay ildren,chay otnay emarkablyray all,smay
areay atay en.”tay Ethay orstway ofay itay asway atthay ehay idday otnay improveay inay ishay ewnay
environment.ay

Ethay Andgray Uke’sday italityvay asway owlay. Eneverwhay anythingay entway ong,wray ehay
ellfay illay anday ehay ecoveredray utbay owlyslay. Ethay orbidmay elationray etweenbay
imselfhay anday ishay overnorgay Erbrümmay ontinuedcay unabateday underay ethay auspicesay
ofay ishay adoringay utbay ignorantay aunt.ay Enesscay ofay iolencevay ooktay aceplay ichwhay
ademay ethay amiableay Ehlin’sstay airhay andstay onay enday utbay ichwhay ehay oncealedcay
omfray ethay easy-goingay Empress.ay Ishay upilpay asway errorizedtay anday owbeatenbray
ybay ethay Ussianpray officeray anday ethay oolishfay oybay adhay onay otheray ideaay ofay
elf-defensesay anthay otay ightfay ackbay ithway usteringblay impotentay ageray. Ehay entway
osay arfay asay otay eatenthray Erbrümmay ithway ishay aggerday. Undoubtedlyay ethay eakway oybay
ouldcay ebay irritating.ay

Ustjay eforebay Istmaschray 1743,ay Eterpay ellfay esperatelyday ill.ay Ishay auntay asway
inay aay anic;pay eathday adhay obbedray erhay osay often.ay Ereway allay erhay ansplay otay ebay
oughtbray otay aughtnay onay ethay eveay ofay eirthay ightbray ulfilment?fay Eshay astcay allay
autioncay otay ethay indsway anday ecidedday otay ingbray ethay Ermangay Incesspray otay Ussiaray
atay once.ay Erbrümmay asway entsay otay itewray aay etterlay invitingay ethay othermay anday
aughterday orfay aay isitvay. Arcelyscay asway isthay etterlay ispatchedday anthay Erbrümmay
asway entsay otay itewray anotheray iddingbay ethay adieslay otay akemay astehay. Elisabethay
asway off;ay othingnay ouldcay opstay erhay ownay. Erhay ustomarycay indolenceay aidlay
aside,ay eshay ummonedsay Erbrümmay againay afteray aay ewfay aysday adhay elapseday anday
emandedday otay owknay etherwhay ethay uestsgay omfray Erbstzay ereway otnay alreadyay onay
eirthay ayway. Ethay officeray ayedplay ishay artpay etweenbay ethay otway adieslay ellway. Otay
ethay Empressay ehay aidsay atthay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay ishedway onlyay orfay ingsway
otay omecay yingflay otay erhay Ajestymay. Otay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay ehay otewray atthay
ethay invitationay asway ueday otay ishay evotedday ervicessay onay ehalfbay ofay ethay Ousehay
ofay Olsteinhay. Ehay ontinuedcay otay ullybay ethay ospectivepray idegroombray ustjay asay
uchmay asay ever.ay


2ay

Ilewhay Er’sbrümmay etterlay asway avelingtray omfray Etersburgpay otay Erlin,bay
ethay Ettinstay amilyfay asway endingspay Istmaschray inay Erbstzay ithway Uncleay
Ohannjay Udwiglay. Erethay ereway eethray ildrenchay atay isthay ime:tay Ike,fay Itzfray
anday Ischen,lay ethay abybay owhay adhay eenbay amednay orfay ethay oriousglay Ussianray
inswomankay. Istmaschray atay Erbstzay asway aay obersay Utheranlay Estivalfay ithway
uchmay ymnhay ingingsay inay ichwhay Ikefay idday otnay ine,shay anday iftsgay ofay andiworkhay
inay ichwhay eshay excelled.ay Amecay Ylvesterabend,say enwhay ethay uturefay ancay ebay
impsedglay inay andle-flames,cay inay itsbay ofay oltenmay ead,lay anday imilarsay angestray
essengersmay ofay atefay. Itay asway aay ightnay orfay Uleinfräay Aynkhay otay eesay ostsghay
ifay eshay everay awsay em,thay orfay aay ouriercay asway idingray omfray Erlinbay otay Erbstzay
earingbay estinyday inay ethay ormfay ofay Er’sbrümmay etterlay.

Onay ethay orningmay ofay Ewnay Year’say ayday ethay amilyfay allay entway otay urchchay. Enwhay
ethay ellsbay eganbay otay ingray ethay ittlelay ocessionpray emergeday omfray ethay astle,cay
otway iffstay olday enmay anday aay ailfray ittlelay ine-year-oldnay oybay accompanieday
ybay eirthay umerousnay omenway olk,fay amongay omwhay ethay youthfulay Ophiesay alkedway
asay alltay asay anyay ofay emthay. Itay asway imetay atthay eshay ouldshay ebay arried,may utbay
owerlessday anday ainplay owhay asway eshay otay indfay aay usband?hay Ike’sfay oughtsthay
ereway atay isthay imetay ixedfay onay erhay Uncleay Eorge,gay aay youngeray otherbray ofay erhay
other’smay owhay adhay eenbay ayingpay erhay ourtcay. Althoughay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay
adhay encourageday erhay other’sbray uit,say iewingvay imhay avorablyfay asay aay irdbay inay
ethay and,hay ethay elancholymay Eorgegay adhay otnay eallyray askeday ishay iecenay otay arrymay
imhay. Ill,stay onay isthay Ewnay Year’say ayday Ike’sfay oughtsthay ereway ithway erhay uncleay
asay eshay angsay outay ofay eykay ithway ethay othersay ethay ong,lay antingchay ymnshay ofay ethay
Utheranlay ervicesay.

Ilewhay ethay amilyfay atsay atay innerday ethay ouriercay arrived.ay Aay ackagepay ofay
etterslay asway andedhay otay ethay Eneralgay owhay oretay offay ethay outsideay overingcay anday
avegay aay ickthay issivemay otay ishay ifeway. Asay ethay Incesspray ead,ray erhay aughterday
ittingsay extnay otay erhay aughtcay ightsay ofay ethay ordsway “..ay. ithway ethay Incesspray
youray eldestay aughter.”day Omfray atthay omentmay Uncleay Eorgegay asway orgottenfay.
Ethay ewdshray irlgay uessedgay ethay ontentscay ofay ethay elve-pagetway etterlay inay erhay
other’smay andshay althoughay othingnay asway aidsay otay erhay. Erhay arentspay utshay
emselvesthay upay inay ethay ibrarylay orfay eethray aysday ithway ostentatiousay ecrecysay
ilewhay ethay estray ofay ethay ouseholdhay uzzedbay ithway excitement.ay Ehindbay ethay
osedclay oorsday ethay olday Eneralgay asway uttingpay upay aay ubbornstay esistanceray. Ehay
idday otnay ishway otay endsay ishay aughterday otay Ussiaray orfay ethay amesay easonray atthay
Ederickfray idday otnay ishway otay endsay ishay istersay erethay.

At“ay ethay expressay anday articularpay ommandcay ofay erhay Imperialay Ighness,”hay aidsay
Er’sbrümmay etter,lay I“ay avehay otay informay you,ay Adame,may atthay ethay Empressay
ishesway atthay youray Ighnesshay accompanieday ybay ethay Incesspray youray eldestay
aughter,day allshay omecay itherhay asay oonsay asay ossiblepay anday ithoutway osslay ofay
imetay anday epairray otay ateverwhay aceplay ethay Imperialay Ourtcay atay ethay omentmay aymay
ebay. Youray Ighnesshay isay ootay everclay otnay otay understanday ethay uetray eaningmay ofay
ethay impatienceay ofay ethay Empressay otay eesay youay erehay asay ellway asay ethay Incesspray
youray aughterday ofay omwhay eportray ashay aidsay osay uchmay atthay isay ovelylay. Erethay areay
imestay enwhay ethay oicevay ofay ethay orldway isay otnay otheray anthay ethay oicevay ofay Odgay.

At“ay ethay amesay imetay ouray incomparableay Onarchmay ashay expresslyay argedchay emay otay
informay youray Ighnesshay atthay ishay Ighness,hay youray onsort,cay allshay underay onay
ircumstancescay omecay ithway you.ay Erhay Ajestymay ashay eryvay importantay easonsray
orfay ishingway itay osay. Aay ordway omfray youray Ighnesshay ill,way Iay elieve,bay ebay allay
atthay isay ecessarynay otay ulfillfay ethay illway ofay ouray ivineday Empress.”ay Erbrümmay
encloseday anay orderay orfay entay ousandthay ublesray ayablepay inay Erlinbay anday anotheray
editcray orfay otway ousandthay ublesray ayablepay inay Etersburgpay.

Aay econdsay ouriercay arriveday otway ourshay aterlay ingingbray aay etterlay omfray Ingkay
Ederickfray o,whay ikelay Er,brümmay ooktay allay ethay editcray orfay ethay invitation,ay
urgeday ethay eednay ofay ecrecy,say anday epeatedray ethay injunctionay ofay ethay Empressay
aboutay eavinglay ethay Eneralgay atay omehay. Elisabethay Etrovnapay uessedgay atthay
Ike’sfay atherfay ouldway ebay aay indrancehay otay erhay ansplay. Eshay adhay oughtbay offay
ethay uardiangay ofay Arlkay Eterpay Ulrichay ybay ansferringtray otay imhay ethay oy’sbay ownay
aimclay otay ethay Edishsway onethray. Inay ethay amesay annycay irit,spay eshay imitedlay erhay
ealingsday otay ethay othermay ofay ethay idebray omwhay eshay antedway orfay ethay Andgray Ukeday
anday excludeday ethay irl’sgay atherfay omfray anyay areshay inay ethay egotiationsnay.
Avinghay utpay ethay Eneralgay irmlyfay inay ishay aceplay eshay eftlay itay otay ishay
over-lord,ay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussia,pray otay eepkay imhay erethay. Evenay adhay ethay Incepray
eenbay aay anmay ofay aggressiveay aracter,chay ichwhay ehay ertainlycay asway ot,nay ishay
andshay ouldcay otnay avehay eenbay iedtay oremay effectively.ay

Eethray aysday ufficedsay otay emolishday ethay Eneral’sgay esistanceray. Onay ethay ourthfay
ofay Anuary,jay ethay Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay ennedpay erhay epliesray otay ethay
etterslay. Erhay orrespondencecay ithway Elisabethay ashay unfortunatelyay eenbay ost;lay
ethay Empressay asway otoriouslynay arelesscay ithway etterslay. Inay erhay answeray otay
Ederickfray ethay Incesspray eclaredday erhay intentionay ofay owingbay otay ethay illway
ofay Ovidencepray anday ofay ollowingfay ethay instructionsay ofay ethay Empressay otay ethay
astlay etailday exceptingay one.ay I“ay understanday ompletelycay ethay ecessitynay orfay
ecrecysay ichwhay youray Ajestymay ashay ecommendedray. Yetay orfay ariousvay easons,ray
ichwhay ancay ebay oremay easilyay understooday anthay itten,wray Iay avehay eenbay obligeday
otay initiateay ethay Ince,pray osewhay iscretionday Iay illway uarantee,gay intoay ethay
ecretsay. Iay opehay erebythay otay avehay eritedmay onay eproach.”ray Eshay adhay eallyray
onsideredcay ethay ossibilitypay ofay akingtay Ikefay offay otay Ussiaray ithoutway erhay
ather’sfay owledgeknay.

Eparationspray orfay ethay ourneyjay ereway implesay. Ethay ousseautray ofay ethay Ermangay
Incesspray onsistedcay ofay ittlelay oremay anthay aay avelingtray apprenticeay ightmay
avehay arriedcay inay ishay undlebay. Eethray esses,dray aay ozenday emises,chay anday asay
anymay andkerchiefshay ereway allay atthay Ikefay adhay otay ackpay orfay atthay id-wintermay
ourneyjay. Ethay Aronessbay onvay Inzenpray owhay afterwardsay aidsay inay erhay emoirsmay
atthay eshay adhay elpedhay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray otay ackpay erhay unkstray orfay Ussiaray
atherray overstateday ethay asecay. Ethay ackingpay ofay Ike’sfay unkstray ustmay avehay
eenbay aay implesay attermay. Itay asway aay ourcesay ofay ife-longlay agrinchay otay erhay
atthay eshay amecay otay Ussiaray ithoutway aay idalbray estchay. Erhay othermay atay eastlay
adhay adhay atthay. Eshay adhay onay ed-linenbay ofay erhay ownay anday asway obligeday otay useay
erhay other’smay eetsshay. Onay eeperday umiliationhay orfay aay Ermangay idebray ancay
ebay imagined.ay Evenay asay anay olday omanway Ikefay ouldcay otnay orgetfay it.ay Itay asway
omethingsay ichwhay eshay adhay alwaysay otay akemay up.ay Ecausebay eshay adhay omecay ithoutway
eetsshay otay Ussiaray eshay asway obligeday otay utpay oughthray ethay Artitionpay ofay Olandpay.

Onay ethay 10thay ofay Anuary,jay 1744,ay Ike’sfay othermay etsay orth,fay ostensiblyay
orfay ethay Erlinbay Arnivalcay. Ethay artypay onsistedcay ofay ethay Eneral,gay owhay asway
otay accompanyay emthay asay arfay asay Edt,schway ethay Incesspray anday erhay aughter,day
otway attendantay Uleins,fräay anay officeray amednay Attorf,lay anday aay ookcay. Eythay
ademay eirthay irstfay opstay inay Erlinbay. Ethay Incesspray astenedhay otay anay audienceay
ithway ethay Ingkay anday Inistermay onvay Odewilspay owhay investeday erhay ithway ethay
esponsibilityray ofay urtheringfay ethay Ussianpray ausecay ithway ethay Ussianray
Empress.ay

Inay Erlin,bay ethay Incesspray ontinuedcay asay ormerlyfay otay eglectnay erhay aughterday.
Erhay actlessnesstay asway illustrateday ybay anay incidentay escribedday inay Ike’sfay
emoirsmay. En“Whay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussia,pray owhay ewknay exactlyay ethay objectay ofay ethay
ourney,jay earnedlay atthay Iay adhay arriveday inay Erlin,bay ehay ishedway ithoutway ailfay
otay eesay emay. Ymay othermay aidsay Iay asway ill.ay Otway aysday aterlay ehay ausedcay erhay otay ebay
inviteday otay innerday ithway ethay Ueen,qay ishay onsort,cay anday expresslyay equestedray
erhay otay ingbray emay ithway erhay. Ymay othermay omisedpray utbay enwhay ethay imetay amecay
eshay entway aloneay otay ethay ourtcay. Enwhay ethay Ingkay awsay erhay ehay inquireday aboutay
emay. Eshay epliedray atthay Iay asway ill.ay Ereuponwhay ehay epliedray atthay ehay ellway ewknay
atthay itay asway otnay uetray. Enthay eshay aidsay atthay Iay asway otnay esseddray orfay ourt,cay
otay ichwhay ehay answereday atthay ehay ouldway ostponepay ethay innerday orfay emay untilay ethay
extnay ayday. Inally,fay ymay othermay aidsay atthay Iay adhay onay ourtcay essdray. Ehay ordereday
atthay oneay ofay ishay isterssay ouldshay endsay emay one.ay Atay astlay ymay othermay awsay erethay
asway onay ayway outay ofay itay anday entsay emay ordway atthay Iay ouldshay essdray yselfmay anday
omecay otay ethay alace.”pay

Itay asway atelay inay ethay afternoonay enwhay Inderellacay arrived.ay Uringday uppersay eshay
atsay atay ethay ightray andhay ofay ethay Ing,kay owhay aidpay erhay elaborateay eighteenthay
enturycay omplimentscay. Ethay yshay irlgay ushedblay uriously,fay utbay eptkay erhay eadhay.
Itay asway ethay oneay anday onlyay eetingmay ofay esethay otway eatgray onarchsmay. Etweenbay
ethay Incesspray ofay ourteenfay anday ethay Ingkay ofay irty-onethay onay italvay ontactcay
asway ade;may itay asway anay officialay occasion.ay Utbay ishay atteryflay ingeredlay ithway
erhay alwaysay ikelay aay easantplay eamdray. Eshay onlyay atedhay istersay Ulrica,ay owhay asway
ootay eciouspray otay ebay entsay otay Ussiaray anday osewhay essdray ethay Ingkay adhay offereday
otay endlay erhay.

Inay ethay iddlemay ofay Anuary,jay ethay Incess’spray oachcay olledray outay ofay Erlinbay.
Umberinglay oughthray ethay eepday ozenfray utsray ofay ethay outeray eets,stray itay ooktay
aay ortherlynay irectionday asay ifay omewardhay oundbay orfay Ettinstay. Ethay owlesssnay
interway obligeday ethay artypay otay aveltray onay eelswhay asay arfay asay Iga,ray ilewhay ethay
itterbay indsway eepingsway ownday omfray ethay Alticbay atersway ademay ethay ourneyjay aay
everesay ordeal.ay Eythay ostlay onay ime,tay oweverhay. Ederickfray adhay ordereday eshfray
elaysray ofay orseshay atay everyay ostpay. Onay expenseay adhay eenbay ared;spay ereway otnay
ethay ublesray ofay ethay Ussianray Empressay otay aypay orfay everything?ay Utbay ealray
omfortcay asway otnay ocurablepray atay anyay icepray. Ewfay avellers,tray exceptay ethay
ouriers,cay ooktay ethay ostpay oadray omfray Erlinbay otay Etersburgpay atay isthay imetay ofay
ethay year.ay Ethay uartersqay inay ichwhay ethay artypay oughtsay eirthay ight’snay odginglay
ereway ustjay endurable.ay As“ay ethay oomsray inay ethay ationsstay ereway otnay eated,”hay
ethay Incesspray otewray erhay usband,hay E“way ereway obligeday otay ogay intoay ethay ommoncay
oomray ichwhay asway otnay unlikeay aay ig-sty;pay ethay astermay anday istress,may ethay ousehay
og,day ethay ockcay anday ethay ildren,--childrenchay everywhere,ay inay adles,cray inay
eds,bay onay ethay ove,stay onay attresses--everythingmay asway olledray ogethertay inay
isorderday ikelay eedsway anday ootsray. Erethay asway othingnay elseay otay ebay one;day Iay
ordereday aay enchbay otay ebay oughtbray anday aylay ownday inay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay oom.”ray

Inay itespay ofay ethay oldcay anday iscomfort,day eythay astenedhay onward,ay oughthray ethay
ortshay aysday anday ethay onglay ightsnay. Ethay Incesspray otewray erhay usbandhay aboutay anay
encounteray ithway obbersray utbay erhay aughter’sday escriptionday ofay ethay ourneyjay
ontainscay onay eferenceray otay anyay adventureay ofay isthay indkay. Oremay excitingay
orfay Ikefay asway ethay eatgray ometcay ofay 1744ay ichwhay eythay awsay ilewhay ossingcray
Ourlandcay. Againstay ethay ackgroundbay ofay ethay onglay ackblay ightsnay anday ethay
ediumtay ofay ethay ever-endingnay ourney,jay accenteday ybay ethay oof-beatshay ofay ethay
yingflay orses,hay ethay ometcay ingeredlay inay ethay irl’sgay emorymay asay omethingsay
awfulay anday unforgettable.ay Ethay oldcay ewgray orseway anday orseway. Ethay adieslay oreway
oollenway asksmay otay eepkay eirthay acesfay omfray eezingfray. Ike’sfay eetfay uccumbedsay
otay ethay ostfray anday ereway osay ollensway atthay eshay adhay otay ebay arriedcay otay anday omfray
ethay arriagecay. Eshay alsoay ademay erselfhay illay inkingdray eerbay. In“ay esethay astlay
aysday Iay adhay aay ittlelay indigestion,”ay eshay otewray otay earday Apa,pay Ut“bay itay ashay
adhay onay urtherfay onsequencescay. Iay asway artlypay yselfmay otay ameblay ecausebay Iay
adhay unkdray allay ethay eerbay Iay ouldcay indfay alongay ethay ayway. Earday Amamay ashay utpay aay
opstay otay at,thay anday Iay amay ellway again.”ay Isthay asway iggishpray Ikefay avellingtray
otay Ussiaray inay erhay ifteenthfay year.ay Eshay obeyeday erhay earday Amamay utbay earday Apapay
ouldcay understanday erhay etterbay aboutay ethay eerbay.

Avinghay aidsay oodbyegay atay Edt,schway ethay Eneralgay eturnedray otay Ettinstay ithway
ishay ecretsay. Ethay owntay arkedmay ethay isappearanceday ofay ishay ifeway anday aughterday
anday umorsray eganbay otay irculatecay. Eythay ademay ethay Incepray uncomfortable.ay
Ehay otewray aay etterlay ichwhay overtookay ethay Incesspray atay Inköslay anday askeday
ermissionpay otay announceay ethay ourneyjay inay ethay ewspapersnay. Utbay ethay Incesspray
aidsay onay. It“ay eemssay otay emay essentialay atthay youay ouldshay oldhay ackbay ethay
announcementay inay ethay ewspapersnay ofay ymay ourneyjay untilay Iay avehay assedpay Emelmay.
Ikewiselay ethay ayerspray orfay aay afesay ourneyjay ichwhay youay anplay otay avehay aidsay inay
ethay urcheschay ofay Erbstzay ustmay ebay ostponed.”pay Asay arfay asay Emel,may eshay eltfay
atthay eshay ouldcay anagemay ethay iptray ithoutway anyay ecialspay aiday omfray Ovidencepray.
Omfray Igsbergkönay eshay otewray otay Ike’sfay andmother,gray owhay ewdray aay yearlyay
ensionpay ofay entay ousandthay ublesray omfray ethay Ussianray Empress.ay Ethay ageday
Uchessday asway ethay onlyay oneay ofay Ophie’ssay elativesray owhay idday otnay oinjay ethay
otestpray againstay ethay arriagemay. Ethay Abbessay ofay Uedlinburgqay anday ethay Uchessday
ofay Unswickbray ereway outraged.ay Eythay eapedhay eproachesray onay ethay eadhay ofay ethay
Eneralgay om,whay ithoutway egardray otay ustice,jay eythay ademay ethay apegoatscay orfay
ishay ife’sway oceedingspray. Eythay ombardedbay ethay Incepray ithway onglay etterslay
ichwhay emindedray imhay ofay ethay agictray atefay ofay Incesspray Arlottechay owhay adhay
arriedmay Alexeiay Etrovichpay anday ethay adsay ightplay ofay ethay Unswickbray amilyfay
imprisoneday ybay Elisabeth.ay Ethay Incepray asway arassedhay ybay Olsteinhay anday Anhaltay
elativesray atay ethay amesay ime,tay incesay ehay adhay uckilylay emainedray erewhay othbay
idessay ofay ethay amilyfay ouldcay etgay atay imhay anday elieveray eirthay eelingsfay. Ethay
Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay asway otnay urprised;say eshay adhay otnay expecteday
eirthay upportsay.

I“ay idday otnay oubt,”day eshay otewray otay erhay usband,hay At“thay ouray ourneyjay otay
Oscowmay ouldway irstay upay aay ormstay. Eligionray anday ivalryray ivegay ethay estbay
oundsgray orfay atthay. Utbay ethay Antetay E[thay Abbess]ay asay ittlelay asay eway ouldway avehay
adhay ethay owerpay otay urntay asideay ethay iseway ecreesday ofay Ovidencepray. Eway annotcay
ascribeay ymay ourneyjay erehay anday ethay entireay ircumstancecay otay anythingay elseay
anday eway ancay ebay assureday atthay ethay All-Wiseay Oneay ulfilsfay erebythay urposespay
orfay usay inscrutable.”ay Otay argumentsay ikelay isthay ethay iouspay Eneralgay adhay onay
eplyray. Utbay illstay isturbedday ybay emoriesmay ofay ethay unhappyay arriagemay ofay
Incesspray Arlotte,chay ehay askeday ishay ifeway otay iffenstay ethay ermstay onay Ophie’ssay
ehalfbay inay ethay arriagemay ontractcay. Ehay antedway orfay ishay aughterday ethay
uaranteegay ofay aay ensionpay ithway aay omehay ifay ossiblepay inay Olsteinhay ifay otnay inay
Ivonialay. Othingnay ofay ethay indkay asway everay evenay iscussedday ybay ishay ifeway afteray
erhay arrivalay inay Ussiaray.

Anksthay otay ethay oresightfay ofay ethay Incess,pray onenay ofay isthay oppositionay asway
artedstay untilay othermay anday aughterday ereway afesay eyondbay ethay Ussianray orderbay.
Asay arfay asay Iga,ray ethay Incesspray avelledtray underay ethay amenay ofay ethay Ountesscay
ofay Einbeck,rhay ethay ognomencay ichwhay Erbrümmay adhay uggestedsay orfay ethay urposepay.
Inay Ike’sfay emoirs,may eshay ayssay atthay erhay othermay assumeday aay ictitiousfay amenay
orfay ethay ourneyjay utbay eshay ouldcay onay ongerlay ememberray it.ay Atay Igaray ethay
avellerstray ereway etmay ybay escorts,ay omplimentscay anday esentspray. At“ay id-day,”may
otewray ethay Incess,pray I“ay etmay Amberlainchay Arishkin,nay omwhay erhay Imperialay
Ajestymay adhay acedplay atay ethay eadhay ofay aay uardgay ofay onorhay atthay amecay otay eetmay
emay asay aay arkmay ofay istinctionday. Ehay oughtbray emay etterslay anday eetingsgray omfray
erhay Ajestymay owhay overwhelmeday emay ithway onorshay anday omplimentscay. Aay uarterqay
ofay aay ilemay omfray ethay itycay Iay asway etmay ybay Ice-Governorvay Incepray Olgorukovday.
Eway ovedray acrossay ethay iceay ofay ethay Inadway. Asay ethay arriagecay inay ichwhay Iay asway
ittingsay asway ustjay eyondbay ethay enday ofay ethay eatgray idge,bray ethay irstfay alvosay
asway iredfay omfray ethay eatgray unsgay onay ethay ortressesfay. Iay oundfay eadyray otay apwray
usay inay ethay eighslay otway endidsplay ablessay overedcay ithway oldgay ocadebray orfay ymay
aughterday anday yself,may otway ollarscay ofay ethay amesay urfay anday aay overletcay ofay
anotheray ur,fay uiteqay asay eautiful.”bay

Appedwray inay eirthay ichray ables,say ethay avellerstray imbedclay intoay ethay onglay
Ussianray eigh,slay esignedday ybay Eterpay ethay Eat,gray anday ewflay overay ethay owysnay
ausséeschay atthay edlay otay Etersburgpay. Onay aay ittlebray Ebruaryfay ayday eythay
arriveday atay ethay Interway Alacepay. Ethay Empressay anday ethay ourtcay adhay onegay awayay
otay Oscowmay. Etersburgpay asway empty,ay utbay aay allsmay oupgray ofay ourtierscay adhay
emainedray otay elcomeway ethay Ermangay uestsgay. Ethay Incesspray asway oremay anthay
edazzledbay ybay ethay eceptionray eythay avegay erhay. It“ay eemssay asay ifay Iay ereway inay
ethay uitesay ofay erhay Imperialay Ajestymay oray ofay omesay eatgray onarchmay. Itay oesday
otnay eemsay ealray atthay allay isthay ancay appenhay otay oorpay e,may orfay omwhay atay onlyay aay
ewfay acesplay aay umdray asway everay irredstay anday atay othersay otnay evenay atthay. Erehay
everythingay oesgay onay inay uchsay agnificentmay anday espectfulray ylestay atthay itay
eemedsay otay emay enthay anday ownay atay ethay ightsay ofay ethay uxurylay urroundingsay emay asay
ifay itay allay ereway onlyay aay eam.”dray

Ike’sfay emoriesmay ofay erhay arrivalay inay Etersburgpay areay appropriateay otay aay
ourteen-year-oldfay irlgay. Eshay ememberedray ethay amesnay ofay ethay ourfay youngay
adieslay ofay onorhay owhay amecay orwardfay otay elcomeway erhay anday ethay amesnay ofay
ethay enmay eythay ubsequentlysay arried;may ethay ourteenfay elephantsay ichwhay ethay
Ahshay ofay Ersiapay adhay ivengay otay ethay Empressay anday ichwhay actuallyay erformedpay
ickstray inay ethay owysnay alacepay ourt-yard;cay ethay arnivalcay anday ethay onderfulway
oastingcay expeditionay edlay ybay Emionsay Yrilovichkay Arishkin;nay aboveay allay eshay
ememberedray anday escribedday otay ethay astlay otknay anday ingletray ethay extraordinaryay
ylestay ofay air-dressinghay avoredfay ybay erhay ewnay Ussianray iendsfray. Onceay inay
ethay Etersburgpay alace,pay ethay irlgay omptlypray orgotfay allay ethay ardshipshay ofay
ethay ourneyjay. Erhay other,may aay ittlelay iredtay utbay everay usybay ithway erhay en,pay
ontinuedcay erhay eamstray ofay orrespondencecay ithway Erbstzay anday Erlinbay. Ike“Fay
earsbay ethay atiguefay etterbay anthay I,ay yetay eway areay othbay ell,way aisepray ebay otay
Odgay. Aymay Ehay ontinuecay otay uidegay anday irectday us.”ay Isthay otay erhay usband,hay ethay
Eneral;gay otay Ingkay Ederick,fray eshay otewray atherray esslay iously:pay Onsidering“Cay
ethay ardshipshay ofay ethay eason,say ethay ourneyjay anday ethay angechay ofay air,ay Iay
ouldshay eednay otay avehay anay ironay onstitutioncay otay eepkay upay ymay esistanceray. Ymay
aughterday isay oremay ortunatefay. Erhay youthay upportssay erhay ealthhay anday ikelay
youngay oldierssay owhay ornscay angerday ecausebay eythay owknay othingnay aboutay it,ay eshay
elightsday inay ethay endorsplay ybay ichwhay eshay isay urrounded.”say

Inay omesay ubtlesay ay,way ethay onqueringcay iritspay ofay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay
eganbay otay ailfay erhay asay oonsay asay eshay arriveday inay Ussiaray. Itay asway equallyay
evidentay atthay Ike,fay omfray ethay omentmay enwhay Arishkinnay elpedhay erhay ithway aay
estjay intoay ethay eighslay atay Iga,ray asway immingsway ithway ethay urrentcay. Otnay atthay
ethay Incesspray asway awareay ofay allingfay ehindbay inay ethay aceray. Ourageouscay anday
onfident,cay eshay attackeday ethay eatgray asktay eforebay er,hay erhay iplomaticday
issionmay omfray Ingkay Ederickfray anday onvay Odewilspay. Eshay adhay oundfay everythingay
inay Etersburgpay ustjay asay eythay adhay aidsay. Ingsthay adhay otay ebay angedchay.
Estushev,bay ethay enemyay ofay Ussia,pray ustmay ogay. Ilewhay erhay othermay ursuedpay
esethay oliticalpay interests,ay Ikefay asway earninglay otay andstay onay erhay ownay eetfay
inay aay angestray environment.ay Orfay ethay irstfay imetay eshay alloweday erselfhay ethay
uxurylay ofay aay old-bloodedcay udgmentjay ofay ethay Incess’spray aracterchay. Itay
appenedhay onay ethay ourneyjay omfray Etersburgpay otay Oscowmay.

After“ay ethay epartureday omfray Etersburg,”pay ayssay Ike,fay E“thay eighslay inay ichwhay
ymay othermay anday Iay ereway avelingtray uckstray inay urningtay againstay aay ouse,hay
erebywhay anay ironay ookhay ecamebay islodgedday anday ell,fay ikingstray ymay othermay
onay ethay eadhay anday ouldershay. Eshay insisteday atthay eshay asway everelysay urthay
utbay outwardlyay erethay asway othingnay otay ebay een,say otnay evenay aay uisebray. Isthay
incidentay elayedday ouray ourneyjay ybay everalsay ours.”hay Inay escribingday ethay
accident,ay erhay othermay ays,say I“ay elievedbay yselfmay otay ebay oundedway utbay Iay asway
otnay. Ethay owblay adhay uckstray ithway ullfay engthstray againstay ethay ur;fay otherwise,ay
ithoutway oubt,day ymay ead,hay ecknay anday armay ouldway avehay eenbay ushed.”cray Onlyay ethay
ostlycay ursfay ivengay ybay ethay Empressay adhay avedsay erhay.

Ithway isthay oneay interruption,ay ethay aintray ofay irtythay eighs,slay eachay awndray
ybay entay orses,hay ashedday onwarday ithoutway ausepay. Eythay intendeday otay arriveay
inay Oscowmay eforebay ethay Andgray Uke’sday irthday,bay onay ethay enty-firsttway ofay
Ebruaryfay. Ethay ayway asway eparedpray. Onfiresbay urnedbay atay ightnay alongay ethay
owysnay ighwayhay. Ost-stationspay angspray upay uddenlysay outay ofay ethay ow-drifts,snay
eadyray ithway othay offeecay anday ishfay oup,say ilewhay eshfray orseshay oodstay aitingway
inay eirthay ugasday. Ethay excitementay asway intense.ay Atay ourfay o’clockay onay ethay
irdthay ay,day ethay yingflay aintray amecay uddenlysay otay aay althay ithinway eventysay
erstsvay ofay Oscowmay. Anay envoyay omfray ethay Empressay etmay ethay artypay erehay ithway
ethay equestray atthay eythay ouldshay elayday eirthay entranceay intoay Oscowmay untilay
afteray arknessday adhay allenfay. Ilewhay eythay aited,way ethay avellerstray arrayeday
emselvesthay ithway asay uchmay arecay asay ossiblepay. Ikefay utpay onay aay ose-fittingclay
essdray ofay ose-coloredray oirémay ilk,say immedtray ithway ilversay.

Ethay orseshay ereway againay utpay otay ethay eighs,slay isthay imetay ixteensay insteaday
ofay entay otay each,ay anday ethay aintray eapedlay orwardfay. Ievers,say ethay Empress’say
envoy,ay eatedsay imselfhay esidebay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbst,zay anday urgeday ethay
oachmancay orwardfay atay everyay eathbray inay uetray Ussianray ylestay. Ethay ocessionpray
ewdray upay eforebay ethay Olovingay Alacepay atay eightay o’clockay inay ethay evening.ay Itay
asway ustjay ixsay eeksway incesay ethay ountrycay ousinscay adhay ivendray ithway osay uchmay
autioncay anday ecrecysay outay ofay ethay ittlelay Utheranlay owntay ofay Erbstzay.

Eythay ereway eceivedray onay ethay airwaystay ybay ethay Incepray onvay Essen-Homberg,hay
Eneralgay Adjutantay ofay ethay Empress,ay owhay onductedcay emthay otay eirthay amberschay.
Arcelyscay adhay eythay aidlay asideay eirthay eavyhay ablessay enwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday
amecay unningray intoay eirthay oom,ray unableay ongerlay otay ontrolcay ishay impatienceay
otay eesay emthay. Atay entay o’clockay Estocqlay appeareday ithway eetinggray anday aay
ummonssay omfray ethay Empress.ay Attendeday ybay ethay Incepray onvay Essen-Homberghay
anday ethay Andgray Uke,day ethay otway Incessespray ademay eirthay ayway otay ethay Empress’say
eceptionray oomray. Asay eythay assedpay omfray oomray otay oom,ray ethay ourtcay adieslay
anday entlemengay ereway esentedpray anday owedbay owlay otay emthay. It“ay isay impossibleay
otay aysay owhay allay osethay esentpray aredstay atay esethay Ermansgay omfray eadhay otay
oot,”fay otewray ethay Incesspray otay erhay usbandhay. Yetay osethay ustymay olday auntsay atay
Uedlinburgqay owhay opposeday ethay ourneyjay ouldway avehay ishedway ethay Incesspray ofay
Erbstzay otay oregofay isthay iumphtray.

Ethay Empressay advanceday otay erhay esholdthray otay eetmay emthay. E“Shay alloweday e,”may
exulteday ethay Incess,pray Arcely“scay imetay otay aketay offay ymay ovesglay anday embraceday
e,may Iay ustmay ay,say ithway enderness.”tay Inay etoricalrhay Ench,fray ethay Incesspray
eliveredday anay addressay ofay atitudegray orfay allay ethay Empressay adhay oneday orfay ethay
Olstein-Gottorphay amilyfay. Ethay Empressay epliedray atthay erhay ownay oodblay asway
otnay oremay earday otay erhay anthay atthay ofay ethay Incesspray anday atthay allay eshay adhay
oneday asway othingnay inay omparisoncay ithway atwhay eshay intendeday otay oday. Itay asway aay
eetingmay ofay Eekgray ithway Eekgray. Ikefay asway atay astlay esentedpray anday embraced.ay
Ethay Empressay inviteday ethay ompanycay otay ebay eated,say ut,bay incesay eshay erselfhay
asway ootay exciteday otay itsay own,day obodynay elseay ouldcay oday osay. Ethay eceptionray
astedlay orfay alfhay anay ourhay. Atay oneay ointpay ethay Empressay abruptlyay eftlay ethay
oomray otay oncealcay ethay earstay eshay asway obligeday otay edshay. Eythay ereway alledcay
orthfay ybay ethay ongstray esemblanceray etweenbay ethay Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay
anday erhay eceasedday otherbray onceay etrothedbay otay ethay Empressay Elisabeth.ay
Ike’sfay emoirsmay aysay othingnay ofay esethay ears,tay althoughay erhay othermay asway uchmay
affecteday ybay emthay.

Ikefay eservedpray orfay us,ay owever,hay ethay appearanceay ofay ethay Empressay atay isthay
ime:tay Ore“May anthay anythingay else,ay Iay asway astonisheday ybay erhay eatgray eight,”hay
eshay ayssay. I“ay ustmay aysay oneay ouldcay otnay eholdbay erhay orfay ethay irstfay imetay
ithoutway astonishmentay atay erhay eautybay anday erhay ajestymay. Eshay asway alltay and,ay
oughthay atherray out,stay itay idday otnay etract,day asay onay acklay ofay eedomfray asway
oticeablenay inay erhay ovementsmay. Erhay eadhay asway eryvay eautifulbay. Onay isthay ayday
eshay oreway anay enormousay oop-skirt,hay ichwhay eshay ovedlay otay oday enwhay eshay ademay
aay andgray oilettetay anday ichwhay eshay onlyay idday enwhay eshay owedshay erselfhay inay
