ublicpay. Erhay essdray asway ofay immeringshay ilversay affetatay immedtray ithway oldgay
ace;lay eshay oreway aay ackblay eatherfay onay erhay eadhay andingstay uprightay aay ittlelay
otay oneay idesay ithway anymay iamondsday inay aay oiffurecay ofay erhay ownay air.”hay Ethay
youngay irlgay inay ethay ose-coloredray oirémay ockfray evernay orgotfay ethay icturepay.

Ethay extnay orning,may ethay Incesspray anday erhay aughterday ereway ummonedsay otay ethay
audienceay amberchay ybay ethay Empress.ay A“ay ewfay omentsmay ater,lay ethay Empressay
inay andgray attireay amecay omfray erhay essing-roomdray. Eshay oreway aay ownbray essdray
embroidereday inay ilversay anday uite,qay atthay isay asay arfay asay ead,hay ecknay anday aistway
ereway oncerned,cay overedcay ithway ewels.”jay Eshay esentedpray ethay ibbonray anday arstay
ofay Aintsay Atherinecay otay erhay uestsgay. Enthay eshay assedpay onay otay assmay. Enwhay
eythay extnay awsay er,hay eshay asway onay erhay ayway otay onfession;cay ethay extnay ime,tay otay
ommunioncay. Aay ewfay aysday ater,lay onay erhay ayway otay ethay Oitskytray Onastery,may eshay
amecay otay aysay arewellfay In“ay aay ong-sleevedlay owngay ofay ackblay elvetvay adorneday
ithway allay ethay Ussianray orders;ay atthay is,ay ethay orderay ofay Aintsay Andreway asay aay
arf,scay ofay Aintsay Alexanderay aboutay ethay eck,nay anday ofay Aintsay Atherinecay onay
ethay eftlay ide.”say Erethay eemedsay onay ossiblepay imitlay otay allay isthay andeurgray.
Elisabethay adhay entay ousandthay essesdray anday ivefay ousandthay airspay ofay oesshay.

Utbay Ike,fay erhay other’smay ownay ild,chay asway otnay over-awed.ay Eshay expandeday inay anay
atmosphereay erewhay ostentationay asway ethay uleray. Ithway ecociouspray act,tay ichwhay
eshay oweday eitheray otay erhay ownay andsglay oray otay Abetbay Ardelcay utbay arcelyscay otay
erhay other,may eshay establisheday erselfhay ecurelysay inay isthay itteringglay anday
eacheroustray environment.ay


4ay

Incepray Istianchray Augustay adhay ivengay ishay aughterday aay ookbay asay aay artingpay
iftgay. Itay asway aay eatisetray ybay aay ofessorpray atay Allehay ichwhay iscussedday
atay edioustay engthlay ethay ifferencesday etweenbay eligiousray eedscray. Ehay
adhay eparedpray otay ogay ithway isthay ookbay aay emorandummay ofay instructionsay orfay
ishay aughter’sday use.ay Itay asway eaded:hay O“Pray Emoria,may osay ichay einermay
emahlengay itgegeben.”may Omewheresay alongay ethay oute,ray owhay attentivelyay
ancay ebay imagined,ay Ikefay adhay eadray isthay ocument,day anday adhay ittenwray oneay
ofay erhay immestpray etterslay otay earday Apapay ankingthay imhay orfay ishay Acious“gray
instructions.”ay Ethay irstfay alfhay ofay ethay emorandummay asway akentay upay ithway
eligiousray ounselcay anday ethay econdsay alfhay ithway erhay uturefay arriagemay. Ethay
Eneral’sgay ylestay isay anay awkwarday ontrastcay otay ethay uentflay eciositypray ofay ishay
ifeway. Ehay addresseday ishay aughterday inay ethay irdthay ersonpay anday outlineday erhay
uturefay utiesday us:thay

Ext“Nay otay ethay Empress,ay erhay Ajesty,may eshay ashay otay espectray ethay Andgray Ukeday
aboveay allay asay erhay Ord,lay Ather,fay anday Overeign;say anday ithalway otay inway ybay arecay
anday endernesstay atay everyay opportunityay ishay onfidencecay anday ovelay. Erhay Ordlay
anday Ishay illway areay otay ebay eferredpray otay allay ethay easuresplay anday easurestray ofay
ethay orld;way anday oday othingnay ichwhay ehay islikesday oray ichwhay ausescay imhay onlyay aay
ittlelay ain;pay anday illstay esslay otay insistay onay erhay ownay illway.

Ever“Nay otay enteray intoay amiliarityfay oray adinage,bay utbay alwaysay avehay espectray
asay uchmay asay ossiblepay.

O“Tay egardray ethay omesticsday anday avoritesfay ofay erhay Ordlay ithway aay aciousgray
ien;may otnay otay emandday ethay ervicessay ofay erhay Ordlay utbay everay otay espondray otay ethay
avorfay anday ovelay ofay erhay Ordlay.

O“Tay eakspay ithway onay oneay aloneay inay ethay audienceay amberchay anday otay onductcay
erselfhay alwaysay accordingay otay etiquetteay erethay.

O“Tay etestday anday avoiday ayingplay ardscay orfay ighhay akes,stay ichwhay isay aay arkmay ofay
avariceay anday elf-interestsay.

O“Tay aketay argechay erselfhay ofay ethay ocketpay oneymay ichwhay aymay ebay ivengay er,hay
otay uardgay itay anday otay aypay itay outay aduallygray otay aay ervantsay onay anay account,ay
inay orderay atthay eshay aymay otnay ubmitsay erselfhay otay ethay usteeshiptray ofay aay
overness;gay otay employay itay orfay erhay useay anday easure,play anday ithway itay otay oday
ood,gay inay orderay atthay eshay aymay inway orfay erselfhay anday otnay orfay othersay insteaday
ofay erhay ethay ovelay anday inclinationay ofay erhay ependentsday.

O“Tay intercedeay orfay onay one,ay ecausebay oneay aymay otnay understanday ethay awslay anday aay
one-sideday eportray annotcay ebay usted,tray anday ethay idesay iscriminatedday againstay
ecomesbay aay isgruntledday enemy;ay anday ehay omwhay oneay elpshay outay ithway uchsay
intercessionsay orgetsfay ethay oodgay eedday anday oesgay anday inssay again.ay

Especially“ay otay enteray intoay onay affairsay ofay overnmentgay inay orderay otnay otay
irritateay ethay Enate.”say

Atay ifteenfay Ikefay asway otnay aturemay enoughay otay appreciateay ethay ironyay ofay isthay
ocumentday anday obablypray eshay evernay amecay otay ebay. Ethay abjectay ubmissivenesssay
ichwhay erhay atherfay oughtthay appropriateay otay erhay atusstay asay aay ifeway adhay
ertainlycay evernay eenbay exemplifieday ybay erhay ivaciousvay othermay. Eshay ustmay avehay
eenbay awareay atthay erhay atherfay ayedplay aay inormay artpay inay ethay amilyfay ifelay atay
Ettinstay anday atay Erbst,zay utbay itay asway aay onditioncay inay erhay ittlelay orldway ichwhay
omfray eershay amiliarityfay eemedsay onlyay aturalnay. Atwhay ouldcay ebay oremay ormalnay
anthay atthay ethay anmay ofay ethay amilyfay ouldshay ebay eptkay inay eadinglay ings?stray Ewfay
irlsgay inay erhay ituationsay ouldway avehay ontrastedcay erhay ather’sfay eoriesthay ithway
ishay actionsay anday Ikefay ertainlycay idday otnay.

Ederickfray ethay Eatgray alwaysay eptkay ethay elusionday atthay ehay adhay ayedplay ethay
iefchay erôlay inay isthay Erman-Russiangay arriagemay. Utbay ehay over-estimateday ishay
actualay artpay. Ifay Elisabethay adhay oundfay itay ecessarynay otay iritspay ethay youngay
Incesspray awayay againstay ishay oyalray illway eshay ouldway avehay oneday osay. Incesay itay
asway otnay ecessarynay eshay elcomedway ishay imelytay anday usefulay aid.ay Atay ethay ightray
omentmay Ederickfray omotedpray Incepray Istianchray Augustay otay ethay ostpay ofay Ieldfay
Arshal,may anday afteray Ikefay adhay onegay otay Ussiaray ehay elpedhay otay econcileray erhay
atherfay otay erhay onversioncay. Y“May oodgay Incepray ofay Erbstzay asway eryvay estiveray onay
isthay oint,”pay ehay otewray. I“ay adhay aay eatgray ealday ofay oubletray inay overcomingay ishay
eligiousray uplesscray. Ehay espondedray otay allay ymay epresentationsray ith:way Eine‘May
Ochtertay ichtnay Iechischgray erden!’”way Ishay ugglesstray iedday awayay aduallygray
underay ethay actfultay eatmenttray ofay ishay ee-thinkingfray Ingkay owhay ersuadedpay
imhay atthay Eekgray anday Utheranlay ereway ethay amesay. Utherisch-Griechisch,“Lay
Iechisch-Lutherisch,gray asday ehetgay an,”ay ethay ubmissivesay Eneralgay epeatedray.
Ifay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray aidsay osay atwhay elseay ouldcay aay Ussianpray officeray eply?ray

Ethay arriagemay asway ademay ybay eethray omenway. Itay asway egunbay ybay ethay Incesspray
ofay Erbstzay anday ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray anday arriedcay oughthray ybay ethay
ifteen-year-oldfay Ikefay owhay ooktay argechay ofay ethay ampaigncay erselfhay enwhay
erhay other’smay acticstay ailedfay. Onenay ofay ethay en-folkmay owhay ightmay avehay eenbay
expecteday otay influenceay ethay ituationsay idday osay. Osethay ikelay Estocqlay anday ethay
Incepray ofay Erbstzay owhay offereday ontrarycay adviceay ereway over-ridden.ay Ethay
othersay ereway ermittedpay otay ayplay ethay artpay ofay enevolentbay ystandersbay.

IKEfay ECOMESbay ATHERINEcay


Y“May aughter,”day otewray Ike’sfay ather,fay Is“ay alreadyay osay ellway oundedgray inay erhay
eligionray atthay eshay owsknay ethay inciplespray ofay ethay uetray edeemingray aith,fay anday
atthay onay oneay ancay inway oray attainay itay ybay ishay ownay orks,way owsvay oray ethay ordsway ofay
ethay aints,say utbay atthay allay ustmay oceedpray aloneay omfray ethay eritmay ofay Ist,chray
ethay Onsay ofay Odgay. Ateverwhay esemblesray isthay aithfay eshay ancay erselfhay ovepray anday
accept;ay ethay otheray ot...nay. Otay ompelcay oray ersuadepay ymay aughterday otay acceptay
aay angestray eligionray inay ichwhay eshay erselfhay indsfay errorsay isay evernay otay ebay
advised....ay Anday atherray eventuallyay otay ivegay upay ethay egencyray anthay otay uffersay
offenseay inay erhay onscience.”cay

Esethay olemnsay ordsway ademay aay eepday impressionay onay ethay irlgay. Ethay admonitionsay
ichwhay elatedray otay erhay arriage,may ethay Empress,ay anday ethay Enatesay ereway otnay
osay erioussay. Eshay eltfay erselfhay ableay otay opecay ithway esethay oncretecay orcesfay
utbay ethay abstractionay alledcay onsciencecay isay aay oremay errifyingtay ingthay. I“ay
eseechbay you,”ay eshay ote,wray eplyingray otay erhay atherfay inay ishay ownay ein,vay O“tay ebay
assureday atthay youray admonitionsay anday eceptspray illway ebay oreverfay implanteday
ithinway ymay eart,hay asay isay ethay eed-cornsay ofay ouray olyhay eligionray inay ymay oulsay.
Iay aypray Odgay otay ivegay emay ethay engthstray ichwhay Iay eednay otay ithstandway ethay
emptationstay otay ichwhay Iay allshay ebay ubjectedsay. Oughthray ethay ayerspray ofay youray
Ighnesshay anday ofay ymay earday other,may Odgay illway antgray emay isthay acegray ichwhay ymay
youthay anday eaknessway annotcay ive.”gay

Ikefay illstay elievedbay enwhay eshay ennedpay esethay ineslay atthay eshay ouldway ebay
acceptableay inay Ussiaray asay anay Evangelicalay Andgray Uchessday. Inay ommoncay ithway
erhay Od-fearinggay atherfay eshay utpay erhay usttray inay ethay ecedentpray uppliedsay
ybay ethay Andgray Uchessday Arlottechay. Eirthay usttray asway isplacedmay. Eterpay ethay
Eatgray asway iberallay inay eligiousray atters,may utbay ishay aughterday asway orthodox.ay
Eterpay idday otnay imselfhay ogay otay urchchay anday ooktay easureplay inay exposingay ethay
amshay iraclesmay ofay ethay onder-workingway Irginsvay ofay Ussiaray owhay ereway ableay otay
edshay ealray earstay eforebay eirthay orshippersway. Ishay aughterday idday otnay inheritay
ishay epticalskay iritspay. Eshay asway oyallay otay ethay Ussianray Urchchay anday aay overlay
ofay iraclesmay. Erhay other’smay illway ovidedpray atthay onay oneay ouldshay occupyay ethay
Ussianray onethray owhay idday otnay ofesspray ethay orthodoxay aithfay. Ikefay erceivedpay
ethay inalityfay ofay isthay atay once.ay Om“Fray ymay entranceay intoay ethay empire,”ay eshay
aid,say I“ay adhay eenbay irmlyfay onvincedcay atthay ethay eavenlyhay owncray ouldcay otnay
ebay eparatedsay omfray ethay earthlyay one.”ay Onay ethay esholdthray ofay erhay ewnay ifelay
eshay asway ungedplay intoay aay onflictcay ithway erhay onsciencecay. Eshay estledwray ithway
emptationtay anday ethay arsscay ofay erhay ugglestray emainedray ithway erhay oughthray ifelay.

E“Thay angechay ofay eligion,”ray otewray Ardefeldmay otay Ingkay Ederick,fray Ives“gay ethay
Incesspray infiniteay ainpay anday erhay earstay owflay abundantlyay enwhay eshay isay aloneay
ithway ersonspay ofay omwhay eshay isay otnay uspicioussay. Everthelessnay ambitionay isay
aininggay inallyfay ethay upperay and.”hay Ememberingray ethay eligiousray onflictcay
ofay ishay ownay youth,ay Ederickfray asway alarmed.ay Utbay ehay utpay ishay aithfay inay ethay
Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabeth.ay It“ay onlyay emains,ray Adame,may orfay emay otay egbay
youay otay overcomeay ethay epugnanceray ofay youray aughterday orfay ethay Eekgray Urch,chay
afteray ichwhay youay illway avehay ownedcray youray ork.”way

Ikefay asway onvertedcay ybay Imonsay Odorskytay. Avinghay udiedstay ourfay yearsay atay
ethay Universityay ofay Alle,hay atay atthay imetay aay ot-bedhay ofay eology,thay ehay ewknay
ethay anguagelay ofay Utherlay ellway. Atwhay asway oremay otay ethay ointpay inay ealingday
ithway ethay youngay ersonpay omfray Erbst,zay Odorskytay asway amiliarfay ithway ethay
ubtletiessay ofay igherhay iticismcray ichwhay ethay intellectualsay ofay Allehay adhay
ecentlyray invented.ay Esethay ereway ingsthay ofay ichwhay oodgay Astorpay Agner,way
o,whay afteray all,ay asway onlyay anay armyay aplain,chay adhay evernay evenay eameddray.
Ithway ethay assistanceay ofay Odorsky’stay air-splitting,hay Ikefay asway ableay otay
eesay atthay erethay asway eryvay ittlelay ealray ifferenceday etweenbay ethay Utheranlay
anday ethay Eekgray Urchchay. Ifay onlyay erhay atherfay adhay otnay ontinuedcay otay arryhay
erhay onsciencecay. Ou“Thay ouldestshay otnay aketay isthay ialtray ivolously,”fray
ehay ote,wray Ust“may earchsay yselfthay ithway arecay etherwhay outhay artay eallyray inay
ythay earthay inspireday ybay inclination;ay oray ether,whay erhaps,pay ithoutway ythay
eingbay awareay ofay it,ay ethay arksmay ofay avorfay ownshay eethay ybay ethay Empressay anday
otheray igh-placedhay ersonspay avehay influenceday eethay inay atthay irectionday. Eway
umanhay eingsbay oftenay eesay onlyay atthay ichwhay isay eforebay ouray eyes.ay Utbay Odgay inay
Ishay infiniteay usticejay earchessay ethay earthay anday ouray ecretsay otives,may anday
anifestsmay accordinglyay otay usay Ishay ercy.”may

Asay ethay awfulay adesshay ofay Udgmentjay Ayday osedclay aboutay er,hay Ikefay ellfay ill.ay
Onceay eforebay inay ildhoodchay eshay adhay uccumbedsay otay anay attackay ofay eligiousray
errortay omplicatedcay ybay eumoniapnay. Inay Ussiaray eshay epeatedray ethay experience.ay
E“Thay ysiciansphay ascribeay ethay isease,”day otewray erhay other,may O“tay ethay
inflamingay ofay ethay oodblay ausedcay ybay ethay ardhay ourney.”jay Orfay enty-seventway
aysday ethay ildchay overedhay etweenbay ifelay anday eathday. Inay unconsciousnessay anday
eliriumday eshay ademay ethay ecisionday ichwhay erhay atherfay adhay urgeday erhay otay eighway
osay arefullycay. Elievingbay atthay Ikefay ightmay ie,day ethay Incesspray uggestedsay
atthay aay Utheranlay ergymanclay ouldshay ebay alledcay otay erhay edsidebay. Utbay ethay
icksay irlgay aid,say omingcay orfay aay omentmay otay onsciousness,cay Y?“Whay Allcay Imonsay
Odorskytay atherray. Iay ouldway ikelay otay eakspay ithway im.”hay Itay asway aay iumphtray ofay
iplomacy,day anywayay esencepray ofay indmay ichwhay asway otay arrycay Ikefay oughthray
everyay isiscray ofay erhay ifelay.

Uringday erhay onvalescence,cay Ikefay esumedray erhay essonslay ithway ethay Ussianray
iest,pray aay actfay ichwhay erhay othermay arefullycay oncealedcay omfray ethay Incepray
ofay Erbstzay. Asay oonsay asay eshay asway ableay otay oldhay aay en,pay eshay otewray aay iffstay
espectfulray etterlay otay erhay atherfay askingay ermissionpay otay angechay erhay
eligionray. Eshay entsay erhay eetingsgray otay Uncleay Ohannjay Udwiglay anday omisedpray otay
itewray otay imhay ybay ethay extnay ostpay. Y“May andhay isay illstay eryvay eak,”way eshay aid,say
O“say atthay Iay annotcay oday itay o-day.”tay Ethay otway olday Uritanspay atay Erbstzay ithway
eirthay itewhay igsway anday iouspay aysway ereway astlyvay importantay otay Ikefay althoughay
obodynay elseay eltfay atthay eythay adhay otay ebay onciliatedcay.

Inay afteray years,ay enwhay eshay adhay ecomebay Atherinecay ethay Eat,gray Ikefay ademay
ightlay ofay ethay olewhay usinessbay ofay onversioncay. Enwhay erhay aughter-in-lawday adhay
otay ogay oughthray ethay amesay experience,ay eshay okespay ofay itay erelymay asay aay outineray
orechay. As“ay oonsay asay eway avehay erhay erehay eway allshay ogay aboutay ethay onversioncay.
Inay orderay otay onvincecay er,hay eway allshay eednay aboutay ourteenfay aysday. Owhay uchmay
imetay illway ebay eedednay otay eachtay erhay otay eadray ethay onfessioncay ofay aithfay
orrectlycay anday istinctlyday inay Ussian,ray Iay oday otnay ow.”knay Ethay ourteenfay
aysday ereway akentay omfray Ike’sfay ownay experience;ay itay asway afteray otway eeksway ofay
Odorsky’stay air-splittinghay ogmaday atthay eshay adhay uccumbedsay otay eumoniapnay anday
ethay emptingstay ofay ambition.ay Oughthay eshay ouldcay eakspay ofay erhay onversioncay osay
asuallycay inay afteray ifelay itay adhay almostay illedkay erhay atay ethay imetay. Ethay eatgray
imescray ofay ichwhay eshay asway accuseday asay Empressay ademay esslay impressionay onay erhay
onsciencecay. Asay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray eshay identifieday erselfhay ithway Enrihay
elay Andgray ofay Ance,fray atthay illiantbray aywardway onarchmay owhay angedchay ishay
eligionray orfay ethay akesay ofay aay owncray. Itay asway onlyay oneay ofay anymay aysway inay ichwhay
eshay iedtray otay ustifyjay erhay epartureday omfray erhay ather’sfay urchchay.

Onay ethay enty-eighthtway ofay Une,jay alepay omfray aay eethray ays’day ast,fay Ikefay asway
onfirmedcay anday e-christenedray. Ethay Empressay adhay aay owngay ademay orfay erhay
exactlyay ikelay erhay own,ay ofay edray Os_gray eday Our_tay orkedway ithway ilversay. Erhay
odmothergay asway ethay ageday Abbessay ofay ethay Ovodevichenay Onvent,cay owedbay ithway
yearsay anday eepedstay inay anctitysay. Ethay Empressay ithway erhay ondnessfay orfay
ableaux,tay adhay arrangeday all.ay Azny,kray ethay orgeousgay edray osay elovedbay ybay ethay
Ussians,ray ominatedday ethay enescay. Eelingknay onay aay igbay uaresqay ushion,cay ethay
onvertcay ecitedray ethay eedcray inay aay earclay unfalteringay oicevay. Eshay adhay earnedlay
it,ay eshay ays,say Y“bay eart,hay ikelay aay arrot.”pay Indeeday eshay adhay earnedlay itay
ice,tway orfay Imonsay Odorsky,tay ethay iest,pray adhay aughttay erhay ethay Ukrainianay
onounciation,pray anday Asilbay Adadurov,ay ethay utor,tay adhay aughttay erhay ethay
Ussianray. Orfay ethay ublicpay eremonycay eshay osechay ethay Ussianray. Asay erhay earclay
youngay oicevay angray outay inay ethay irstfay esponse,ray ethay earstay ofay ethay assembleday
ompanycay ushedgay orthfay. Ikefay aintainedmay erhay elf-control,say ichwhay avegay anay
impressionay ofay eepday inceritysay anday eligiousray ervorfay anday asway uchmay aisedpray.
Er“Hay earingbay omfray ethay omentmay enwhay eshay irstfay entereday ethay urch,”chay otewray
erhay other,may And“ay oughoutthray ethay entireay eremonycay asway osay ullfay ofay obilitynay
anday ignityday atthay Iay ouldshay avehay admireday erhay adhay eshay otnay eenbay otay emay atthay
ichwhay eshay is.”ay

Andingstay eforebay erhay inay embroidereday anday ejewelledbay obes,ray ethay
Archbishopay ofay Ovgorodnay intoned:ay Erefore“Whay artay outhay omecay otay ethay Olyhay
Orthodoxay Urchchay ofay Odgay anday atwhay eekestsay outhay omfray er?”hay Anday Ikefay
ecitedray inay ereo-typedstay asesphray aay onglay elodiousmay eed,cray inay ichwhay amongay
otheray ingsthay eshay ofessed:pray I“ay elievebay anday onfesscay atthay aithfay aloneay
isay otnay ufficientsay orfay ouray ustification,jay utbay atthay oodgay orksway alsoay
ichwhay oceedpray omfray aithfay anday arity,chay ithalway asay adgesbay ofay Istchray areay
ecessarynay otay alvation;say ithoutway ethay amesay aithfay isay eadday accordingay otay ethay
estimonytay ofay olyhay it...wray.

I“ay elievebay anday onfesscay atthay ethay icturespay ofay Istchray anday ethay othermay ofay
Od,gay ethay Irginvay Ary,may asay osethay ofay otheray aintssay ouldshay ebay eservedpray anday
ouldshay ebay ulyday enerated,vay utbay ouldshay otnay ebay orshipped.”way

Ike’sfay othermay entsay anay enthusiasticay utbay iscreetday escriptionday ofay ethay
eremonycay otay erhay ousespay. Itay asway aay etailday otay erhay atthay erhay aughter’sday amenay
adhay eenbay anged,chay utbay ethay irl’sgay atherfay anday erhay auntsay ouldway obablypray
ebay urthay. Ethay amenay Ophiesay asway aay oodgay Ussianray ame,nay onenay etter,bay utbay
itay appenedhay otay ebay atthay ofay ethay ebelliousray istersay omwhay Eterpay ethay Eatgray
adhay ockedlay upay inay aay onventcay. Ereforethay Elisabethay atedhay it.ay Osay Ikefay asway
aptizedbay Atherinecay Alexeievnaay orfay Elisabeth’say othermay anday Ophiesay Augusteay
Iedrikefray easedcay otay exist.ay Ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay okebray ethay ewsnay otay
erhay usbandhay asay actfullytay asay ossiblepay. In“ay orderay otay ealsay ubliclypay uchsay
aay onfirmation,”cay eshay ote,wray A“ay amenay isay added;ay ouray aughterday illway ebay
Atherinecay anday ethay Alexeievnaay ollowsfay ethay ustomcay ofay ethay ountrycay anday
eansmay aughterday ofay August;ay orfay ethay amenay August,ay accordingay otay ethay ialectday
ere,hay ancay otnay ebay enderedray otheray anthay Alexei.”ay Ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay
adhay akentay essonslay inay ethay Ussianray anguagelay otay easeplay ethay Empressay utbay erhay
ogresspray adhay otnay eenbay osay eatgray. Itay isay ossiblepay atthay eshay elievedbay atthay
Augustay anday Alexeiay ereway ethay amesay inay Ussianray oughthay obablypray eshay ewknay
etterbay. Inay anyay asecay erhay ittlelay ictionfay ouldway arcelyscay ebay iscoveredday ybay
ethay Ermangay Eneralgay. Ethay umblingsray omfray Erbstzay anday Ettinstay iedday ownday.
Ethay Incepray asway easedplay ecausebay ishay aughterday asway aay Andgray Uchessday anday
addresseday erhay ybay isthay onoroussay itletay. Ethay Incesspray ontinuedcay otay allcay
erhay aughterday Ikefay anday arpedcay atay erhay usbandhay orfay adoptingay ethay itletay
ofay Andgray Uchessday. Ike“Fay illway inkthay atthay youay onay ongerlay ovelay er,”hay eshay
otewray. Utbay ethay Incepray ontinuedcay otay ebay espectfulray. Asay ishay aughterday adhay
onceay ustedtray imhay otay understanday erhay eaknessway orfay eerbay ehay ownay ustedtray erhay
otay understanday ishay eaknessway orfay etiquette.ay Ehay asway aggeringsway orfay emthay
othbay.

Afteray erhay onfirmation,cay Atherinecay Alexeievnaay ollowedfay ethay Empressay omfray
oisterclay otay oister,clay orfay Elisabethay adhay omecay otay endspay oremay anday oremay
ofay erhay imetay asay aay iouspay ilgrimpay. Eshay adhay apartmentsay inay ethay Oitskytray
Onasterymay erewhay eshay ometimessay ivedlay ithway erhay ourtcay. Ethay Abbotay ofay
Oitskytray anday ethay Ishopsbay ofay Oscowmay anday Etersburgpay accompanieday erhay
everywhere.ay Ithway erhay eethray iests,pray eshay appeareday inay ethay oxbay atay ethay
operaay anday evenay atay asquerademay allsbay. Ethay youngay Andgray Uchessday ouldcay otnay
imagineay oodgay Astorpay Agnerway inay ethay erôlay ofay olitepay escortay anday avaliercay.
Erhay ewnay urchchay adhay undreamed-ofay ossibilitiespay ofay omanceray. Iev,kay ichwhay
eshay isitedvay ithway erhay aunt,ay eemedsay aay indkay ofay orthodoxay Arabianay Ightsnay.
Ere“Hay asay inay allay itiescay ichwhay eway adhay ouchedtay incesay Oscow,”may eshay ote,wray
E“thay ergyclay ofay Ievkay amecay otay eetmay us.ay Asay oonsay asay ethay urchchay annersbay ereway
isible,vay eway eftlay ethay arriagescay anday entereday ethay itycay onay ootfay ehindbay
ethay osscray. Ethay Empressay etookbay erselfhay otay ethay Etcherskypay Oisterclay anday
entereday ethay urchchay ontainingcay ethay onder-workingway ortraitpay ofay ethay Olyhay
Irginvay aidsay otay avehay eenbay aintedpay ybay Aintsay Ukaslay. Evernay inay ymay olewhay ifelay
avehay Iay eenbay osay impresseday asay ybay ethay agnificentmay endorsplay ofay ethay urch,chay
inay ichwhay allay ethay aints’say icturespay ereway overedcay ithway old,gay ilversay anday
ewels....”jay

Oward“Tay ethay enday ofay ouray aystay inay Iev,kay ethay Empressay isitedvay ithway usay aay
onasterymay erewhay aay omedycay asway otay ebay ayedplay. Ethay erformancepay eganbay
atay evensay inay ethay evening.ay Eway adhay otay ogay oughthray ethay urchchay otay eachray
ethay eatrethay. Ethay ayplay onsistedcay eallyray ofay everalsay ays:play erethay ereway
ologues,pray allets,bay aay iecepay inay ichwhay Arcusmay Aureliusay adhay ishay avoritefay
anged,hay aay attlebay inay ichwhay Ossackscay oughtfay ithway ethay Oles,pay aay ishingfay
enescay onay ethay Ieper,dnay anday oruseschay ithoutway umbernay. Ethay Empressay eldhay outay
untilay aboutay otway o’clockay inay ethay orning;may enthay eshay entsay otay askay etherwhay
itay ouldway otnay enday oonsay. Ethay answeray amecay ackbay atthay onlyay alfhay ofay ethay
erformancepay adhay eenbay ivengay utbay ifay erhay Ajestymay osay ordereday eythay ouldway
opstay atay once.ay Eshay epliedray atthay eythay ouldshay inishfay oon;say eythay eggedbay
onlyay orfay ermissionpay otay urnbay omesay ire-works....”fay

Uchsay asway Istianitychray inay Ussia:ray imagesay overedcay ithway oldgay anday
ilver,say iecespay aboutay aay aganpay amednay Arcusmay Aurelius,ay anday outburstsay ofay
ire-worksfay. Asay ethay upilpay ofay Astorpay Agner,way anday ethay aughterday ofay erhay
ather,fay Atherinecay ouldcay otnay ailfay otay ealizeray atthay esethay ingsthay oceededpray
omfray Atansay anday omfray Atansay alone.ay Eshay ewknay oughthay eshay aredday otnay admitay
itay atthay eythay ereway idolatrous.ay Anday yetay eshay eveledray inay emthay. dray. Artinmay
Utherlay adhay ownthray anay ink-standay atay ethay Evilday enwhay ehay utpay ishay eadhay
oughthray ethay indowway. Everyay uetray Istianchray ewknay ethay Evilay Oneay onay ightsay
anday ademay ortshay iftshray ofay imhay. Ethay Incepray ofay Erbst,zay erhay ather,fay adhay
onceay encountereday imhay. Itay asway uringday aay isitvay ofay ethay Incepray atay Omeray atthay
ethay Opepay adhay emptedtay imhay otay ecomebay aay Atholiccay. Utbay ethay Incepray adhay otnay
yieldeday otay ethay andishmentsblay ofay anti-Christay ecause,bay ikelay ethay eroichay
Octorday Uther,lay ehay ecognizedray ethay Ickedway Oneay inay itespay ofay ishay ompouspay
isguiseday. Ethay Incepray ofay Erbstzay eturnedray otay ishay armyay anday ishay urchchay
unharmed.ay Asay aay attermay ofay actfay itay isay oubtfulday etherwhay ehay adhay everay eensay
Omeray anday illstay oremay oubtfulday etherwhay ethay Opepay adhay aidpay anyay attentionay otay
anay obscureay Ermangay Otestantpray. Utbay egendlay isay asay oodgay asay istoryhay ifay ethay
egendlay isay elieved,bay anday ethay Ince’spray aughterday adhay eenbay oughtbray upay otay
admireay isthay eroichay eadfastnessstay ofay erhay ather’sfay. Ofay oursecay ethay Ussianray
Urchchay asway ikelay ethay Utheranlay anday otnay ethay Oman,ray asay Atherfay Odorskytay
adhay explaineday otay erhay anday asay eshay adhay explaineday otay earday Apapay. Atherinecay
Alexeievna,ay owever,hay ebaptizedray inay ethay Eekgray aith,fay oundfay itay actfultay otay
oncealcay aay eatgray ealday omfray erhay atherfay aboutay erhay ewnay aithfay anday ethay ingsthay
ethay Ussiansray idday inay ethay amenay ofay eirthay eligionray.


2ay

Ethay Empress’say attachmentay otay ethay youngay Incesspray adhay eenbay engthenedstray
ybay erhay illness,ay ilewhay ethay otway elderay omenway adhay eenbay alienateday omfray
eachay other.ay Enwhay Atherinecay ellfay illay ethay Empressay asway ojourningsay inay erhay
Oitskytray etreatray. Ethay ourtcay ysicianphay ushedray otay ethay icksay irl’sgay aiday anday
eparedpray otay eedblay erhay. Otay eirthay astonishmentay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay
orbadefay ethay operation.ay Eshay adhay alwaysay eenbay anickypay aboutay ood-letting,blay
anday eshay ubbornlystay efusedray otay avehay erhay aughterday edblay. Ethay octorsday ereway
outraged.ay Eythay entsay aay essengermay inay astehay otay eirthay Empressay owhay ouldcay otnay
elievebay erhay ears.ay Eshay ordereday erhay arriagecay anday erhay avoritefay anday ostedpay
otay Oscowmay.

Arrivingay afteray andle-light,cay Elisabethay anday Azumovskyray entereday ethay
ick-roomsay anday oundfay ethay atientpay unconscious.ay Ethay Empressay eatedsay erselfhay
onay ethay idesay ofay ethay ed,bay ooktay ethay irlgay inay erhay arms,ay anday oldtay ethay octorsday
otay ogay ahead.ay Ethay othermay asway ummarilysay excludeday omfray ethay oomray anday
Estocqlay oltedbay ethay oorday. Uringday erhay illness,ay Atherinecay asway edblay ixteensay
imes,tay oftenay asay uchmay asay ourfay imestay aay ayday. Erhay other’smay oppositionay asway
etsay ownday ybay ethay ourtcay asay owingshay aay acklay ofay aturalnay aternalmay affection.ay
Ethay Empressay aisedpray ethay irl’sgay ouragecay anday esentedpray erhay ithway aay airpay ofay
ear-ringsay anday aay ecklacenay orthway enty-fivetway ousandthay ublesray. Eshay emovedray
ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay asay eadhay ursenay anday utpay ethay Ountesscay Umiantsovray inay
erhay aceplay. Ethay asmchay etweenbay ethay othermay anday aughterday asway oadeningbray.

Oughthay urthay ybay allay esethay ights,slay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay ouldcay otnay
earnlay ybay experience.ay Ethay imaxclay ofay erhay actlessnesstay amecay atay Easter.ay
Atherinecay adhay aay iecepay ofay ueblay anday ilversay ocadebray ichwhay Uncleay Ohannjay
Udwiglay adhay ivengay otay erhay inay arting,pay aay ichray abricfay ovenway ybay oneay ofay
ethay oomslay ofay Erbstzay. Erhay othermay ovetedcay ethay iecepay anday atay astlay entsay
aay essengermay otay askay orfay itay outright.ay Atherinecay esignedray erhay easuretray
eluctantly,ray ichwhay ethay Ountesscay Umiantsov,ray owhay acteday asay yspay asay ellway
asay urse,nay observeday anday eportedray otay ethay Empress.ay Elisabethay orthwithfay
entsay otway orgeousgay engthslay ofay uffstay otay ethay onvalescentcay irlgay anday openlyay
expresseday erhay opinionay ofay isthay oughtlessthay othermay. Eforebay eythay adhay eenbay
inay Ussiaray otway onths,may Atherinecay adhay onway anay allyay inay ethay Empressay ilewhay
erhay othermay adhay eatedcray inay erhay aay itterbay enemy.ay

Inay ethay eantimemay ethay oreignfay officesay ofay Ussia,pray Ancefray anday Edensway ereway
eaninglay ardhay onay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay otay omwhay eythay ookedlay orfay aiday
inay ormingfay anay allianceay ithway Ussiaray. Ethay Incesspray asway ascinatedfay ybay
erhay oliticalpay issionmay anday idday otnay ealizeray atthay erhay ismanagementmay ofay
erhay aughter’sday affairsay ailedfay otay elphay ethay ausecay ofay Ussiapray ithway ethay
Empress.ay Ethay Ussianray Inistermay ofay Oreignfay Affairs,ay Estushev,bay avoredfay anay
allianceay ithway Austriaay againstay Ussiapray. Ehay alledcay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray
Edatory”“pray anday ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray alledcay Estushevbay Orrupt.”“cay Istoryhay
ashay ownshay atthay othbay entlemengay ereway orrectcay.

Estushev’sbay influenceay ithway Elisabethay asway upremesay ecausebay ehay adhay eenbay
aay otégépray ofay erhay ather’sfay. Atay ifteenfay ehay adhay eenbay entsay abroaday anday
educateday ybay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Ehay enthay entereday ethay iplomaticday ervicesay anday
ivedlay orfay entytway yearsay oray oremay inay esternway Europe.ay Estushevbay asway oneay ofay
ethay ostmay ersatilevay anday iftedgay Ussiansray ofay ishay ayday. Ishay amenay asway ownknay
oughoutthray Europeay asay ethay inventoray ofay aay edicinemay alledcay Estushev’sbay
Ops,dray ichwhay asway opularlypay egardedray othbay asay anay elixiray ofay ifelay anday alsoay
asay aay ealinghay oseday orfay ystericalhay adieslay. Enwhay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray
ascendeday ethay one,thray eshay oughtbay ethay ormulafay orfay Estushev’sbay Opsdray anday
ublishedpay itay asay aay enefactionbay otay ethay umanhay aceray. Ithway allay erhay ornscay
ofay octorsday eshay adhay eatgray espectray orfay Estushev’sbay Opsdray. Eshay useday emthay
alwaysay inay erhay ownay amilyfay.

Estushev’sbay esearchesray inay ethay ackblay artsay adhay otheray onsequencescay. Ehay
employeday inay ethay epartmentday ofay oreignfay affairsay aay Ermangay ybay ethay amenay ofay
Oldbach,gay owhay amperedtay ientificallyscay ithway ailmay. Inay uchsay attersmay ethay
Ussiansray uppliedsay ethay illway utbay eythay usuallyay employeday aay Ermangay otay oday ethay
eedday. Oldbachgay openeday ethay Enchfray Ambassador’say etterslay anday eadray erethay aay
eatgray ealday atthay asway otnay intendeday orfay ethay eyesay ofay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray.
Ehay ereforethay aidlay ethay orrespondencecay eforebay Elisabethay owhay eadray atthay eshay
asway ivolousfray anday indolentay anday atthay erhay iefchay interestay inay ifelay asway inay
angingchay erhay ostumecay ourfay oray ivefay imestay aay ayday. Eshay urthermorefay earnedlay
ofay ethay ecretsay orrespondencecay oinggay onay etweenbay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray anday
ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay anday ofay ethay ongstray influenceay ichwhay ethay Incesspray
asway upposedsay otay ieldway uponay erselfhay. Itay ouldway ebay ildmay otay aysay atthay ethay
Empressay asway angry.ay Estushev’sbay ethodmay ofay aininggay ishay enday asway implesay anday
uccessfulsay.

Ethay Empressay uckstray atay once.ay Eshay ordereday ethay Enchfray Ambassadoray otay eavelay
Oscowmay ithinway enty-fourtway ourshay anday otay akemay orfay Igaray ithoutway evenay
ouchingtay Etersburgpay. Itay asway ethay amesay Etardiechay owhay adhay ovidedpray Enchfray
oneymay orfay erhay evolution,ray utbay ehay entway atay once.ay Itay asway aay amousfay exit.ay
Estushevbay ontinuedcay uietlyqay otay ixmay ethay ardscay. Ehay asway ownay afteray ethay eadhay
ofay ethay eddlingmay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay.

Atay Oitskytray ethay Empressay anday erhay aintray occupieday aay uitesay ofay easantplay
amberschay ithway owlay eilings,cay Englishay ocks,clay anday Utchday ovesstay. Eshay adhay
omesticday astestay anday armway affectionsay anday atisfiedsay inay isthay etreatray erhay
esireday orfay aay uietqay amilyfay ifelay. Erehay anday atay Onplaisir,may erewhay eshay adhay
aay ummersay itchenkay inay ichwhay eshay ookedcay ithway erhay ownay ands,hay eshay ivedlay
erhay appiesthay omentsmay. Ethay osycay amilyfay atmosphereay asway interrupteday ybay aay
ainfulpay explosionay ichwhay ooktay aceplay etweenbay ethay Empressay anday ethay Incesspray
ofay Erbstzay afteray Estushevbay adhay ulledpay ethay ingsstray uietlyqay otay isthay end.ay

Ethay Empressay anday erhay uestsgay adhay ustjay arriveday omfray Oscowmay. Ethay Empressay
adhay ademay ethay ourneyjay onay oot,fay eavinglay ethay othersay otay overtakeay erhay
inay arriagescay. Ethay entireay artypay entereday ethay atesgay inay ethay ormfay ofay
aay ocession,pray ichwhay irstfay urnedtay intoay ethay Athedralcay orfay assmay anday
afterwarday ecamebay aay ortsay ofay Englishay ouse-partyhay inay ichwhay affairsay ofay
atestay anday ociabilitysay ereway indiscriminatelyay ixedmay. After“ay ethay iddaymay
eal,”may Atherinecay ays,say En“whay ethay Andgray Ukeday adhay omecay otay ouray ambers,chay
ethay Empressay entereday unexpectedlyay anday ommandedcay ymay othermay otay ollowfay
erhay intoay ethay extnay oomray. Ountcay Estocqlay entway inay ithway emthay. Awaitingay ymay
other’smay eturn,ray Iay eatedsay yselfmay ithway ethay Andgray Ukeday uponay ethay indowway
edge,lay anday eway attedchay. Ethay onversationcay inay ethay osedclay oomray astedlay aay
onglay ime.”tay

Ethay irstfay otay appearay asway Ountcay Estocqlay o,whay assumingay ishay estbay Ermangay
anners,may aidsay otay ethay youngay irl,gay Ere“Thay isay othingnay eftlay orfay youay utbay otay
ackpay youray ings;thay youay illway artstay atay onceay onay youray ome-wardhay ourney.”jay
Estocqlay idday otnay asteway ourtesycay onay allenfay avorites,fay utbay ehay asway otnay
alwaysay ewdshray enoughay otay owknay owhay adhay allenfay anday owhay adhay otnay. Enthay
ethay Empressay appeareday atay ethay oorday. Orfay aay omentmay erhay imposingay igurefay
oweredtay eneathbay ethay owlay eiling,cay erhay ueblay eyesay ashingflay ithway anger.ay
Ehindbay erhay appeareday ethay ulprit,cay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbst,zay erhay eyesay edray
ithway eepingway. Ethay otway youngay eoplepay astilyhay angspray ownday omfray ethay ighhay
indow-seatway anday oodstay inay attitudesay ofay espectray. Ethay impulsiveay Elisabethay
aughed,lay issedkay ethay oybay anday irlgay owhay ereway otay akemay upay otay erhay orfay ethay
omanticray arriagemay eshay adhay issed,may anday assedpay uicklyqay outay ofay ethay oomray.
Estocq’slay ophecypray asway otnay ulfilledfay. Ethay Incesspray anday erhay aughterday
ereway otnay entsay omehay.

Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway otay eelfay ethay effectsay ofay isthay amilyfay uarrelqay
inay ethay Evensay Yearsay Arway. Elisabeth’say islikeday ofay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay asway
eatlygray engthenedstray ybay ethay explosionay atay Oitskytray. Ethay Incesspray ofay
Erbstzay eshay evernay orgavefay. Ardefeld,may ethay Ussianpray inister,may asway alloweday
otay ingerlay orfay aay ime,tay utbay enwhay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay eturnedray otay
Ermany,gay ethay Empressay emandedday Ardefeld’smay ecallray. Eshay ithay uponay ethay
umiliatinghay eviceday ofay equiringray ethay Incesspray erselfhay otay ogay otay ethay Ingkay
ofay Ussiapray anday eliverday ethay essagemay equestingray ishay inister’smay ecallray.
Ethay Ussianpray Ambassador,ay owhay adhay urvivedsay entytway yearsay atay ethay Ussianray
ourtcay anday adhay andedlay onay ishay eetfay afteray otway alacepay evolutions,ray asway
inallyfay eckedwray ybay ishay allianceay ithway ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay. Ederickfray
ethay Eatgray ostlay ubstantiallysay enthay anday afterwarday ybay enlistingay ethay
iplomacyday ofay Atherine’scay othermay. Ehay idday otnay orgetfay it.ay


3ay

Inay allay erhay ifficulties,day Atherinecay ouldcay ooklay orfay onay upportsay omfray erhay
aturalnay otectorpray anday uturefay onsortcay. Ifay eshay adhay eenbay anay averageay irl,gay
ethay efectiveday Eterpay ouldway illstay avehay eenbay aay ildchay esidebay erhay. Utbay eshay
asway arfay omfray eingbay anay ordinaryay irlgay. Ethay ifteen-year-oldfay Incesspray asway
oremay anthay aay atchmay orfay ethay otway adultay omenway owhay anciedfay eythay ereway eadinglay
erhay. Otay eerstay erhay oursecay etweenbay ethay Empressay anday erhay othermay ooktay allay
erhay attentionay atay irstfay. Orfay aay imetay eshay isregardedday ethay Andgray Ukeday asay aay
actorfay inay ethay ituationsay.

Erhay accountay ofay eirthay elationshipray owsshay atthay eythay etmay ikelay ildren,chay
ithoutway anyay oughtthay ofay aay oremay aturemay elationshipray. E“Thay Andgray Ukeday
appeareday otay ejoiceray atay ymay arrival.ay Inay ethay irstfay aysday ehay asway eryvay
omplaisantcay owardtay e.”may Uringday erhay illness,ay ishay oodgay illway ontinuedcay.
Uring“Day ymay icknesssay ethay Andgray Ukeday adhay ownshay emay uchmay attention.ay Enwhay
Iay ecamebay etterbay ehay ontinuedcay isthay. Iay eemedsay otay easeplay im;hay utbay Iay ancay
eithernay aysay atthay ehay easedplay emay ornay ispleasedday emay. Iay onlyay ewknay owhay otay
obeyay anday ymay othermay adhay otay arrymay e.”may Ethay oybay avegay erhay ishay onfidence,cay
atteringchay ikelay aay ildchay aboutay everythingay atthay amecay intoay ishay eadhay. Ehay
onfidedcay otay erhay ishay ormerfay ovelay orfay Incesspray Apukinlay omwhay ethay Empressay
adhay anishedbay omfray ethay ourtcay anday osewhay aceplay adhay eenbay akentay ybay Atherinecay
erselfhay. Ethay irl,gay owhay asway assionatelypay oud,pray ouldcay otnay understanday
atthay esethay ereway ethay outpouringsay ofay aay agilefray exlesssay oybay. Eshay onlyay awsay
atthay erhay overlay asway indifferentay anday etendedpray otay ethay othersay atthay eshay idday
otnay eesay it.ay

En“Whay ethay airfay eatherway amecay eway ovedmay overay intoay ethay Ummersay Alacepay. Erehay
ethay isitsvay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday ewgray esslay equentfray. Iay ustmay aysay isthay acklay
ofay attentionay anday ishay oldnesscay osay otay eakspay onay ethay eveay ofay ouray eddingway idday
otnay exactlyay inclineay emay inay ishay avorfay. Ethay earernay ethay imetay ame,cay ethay esslay
ouldcay Iay idehay omfray yselfmay ethay ossibilitypay atthay ymay arriagemay ightmay ebay eryvay
unhappy.ay Utbay Iay adhay ootay uchmay idepray anday ootay uchmay elf-respectsay otay alloway
ethay orldway otay uspectsay atthay Iay oughtthay yselfmay unloved.ay Iay egardedray yselfmay
ootay ighlyhay otay elievebay atthay Iay asway ontemptiblecay. Ethay Andgray Ukeday adhay aay
omewhatsay eefray annermay ithway ethay adies-in-waitinglay ofay ethay Empressay ichwhay
idday otnay exactlyay easeplay e,may utbay Iay estrainedray yselfmay omfray eakingspay aboutay
itay anday onay oneay ewknay ymay eepestday eelingsfay. Iay iedtray otay istractday yselfmay ybay
ompingray inay ymay amberchay ithway ymay aidens.”may

Ethay Andgray Uchessday idday otnay understanday atthay ethay Andgray Uke’sday attachmentsay
otay otheray adieslay asway asay ildishchay anday unvirileay asay ishay attachmentay otay
erselfhay. Eshay ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay atthay atay isthay imetay eshay arcelyscay ewknay
ethay ifferenceday etweenbay ethay exessay. Utbay ealousyjay asway anay olday amiliarfay
eelingfay. Arfay ackbay amongay ethay imday emoriesmay ofay erhay Ettinstay ildhoodchay asway
ethay adowshay ofay aay eadfuldray ayday enwhay aay abybay otherbray adhay upsetay erhay orldway.
Eshay idday otnay ikelay osethay emoriesmay. I“ay ouldshay avehay eenbay ethay ostmay unhappyay
eaturecray inay ethay orldway ifay Iay adhay alloweday yselfmay otay ebay arriedcay awayay ybay
eelingsfay ofay endernesstay orfay im,”hay eshay ayssay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday. E“Hay ouldway
avehay ill-repaiday emay anday Iay ouldshay avehay iedday ofay ealousy,jay ichwhay ouldway avehay
oneday obodynay anyay oodgay. Osay Iay iedtray otay ontrolcay yselfmay inay orderay atthay Iay
ightmay otnay ebay ealousjay ofay aay anmay atthay idday otnay ovelay emay. Utbay inay orderay otnay otay
ebay ealousjay erethay asway onlyay oneay eans:may otnay otay ovelay im.”hay

Ethay Andgray Uchessday ewgray igh-strunghay anday ervousnay. Itay asway otnay ethay irstfay
imetay atthay eshay adhay ailedfay otay eetmay ethay equirementsray ofay anay importantay
ituationsay. Ornbay aay irl,gay eshay adhay isappointedday erhay arents’pay opeshay ofay
ethay uccessionsay atay Anhalt-Zerbst.ay Ackinglay eauty,bay eshay adhay otnay eenbay
attractiveay otay uitorssay. Anday ownay atthay erhay uturefay usbandhay idday otnay ovelay
er,hay eshay adhay otay eassureray erselfhay atthay eshay asway otnay Ontemptible.”“cay Underay
ethay essstray ofay uisedbray elf-feeling,say eshay ecamebay apriciouscay anday asterfulmay
ithway erhay aidensmay. Overingcay ethay oorflay ofay erhay oomray ithway attresses,may eshay
adhay allay eightay ofay emthay eepslay inay erhay oomray. Anotheray imetay eshay edlay ethay
amselsday outay orfay aay idnightmay alkway oughthray ethay ardensgay ofay Eterhofpay orfay
ichwhay eythay ereway allay oundlyray oldedscay. Ikelay aay Ultanasay eshay ividedday ethay
ustodycay ofay erhay ossessionspay amongay em,thay entrustingay erhay ewelsjay otay one,ay
erhay aceslay otay another,ay erhay inenlay otay anotheray anday osay on.ay Eshay utcay erhay ontfray
airhay ort,shay oreway itay inay aay indkay ofay izzledfray angbay anday ordereday erhay irlsgay otay
oday ethay amesay. Omesay ofay emthay eptway anday eadedplay utbay ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay
issueday aay ukas.ay Eshay ouldway otnay ebay ovedmay. Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay otnay elentedray
enwhay olday enmay eptway anday eggedbay otay ebay alloweday otay eepkay eirthay eardsbay. Etlay
Ariamay Etrovna,pay ethay Orodovskay isters,say anday ethay otway arfsdway ydray eirthay
earstay anday orderay inay ethay arberbay atay onceay otay utcay offay eirthay airhay exactlyay
ikelay ethay Andgray Uchess...day. Inay additionay otay erhay elaborateay air-dressing,hay
Atherinecay adhay akentay onay ethay abithay ofay aintingpay erhay acefay.


4ay

Ethay Empressay arrangeday ethay arriagemay orfay erhay otway adopteday ildrenchay asay ifay
eythay adhay eenbay uppetspay oray alletbay ancersday. Onay uchsay arriagemay adhay everay
eenbay eensay inay Ussiaray exceptay erhapspay ethay amousfay iceay estivalfay inay ethay
eignray ofay Annaay Ivanovna,ay enwhay Incepray Alitsingay arriedmay ishay Illiputianlay
idebray. Otay atisfysay aay imwhay ofay eirthay Empressay ethay ouplecay adhay eenbay escorteday
otay anay illuminateday ice-palaceay onay ethay Evanay anday utpay uponay aay edbay ademay ofay
ice.ay Ortunatelyfay orfay Atherinecay anday Eterpay eythay ereway otay ebay arriedmay inay
id-summermay. Ethay ateday asway originallyay etsay orfay Ulyjay ethay irst,fay utbay asway
ostponedpay icetway. Otnay untilay atelay inay Augustay asway everythingay inallyfay eadyray.
Allay ummersay onglay ethay Empressay asway osay akentay upay ithway eparationspray atthay
eshay uspendedsay allay affairsay ofay atestay. Erhay ownay inistersmay anday ethay oreignfay
ambassadorsay adhay othingnay otay oday utbay ayplay ardscay anday ivedray inay ethay Evskynay
Ospectpray.

Orfay onthsmay inay advanceay ethay ashionablefay orldway asway usybay ovidingpray itselfay
ithway E“thay ichestray othesclay ossible”pay incesay othingnay esslay asway ecifiedspay ybay
ethay ukasay issueday ybay ethay Empress.ay Alesbay ofay ilk,say elvet,vay anday ocadebray ereway
onstantlycay arrivingay omfray Englanday anday Ermany,gay orfay ethay Ussiansray ereway onay
eaversway. Ethay Englishay ambassadoray otewray omehay omplainingcay ofay ethay Empress’say
eglectnay ofay officialay usinessbay enwhay ehay ightmay avehay etterbay ongratulatedcay
ishay ountrycay onay ethay increaseday importationay ofay Englishay oodsgay inay Ussiaray.
Omfray Ermangay oomslay amecay ethay eavyhay oth-of-silverclay omfray ichwhay Atherine’scay
eddingway owngay asway ademay. Itay asway aay igidray ucturestray ithway aay odicebay apedshay
overay aay oodenway orm,fay otay ichwhay asway uspendedsay aay aintray oremay anthay eethray
yardsay onglay. Ethay abricfay asway unspay ilversay anday ethay olewhay ingthay eighedway uponay
erhay ikelay aay uitsay ofay armor.ay

Adclay inay isthay unyieldingay armentgay anday earingbay onay erhay eadhay aay onderouspay
owncray ofay ewelsjay ethay Andgray Uchessday entspay aay iserablemay ayday. Eshay eldhay outay
avelybray uringday ethay eddingway eremonycay inay ethay urchchay ofay Ouray Adylay ofay Azankay
anday oughoutthray ethay atestay epastray inay ethay Interway Alacepay afterwards.ay Utbay
ustjay eforebay ethay allbay egan,bay eshay umbledhay erhay idepray anday eggedbay otay avehay
ethay owncray emovedray orfay aay ewfay inutesmay. Ethay Empress,ay owhay oughtthay isthay
ightmay ingbray adbay uck,lay eluctantlyray onsentedcay.

Ethay eddingway asway aay iumphtray orfay Elisabeth’say aternalmay idepray. Eshay ordereday
everyay etailday ofay ethay eremonycay ithway ealousjay yranny,tay otnay omittingay otay
ommandcay ethay idebray otay aketay aay athbay ethay eveningay eforebay. Earlyay extnay orningmay
eshay entsay orfay Atherinecay otay omecay otay erhay amberchay otay ebay obedray inay atestay.
Erethay ensueday aay eatedhay argumentay etweenbay ethay Empressay anday ethay arberbay
oncerningcay ethay ide’sbray ylestay ofay air-dressinghay. Atherinecay atsay eforebay ethay
irrormay anday eemedsay otay aketay onay artpay. Erethay asway otnay aay iftray onay isthay ayday
inay erhay oodgay elationsray ithway ethay Empress.ay Aay upremesay atisfactionsay inay ethay
eatgray eventay uniteday emthay ompletelycay.

Althoughay itay asway alsoay ethay eddingway ayday ofay ethay Andgray Uke,day ehay ayedplay aay
atherray inormay artpay. Ethay ill-starreday oybay adhay anagedmay otay ontractcay ethay
allpoxsmay ecentlyray anday appeareday atay ishay uptialsnay ithway aay eadfullydray
ockmarkedpay acefay. Ishay augustay auntay alwaysay eadeddray ishay ublicpay appearancesay
estlay omesay iecepay ofay ildishchay isbehaviourmay onay ishay artpay ouldshay isgraceday
ethay Omanovray amilyfay. Eterpay orebay imselfhay ufficientlysay ellway onay ishay eddingway
ay,day owever,hay otay ausecay onay ommentcay amongay ethay on-lookers.ay Ishay onlyay
apricecay asway otay offenday ishay idebray. Ilewhay ethay youngay ouplecay ereway illstay
eelingknay oppositeay otay eachay other,ay aitingway ethay inalfay ordsway ofay ethay iest,pray
oneay ofay ethay ourtcay adieslay isperedwhay inay ethay Andgray Uke’sday ear.ay I“ay eardhay
imhay aysay otay er,”hay ayssay Atherine,cay Ear“‘Clay out!ay Uchsay onsense!’nay Enthay ehay
urnedtay otay emay anday oldtay emay atthay eshay adhay adviseday imhay otnay otay urntay ishay eadhay
ilewhay ehay oodstay eforebay ethay iest,pray orfay oeverwhay ofay usay irstfay urnedtay ouray
eadhay ouldway ieday irstfay anday eshay idday otnay ishway imhay otay ebay atthay one.ay Iay oughtthay
isthay omplimentcay otnay eryvay iendlyfray onay ouray eddingway ayday utbay Iay idday otnay
alloway yselfmay otay oticenay it.ay Eshay aw,say owever,hay atthay ehay adhay epeatedray otay
emay erhay oodgay advice.ay Eshay ewgray edray anday ademay eproaches,ray ichwhay ehay againay
epeatedray otay e.”may

Atay entay o’clock,ay ethay Empressay erselfhay onductedcay ethay youngay eoplepay otay eirthay
apartmentay anday eftlay ethay Andgray Uchessday ithway erhay aidensmay. Eshay asway elievedray
ofay erhay urdensomebay eddingway armentsgay anday utpay otay edbay eneathbay aay elvetvay
overletcay. All“ay ofay emthay entway away,”ay Atherine’scay arrativenay elates,ray I“ay
emainedray aloneay oremay anthay otway ourshay anday idday otnay owknay atwhay Iay ouldshay oday.
Ouldshay Iay etgay upay again?ay Ouldshay Iay emainray inay ed?bay Iay ewknay othingnay. Inallyfay
ymay ewnay adylay ofay onor,hay Adamemay Use,kray amecay anday informeday emay ithway eatgray
errimentmay atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway aitingway orfay ishay uppersay ichwhay asway
aboutay otay ebay arriedcay upay otay imhay. Afteray ishay Imperialay Ighnesshay adhay uppedsay
ell,way ehay amecay otay ed;bay anday asay ehay aidlay imselfhay own,day ehay eganbay otay alktay
ofay owhay itay ouldway amuseay ishay ervantsay inay ethay orningmay otay eesay usay othbay inay
edbay. Enthay ehay ellfay asleepay anday eptslay oundlysay untilay ethay extnay orningmay. Ethay
othsclay ofay inefay inenlay onay ichwhay Iay aylay ereway eryvay uncomfortableay owingay otay
ethay ummersay eatherway anday onsequentlycay Iay eptslay adly;bay allay ethay oremay asay ethay
orningmay aygray ofay ethay aylightday isturbedday emay onsiderably,cay orfay ethay edbay adhay
onay urtains,cay althoughay otherwiseay urnishedfay agnificentlymay inay edray elvetvay
ithway ilversay embroidery.ay Adamemay Usekray attempteday ethay extnay orningmay otay
uestionqay usay youngay arriedmay eoplepay. Erhay opeshay oweverhay ovedpray unfounded.ay
Anday inay isthay onditioncay ouray affairsay emainedray uringday ethay extnay inenay yearsay
ithoutway ethay eastlay ange.”chay

Ethay Empressay asway otnay atisfiedsay ithway oneay ay’sday elebrationcay ofay ethay
arriagemay. Ethay estivitiesfay ereway olongedpray orfay entay aysday. Ethay eetsstray ereway
ivengay overay otay erry-making;may eraldshay onay orseback,hay ountainsfay outingspay
ine,way ire-worksfay anday itewhay ights,nay anday allay ethay ellsbay anday annonscay ofay
Etersburgpay ademay aay ontinuouscay arnivalcay. Anay unbrokenay uccessionsay ofay
inners,day operas,ay asquerades,may anday uadrillesqay owdedcray uponay eachay other.ay

Ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay asway ardhay utpay otay itay otay escribeday esethay estivitiesfay
adequatelyay otay erhay ousespay. Orfay ehay asway otnay esentpray. Omehowsay ethay
invitationay ichwhay ouldshay avehay oughtbray ethay Incepray ofay Erbstzay otay ishay
aughter’sday eddingway adhay evernay eenbay entsay. Ehay adhay expecteday itay omfray eekway otay
eek,way incesay Ederickfray adhay oldtay emthay atthay itay ouldway urelysay omecay. Inay ethay
end,ay ethay olday Incepray asway overlookeday anday adhay otay onsolecay imselfhay ithway ishay
ife’sway escriptionday ofay ishay aughter’sday eddingway. Ethay exuberantay Incesspray
ote,wray E“Thay Andgray Uchessday endssay youay erhay espects,ray utbay ashay onay imetay otay
ite,wray incesay itay isay illstay osay ewnay orfay erhay otay ebay ithway erhay usbandhay. Eythay
ancay arcelyscay ebay eparatedsay orfay aay uarterqay ofay anay our.”hay

Ethay ittlelay Andgray Uchessday ovedmay oughthray everythingay ikelay anay automaton.ay
Eshay eppedstay oughthray ethay itewhay anday oldgay uadrillesqay ithway earstay inay erhay
eyes.ay Ever“Nay inay ymay ife,”lay aidsay eshay afterward,ay Ave“hay Iay eensay aay oremay
oefulway anday upidstay amusementay anthay ereway osethay uadrilles.”qay Ethay eginningbay
ofay erhay oneymoonhay asway ustjay asay oefulway. After“ay ymay edding,”way eshay aid,say I“ay
eltfay estbay enwhay Iay asway ithway ymay othermay. Iay ovestray allay ethay oremay eagerlyay otay
aystay ithway erhay asay ymay ouseholdhay ouldcay arcelyscay ebay alledcay easantplay. Ethay
Andgray Ukeday adhay othingnay utbay ild’schay ayplay inay ishay ead;hay ehay avegay imselfhay
upay otay ayingplay atay oldiers,say urroundedsay ybay ishay enialsmay inay omwhay aloneay ehay
owedshay anyay interest.”ay

Ivay

ATHERINEcay ECOMESbay Aay OTHERmay


Otway eeksway afteray ethay edding,way ethay Empressay entsay ethay youngay arriedmay airpay
ithway ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay otay Arskoeczay Elosay. Itay asway ethay onthmay ofay
Eptembersay anday ethay irchesbay ereway urningtay otay oldgay. Utbay ethay idebray adhay
uddenlysay ostlay erhay enthusiasmay orfay ethay Ussianray enescay. Orfay ethay irstfay imetay
eshay asway omesickhay orfay Ermanygay anday eadeddray ethay omentmay ofay erhay other’smay
epartureday. At“ay atthay imetay Iay ouldway avehay ivengay uchmay ifay Iay ouldcay avehay eftlay
ethay ountrycay ithway er.”hay

Eshay asway ustained,say owever,hay ybay aay ewnay ensesay ofay owerpay anday importanceay
ichwhay amecay omfray avinghay oneymay inay erhay ocketpay. Isthay enableday erhay otay
atronizepay erhay othermay ybay assumingay erhay ebts,day orfay ethay extravagantay
Incesspray adhay obligationsay amountingay otay eventysay ousandthay ublesray anday onay
ideaay owhay eshay asway everay oinggay otay eetmay emthay. Atherinecay omisedpray otay aypay
inay erhay other’smay eadstay aay umsay ichwhay asway absurdlyay eyondbay erhay eans,may orfay
ethay Empressay alloweday erhay onlyay irtythay ousandthay ublesray aay year.ay Iftedlay osay
uddenlysay omfray ethay eagermay ircumstancescay ofay erhay Ettinstay ife,lay ethay Andgray
Uchessday adhay onay easuremay orfay erhay ewlynay acquireday ichesray. Eythay eemedsay otay
erhay imitlesslay. Ofay oursecay eshay asway inay aay ositionpay otay omecay otay erhay other’smay
assistanceay anday eshay amecay. Evenay ifay erhay ewnay usbandhay idday otnay ovelay erhay eshay
asway aay ichray omanway ownay anday ouldcay afforday otay ebay enerousgay. Isthay asway ethay
eginningbay ofay aay abyrinthlay ofay ebtday inay ichwhay eshay ogressivelypray involveday
erselfhay untilay itay oughtbray erhay ithinway aay ewfay yearsay otay ethay ergevay ofay
ankruptcybay.

Atay ethay enday ofay Eptembersay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay anday Uleinfräay Aynkhay
etsay orthfay onay eirthay omewardhay ourneyjay. Eythay ereway adenlay ithway esentspray
omfray ethay Empress.ay Otway estschay illedfay ithway Inesechay anday Amasceneday uffsstay
accompanieday ethay avellers;tray anday otay onsolecay ethay ong-neglectedlay Incepray ofay
Erbst,zay ishay ifeway arriedcay ithway erhay asay iftsgay omfray ethay Andgray Ukeday iamondday
oe-buckles,shay iamondday oat-buttons,cay anday aay iamond-studdedday aggerday. Ethay
artypay asway escorteday ybay Atherinecay anday Eterpay asay arfay asay Asnoe-Selo,kray ethay
olday Edray Illagevay ofay ethay Ars,czay erewhay ethay Incesspray anday erhay aughterday awsay
eachay otheray orfay ethay astlay imetay. I“ay eptway aay eatgray eal,”day ayssay Atherine,cay
And“ay inay orderay otnay otay akemay emay illstay oremay adsay ymay othermay entway awayay ithoutway
akingtay eavelay ofay e.”may

Asay oonsay asay eshay arriveday ome,hay ethay Andgray Uchessday entway otay indfay erhay
avoritefay aidenmay Ariamay Etrovnapay Ukov,shay otay omfortcay erhay inay erhay
onelinesslay. Utbay ethay irlgay adhay isappearedday uringday Atherine’scay absence.ay
Itay evelopedday atthay eshay adhay eenbay entsay awayay atay ethay uggestionsay ofay ethay
Incesspray ofay Erbstzay. Ethay Incesspray anday ethay Empressay adhay utpay eirthay eadshay
ogethertay overay ethay unpromisingay atusstay ofay ethay ewly-madenay arriagemay anday
ethay anishmentbay ofay Ariamay asway ethay esultray. Eythay ememberedray ethay artpay ichwhay
Uliejay onvay Engdenmay adhay ayedplay inay alienatingay ethay ormerfay egent,ray Annaay
Eopoldovna,lay omfray erhay usband,hay anday eythay earedfay atthay Ariamay Ukovshay ightmay
ayplay aay imilarsay artpay ybay increasingay ethay estrangementay etweenbay Atherinecay
anday Eterpay. Ethay Andgray Uchessday earnedlay enthay atthay eshay ouldcay evernay avehay aay
onfidantecay inay ethay uturefay.

Anythingay ichwhay emindedray Elisabethay ofay Annaay Eopoldovna’slay amilyfay asway
atefulhay otay erhay. Eshay ishedway otay orgetfay ethay eposedday Egentray ifay ossible,pay
utbay ethay etchedwray oman,way asay ifay otay evengeray erselfhay onay ethay Empress,ay adhay
ontinuedcay otay increaseay erhay amilyfay atay egularray intervals.ay Ourfay ildrenchay
adhay eenbay ornbay otay erhay atay Olmogory,kay otway ofay omwhay ereway onssay. Ethay Ajormay inay
argechay entsay aay aithfulfay eportray ofay eachay irthbay otay ethay Empress,ay owhay oretay
ishay eportsray otay iecespay. Atay astlay ehay entsay aay eportray ichwhay eshay idday otnay eartay
intoay iecespay. Ethay olificpray Annaay adhay iedday inay ildbedchay. Ethay Empressay avegay
ordersay atthay ethay odybay ofay ethay eceasedday Egentray ouldshay ebay issected,day anday
oughtbray otay Etersburgpay orfay urialbay. Accompanieday ybay ethay Andgray Uchess,day
othbay apeddray inay eavyhay ack,blay eshay attendeday ethay uneralfay eremoniescay inay ethay
Alexanderay Evskynay Athedralcay erewhay ethay ill-starreday Annaay asway aidlay otay estray
etweenbay erhay andmothergray anday erhay othermay. Erhay andmothergray asway ethay olday
Arinaczay Ascoviapray Eodorovna,fay owhay adhay aidlay aay ursecay onay erhay aughter,day
anday erhay othermay asway ethay aughterday owhay adhay eenbay ursedcay. Ethay unluckyay Annaay
eighedway onay Atherine’scay onsciencecay otnay aay ittlelay.

Ethay eathday ofay Annaay occurreday aboutay inenay onthsmay afteray ethay arriagemay ofay ethay
Andgray Ucalday airpay. Ethay Empressay avegay emthay anotheray onthmay ofay acegray ilewhay
eshay epairedray ithway erhay avoritefay otay endspay Aymay atay Arskoeczay Elosay. Esentlypray
eshay eturned,ray advancingay uponay ethay erilestay ouplecay ikelay aay eateningthray
Unojay. Eshay adhay apparentlyay expecteday atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday ould,way ithoutway
eliminarypray arningway oray ymptoms,say esentpray erhay ithway aay Omanovray eirhay inay ethay
inthnay onthmay afteray arriagemay. Isappointedday inay erhay opes,hay eshay ooktay asticdray
easuresmay otay emedyray ethay ituationsay.

Isthay imetay itay asway Estushevbay anday ethay Empressay owhay utpay eirthay eadshay
ogethertay. Estushev,bay itay illway ebay emembered,ray adhay otnay avoredfay isthay
arriagemay anday Elisabeth’say iscontentmentday ithway itsay esultsray irectedday
erhay oughtsthay owardtay imhay. Atay erhay its’way end,ay eshay askeday imhay otay eviseday aay
ime,régay aay ogram,pray orfay ethay youngay eople,pay ichwhay ehay idday ithway iritspay anday
enthusiasm.ay Ehay avegay ethay Empressay anay elaborateay emorandummay oncerningcay ethay
ehaviourbay ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday anday aay illstay oremay elaborateay emorandummay
oncerningcay ethay ehaviourbay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday. Ethay instructionsay ereway
orfay ethay useay ofay ethay uardiansgay owhay ereway otay aketay argechay ofay ethay airpay.
Estushev’sbay ocumentday ehearsedray atay engthlay ethay aultsfay ofay ethay Andgray Uke:day
ishay isrespectfulday ehaviourbay inay urch;chay ishay eaknessway orfay oystay anday intay
oldiers;say ishay amiliarityfay ithway agespay anday ackeys;lay ishay owlay anguage,lay
ishay imaces,gray ishay indecenciesay atay abletay. Inay ort,shay ethay Ice-Chancellorvay
ewdray aay icturepay ofay ethay Ussianray eir-apparenthay atthay ightmay avehay eenbay
istakenmay orfay ethay ortraitpay ofay aay ildchay inay ibsbay. Allay ofay itsay atementsstay areay
onfirmedcay ybay Atherinecay inay erhay emoirsmay. Ethay ulesray ichwhay ehay eparedpray orfay
ethay Andgray Uchessday onsistedcay entirelyay ofay ohibitions,pray iefchay ofay ichwhay
asway aay anbay onay allay ivatepray orrespondencecay ithway erhay other,may ethay Incesspray
ofay Erbstzay. Isthay ovedray ethay irlgay otay undergrounday ommunicationscay inay ichwhay
eshay ecamebay atay astlay eryvay ilfulskay anday earnedlay otay useay itay orfay oliticalpay
ends.ay

Ethay eystonekay ofay ethay ewnay imerégay asway ethay appointmentay ofay aay arriedmay ouplecay
asay uardiansgay. Ethay Oglokovschay ereway osenchay orfay ecialspay easonsray. Ariamay
Oglokovchay adhay arriedmay erhay usbandhay orfay ovelay anday asway ownknay otay allay ethay
ourtcay asay ethay atternpay ofay aay aithfulfay anday evotedday ifeway. Estushevbay oughtbray
ethay youngay atronmay otay ethay Andgray Uchess’sday apartmentay anday introduceday erhay asay
ethay ewnay overnessgay oray uennaday. Immediately,”“ay ayssay Atherine,cay I“ay eganbay otay
eepway iolently.”vay Isthay idday otnay elphay otay ingratiateay erhay overnessgay. Ethay
atmosphereay ecamebay ystericalhay. Atherinecay entway otay edbay orfay aay olewhay ayday anday
adhay otay ebay edblay ethay extnay orningmay. Ethay Empressay amecay anday oldedscay angrily.ay
Youngay ivesway owhay idday otnay ovelay eirthay usbandshay alwaysay ept;way Atherine’scay
othermay adhay assureday erhay atthay Atherinecay adhay onay objectionay otay arryingmay ethay
Andgray Uke;day e,shay ethay Empress,ay adhay otnay orcedfay erhay otay arrymay im;hay and,ay
inally,fay ownay atthay eythay ereway alreadyay arriedmay erethay asway onay useay inay yingcray
aboutay it.ay Oroughlythay ightenedfray atay ethay Empress’say isplayday ofay emper,tay
Atherinecay urmured,may Ittle“Lay other,may orgivefay e,may Iay amay inay ethay ong.”wray Eshay
earedfay atthay ethay Empressay ouldway actuallyay eatbay erhay asay eshay idday ometimessay
eatbay ethay adieslay anday entlemengay ofay ethay ourtcay.

Ethay ewnay uennaday erformedpay erhay utiesday ell,way ettingsay ethay oodgay exampleay
ichwhay ethay Empressay adhay expecteday ofay erhay. Om“Fray 1746ay untilay ethay eathday ofay
erhay usband,”hay ayssay Atherine,cay O“whay iedday inay ethay yearay 1754,ay eway eallyray
evernay awsay erhay exceptay egnantpray oray inay ildbed.”chay Ethay Andgray Uchessday
atedhay ethay olificpray Ariamay anday onay onderway. Arcelyscay asway ethay etchedwray
Annaay Eopoldovnalay ellway undergrounday anthay isthay ewnay anday ividvay eproachray
angspray upay eforebay erhay eryvay eyes.ay Ethay Olmogorykay amilyfay adhay eenbay atay eastlay
invisibleay utbay Aria’smay abiesbay ereway ornbay underay erhay eryvay eyesay anday ereway
eraldedhay asay importantay ublicpay events.ay Estushevbay otewray otay Ountcay Orontsovvay
inay Ondon,lay In“ay esethay aysday itay ashay easedplay erhay Imperialay Ajestymay otay
ommissioncay Icolainay Aumovichnay Oglokovchay otay ourneyjay otay ethay Omanray Emperoray
otay ongratulatecay imhay onay ethay attainmentay ofay ishay ighhay istinction;day ehay illway
ot,nay owever,hay epartday eforebay ishay ifeway ashay eenbay elivered;day atthay is,ay ethay
iddlemay ofay Arch.”may Onay ethay 14thay ofay Archmay Estushevbay added:ay In“ay esethay aysday
Ariamay Emionovnasay ..ay. ashay ivengay irthbay otay anay infantay aughterday. Anday Icolainay
Aumovichnay illway epartday oonsay omfray erehay otay Ienna.”vay

Ethay Empressay opedhay apparentlyay atthay Aria’smay ertilityfay asway omethingsay ichwhay
ethay Andgray Uchessday ightmay acquireay ybay associationay anday imitation.ay Yetay yearay
afteray yearay assedpay ybay anday ethay iraclemay idday otnay appenhay. Atherinecay emainedray
ildlesschay ilewhay Ariamay orebay aay ildchay everyay year.ay Inay itingwray erhay emoirsmay
opsdray ofay allgay allfay omfray erhay enpay eneverwhay eshay eaksspay ofay ethay Oglokovschay.
Although“ay ehay asway ovedlay osay uchmay ehay asway otnay atay allay ovablelay. Ofay allay ethay
eoplepay inay ethay orld,way ehay asway ethay ostmay uffedpay upay anday onceited;cay ehay
oughtthay imselfhay extraordinarilyay eautifulbay anday everclay. Ehay asway aay upidstay
oxcomb,cay arrogantay anday iteful,spay anday atay ethay eastlay uiteqay asay aliciousmay asay
ishay ife,way owhay asway osay otnay aay ittle.”lay Ethay Andgray Uchessday alloweday erselfhay
allsmay evengesray atthay ereway otnay uiteqay efinedray. Oneay ofay erhay aidensmay adhay
aay icktray ofay imitatingay ithway aay illowpay ethay alkway ofay ethay egnantpray Ariamay.
Atherinecay encourageday erhay inay isthay erformancepay ybay ealspay ofay appreciativeay
aughterlay. Erhay itefulnessspay extendeday itselfay otay Aria’smay istersay Arfamay.
Ow“Hay arfay ethay upiditystay ofay isthay omanway entway isay ownshay ybay ethay ollowingfay
ettypray ory:stay eshay asway uiteqay astonisheday atay ethay evernessclay ofay ethay idwifemay
owhay ophesiedpray atthay eshay ouldway ingbray eitheray aay oybay oray aay irlgay intoay ethay
orldway. Eshay ouldcay otnay understanday encewhay ethay idwifemay adhay isthay owledge.”knay

Adamemay Oglokovchay anday erhay istersay ereway Avronskys,skay iecesnay ofay ethay
Empress.ay Eythay epresentedray ethay ockstay omfray ichwhay Elisabethay adhay ungspray onay
erhay other’smay idesay. Ethay Avronskysskay ereway oremay ominentpray inay ethay Empress’say
environmentay anthay ethay Omanovray idesay ofay erhay amily,fay anday Atherinecay
ikedlay otay ememberray atthay ethay Empressay asway aay Avronskyskay. Ethay ouseshay ofay
Erbstzay anday Olstein,hay althoughay impoverished,ay idday otnay oducepray omenway asay
eak-wittedway asay ethay Empress’say iecesnay. Atherinecay oundfay inay atthay omparisoncay
aay atisfactionsay orfay erhay esentmentray anday ealousyjay.


2ay

Erhay emoirsmay escribeday aay ine-years’nay urgatorypay ofay entalmay anday ysicalphay
ufferingsay. Eshay ayssay utbay ittlelay ofay erhay attitudeay owardtay ethay Andgray Ukeday
utbay atthay ittlelay isay ignificantsay. Enwhay ethay Empressay accuseday erhay ofay otnay
ovinglay im,hay eshay okespay ethay uth,tray orfay Atherinecay ayssay erselfhay at,thay asay
aay otectionpray againstay ealousyjay eshay ooledschay erselfhay otay ebay indifferentay
owardtay erhay usbandhay.

Eter,pay owhay adhay allay ethay idepray ichwhay oesgay ithway aay eakway ersonality,pay
iedtray otay onsolecay imselfhay inay ethay usualay ayway. Ehay ecamebay aay oodgay ealday ofay
aay adies’lay anmay. Inay endertay ancesglay anday inay omplimentscay ehay asway otnay atay
allay ackward;bay ehay ouldcay ivegay anay excellentay imitationay ofay aay youngay anmay inay
ovelay. Ishay osepay asway osay oodgay atthay itay eceivedday ishay auntay anday umiliatedhay
ishay ifeway. Ehay ecamebay etterbay anday etterbay atay it.ay Inallyfay ehay entereday intoay aay
elationshipray ithway Elisabethay Orontsovvay owhay amecay otay ebay egardedray asay aay ealray
istressmay. Atherinecay ewknay atthay Eterpay asway incompetentay otay avehay aay ysicalphay
elationshipray utbay eshay ealizedray atthay othersay idday otnay owknay it.ay Asay Eter’spay
affectationsay ewgray ishay actualay onditioncay ecamebay orseway. Ornay idday ethay onystay
indifferenceay ofay ishay ifeway elphay otay akemay adbay attersmay anyay etterbay. Onay ethay
ontrary,cay itay elpedhay otay akemay emthay orseway. Ethay Andgray Ukeday ystallizedcray
intoay aay ittlelay anikinmay incapableay ofay eelingsfay ofay anyay indkay.

Atherine’scay ifelay asway ullfay ofay illnessay anday ypochondriahay. Aay ataloguecay ofay
erhay ailmentsay ancay ebay ademay upay omfray erhay eminiscencesray. Eshay illsfay upay agespay
ithway oriesstay ofay eadaches,hay oothaches,tay insomnia,ay influenzaay anday easlesmay.
Eshay escribesday esethay afflictionsay ithway aay erioussay attentionay otay etailday
ichwhay eshay arcelyscay achieveday inay escribingday ethay Urkishtay Arsway ofay erhay
aterlay years.ay Eshay ayssay impressivelyay atthay erhay oldscay ereway osay everesay atthay
eshay useday elvetway ocket-handkerchiefspay aay ayday. Atay oneay imetay erhay ysicianphay
oughtthay eshay adhay uberculosistay. Ehay ordereday erhay otay edbay anday utpay erhay onay aay
ietday ofay ass’say ilkmay. Eshay ufferedsay omfray aay onsumingcay earfay ofay allpoxsmay anday
everyay imetay anythingay entway ongwray ithway erhay eshay elievedbay erselfhay ickenstray.
Onceay itay urnedtay outay onlyay otay ebay easles,may utbay erhay ots,spay eshay assuresay us,ay
ereway asay argelay asay ublesray. Allay ofay erhay illnessesay anday afflictionsay uringday
osethay yearsay ereway ethay orstway atthay ouldcay ebay ufferedsay anday urvivedsay.

Ethay orystay ofay erhay ull-bonesskay ashay aay amaticdray imaxclay anday aay appyhay ending.ay
Uring“Day isthay entireay year,”ay ayssay ethay eroine,hay I“ay ufferedsay ontinuallycay
omfray eadachehay anday eeplessnessslay. Adamemay Usekray oughtbray emay asay aay o-calledsay
edicinemay aay assglay ofay Ungarianhay ineway afteray Iay aylay inay ed,bay ichwhay Iay asway
upposedsay otay inkdray egularlyray everyay evening.ay Iay efusedray isthay emedyray orfay
eeplessnessslay anday Aufray Usekray ankdray itay inay ymay eadstay anday otay ymay ealthhay.
Afteray Iay adhay eturnedray otay ethay ity,cay Iay omplainedcay otay dray. Oerhaavebay ofay
ymay ufferingssay. Ehay asway aay eryvay ympatheticsay an;may ehay alsoay ewknay ethay indkay
ofay ifelay Iay ivedlay anday ewknay ymay elationray otay ymay usbandhay asay ellway asay otay ymay
environment.ay Ehay adebay emay owshay imhay ymay eadhay omesay orningmay eforebay ymay airhay
asway esseddray anday arefullycay ehay entway overay ethay ullskay. Inallyfay ehay aidsay at,thay
althoughay Iay asway eventeensay yearsay old,ay ymay eadhay adhay ethay ormationfay ofay aay
ix-year-oldsay ild;chay atthay Iay ustmay ebay eryvay arefulcay anday evernay alloway ethay
upperay artpay ofay ymay ullskay otay etgay old;cay inay ort,shay ethay onesbay ofay ymay eadhay adhay
evernay yetay osedclay up.ay Ehay elievedbay atthay ethay onesbay ouldway onlyay oseclay upay
enwhay Iay adhay eachedray ethay ageay ofay enty-fivetway oray enty-sixtway anday atthay isthay
asway ethay ausecay ofay ymay eadacheshay. Iay ollowedfay ishay adviceay anday itay asway aay actfay
atthay ethay eparationsay etweenbay ethay ull-bonesskay isappearedday onlyay enwhay Iay asway
enty-fivetway oray enty-sixtway yearsay olday asay ehay adhay ophesied.”pray

Isthay appyhay urecay ofay Atherine’scay ullskay oincidedcay ithway ethay irthbay ofay erhay
irstfay ildchay ichwhay occurreday enwhay eshay asway alfwayhay etweenbay enty-fivetway

accurateay atesday.

Atherinecay icturespay erhay experienceay ithway oothachetay anday ooth-pullingtay
ithway oremay anthay Ussianray ealismray. Enty-fivetway yearsay afteray eshay adhay ostlay

iscoveredday atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay ostlay aay iecepay ofay aw-bonejay As“ay

Atherinecay asway apablecay ofay ashesflay ofay ychologicalpsay insight.ay

Y“May ituationsay asway eallyray otnay otay ebay aughedlay at,”ay eshay ayssay. I“ay oodstay

oneay idesay. Alreadyay Iay eptway uchmay esslay enwhay Iay asway aloneay anthay inay ethay irstfay

Ethay Empressay adhay ivengay Oranienbaumay otay Eterpay orfay aay ummersay esidenceray.
Erehay ethay youngay eoplepay edlay aay omparativelycay eefray ifelay. Atherinecay useday

ethay ummersay awn,day erhay omanticray usingsmay ereway ingledmay ithway ambitiousay
oughtsthay. At“ay atthay imetay Iay eadray onlyay omancesray ichwhay eatedhay ymay antasy,phay

erhay oughtsthay ereway occupieday arfay oremay anthay Elisabeth’say adhay everay eenbay ithway
oughtsthay ofay ethay owncray anday ethay uccessionsay.

Ometimessay orfay asay uchmay asay irteenthay ourshay aay ayday eshay oderay orsebackhay. Itay
asway anay exerciseay ichwhay eshay assionatelypay ovedlay. Eneverwhay eshay ouchestay

iding-bootray. Ethay actressay inay ueblay elvetvay omwhay ittlelay Ikefay adhay eensay atay
ethay ageay ofay eethray ouldcay ardlyhay avehay expecteday ore!may Atherine’scay orsebackhay

Empress.ay Eshay eferredpray otay ideray astrideay anday ethay Empressay earedfay atthay

3ay

Inay Estushevbay anday ishay asticdray Instructions,ay Elisabethay adhay exhausteday erhay

Ukeday isay aay itnessway atthay Iay avehay oneday everythingay otay ersuadepay imhay alsoay otay

Yetay ethay Empressay alledcay er,hay Ochen“ay upriany,”ay eryvay ubborn,stay anday efusedray

Uringday ethay econdsay ingspray ollowingfay erhay arriage,may Atherinecay eceivedray

Ethay Empress’say irritationay ademay erhay ariablevay empertay oremay ariablevay anthay

assmay ilewhay ethay ourshay owlyslay assedpay omfray ourfay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay otay

Ethay ishesway ofay ethay youngay ourtcay ereway evernay onsulted,cay evenay ormally,fay

Atherine’scay ewnay oman,way Ascoviapray Ikitichnanay Adislav,vlay ademay anay

Eterpay ouldway otnay istenlay otay Ascoviapray. Ehay asway omesickhay orfay Olsteinhay anday

inallyfay isappearedday ompletely,cay ishay Eimwehhay increased.ay Ethay astlay otay ogay

Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay anday inallyfay anishedbay otay Uglitch.ay Ethay Empressay
asway oneday ithway Ermansgay orfay allay imetay.

Atherinecay eemedsay otay orgetfay eryvay easilyay ethay olday iendsfray ofay erhay other’smay

ircumstancescay. Orfay erethay isay onay enyingday eythay ereway intenselyay yingtray.
Or“Fay eighteenay years,”ay eshay ites,wray I“ay avehay edlay aay ifelay omfray ichwhay entay
othersay ouldway avehay onegay insaneay anday entytway inay ymay aceplay ouldway avehay iedday ofay

Ethay ettypay ersecutionspay ofay ethay Empressay ereway ethay onlyay ingthay atthay ewdray ethay

Uringday ethay irstfay eekway ofay Ent,lay ethay Empressay ordereday Atherinecay anday Eterpay
otay ogay otay ethay eamstay ath,bay asay aay artpay ofay ethay egularray eparationpray orfay

adhay erishedpay omfray isobedienceday. Uch“May ofay is,”thay Atherinecay eflected,ray
atchingway Adamemay Oglokov,chay Omes“cay omfray erselfhay utbay uchmay isay omfray ethay
Empress.ay Iay amecay otay ethay onclusioncay atthay ethay eatthray ofay ethay ortressfay
ustmay avehay omecay omfray ethay onarchmay anday Iay awsay inay itay aay ignsay ofay erhay ongstray
esentmentray againstay ethay Andgray Uke.”day

Ethay ischief-makingmay Ariamay eportedray allay isthay ackbay otay ethay Empress,ay osewhay
athwray aredflay outay inay erhay usualay ongstray anguage:lay Ery“Vay ood;gay ifay ehay isay
osay isobedientday owardtay e,may Iay illway otnay isskay ishay amnedday andhay anyay ore.”may
Isthay asway aithfullyfay arriedcay ackbay otay ethay Andgray Ukeday owhay aid,say At“Thay
ependsday onay erselfhay. Utbay Iay illway evernay ogay intoay ethay athbay. Iay annotcay earbay
ethay eat.”hay Ethay Empressay eptkay erhay ordway anday erhay ephewnay eptkay ishay. Yetay eshay
evernay avegay upay ethay attemptay otay orcefay imhay intoay ethay athbay. Ehay asway otnay againay
