4ay

Elisabeth’say apriciousnesscay increased.ay Avinghay angedchay erhay urniturefay
anday everythingay elseay inay erhay environmentay atthay ouldcay ebay anged,chay atay astlay
eshay angedchay erhay avoritefay. Ethay easy-goingay Azumovskyray asway isplacedday anday
elegatedray ithway onorshay anday ichesray otay ivatepray ifelay. Erethay isay aay aditiontray
atthay ethay Ountcay adhay eenbay ecretlysay arriedmay otay Elisabeth.ay Etherwhay isthay
ebay uetray oray otnay oesday otnay attermay uchmay. Ethay imetay adhay omecay orfay imhay otay ogay.
Ethay iscardedday overlay etiredray otay ethay Anitchkovay Alacepay ichwhay ethay Empressay
adhay uiltbay orfay imhay anday erewhay ehay eameddray awayay ishay ifelay orfay anotheray entytway
years.ay Azumovskyray asway aay armingchay ecorationday onay ethay earlyay eignray ofay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay. Ehay asway ollywhay impracticalay anday ithoutway ambitionay ofay
anyay ind,kay aay oeticpay indolentay Ukrainian.ay Ehay asway oyallay otay ishay istressmay otay
ethay enday anday evotedday otay erhay uccessor,say Atherinecay ethay Eatgray.

Ivanay Ivanovichay Uvalov,shay ethay ewnay avorite,fay asway aay ousincay. Asay ethay Empressay
ewgray olderay eshay ufferedsay increasinglyay omfray elancholymay ichwhay eshay ovestray
otay ightenlay ybay awingdray ethay irclecay ofay elativesray oserclay arounday erhay. Ivanay
Ivanovichay asway ablyay upportedsay inay ishay ewnay utiesday ybay ishay amilyfay. Ehay adhay aay
ister,say aay eerfulchay ersonpay omwhay ethay Empressay eliedray uponay otay escueray erhay
omfray owlay iritsspay. Ehay adhay esidesbay otway othersbray owhay uardedgay imhay onay othbay
anksflay anday eapedray aay ichray arvesthay ofay onopoliesmay. Ethay Uvalovshay othersbray
ereway ambitiousay anday aspinggray asay ethay Azumovskysray adhay evernay eenbay. Eirthay
adventay ademay aay eatgray ifferenceday atay ourt,cay orfay ethay Empress,ay owhay ecamebay
oremay indolentay anday antasticfay everyay ay,day avegay oremay anday oremay owerpay otay
ethay Uvalovsshay. Eshay adhay ailedfay inay erhay earestday eme:schay erhay ephewnay anday
uccessor,say ethay Andgray Ukeday Eter,pay adhay onay eirhay.

Ithway ethay yearay 1750ay ethay oblempray ofay anay eirhay eemedsay otay owgray esperateday.
Inay ethay Andgray Ucalday ampcay aay ealisticray iewvay asway owinggray up.ay Itay asway
epresentedray ieflychay ybay Adamemay Adislav,vlay Atherine’scay ady-in-waiting,lay
anday ybay ethay othermay ofay youngay Ergeisay Altikov,say aay youngay amberlainchay ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Owlyslay ethay ideaay ooktay apeshay ithoutway anybody’say expressingay
itay atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday ight,may ybay erelymay ansgressingtray erhay arriagemay
ows,vay edeemray ethay ituationsay. Ybay omesay eansmay isthay ideaay asway insinuateday
intoay ethay eadshay ofay ethay upidstay Oglokovschay owhay afterwardsay oughtthay eythay
adhay inventeday it.ay Ariamay Oglokovchay uggestedsay itay otay Atherine;cay utpay itay otay
er,hay osay otay eak,spay asay erhay atrioticpay utyday. Itay eemssay atherray odday atthay allay
ofay emthay adhay eenbay osay owslay inay omingcay otay isthay anplay. Apparentlyay Atherinecay
ouldway avehay onegay onay indefinitelyay inay ethay ilemmaday ifay ethay olderay arriedmay
omenway adhay otnay inallyfay uggestedsay aay ayway out.ay

Atherinecay otewray otway accountsay ofay erhay affairay ithway Ergeisay Altikovsay. Oneay
asway etsay ownday onlyay eethray oray ourfay yearsay afteray itay asway over,ay anday ethay otheray
eshay otewray inay erhay olday age.ay Ethay olday ady’slay orystay isay aay ivelylay omance,ray
ortrayingpay anay ardentay ourtship,cay aay orsebackhay ide,ray aay onelylay island,ay anday
anay importunateay overlay. Ethay youngay oman’sway orystay isay esslay omanticray anday
oremay oliticalpay. Eshay ayssay inay isthay ersion:vay Adame“May Oglokovchay useday allay
ossiblepay artsay ofay ersuasionpay otay educesay emay. Isthay anday ethay attractivenessay
anday alentstay ofay imhay orfay omwhay eshay okespay ouldway avehay oundfay esslay esistanceray
inay anotheray anthay inay emay. Itay isay eallyray uetray atthay Iay asway istinguishedday ybay
iscretionday anday exemplaryay innocence.”ay

Ergeisay Altikovsay asway aay errymay anday irresponsibleay youthay ithoutway ulterioray
ambitions.ay Ishay elationsray ithway ethay Andgray Uchessday eganbay inay ethay yearay 1752,ay
Inay Ecemberday ofay atthay yearay ethay Andgray Uchessday eportedray iscarriagemay. Ethay
ollowingfay Ulyjay ethay amesay isfortunemay efellbay erhay. Eshay eemedsay oomedday otay
adbay ucklay anday elayday. Otnay untilay ethay 20thay ofay Eptember,say 1754,ay idday eshay
actuallyay ecomebay aay othermay. Onay atthay ateday eshay orebay aay onsay. Ere“Thay asway
inexpressibleay oyjay overay it,”ay isay erhay aconiclay ommentcay. Itay asway aboutay isthay
ime,tay accordingay otay erhay emoirs,may atthay erhay ull-bonesskay osedclay up.ay

Etherwhay ethay Empressay asway awareay ofay ethay intrigueay etweenbay Atherinecay anday
Ergeisay Altikovsay eway oday otnay owknay. Eway oday ow,knay owever,hay atthay ithway ethay
yearay 1754ay erhay attitudeay owardtay ethay youngay ountcay underwentay aay ecidedday
angechay. Oglokovchay anday ishay ifeway awsay eatgray ossibilitiespay orfay ethay uture,fay
opinghay otay eapray ethay editcray orfay ethay ewnay anday atifyinggray urntay ofay events.ay
Enwhay ethay Empressay eganbay otay urntay aay iendlyfray azegay uponay ethay youngay ourt,cay
Oglokovchay ostlay ishay eadhay anday iedtray otay ooway erhay. Atherinecay admitsay atthay eshay
anday erhay ischievousmay Ergeisay encourageday isthay indiscretionay ichwhay inviteday
angersday unforeseenay ybay eirthay inexperienceay anday youth.ay Ethay othersbray
Uvalovshay ereway onglystray intrencheday anday ereway eadyray otay akemay ortshay iftshray
ofay anyay ivalray. Atay aay asquerademay all,bay ethay oftenedsay Empressay encourageday
Oglokovchay ithway endertay ancesglay. Ivanay Ivanovich,ay ethay avorite,fay awsay emthay
anday ishay anclay osedclay inay arounday er,hay atay once,ay anday insidiously.ay Inay ethay
enday Oglokovchay asway insulteday ybay ethay Empressay inay ublicpay. E“Shay alledcay im,”hay
ayssay Atherine,cay In“ay aay ublicpay onversationcay atay innerday aay ockheadblay anday
aay aitor,tray ichwhay ehay osay ooktay otay earthay atthay ehay ellfay intoay ethay aundicejay.
Andoid,kay ethay Uvalov’sshay an,may asway alledcay in,ay and,ay asay ehay adhay onglay ownknay
atthay ethay atientpay asway anay enemyay ofay eirs,thay elievedbay atthay ehay ouldway oday emthay
aay avorfay ybay urderingmay imhay. Atay eastlay allay ethay octorsday owhay ereway alledcay
inay uringday ishay astlay aysday aintainedmay atthay ehay adhay eenbay eatedtray ikelay aay
eaturecray omwhay oneay ishedway otay illkay. Ourfay aysday afteray ishay eathday ishay ifeway
asway oldtay atthay eshay ouldcay emainray inay Oscow...may. Iay elievebay atthay Altikovsay
ouldway avehay eenbay anishedbay atay atthay imetay ootay ifay Iay adhay otnay eenbay egnantpray
anday eythay adhay otnay earedfay otay afflictay emay ithway isthay ief.”gray

Atay astlay ethay idwifemay eclaredday atthay ethay omentmay asway atay andhay. Ethay Empress,ay
owhay occupieday adjoiningay ambers,chay asway ummonedsay omfray erhay edbay atay otway
o’clockay inay ethay orningmay. Eshay eptsway uponay ethay enescay inay aay antlemay ofay ueblay
atin,say orfay ethay oomray asway oldcay ithway ethay illchay ofay aay atelay Eptembersay awnday.
Atay oondaynay ethay ildchay asway ornbay. Ethay Empressay aitedway onlyay orfay ethay idwifemay
otay athebay anday addlesway ethay infant.ay Enthay eshay alledcay ethay iestpray anday adhay
imhay istenedchray Aulpay. Isthay asway ethay amenay ofay ethay irstfay ildchay ornbay otay
erhay othermay anday Eterpay ethay Eat,gray aay astardbay onsay owhay adhay iedday atay ethay
ageay ofay eethray. Ommandingcay ethay idwifemay otay arrycay ethay ildchay inay ontfray ofay
er,hay ethay Empressay etiredray otay erhay ownay apartmentsay erewhay eshay arrangeday aay
urserynay anday aredcay orfay imhay ithway erhay ownay andshay. Ifay ehay imperedwhay eshay
anray otay imhay atay once;ay erhay evotionday ecamebay ethay ubjectsay ofay ideway ommentcay
anday eneralgay aisepray. Itay avegay iseray otay ethay umorray atthay ethay ildchay asway
actuallyay Elisabeth’say ownay anday otnay Atherine’scay atay all.ay Ethay Empressay asway
otnay ispleasedday ithway ethay umor;ray erethay ereway omentsmay inay erhay astlay years,ay
yearsay ivengay overay otay aporsvay anday oods,may enwhay eshay almostay elievedbay ethay ythmay
erselfhay. Atthay eshay adhay oneday iolencevay otay ethay youngay othermay inay idnappingkay
erhay ildchay evernay entereday erhay eadhay. Eshay askeday Ariamay Eresathay ofay Austria,ay
atthay olificpray othermay omwhay eshay adhay alwaysay envied,ay otay ebay odmothergay otay erhay
ildchay. Austriaay ouldshay ealizeray atthay Ussiaray alsoay adhay anay eirhay.


5ay

Eryvay ittlelay isay ownknay ofay ethay atherfay ofay Aulpay. Ethay unhappyay ifelay ofay
Atherine’scay onsay anday ishay inalfay insanityay avehay etsay anymay iterswray anday
istorianshay atay orkway iscussingday ishay eredityhay. Utbay eythay alwaysay avehay
assumeday atthay ishay atherfay asway Eterpay IIIay anday atthay ishay andfathergray asway
Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Ifay isthay ereway ue,tray ethay eficienciesday ofay Atherine’scay onsay
ouldway ebay easyay otay explain,ay orfay eredityhay onay ethay Omanovray idesay eftlay uchmay otay
ebay esiredday. Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay aay eak-wittedway otherbray anday Eterpay IIIay adhay
aay entalmay isttway. Utbay allay isthay ashay othingnay otay oday ithway Aul,pay owhay asway otnay aay
Omanovray utbay aay Altikovsay.

Eway ustmay elyray uponay Atherine’scay emoirsmay orfay ethay ittlelay atthay eway owknay aboutay
ethay Altikovssay. Ergeisay anday Eterpay ereway othersbray inay ethay ervicesay ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Eirthay atherfay asway ethay Eneralgay Altikovsay owhay adhay elcomedway
Atherinecay anday erhay othermay inay Igaray onay eirthay ayway otay Ussiaray. Ethay othermay
ofay ethay Altikovsay othersbray adhay eenbay aay Incesspray Alitsingay anday aay oyallay
elperhay ofay ethay Empressay Elisabethay enwhay Elisabethay eizedsay ethay onethray.
Ethay aditiontray isay atthay Ariamay Altikovsay adhay uanderedsqay erhay irtuevay orfay
Elisabeth’say ausecay. Oweverhay isthay aymay avehay een,bay ethay Empressay asway evotedday
otay isthay adylay anday attacheday erhay otway onssay otay ethay ourtcay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday.
Ergeisay asway aay eatgray avoritefay ofay Eter’spay anday oftenay eptslay ithway imhay. Atay ethay
imetay enwhay Ariamay Altikovsay omotedpray ethay affairay etweenbay erhay onsay anday ethay
Andgray Uchessday eshay asway aay onfirmedcay invalid,ay utbay eshay eemssay otay avehay eptkay
erhay initiativeay anday energyay otay ethay astlay. Asay eshay adhay elpedhay erhay Empressay
aingay aay onethray eshay ownay oodstay eadyray otay elphay erhay aingay anay eirhay orfay it.ay

Ergeisay Altikovsay asway aay ypicaltay e’er-do-wellnay. Atherinecay iedtray otay akemay
ethay ostmay ofay erhay overlay inay erhay emoirsmay utbay otnay aay eatgray ealday ouldcay ebay ademay
ofay imhay. Ehay asway aay errymay ellow,fay aay unet,bray owhay aidsay ofay imselfhay enwhay ehay
asway onceay attireday inay aay ilversay ostumecay atthay ehay ookedlay Ike“lay aay yflay inay ethay
ilk.”may Atherinecay ayssay ofay imhay atthay ehay As“way eautifulbay asay ethay ay;day onay oneay
ouldcay omparecay ithway im,hay evenay inay ethay eatgray ourt,cay illstay esslay inay ouray
own.ay Ehay asway otnay ithoutway iritspay anday ossessedpay osethay armingchay annersmay
ichwhay oneay acquiresay omfray ivinglay inay ethay orldway ofay ashionfay anday especiallyay
atay ethay ourtcay. Inay ethay yearay 1752ay ehay asway enty-sixtway yearsay old.ay Ishay irthbay
anday otheray ualitiesqay ademay imhay anay outstandingay ersonalitypay. Ehay adhay ishay
aults,fay ichwhay ehay ewknay owhay otay onceal;cay ishay eatestgray aultsfay ereway aay
endencytay otay intrigueay anday aay acklay ofay ongstray inciplespray. Isthay oweverhay asway
unknownay otay emay atay atthay ime.”tay

Eshay enthay assespay onay otay ishay otherbray Eter,pay omwhay eshay esentspray inay uiteqay aay
ifferentday ightlay. Eterpay As“way aay oolfay inay ethay ullestfay ensesay ofay ethay ord,way
anday adhay ethay ostmay upidstay ysiognomyphay atthay Iay avehay everay eensay inay ymay ife:lay
eatgray eadenlay eyes,ay aay urned-uptay ose,nay aay outhmay alwaysay alfhay open.ay Esidesbay
ehay asway aay erribletay attle-tale.”tay Evidentlyay Eterpay asway onay editcray otay ethay
Altikovsay amilyfay. Yetay ehay appenedhay otay ebay ethay uncleay ofay erhay onsay.

Itay asway afterwardsay aidsay ofay Aul,pay enwhay ehay ecamebay Aulpay Iay ofay Ussia,ray atthay
ishay ysiognomyphay ithway itsay urned-uptay osenay asway onsideredcay evenay ybay imselfhay
ootay uglyay otay ebay imprinteday onay ishay oins;cay anday atthay enwhay ethay owdscray ofay
Arispay atheredgay otay ooklay atay imhay eythay iedcray out,ay Y“May Od,gay owhay uglyay ehay
is!”ay Ishay ooks,lay eway ightmay airlyfay onclude,cay ereway aay iftgay ichwhay ethay adbay
airiesfay ofay eredityhay adhay orrowedbay omfray Uncleay Eterpay. Erethay ereway otheray
isadvantagesday ichwhay ethay adbay airiesfay oubtlessday ooktay omfray ethay Altikovsay
amily,fay orfay Aulpay asway afflicteday inay everalsay aysway ichwhay alwaysay emainedray aay
uzzlepay otay ishay othermay.

IIvay

ONIATOVSKYpay


Afteray ethay irthbay ofay erhay on,say ethay Andgray Uchessday ecuperatedray utbay owlyslay.
Ethay icyay indsway omfray ethay Evanay enetratedpay erhay apartmentay anday eshay ufferedsay
ontinuallycay omfray oldscay. Eshay asway uerulousqay. Erhay amber,chay inay ichwhay eshay
asway obligeday otay asspay allay erhay imetay asay aay onvalescent,cay asway ootay allsmay.
Eightay archinsay inay oneay irectionday anday ourfay inay ethay other,ay itay easuredmay utbay
ittlelay oremay anthay ethay umblehay oomray inay Ettinstay inay ichwhay Atherinecay erselfhay
adhay eenbay ornbay. Asay aay Andgray Uchess,day eshay esentedray esethay arrownay alls;way eshay
esentedray ethay adlybay awndray icturespay onay ethay ilestay ofay erhay Utchday ove;stay eshay
esentedray ethay Andgray Uke’sday obaccotay okesmay ichwhay invadeday erhay emises;pray
anday eshay esentedray ethay Etched“wray iecespay ofay ewelry”jay ichwhay ethay Empressay
adhay eenbay easedplay otay ivegay erhay. Ethay esentpray ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray
ichwhay accompanieday ethay ewelsjay asway ethay olesay ightbray ininglay ofay erhay oudclay.
Atherinecay alwaysay eedednay oneymay.

Utbay evenay isthay oyjay asway arnishedtay ybay ethay actfay atthay ethay Empressay
immediatelyay orrowedbay ethay olewhay umsay ackbay againay anday idday otnay epayray erhay
untilay ethay ollowingfay Anuaryjay. Ethay Empressay ecalledray ethay oneymay ecausebay ethay
Andgray Uke,day onay earinghay atthay ishay ifeway adhay eceivedray it,ay aisedray aay eatgray
outcryay onay ishay ownay ehalfbay. Asay erethay asway onay oneymay inay ethay easurytray ithway
ichwhay otay ilencesay im,hay ethay Empressay astilyhay entsay otay ethay Andgray Uchessday
anday askeday orfay ethay oanlay ofay erhay easuretray. Obviouslyay Atherinecay asway inay onay
ositionpay otay efuse;ray esidesbay eshay eventuallyay otgay itay ackbay again.ay Itay asway
otnay osay ithway erhay aby,bay ichwhay ethay Empressay adhay akentay awayay ithoutway onceay
ayingsay ybay youray eavelay anday ichwhay asway evernay estoredray otay erhay. Erehay also,ay
apparently,ay ethay youngay othermay elievedbay erselfhay inay onay ositionpay otay efuse,ray
orfay eshay alloweday ethay Empressay otay obray erhay ithoutway aay inglesay otestpray. Erhay
acquiescenceay asway ompletecay. Eshay asway ermittedpay otay eesay ethay ildchay utbay
arely,ray anday enwhay eshay idday onsoledcay erselfhay ithway iticismscray ofay ethay ayway
ishay oster-motherfay ooktay arecay ofay imhay. Om“Fray eershay over-carefulness,ay ehay
asway iterallylay otheredsmay. Ehay aylay inay aay eryvay othay oomray entirelyay appedwray
inay annel,flay inay aay ibcray ademay ofay ackblay oxfay urfay anday overedcay ithway aay addedway
atinsay overletcay. Aboveay isthay asway aay edray elvetvay overletcay inedlay ithway ackblay
oxfay ur...fay. Ethay eatsway anray ownday ishay acefay anday ownday ishay olewhay ody.”bay Yetay
eshay ademay onay attemptay otay escueray imhay. Otay ytray itay ouldway avehay eenbay useless,ay
orfay ethay autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussiasray asway easilyay upremesay inay erhay ownay
ouseholdhay. Atherinecay alsoay obablypray adhay ootay ittlelay onfidencecay inay erhay ownay
ightsray ofay ossessionpay.

Eethray eeksway afteray ethay ild’schay irth,bay Altikovsay asway entsay otay Edensway otay
announceay ethay event.ay At“Thay epressedday emay eatly,”gray ayssay Atherine,cay
Ecause“bay Iay asway erebythay exposeday otay ethay alktay ofay ethay olewhay orld.”way Eshay
ustmay avehay eltfay evenay atay atthay earlyay ateday atthay erhay ecretsay asway ettypray
idelyway ownknay. Itay ouldcay avehay eenbay onay omfortcay otay er,hay ittingsay aloneay
inay erhay ittlelay afty,dray oke-filledsmay oom,ray otay ear,hay asay eshay oonsay id,day
atthay ethay ivolousfray Altikovsay asway ontinuingcay ishay Onday Uanjay areercay inay ethay
Edishsway apitalcay. I“ay eldhay astfay otay atwhay Iay adhay egun,”bay eshay ites,wray Ess“lay
omfray inclinationay anthay omfray eadfastness,stay anday orkedway orfay ishay eturn,ray
irelesslytay onqueringcay obstaclesay anday attlingbay ithway allay ymay engthstray
againstay everyay indrance.”hay Oughthray erhay ewnay allianceay ithway Estushevbay
uccesssay asway achieved.ay Ergeisay Altikovsay eturnedray otay Etersburgpay uringday ethay
Arnivalcay easonsay.

Ithway eatgray ifficultyday ethay Andgray Uchessday arrangeday aay endezvousray anday
aitedway untilay eethray o’clockay inay ethay orningmay orfay aay overlay owhay evernay
amecay. Erethay asway anay elaborateay explanation,ay owhay ehay adhay eenbay aggeddray
intoay aay Eemasonfray odgelay ybay oneay ofay ethay Olgorukys,day anday ouldcay otnay
escape.ay Utbay ethay Andgray Uchess,day uchmay asay ifay eshay adhay eenbay anay onesthay
ife,way asway otnay eceivedday. Eshay onay ongerlay opposeday ethay anplay ichwhay adhay
eenbay uggestedsay ofay endingsay Altikovsay otay Amburghay asay esidentray envoy.ay Ishay
epartureday asway elayedday omfray eekway otay eek,way utbay Atherine’scay influenceay
asway otnay ausingcay ethay elayday. Ethay Empressay idday otnay etgay arounday otay igningsay
ishay officialay apers,pay anday isthay asway atwhay eptkay ethay youngay anmay aitingway.
Elisabethay Etrovnapay asway owinggray oremay anday oremay ilatoryday everyay ayday inay ethay
erformancepay ofay erhay uties,day oremay anday oremay irregularay inay erhay abits,hay oremay
anday oremay uncertainay inay erhay ealthhay. Erhay assionatepay attachmentay otay ethay abybay
inay ethay ox-furfay adlecray adhay otnay ivengay erhay ethay ewnay easelay onay ifelay ichwhay
ightmay avehay eenbay expected.ay

Ethay effectay ofay Altikov’ssay eglectnay onay ethay eelingsfay ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday
asway oonsay apparent.ay Eshay ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay at,thay oodingbray inay erhay
interway ofay olitude,say eshay ecidedday efinitelyday otay assertay erself,hay otay
etlay erhay environmentay owknay atthay eshay ouldway otnay uffersay insultay ithoutway
etaliationray. Adhay eshay otnay afteray allay isenray otay erhay upremesay obligation?ay
Adhay eshay otnay ivengay otay Ussiaray anay eir?hay Eshay asway entitleday otay onsiderationcay
anday asway eterminedday otay avehay it.ay Ookinglay aboutay orfay aay apegoat,scay eshay idday
otnay avehay arfay otay eeksay. Altikovsay asway afelysay outay ofay eachray inay Amburghay
anday ethay Empressay asway aptray inay erhay antasyphay oudclay. Utbay ethay othersbray
Uvalovshay emainedray ithinway each,ray anday eshay oundfay otay erhay oyjay atthay eythay
ereway ulnerablevay. Eithernay ofay ethay othersbray asway everclay anday Alexanderay asway
isfiguredday ybay aay imace--angray uglyay acialfay Ic__tay. Itay asway easyay otay akemay
eoplepay aughlay atay ethay Uvalovsshay anday erhay On_bay ots_may atay eirthay expenseay anray
oughthray ethay owntay ikelay ild-fireway. Eshay ayssay atthay erhay attackay asway upportedsay
ybay Ountcay Azumovsky,ray ex-favoriteay ofay ethay Empress,ay anday ishay otherbray
Yrilkay. Utbay eirthay upportsay ustmay avehay eenbay eak,way oweverhay illingway. Ethay otway
Azumovskysray ereway artistsay anday eamersdray anday eeblefay ightersfay evenay orfay
eirthay ownay ausecay.

Atherinecay ovethray onay erhay ewnay aggressiveness.ay Oonsay anotheray enemyay asway
addeday otay erhay istlay. Aay ysteriousmay Errhay Ockdorfbray adhay omecay upay omfray
Olsteinhay anday adhay uietlyqay establisheday imselfhay inay ethay etinueray ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Ethay Andgray Uchessday idday otnay ikelay Errhay Ockdorfbray anday ursuedpay
imhay ithway erhay ockerymay. Eshay avegay imhay aay ickname,nay Aba-ptitza”“Bay A(ay elicanpay
orfay ugliness!)ay anday ereverwhay ethay ombersay Olsteinerhay entway ehay eardhay itay
isperedwhay afteray imhay.


2ay

Ollowingfay ethay irthbay ofay Aul,pay ethay eachbray etweenbay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday
ethay Andgray Uchessday idenedway. After“ay ymay onfinement,”cay ayssay Atherinecay inay
erhay emoirs,may E“hay usuallyay eptslay inay ishay ownay amber.”chay Ethay angechay ofay
abithay okebray ethay onlyay ietay ichwhay existeday etweenbay emthay. Orfay inenay yearsay
ehay adhay eptslay inay astitychay esidebay ishay ifeway. Utbay omethingsay isturbing,day
incomprehensibleay adhay omecay etweenbay em,thay anday ehay asway onay ongerlay atay easeay
inay ishay ife’sway edbay. Ehay ademay utilefay effortsay otay attachay imselfhay otay otheray
adieslay ofay ethay ourt,cay utbay ishay enthusiasmay anderedway anday ailedfay otay ikestray
ootray anywhere.ay Ishay interestay inay ilitarymay occupationsay eganbay otay absorbay allay
others.ay

Oremay anday oremay ehay occupieday imselfhay ithway ishay avoritefay oys,tay oldierssay
ademay ofay ead,lay ood,way arch,stay oray axway. Olewhay egimentsray ereway etsay upay onay
ablestay anday operateday ybay eansmay ofay ingeniousay echanicalmay evices,day inay akingmay
ichwhay ethay youth,ay owhay adhay evernay eenbay ableay otay earnlay anythingay omfray ishay
utors,tay owedshay aay ighhay egreeday ofay illskay. Enteringay ishay oomray oneay ay,day ethay
Andgray Uchessday oundfay aay eadday atray onay aay allowsgay anday asway informeday atthay aay
ilitarymay executionay adhay ustjay akentay aceplay ollowingfay aay ourt-martialcay ofay
ethay ulpritcay. Onay anotheray occasionay enwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway expectingay aay
isitvay omfray aay adylay otay omwhay ehay asway ayingpay ourt,cay ehay alledcay ishay ifeway otay
urveysay ethay owerbay ichwhay ehay adhay eparedpray orfay erhay. E“Hay owedshay e,”may ayssay
Atherine,cay Ow,“hay inay orderay otay easeplay ethay ady,lay ehay adhay ittedfay itay outay ithway
uskets,may ilitarymay aps,cay oulder-belts,shay osay atthay itay ookedlay ikelay aay ornercay
inay anay arsenal.”ay

Ethay yearay ichwhay ollowedfay ethay irthbay ofay Atherine’scay ildchay anday ethay
etreatray ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday omfray erhay edbay awsay aay arkedmay increaseay inay ethay
eoccupationpray ofay ethay atterlay ithway ishay ilitarymay oystay. Ybay ethay imetay erhay
econdsay ildchay asway orn,bay ichwhay asway eethray yearsay ater,lay ishay eoccupationpray
adhay owngray abnormalay anday ehay asway apablecay ofay ethay ollowingfay extraordinaryay
isplayday. Ehay adhay eenbay alledcay ybay ethay idwife,may ayssay Atherinecay inay erhay
escriptionday ofay atthay ight,nay anday afteray omesay elayday utpay inay anay appearance.ay
E“Hay entereday ymay amberchay inay ishay Olsteinhay uniform,ay ootedbay anday urred,spay
ithway aay arfscay arounday ishay odybay anday aay eatgray aggerday atay ishay ide;say atthay is,ay
inay ompletecay egaliaray. Astonisheday atay isthay omppay Iay askeday imhay ethay easonray orfay
isthay elaborateay ostumecay. Ereuponwhay ehay epliedray atthay onlyay inay imetay ofay eednay
ouldcay oneay owknay one’say uetray iends;fray inay isthay ostumecay ehay asway eparedpray otay
oday ishay utyday. Anday ethay utyday ofay aay Olsteinhay officeray asway otay ebay uetray otay ishay
oathay anday efendday ethay Ucalday Ousehay againstay allay enemies.ay Ecausebay Iay asway otnay
ellway ehay adhay omecay otay ymay aid.”ay

Atherinecay ecidedday atthay erhay onsortcay asway unkdray anday entsay imhay ackbay otay edbay.
Althoughay eshay asway anay accurateay observeray ofay ethay Andgray Uke’sday ehaviour,bay
eshay adhay onay ealray omprehensioncay ofay ethay aturenay ofay ishay affliction.ay Ishay
olday utor,tay Ehlin,stay owhay adhay onceay ademay uchsay eroichay effortsay otay eachtay
im,hay asway apparentlyay ethay onlyay ersonpay inay ethay youngay an’smay environmentay
owhay erceivedpay ethay orbidmay elementay inay ishay ehaviourbay. Ehlinstay alledcay itay
ishay Arotte“may ilitaire,”may atthay isay otay ay,say aay indkay ofay Olie“fay ilitaire,”may
omethingsay ichwhay urpassessay ethay imitslay ofay ormalnay youthfulay ollyfay. Ethay
Empressay asway erelymay angereday atay everyay eccentricityay anday urledhay unishmentspay
anday enaltiespay uponay ethay offender’say eadhay. At“Thay amnedday ephewnay ofay inemay ashay
angereday emay unspeakably,”ay eshay ouldway aysay. E“Hay isay aay onster;may aymay ethay evilday
yflay awayay ithway im.”hay

Ethay uxcray ofay ethay Andgray Uke’sday ilitarymay obsessionay asway ishay evotionday otay
Ederickfray ofay Ussia,pray ethay eatestgray ilitarymay eneralgay ofay ishay age.ay Itay asway
earlyclay otnay ethay ingthay orfay ethay eirhay otay ethay onethray ofay Ussiaray otay estowbay
ishay earthay usthay unreservedlyay onay aay oreignfay otentatepay anday especiallyay onay
oneay ithway omwhay Ussiaray asway actuallyay atay arway. Eter’spay angestray evotionday
isay easonablyray explaineday inay Oniatovsky’spay emoirs:may One“ay ustmay assumeay
atthay ishay ursenay anday ishay earliestay eacherstay inay ishay atherlandfay adhay eenbay
Ussianpray anday evotedday otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray. Orfay omfray ildhoodchay onay ehay
ourishednay uchsay aay ongstray anday atay ethay amesay imetay uchsay aay omicalcay eelingfay ofay
enerationvay anday ovelay orfay isthay Incepray atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray onceay aidsay
aboutay isthay assionpay Or(fay itay asway eallyray aay assion):pay I“ay amay ishay Ulcineaday.
Ehay ashay evernay eensay emay anday ashay allenfay inay ovelay ithway emay ikelay Onday Uixote.”qay


3ay

Ethay ilitarymay adnessmay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday oundfay aay ongenialcay allyay inay ethay
ersonpay ofay ethay ysteriousmay anmay omfray Olstein,hay Errhay Ockdorf,bray omwhay
Atherinecay osay ordiallycay etestedday anday icknamednay E“thay elican.”pay Ethay
ed-hairedray Olsteiner,hay owhay oreway aay Iserable,“may iscontentedday ooklay ecausebay
ethay ornerscay ofay ishay outhmay unghay ownday otay ishay in,”chay atedhay ethay Andgray
Uchessday ordiallycay inay eturnray. Ehay epaidray erhay omplimentcay aboutay ethay elicanpay
ybay announcingay atthay ehay adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay Ead“tray uponay ethay erpent,”say
eaningmay erebythay onay otheray anthay Atherinecay erselfhay.

Ockdorfbray asway apparentlyay aay ondescriptnay isitorvay ofay onay ealray oliticalpay
importance,ay utbay ishay influenceay overay Eterpay atay isthay ucialcray eriodpay ashay
ivengay imhay aay aceplay inay istoryhay. Exactlyay atwhay isthay oddlyay assorteday airpay
adhay inay ommoncay isay ardhay otay aysay. Erhapspay itay asway ethay otestantpray omplexcay
ichwhay uniteday emthay. Eway owknay atthay Eter’spay onlyay eadingray asway ethay Utheranlay
ayer-book,pray ichwhay ehay importeday omfray Ermanygay ybay ethay undred,hay anday eway
uspectsay atthay Errhay Ockdorf’sbray eferencesray otay E“thay ake”snay inay Atherinecay
asway ishay etaphoricalmay ayway ofay ayingsay atthay eshay adhay ainedgay ethay eputationray
ofay eingbay anay immoralay omanway. Atay anyay ateray ethay ontestcay etweenbay Atherinecay
anday Ockdorfbray asway intenseay anday eirthay eudfay aay itterbay one.ay Eythay ompetedcay
orfay influenceay overay ethay Andgray Ukeday owhay averedway ackbay anday orthfay etweenbay
emthay asay uidesgay anday advisersay inay ethay anagementmay ofay ethay affairsay ofay ishay
elovedbay Olsteinhay.

Itay asway ortlyshay afteray ethay entranceay ofay Ockdorfbray onay ethay enescay atthay ethay
irstfay ealray uarrelqay ooktay aceplay etweenbay Atherinecay Alexeievnaay anday Eterpay
Eodorovnafay. Ethay encounteray assumeday aay ignificantsay ormfay. Is“Hay Imperialay
Ighnesshay amecay otay ymay oomray oneay eveningay afteray inner,”day ayssay Atherine,cay
And“ay eclaredday otay emay atthay Iay eallyray asway ecomingbay ootay unbearablyay oud,pray
utbay ehay ouldway oonsay ingbray emay otay easonray. Iay askeday imhay ereinwhay isthay idepray
onsistedcay anday ehay epliedray atthay Iay arriedcay yselfmay ootay upright.ay Ereuponthay Iay
askeday imhay etherwhay Iay ouldshay endbay ymay ackbay otay easeplay im,hay ikelay ethay avesslay
ofay ethay Ultan!say Atay isthay ehay ewgray angryay anday epeatedray ehay ouldway oonsay ingbray
emay otay easonray. Iay askeday imhay owhay ehay ouldway oday isthay. Ereuponthay ehay acedplay
imselfhay ithway ishay ackbay againstay ethay all,way alf-wayhay ewdray ishay aggerday anday
owedshay itay otay emay. Iay askeday imhay atwhay atthay eant,may etherwhay ehay ouldway ightfay
emay. Enthay Iay alsoay ustmay avehay one.ay Ehay ustthray ishay alf-drawnhay aggerday againay
intoay itsay eathshay anday aidsay ymay alicemay adhay owngray otay ebay omethingsay uiteqay
amazing....”ay

Itay asway oughthray ethay indkay officesay ofay Ockdorfbray atthay aay egimentray ofay
Olsteinhay oldierssay appeareday atay Oranienbaumay inay ethay earlyay ummersay ofay 1775ay.
Ethay Andgray Uke’sday ilitarymay ayplay adhay uddenlysay ecomebay aay angerousday ealityray.
Oldierssay ofay eadlay anday axway onay ongerlay atisfiedsay imhay. Ehay asway obligeday otay
avehay esh-and-bloodflay oys,tay ongstray urlybay ellowsfay owhay adhay otay ebay ousedhay
anday edfay anday owhay uarreledqay ithway ethay Ussianray uardgay alreadyay ationedstay
atay Oranienbaum.ay Ese“Thay accurseday Ermansgay areay allay oldsay otay ethay Ingkay ofay
Ussia,”pray aidsay ethay Ussiansray. Ey“Thay areay aitorstray oughtbray otay Ussia.”ray

Ethay Andgray Uchessday ealizedray ethay angerday ofay isthay ewnay evelopmentday. Eshay
ecidedday otay eliminateay erselfhay omfray ethay ituationsay asay ompletelycay asay
ossiblepay anday evotedday erhay ummersay otay eclaimingray asteway andlay anday anningplay
aay argelay Englishay ardengay. Ethay Empress’say advisers,ay ethay Uvalovs,shay alsoay
ealizedray atthay ethay esencepray ofay ethay Olsteinhay oldierssay atay Oranienbaumay
asway undesirableay anday yetay eythay oundfay itay uriouslycay impossibleay otay akemay
Eterpay eesay ethay ointpay oray otay ersuadepay imhay otay emoveray isthay eryvay isturbingday
element.ay Ikelay arentspay yingtray otay etgay aay ildchay otay exchangeay aay angerousday oytay
orfay aay afesay one,ay ethay Uvalovsshay ecidedday otay esentpray ethay Andgray Ukeday ithway
ealray Ussianray oldierssay orfay ishay amesgay. Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1756,ay eythay entsay aay
etachmentday ofay oneay undredhay adetscay otay Oranienbaumay orfay Eterpay otay ommandcay.
Utbay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway otnay osay easilyay upedday. Ethay Ussianray adetscay ightmay
emainray utbay ethay umbernay ofay ishay elovedbay Olsteinershay ontinuedcay otay increase.ay
Ethay accommodationsay ofay ethay ittlelay illagevay ereway ained,stray ivinggay iseray otay
oremay ictionfray anday oremay umors...ray.

Ilewhay ethay Andgray Ukeday elightedday inay ayingplay ithway ishay Olsteinhay oldiers,say
ehay oundfay ethay administrationay ofay ethay overnment,gay orfay ichwhay ehay adhay eenbay
esponsibleray incesay ethay ageay ofay ineteen,nay edioustay anday urdensomebay. Ehay
eliedray uchmay onay ethay Andgray Uchessday omwhay ehay alledcay Adamemay alay Essourceray.
Ilewhay Ockdorfbray ontestedcay erhay influenceay inay Olsteinhay affairs,ay eshay
everthelessnay etainedray irstfay aceplay inay ethay onglay unray. Itay asway aay eatgray
eliefray otay Eterpay otay andhay ethay ealsay overay otay erhay alongay ithway allay importantay
anday ifficultday ocumentsday anday otay orgetfay ethay overnmentgay ofay Olsteinhay ilewhay
ehay aradedpay ishay ascinatingfay oldierssay. Inay imetay itay amecay aboutay atthay ethay
iplomatsday owhay adhay anythingay otay aysay aboutay Olsteinhay onsultedcay Atherinecay
irectlyday anday accepteday erhay ecisionday. Ingsthay entway onay inay isthay iseway orfay aay
eriessay ofay yearsay untilay ethay Empress,ay uddenlysay iscoveringday atthay Olsteinhay
asway eingbay uledray ybay ethay Andgray Uchess,day issueday aay ukaseay atthay ethay Andgray
Ukeday ouldshay aketay arecay ofay esethay oliticalpay attersmay imselfhay. Itay asway aay
ukase,ay owever,hay ichwhay ommandedcay ethay impossible.ay


4ay

Inay ethay autumnay ofay 1755ay anay Englishmanay amecay otay Etersburgpay. Ehay asway aay anmay
ustjay astpay iddlemay age,ay aay Ig,whay anday anay aristocrat.ay Ehay adhay eenbay orfay inenay
yearsay inay ethay iplomaticday ervicesay anday asway ownknay orfay ishay austiccay itway anday
elegantay annersmay. Ishay atiricalsay oetrypay asway uchmay admired.ay Esethay alents,tay
owever,hay ereway otnay alwaysay anay asset.ay Ixsay yearsay eviouslypray ehay adhay eenbay
entsay otay Erlinbay asay Ambassadoray atay ethay ourtcay ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Utbay
Ederickfray adhay otnay ikedlay ethay itingbay onguetay ofay ethay anmay anday adhay askeday orfay
ishay emovalray. Ethay Englishmanay asway entsay ackbay otay ishay olday ostpay atay Esdendray
erewhay Augustay ethay Ongstray asway apparentlyay obliviousay otay ishay atiresay. Otnay
eingbay aay atiristsay imself,hay asay asway Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray erhapspay ehay ouldcay
oremay omfortablycay endureay ethay esencepray ofay aay ivalray. Ansferredtray otay ethay
Ourtcay ofay Etersburg,pay ethay ophisticatedsay Englishmanay oundfay imselfhay inay
aay illstay esslay intellectualay atmosphereay anthay atthay ofay ethay Axonsay ourtcay.
Atherinecay ayssay atthay ethay artay ofay onversationcay asway unknownay amongay ethay
Ussianray ourtierscay ofay atthay imetay. Ethay arrivalay ofay aay olishedpay iplomatday owhay
ealtday inay illiantbray alktay anday eparteeray ouldcay otnay ailfay otay akemay aay eatgray
impressionay onay ethay Andgray Uchessday althoughay ostmay ofay ishay arbsbay ereway ostlay
onay ethay ard-playingcay ourtcay ichwhay urroundedsay Elisabeth.ay Ethay amenay ofay ethay
interestingay Englishmanay asway Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway.

Asay Ambassadoray otay ethay Axonsay Ourt,cay Illiamsway adhay entspay uchmay imetay inay
Oland,pay overay ichwhay Augustay ofay Axonysay uledray asay electiveay ingkay. Inay Arsaw,way
ethay Evalierchay adhay ademay iendsfray ithway ethay Artoriskyczay anclay anday ethay
Oniatovskypay amilyfay. Aay ong-mindedstray aughterday ofay ethay Artoriskysczay adhay
arriedmay Ountcay Anislasstay Oniatovskypay anday erhay onsay asway ikewiselay Ountcay
Anislasstay. Ethay youngay anmay asway adoreday ybay ishay othermay anday atronizedpay ybay
erhay others,bray ethay owerfulpay Artoriskysczay. Ishay areercay asway ethay ubjectsay ofay
earnestay amilyfay onclavescay. Enwhay Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway offereday otay
aketay imhay otay Ussiaray asay Ecretarysay itay asway ecidedday atthay Anislasstay ouldshay
ogay. Ethay Ambassadoray asway almostay enty-fivetway yearsay olderay anthay ishay Olishpay
ecretarysay anday alledcay imhay ishay onsay. Inay Etersburgpay eythay ivedlay ogethertay inay
ethay ousehay ofay Ountcay Avronskyskay onay ethay ankbay ofay ethay Evanay.

Ethay Andgray Uchessday etmay emthay othbay orfay ethay irstfay imetay onay stay. Eter’spay
ayday atay Oranienbaum.ay Eshay atsay esidebay Evalierchay Illiamsway atay uppersay anday
onversedcay ithway imhay ilewhay eshay admireday ethay acefulgray ancingday ofay ishay
ecretarysay. Itay asway ethay eginningbay ofay aay oliticalpay anday ersonalpay allianceay
ichwhay apidlyray evelopedday amongay ethay eethray. Oniatovskypay ecamebay erhay over,lay
ilewhay ethay Evalier,chay everay attentiveay omfray ethay ackgroundbay anday egularlyray
orrespondingcay ithway er,hay asway inay omesay uriouscay icariousvay ashionfay alsoay inay
ovelay ithway ethay ascinatingfay anday aggressiveay Atherinecay. Ittingsay atay uppersay
oneay eveningay ithway Oniatovskypay is-à-vis,vay ethay Andgray Uchessday ewthray outay
isthay emark,ray ostensiblyay addresseday otay ethay Enchfray Ambassador,ay Ere“Thay asway
evernay aay omanway olderbay anthay I;ay Iay avehay anay unbridleday emerity.”tay Erethay asway
uchmay ecklessnessray inay erhay atay isthay imetay.

Ethay Englishay Ambassadoray adhay omecay otay Ussiaray ithway aay ecialspay issionmay
omfray Eorgegay II,ay owhay asway anxiousay estlay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ouldshay urntay
ovetouscay eyesay onay Anoverhay asay ehay adhay onay Ilesiasay. Illiamsway asway empowereday
otay offeray anay annualay ubsidysay ofay ivefay undredhay ousandthay ivreslay otay Ussiaray inay
eturnray orfay ichwhay Ussiaray asway otay andstay eadyray otay aiday Anoverhay againstay anyay
ossiblepay epredationsday onay ethay artpay ofay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay. Uchsay aay eatytray
etweenbay Englanday anday Ussia,ray Illiamsway actuallyay otgay ignedsay inay Eptembersay
1755ay. Utbay onay oonersay asway isthay oneday anthay ethay ilyway Ederickfray utpay oughthray
ethay Eatytray ofay Estminsterway inay ichwhay ehay anday ethay Erman-Englishgay Eorgegay
utuallymay uaranteedgay eirthay ossessionspay againstay othbay Ancefray anday Ussiaray.
Isthay eatedcray aay omplicatedcay ituationsay orfay ethay Englishay iplomatday. Ethay
Ussianray Empressay oathedlay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray anday antedway onay alliesay inay
ommoncay ithway imhay. Ussiaray ereforethay isregardedday ethay eatytray egunbay inay ethay
Allfay ofay 1755ay anday efusedray otay acceptay ethay ivefay undredhay ousandthay ivreslay
ichwhay Englanday adhay entsay. Illiamsway entspay ishay imetay inay Etersburgpay yingtray inay
ainvay otay induceay ethay Ussianray overnmentgay otay aketay ishay oneymay. Ehay alsoay oundfay
imselfhay inay ethay uriouscay ositionpay ofay avinghay otay epresentray ethay interestsay ofay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray afteray ehay adhay artedstay otay orkway againstay emthay. Opposeday
otay imhay asway ethay olewhay Enchfray artypay eadedhay ybay ethay owerfulpay Ivanay Uvalov,shay
avoritefay ofay ethay Empress.ay Ethay Evalierchay asway eftlay otay ultivatecay ethay Andgray
Ucalday ourtcay anday isthay ehay idday ithway ole-heartedwhay enthusiasm.ay Ehay adviseday
Atherinecay aboutay ethay overnmentgay ofay Olsteinhay ichwhay asway atay atthay imetay inay
erhay andshay anday ucceededsay inay uyingbay ethay Andgray Ancellorchay Estushevbay ithway aay
ensionpay ofay elvetway ousandthay ublesray aay yearay omfray ethay Englishay Overnmentgay.

Unfortunatelyay orfay ishay emes,schay Estushevbay asway onay ongerlay aay owerpay atay
ourtcay. Ivanay Uvalovshay adhay atheredgay ethay einsray intoay ishay ownay andshay asay ethay
ealthhay ofay ethay Empressay eclinedday. Utbay Illiamsway egardedray Estushevbay asay
aay inefay apturecay. Ehay otewray anay enthusiasticay accountay ofay ishay uccesssay otay
Atherinecay anday oncludedcay ishay etterlay us:thay Ese“Thay areay ethay enesscay ittenwray
inay astehay ichwhay illway akemay elightfulday anecdotesay orfay aay uturefay enturycay.
Youay aloneay avehay ymay ecret;say ymay eart,hay ymay ife,lay ymay oulsay areay yours.ay Iay
egardray youay asay aay eaturecray ollywhay uperiorsay otay yselfmay. Iay adoreay youay anday ymay
adorationay oesgay osay arfay Iay amay ersuadedpay atthay Iay ancay avehay onay eritmay apartay
omfray you....ay Erehay isay ymay astlecay inay Ainspay ichwhay Iay avehay eenbay uildingbay orfay
omesay imetay anday ithway ichwhay Iay oftenay amuseay yselfmay. Enwhay youay omecay otay youray
aceplay onay ethay one,thray Iay allshay otnay ebay erehay. Iay allshay omecay erehay atay once....ay
Iay ouldshay ishway otay omecay ithway ethay aracterchay ofay ambassadoray inay ymay ocketpay
utbay Iay ouldshay otnay ishway otay oducepray it,ay ecausebay atthay ouldway obligeay emay otay
aintainmay aay ankray anday etiquetteay ichwhay ouldway isturbday emay. Anday Iay atterflay
yselfmay atthay Iay ouldshay ivelay uchmay ithway youay asay aay aithfulfay ervantsay anday
umblehay iendfray. Iay ouldshay avehay ethay entréeay otay anday ofitpray ybay youray ourshay ofay
eisure,lay ecausebay Iay alwaysay ovelay Atherinecay etterbay anthay ethay Empress....”ay

Othbay Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway avehay eftlay extensiveay ecordsray ofay eirthay
experiencesay inay Ussiaray. Isthay isay owhay Atherinecay ookedlay atay ethay ageay ofay
enty-sixtway inay ethay eyesay ofay erhay Olishpay overlay. At“ay isthay imetay eshay adhay
attaineday atthay egreeday ofay eautybay ichwhay epresentsray orfay everyay omanway otay
omwhay eautybay isay ivengay atay allay ethay imaxclay ofay itsay evelopmentday. Erhay airhay
asway ack,blay erhay inskay aay azzlingday itewhay anday ividvay ed;ray eshay adhay argelay
ue,blay ound,ray eryvay expressiveay eyes,ay eryvay onglay ackblay ashes,lay aay Eekgray
ose,nay aay outhmay ichwhay eemedsay otay askay orfay isseskay. Erhay armsay anday ouldersshay
ereway urpassinglysay eautiful;bay eshay adhay aay alltay acefulgray igurefay anday erhay
alkway asway eryvay agileay oughthay ullfay ofay obility,nay ethay oundsay ofay erhay oicevay
asway easant,play anday erhay aughlay asay oyousjay asay erhay emperament.”tay Ethay Andgray
Uchessday oundfay inay Ountcay Oniatovskypay ethay omanticray overlay orfay omwhay eshay adhay
allay erhay ifelay eenbay onginglay.


5ay

Uringday ethay ummersay ofay 1756,ay Ountcay Oniatovskypay epartedday orfay Arsawway otay
akemay aay iefbray isitvay. Ehay ailedfay otay eturnray atay ethay expecteday imetay anday ethay
Andgray Uchessday estirredbay erselfhay otay avehay imhay ecalledray otay Ussiaray asay
Olishpay Ambassador.ay Eshay enlisteday Illiamsway anday Estushevbay otay isthay enday anday
oweredshay avorsfay uponay emthay untilay ethay otway elderlyay iplomatsday eganbay otay ebay
ealousjay ofay eachay other.ay Eshay adhay oneday erhay orkway almostay ootay ellway. Atay ast,lay
owever,hay eshay ucceededsay inay erhay urposepay anday ethay Andgray Ancellorchay asway ableay
otay ecuresay ethay youngay Ole’spay eturnray. Ehay imposeday asay aay ondition,cay owever,hay
atthay Oniatovskypay ouldshay onay ongerlay ivelay ithway Illiamsway onay uchsay intimateay
ermstay asay ormerlyfay. Ethay ayway asway ownay earclay orfay Oniatovsky’spay eturn,ray utbay
illstay ehay ingeredlay inay Olandpay. Atwhay asway ethay obstacle?ay Aay etterlay ichwhay ehay
entsay otay Atherinecay explainsay ethay ausecay ofay ishay elayday.

And“ay isthay isay owhay itay is.ay Ybay intday ofay uestioningqay emay ithway allay ethay
endernesstay anday adroitnessay ossible,pay ymay othermay understandsay earlyclay atwhay
itay isay atthay akesmay emay osay ardentlyay ishway otay eturnray otay you....ay Iay essedpray
erhay oremay onglystray otay onsentcay ormallyfay otay ymay eturn;ray eshay aidsay otay emay
ithway earstay inay erhay eyesay atthay eshay oresawfay ithway iefgray atthay isthay affairay
asway oinggay otay ausecay erhay otay oselay ymay affectionay onay ichwhay eshay ependedday orfay
allay ethay appinesshay ofay erhay ife;lay atthay itay asway ardhay otay efuseray omesay ingsthay
utbay inay ethay enday eshay asway eterminedday otnay otay onsentcay. Uponay ichwhay Iay asway
esidebay yself;may Iay ewthray yselfmay atay erhay eetfay anday eggedbay erhay otay angechay
erhay entimentssay. Eshay aid,say eltingmay intoay ears,tay Is‘Thay isay ustjay atwhay Iay
expected.’ay Everthelessnay eshay entway away,ay essingpray ymay and,hay anday eftlay emay inay
ethay ostmay orriblehay ilemmaday Iay avehay everay experienceday inay ymay ife...lay. Oh,ay
Outrespay Is[hay icknamenay orfay Atherine]cay ..ay. areshay ithway Onnbay Illiams][Way
isthay orystay aboutay ymay othermay anday egbay imhay otay itewray ymay atherfay anday askay imhay
otay endsay emay ackbay overay erethay ecausebay Iay amay ecessarynay otay imhay. Orfay amongay
otheray ingsthay eshay isputesday ithway emay atthay Iay amay ecessarynay otay im....”hay

Ithway ethay assistanceay anday encouragementay ofay oneay ofay ishay Artoriskyczay
uncles,ay ethay youngay Ountcay inallyfay escapeday omfray ishay othermay anday arriveday
inay Etersburgpay inay imetay orfay ethay Ussianray Istmaschray ofay 1756ay. Ehay emainedray
inay Ussiaray asay ethay overlay ofay Atherinecay orfay anotheray yearay anday aay alf,hay anday
eftlay ethay ountrycay inallyfay inay Uly,jay 1758ay. Atherine’scay aughter,day ethay Andgray
Uchessday Anna,ay ornbay inay Ecember,day 1757,ay asway Oniatovsky’spay ildchay. Ethay
infantay asway akentay omfray ethay othermay ybay ethay Empressay ustjay asay ethay irstfay oneay
adhay eenbay anday utpay intoay ethay urserynay ithway erhay ee-year-oldthray alf-brotherhay.
Eshay idday otnay onglay urvivesay underay ethay Empress’say imerégay anday eemssay otay avehay
eenbay oonsay orgottenfay ybay erhay othermay anday erhay atherfay. Ethay ifelay anday eathday ofay
ethay ittlelay Andgray Uchessday Anna,ay aftedway osay arelesslycay inay anday outay ofay erhay
other’smay areer,cay asway ethay ightestslay ofay ightslay episodes.ay Atherinecay asway
absorbeday inay oliticalpay intrigue.ay Erhay allianceay ithway Evalierchay Illiamsway
anday Andgray Ancellorchay Estushevbay adhay evelopedday erhay alentstay inay isthay
irection,day anday eshay alloweday erselfhay otay ogay arfay anday otay aketay eatgray isksray.
Eshay awsay ethay eathday ofay ethay Empressay approachingay anday ethay accessionay ofay Andgray
Ukeday Eterpay otay ethay onethray. Atwhay ouldway enthay ebay erhay ositionpay anday atthay ofay
erhay onsay ybay Altikov?say

Aay idnightmay encounteray ichwhay ooktay aceplay etweenbay Oniatovskypay anday ethay
Andgray Ukeday atay Oranienbaumay ausedcay ethay Olepay otay eavelay Ussiaray anday owedshay
Atherinecay owhay esperatelyday uncertainay erhay ootingfay adhay ecomebay. Ethay Ountcay
asway accustomeday otay omecay anday ogay inay isguiseday. Earingway aay ondblay erukepay ehay
ouldway ay,say Usician“May ofay ethay Andgray Uke”day anday ouldway asspay unquestioned.ay
Utbay oneay id-summermay ightnay ishay useray ailedfay otay avesay imhay omfray embarrassingay
evelopmentsday. Oniatovskypay ellstay ethay orystay us:thay On“ay isthay ightnay Iay etmay
unluckilyay inay ethay oodsway atay Oranienbaumay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday ishay olewhay
etinue,ray allay ofay emthay alfhay unkdray. Eythay askeday ymay Izvostchik__ay omwhay ehay
asway ivingdray. Ymay agepay eplied,ray A‘ay ailor.’tay Eway ereway alloweday otay asspay. Utbay
Elisabethay Orontsov,vay ady-in-waitinglay ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday anday istressmay
ofay ethay Andgray Uke,day owhay asway esent,pray ademay aay ewfay okingjay emarksray aboutay
ethay allegeday ailortay ichwhay utpay ethay Andgray Ukeday intoay aay adbay umorhay. Asay Iay
asway eavinglay ethay avilionpay erewhay Iay adhay entspay everalsay ourshay ithway ethay
Andgray Uchessday anday ichwhay eshay occupieday underay ethay etensepray ofay akingtay aay
ater-cure,way Iay asway uddenlysay opped,stay afteray akingtay aay ewfay eps,stay ybay eethray
ountedmay en,may o,whay abressay inay and,hay eizedsay emay ybay ethay ollarcay anday aggeddray
emay eforebay ethay Andgray Uke.”day

Accordingay otay Atherine’scay ory,stay Ockdorfbray ethay elicanpay ayedplay aay
ominentpray artpay inay isthay enescay. Ethay Olsteinerhay adviseday ethay Andgray Ukeday otay
illkay ethay isonerpray. Utbay Eterpay adhay onay uchsay intention;ay ehay onlyay exposeday anday
entilatedvay ethay andalscay. Oniatovskypay asway alloweday otay ogay eefray afteray ethay
episodeay adhay ecomebay ownknay otay ethay entireay ourtcay. Ithway oadbray atronizingpay
okes,jay ethay Andgray Ukeday inviteday ethay Olepay otay Oranienbaumay anday acilitatedfay
ishay eetingsmay ithway ethay Andgray Uchessday. Ethay Uvalovshay iedtray otay eassureray ethay
Ount,cay utbay eithernay Atherinecay ornay erhay overlay ereway eassuredray. I“ay ouldcay otnay
utbay emark,”ray ayssay Oniatovsky,pay At“thay allay asway otnay earclay anday atthay itay asway
imetay orfay emay otay ogay away.”ay Atherinecay ayssay atthay eshay erceivedpay oughthray isthay
episodeay atthay erhay otlay asway inallyfay eparatedsay omfray atthay ofay ethay Andgray Uke;day
atthay eshay ustmay eitheray erishpay ithway imhay anday oughthray imhay oray avesay erselfhay
anday erhay ildrenchay anday ethay atestay omfray ipwreckshay. Afteray Oniatovsky’spay
epartureday orfay Oland,pay ethay Andgray Uchessday entway intoay ictstray etirementray.
Oonsay afteray ehay eft,lay Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway eftlay Ussiaray also.ay
Ethay Evalierchay asway angelystray eluctantray otay ogay away.ay Ehay ouldshay avehay onegay
earlyay inay ethay ummer,say utbay ehay ouldcay otnay ecideday onay ishay itinerary.ay Atay
irstfay ehay annedplay otay ourneyjay oughthray Olandpay utbay angedchay ishay indmay anday
ecidedday otay ogay oughthray Edensway. Ehay otgay asay arfay asay Inlandfay anday enthay amecay
ackbay againay ayingsay atthay ishay orseshay adhay allenfay ill.ay Againay ehay esitatedhay
anday itay asway otnay untilay ethay enday ofay Octoberay atthay ehay inallyfay ooktay eavelay ofay
Atherinecay atay Oranienbaum.ay Eshay asway extremelyay epressedday ybay ishay eavinglay
anday eptway ethay olewhay ayday enwhay ehay amecay otay aysay arewellfay. Ethay eparationsay
eemssay otay avehay addeday ethay astlay awstray otay ethay Evalier’schay unstableay entalmay
onditioncay. Afteray aay ormystay assagepay omfray Onstadt,kray ehay arriveday inay Amburghay
alreadyay aay icksay an,may anday almostay immediatelyay ehay asway eclaredday insaneay ybay
ethay ysiciansphay anday akentay otay England.ay Aay yearay aterlay ehay endeday ishay ifelay ybay
uicidesay anday asway uriedbay inay Estminsterway Abbey.ay

Otway onthsmay afteray ishay eath,day Atherinecay otewray otay ethay Ussianray envoyay inay
Arsawway ethay ollowingfay onfidentialcay essage:may Ount“Cay Oniatovskypay isay outay
ofay umorhay ithway e,may utbay ehay isay ongwray ifay ehay elievesbay atthay obstaclesay oray
otheray incidentsay ancay etachday emay omfray imhay. Iay utpay ymay ofessionpray ofay aithfay
intoay youray ands,hay anday Iay esireday onlyay ethay omentmay ofay ouray eunion;ray Iay ishway
ehay ouldway aceplay imselfhay aboveay allay ulgarvay iflestray. Erethay isay osay uchmay
omplexitycay inay ymay esentpray erôlay atthay Iay avehay eednay ofay atthay enthusiasmay ichwhay
ehay etendspray Iay ometimessay inspire.ay Adversityay allshay otnay onquercay emay anday ifay
itay isay ecessarynay otay iumph,tray ouragecay illway otnay ebay ackinglay. Iay esteemay anday
ovelay Oniatovskypay aboveay allay ethay estray ofay ethay umanhay aceray. Ehay ustmay ebay uresay
ofay at,thay anday ifay Iay avehay oodgay ortunefay eventsay illway ovepray it.ay Inay ethay amenay
ofay Od,gay oday otnay emindray youray earerhay Oniatovsky][Pay ofay ethay enescay ithway ethay
atelay Illiamsway o,whay ilewhay aranguinghay emay eganbay otay ob;say youay illway icturepay
emay inspiringay youay ithway ouragecay anday ethay urfacesay illway ebay iling....”smay

Esethay ypticcray essagesmay indicateay atthay ethay elationshipray etweenbay Atherinecay
anday Illiamsway asway oremay emotionalay anthay ethay oliticalpay ituationsay equiredray.
Ethay omplexitycay ofay erhay erôlay inay Anuary,jay 1761,ay ethay astlay yearay ofay Empressay
Elisabeth’say ife,lay ooktay allay ofay erhay attention.ay Uringday isthay interway
especiallyay eshay ovestray otay ingratiateay erselfhay ithway ethay Ussianray ublic,pay
ossiblypay ecausebay eshay ealizedray atthay erhay ecentray intimacyay ithway oreignersfay
endedtay otay ecallray ethay actfay atthay eshay erselfhay asway otnay aay Ussianray. Erhay
assurancesay ofay affectionay orfay Oniatovskypay ereway illstay inceresay atay isthay imetay
orfay ishay uccessorsay idday otnay arriveay inay Etersburgpay untilay ethay ollowingfay
Archmay. Itay asway otnay ollywhay accidentalay atthay erhay ewnay overlay asway aay Ussianray.


6ay

Ethay artpay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay ayedplay inay ethay Evensay Years’ay
Arway asway eviousday ifay otnay exactlyay aitoroustray. Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1757,ay ethay
Ussianray armyay advanceday againstay Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray ethay Asphemous“blay
Ince”pray omwhay Elisabethay Etrovnapay osay ordiallycay etestedday. Austriaay anday
Ancefray eathedbray aay ighsay ofay eliefray otay eesay eirthay allyay atay astlay inay otionmay.
Utbay Eneralgay Apraxin,ay inay argechay ofay ethay Ussianray orces,fay otgay intoay ethay
ightfay ithway extremeay eliberationday. Ehay apturedcay Emelmay anday Ossjägerndorf,gray
anday en,thay otay ethay astonishmentay ofay allay ethay orld,way eganbay aay ostmay
unaccountableay anday astyhay etreatray owardtay ethay Ussianray orderbay. Etersburgpay
uzzedbay ithway excitement.ay Ethay Enchfray anday Austrianay ambassadorsay emandedday
anay investigation,ay ichwhay ethay outrageday Empressay asway omptpray inay ordering.ay
Eforebay ethay eyesay ofay Europe,ay erhay armiesay adhay etlay ownday erhay allies.ay
Apraxin’say onlyay excuseay orfay ishay etreatray asway atthay ehay asway ootay arfay awayay omfray
ovisionspray.

Inay ethay investigationay ichwhay ollowedfay allay uesclay eemedsay otay eadlay
ysteriouslymay otay ethay Andgray Uchessday utbay onenay ofay emthay everay uiteqay eachedray
erhay. Estushevbay asway arresteday anday ubjectedsay otay anay inquisitionay ichwhay
astedlay intermittentlyay orfay aay year.ay Earlynay allay ethay uestionsqay utpay otay
imhay ybay ethay ommissionerscay elatedray inay omesay ayway otay Atherinecay. Inay ethay
end,ay illstay ithoutway avinghay incriminateday er,hay ehay asway entsay intoay exile.ay
Adadurov,ay Atherine’scay olday eacher,tay anday everalsay otheray ubordinatessay owhay
adhay eenbay onfidentialcay essengersmay etweenbay Estushevbay anday erself,hay ereway
alsoay arrested,ay investigated,ay anday anishedbay otay emoteray artspay ofay Ussiaray.

Inallyfay Apraxin,ay ethay arstay ulpritcay inay isthay istoricalhay affair,ay asway
ecalledray omfray ethay armyay anday arresteday onay ethay orderbay asay ehay entereday Ussiaray.
Aay ourtcay ofay inquiryay asway etsay upay onay ethay otspay anday ethay Eneralgay asway ubjectedsay
otay aay ialtray ichwhay arriedcay onay intoay ethay ummersay. Onay ethay irstfay ofay Augustay
ishay ordealay asway oughtbray otay anay unexpecteday oseclay. Ehay ufferedsay aay okestray ofay
aralysispay anday iedday inay enty-fourtway ourshay. Ikelay Estushev,bay ehay adhay otnay
incriminateday ethay Andgray Uchessday eriously,say evenay oughthay ehay adhay inay ishay
ossessionpay everalsay etterslay ittenwray ybay erhay otay imselfhay. Esethay etterslay
ereway akentay omfray imhay ybay Ountcay Alexanderay Uvalov,shay ethay anmay ithway ethay
imacegray ichwhay Atherinecay adhay osay oftenay idiculed,ray anday ereway afelysay arriedcay
ackbay otay ethay Empressay Elisabeth.ay Exceptay orfay ethay actfay atthay ethay Andgray
Uchessday asway otnay alloweday otay itewray etterslay atay all,ay erethay asway othingnay
incriminatingay inay isthay orrespondencecay.

Onay ealray evidenceay everay amecay outay againstay erhay. Estushevbay adhay oundfay imetay
otay estroyday allay ishay ocumentsday eforebay ehay asway arresteday anday Atherine,cay onay
earinghay ofay ishay arrest,ay estroyedday everyay apscray ofay ittenwray aperpay inay erhay
ossessionpay. Eshay ademay aay eanclay eepsway ofay everything.ay Anay innocentay etchskay ofay
erself,hay ittenwray atay ethay ageay ofay ifteen,fay asway acrificedsay ithway ethay est,ray
aay osslay ichwhay eshay alwaysay egrettedray. Eway ustmay assumeay atthay eshay eltfay atthay
erethay asway onay imetay otay oselay. Allay erhay osestclay iendsfray anday associatesay ereway
iedtray anday onvictedcay. Eshay aloneay urvivedsay ethay isiscray ithoutway erioussay
onsequencescay.

Ethay istorianhay Ilbassovbay asway ableay otay ovepray otay ishay ownay ompletecay
atisfactionsay ybay ethay otaltay absenceay ofay ocumentaryday evidence,ay atthay ethay
Andgray Uchessday Atherine,cay oughoutthray ethay olewhay adyshay Apraxinay usiness,bay
evernay onceay averedway inay erhay oyaltylay otay Ussiaray. Erhay orrespondencecay ithway
Evalierchay Illiams,way owever,hay indicatesay atthay eshay ayedplay ithway irefay atay
isthay imetay anday asway onlyay avedsay omfray ethay argechay ofay easontray ybay erhay amazingay
instinctay orfay elf-preservationsay. Elievingbay ethay Empressay otay ebay onay ethay
ergevay ofay eath--andday apparentlyay ethay infatuateday Illiamsway elpedhay erhay otay ebay
over-confidentay aboutay ethay earnay atificationgray ofay isthay ish--sheway ealizedray
atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday Eterpay ouldway inay atthay eventay instantlyay everseray anyay
attackay onay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Opinghay orfay ethay Empress’say eathday anday
encourageday ybay aay itfay atthay ethay unfortunateay adylay oneay ayday adhay inay ublic,pay
eshay emedschay otay oldhay Apraxinay ackbay omfray ethay Ermangay ampaigncay. Ustjay atwhay
eshay idday otay ausecay ethay Eneralgay otay urntay inay ishay ackstray asay ehay idday anday enwhay
ehay idday isay aay actfay otnay owableknay otay istoryhay incesay Atherinecay urnedbay upay allay
erhay aperspay. Utbay ifay ethay Ussianray eneralgay onay isthay occasionay etrayedbay ishay
Empressay anday ishay ountry,cay ethay Andgray Uchessday asway ithoutway oubtday oneay ofay ethay
influencesay ichwhay edlay imhay intoay isthay erioussay anday atalfay istakemay.

Erethay amecay atay astlay aay amaticdray idnightmay enescay inay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday
acedfay ethay Empressay anday avedsay erselfhay onceay orfay all.ay Afteray ethay arrestay ofay
Estushev,bay eshay entspay anymay eeksway inay anay agonyay ofay uspensesay. Atay astlay eshay
otewray aay etterlay otay ethay Empressay askingay orfay anay interview,ay anday aitedway orfay
anay answeray ixsay eeksway ongerlay. Ybay isthay imetay eshay asway actuallyay anday iterallylay
alkingway ethay oor,flay aay ymptomsay ichwhay eliesbay ethay oodgay onsciencecay ichwhay
Ilbassovbay ouldway avehay usay elievebay eshay enjoyeday atay isthay ucialcray imetay.
Ybay etendingpray otay ebay icksay anday allingcay inay erhay atherfay onfessor,cay owhay
intercededay onay erhay ehalf,bay eshay anagedmay atay astlay otay induceay ethay Empressay otay
eceiveray erhay. Erhay ouragecay anday esourcefulnessray oughoutthray isthay isiscray
ovepray atthay erhay amousfay oastbay ofay intrepidityay ademay otay impressay Oniatovskypay
inay ethay esencepray ofay ethay Enchfray Ambassadoray asway otnay anay emptyay one.ay

Ethay Empress,ay owhay abituallyhay urnedtay ightnay intoay ay,day ummonedsay erhay otay
anay audienceay atay alf-pasthay oneay inay ethay orningmay. Alexanderay Uvalov,shay
imacing,gray amecay otay allcay erhay. Atherinecay icturespay orfay usay ithway iefbray
okesstray ethay oomray inay ichwhay eshay asway eceivedray ybay ethay Empress:ay ethay eethray
indows,way ethay ash-standway ithway oldgay utensils,ay ethay alltay een,scray and,ay
ehindbay ethay een,scray ethay avoritefay ofay ethay Empressay anday ethay efenderday ofay
ethay oliticalpay interestsay ofay Ance--Ivanfray Ivanovichay Uvalovshay. Inay ethay
oldgay ash-basinway eshay awsay ethay umpledcray etterslay ichwhay eshay adhay ittenwray
otay Apraxin,ay aay etailday ichwhay ivesgay usay ybay ethay ayway aay icturepay ofay owhay ethay
Empressay Elisabethay espectedray importantay ocumentsday. Enwhay Atherinecay arriveday
inay isthay oom,ray eshay oundfay ethay Andgray Ukeday alreadyay erethay eforebay erhay. Inay
ishay esence,pray inay atthay ofay Alexanderay Uvalov,shay anday inay atthay ofay ethay iddenhay
Ivanay Ivanovich,--aay olidsay iotray ofay erhay enemies--sheay asway obligeday otay efendday
erselfhay. Ethay annermay inay ichwhay eshay oseray otay ethay occasionay owsshay atthay ethay
omanway ovedlay anger;day eshay ateay itay ikelay akecay.

Eshay eganbay ybay owingthray erselfhay atay ethay Empress’say eetfay anday askingay otay ebay
entsay omehay otay erhay othermay. Elisabethay emindedray erhay atthay eshay adhay ildrenchay
inay Ussia;ray Atherinecay epliedray atthay ethay Empressay asway aay etterbay othermay otay
emthay anthay eshay erselfhay ouldcay ossiblypay ebay. Elisabethay urtherfay emindedray
erhay atthay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay adhay edflay otay Aris;pay Atherinecay epliedray
atthay erhay othermay adhay eenbay ivendray outay ofay Ermanygay ybay ethay ersecutionspay ofay
Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray ethay enemyay omwhay Elisabethay atedhay. Atwhay ancechay adhay
aay eremay emotionalay Empressay againstay astutenessay ikelay is?thay Elisabethay ellfay
ackbay uponay erhay ealray ievancegray.

You“ay areay immoderatelyay oudpray. Oday youay ememberray oneay ayday inay ethay ummersay
ardengay enwhay Iay amecay upay otay youay anday askeday youay ifay youay adhay aay ickcray inay youray
ecknay ecausebay youay arcelyscay eetedgray e?”may

Ah,“ay ymay Odgay. Owhay ouldcay Youray Ajestymay elievebay atthay Iay ouldcay ebay oudpray
owardtay you?ay Iay earsway otay youay atthay Iay adhay otnay ethay eastlay ideaay atthay youray
uestionqay ofay ourfay yearsay agoay ignifiedsay at.”thay

You“ay ancyfay atthay obodynay aliveay isay asay everclay asay yourself.”ay

If“ay Iay eallyray elievedbay isthay ofay yself,may enthay ymay esentpray ituationsay anday
isthay onversationcay eemsay estbay esignedday otay urecay emay ofay ymay error:ay untilay isthay
eryvay ay,day Iay avehay otnay understood,ay outay ofay eremay upidity,stay atwhay youay ishedway
otay aysay otay emay ourfay yearsay ago....”ay

Atay isthay ointpay ethay Andgray Ukeday eganbay otay alktay ithway Alexanderay Uvalovshay inay
ethay ackground,bay akingtay idessay againstay Atherinecay. Orfay aay omentmay ethay otway
omenway alloweday ethay Andgray Ukeday otay enteray ethay uarrel,qay anday enthay excludeday
imhay again.ay Ehay asway otnay eallyray orthyway otay oseclay ithway eitheray ofay emthay inay
ombatcay. Ethay Empressay ushedbray imhay asideay anday eturnedray otay ethay attack.ay

You“ay ixmay intoay allay indskay ofay attersmay ichwhay oday otnay oncerncay you.ay Uringday ethay
Empressay Anna’say ime,tay Iay asway otnay alloweday otay oday atthay. Owhay ouldcay you,ay orfay
example,ay avehay ethay audacityay otay issueay ommandscay otay Ieldfay Arshalmay Apraxin?”ay

I?“ay Itay evernay onceay entereday ymay eadhay otay issueay ommandscay otay im.”hay

An“Cay youay enyday atthay youay avehay ittenwray otay im?hay Youray etterslay ielay erethay inay
ethay asin....”bay

Ethay Andgray Uchessday ewknay ullfay ellway atthay erethay asway othingnay inay ethay etterslay
ichwhay Alexanderay Uvalovshay adhay avelledtray osay arfay otay ingbray omehay otay ethay
Empress.ay Eshay ehearsedray eirthay ontentscay ownay.

Estushev“Bay ays,”say Elisabethay ersisted,pay At“thay erethay ereway anymay oremay
etters.”lay

If“ay Estushevbay ayssay at,thay ehay ies.”lay

Ood“Gay. Ifay ehay ies,lay ehay allshay ebay utpay otay orture.”tay

Itay asway ethay Empress’say astlay otshay anday illstay ethay Andgray Uchessday idday otnay
inchflay. Elisabethay eganbay otay alkway upay anday ownday ethay oom,ray ilewhay Atherinecay
anday ethay Andgray Ukeday ellfay otay uarrellingqay ithway eachay other.ay Itay asway apparentay
omfray ethay Andgray Uke’sday emarksray atthay ehay asway underay ethay influenceay ofay ethay
Orontsovvay amilyfay anday ursednay ethay ideaay ofay uttingpay Elisabethay Orontsovvay inay
ethay aceplay ofay Atherinecay. Ehay asway otnay awareay atthay isthay ojectpray appealeday
eithernay otay ethay Empressay ornay otay Ivanay Uvalovshay ehindbay ethay eenscray. Is“Thay
entway eyondbay ethay entalmay apacitycay ofay ishay Imperialay Ighness,hay owhay elievedbay
allay atthay ehay ished,”way ayssay Atherine,cay And“ay ushedpay asideay everyay otheray
oughtthay ichwhay appenedhay otay interfereay ithway ethay oneay atthay omentarilymay
overnedgay im.”hay

Atay eethray o’clockay inay ethay orningmay ethay Empressay ismissedday emthay. Ethay Andgray
Ukeday eftlay ethay oomray irstfay anday anishedvay ownday ethay orridorcay ithway ishay usualay
onglay yingflay idesstray. Atherinecay eturnedray otay erhay amberchay anday undresseday
erselfhay. Itay asway ethay iddlemay ofay Aprilay anday ethay itewhay awnday illedfay ethay oomray
inay ichwhay orfay osay anymay aysday astpay eshay adhay acedpay ethay oorflay inay uspensesay anday
eeplessnessslay. Eshay entway otay edbay anday eptslay oundlysay.


7ay

Itay asway uetray atthay Atherine’scay other,may ethay Incesspray ofay Erbst,zay adhay
edflay otay Arispay. Ethay edoubtableray Ohannajay Elisabethay ad,hay ybay aay eriessay
ofay oliticalpay errors,ay ucceededsay atay astlay inay eachingray ethay itycay ofay erhay
eams,dray ethay avenhay ofay artay anday ashionfay orfay ichwhay eshay adhay alwaysay ongedlay.
Otay achieveay isthay aradisepay eshay adhay ademay aay ormystay ilgrimage;pay anday erhay oyjay
inay erhay achievementay asway otay ebay ort-lived,shay orfay erhay esidenceray inay Arispay
ovedpray otay ebay erhay undoing.ay

Inay ethay yearay 1758ay eshay asway ivinglay atay Erbstzay ithway erhay on,say Iedrichfray
August,ay ethay eigningray Incepray. Itay ancay otnay ebay aidsay atthay eshay asway ivinglay
altogetheray uietlyqay ere,thay orfay Itzfray adhay arriedmay aay youngay ifeway ithway omwhay
ishay othermay idday otnay etgay onay ellway. Accordingay otay ethay Incess,pray Itzfray alsoay
idday otnay etgay onay ellway ithway ishay ife,way owhay adhay eenbay anay obscureay Incesspray
ofay Essen-Kasselhay. Afteray ivefay yearsay ofay arriage,may eythay illstay adhay onay
ildrenchay. Esumablypray ethay omesticday atmosphereay atay Erbstzay asway anythingay utbay
easant,play althoughay ethay elationsray ofay ethay iotray ithway ethay outsideay orldway
ereway eaceablepay enough.ay Ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay eceivedray aay omfortablecay
ensionpay omfray ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray anday erethay asway atay eastlay aay opehay atthay
ethay uturefay Empress,ay owhay asway Itz’sfray ownay ister,say ouldway oneay ayday ucceedsay
inay akingmay imhay aay ealray Urfürstkay ofay Ermanygay. Ethay Erbstzay amilyfay adhay onlyay otay
ebay oodgay anday awaitay events.ay

Uddenlysay ethay Enchfray oreignfay officeay astcay anay eyeay onay isthay ittlelay
incipalitypray. Ouldway itay otnay ebay ossiblepay otay useay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay otay
influenceay erhay aughter,day ethay Andgray Uchessday ofay Ussia,ray owhay asway uspectedsay
ofay eingbay o-Englishpray anday anti-French?ay Ethay Enchfray officeay ecidedday otay
aketay ethay ancechay. Aay ashingday Enchfray officer,ay ethay Arquismay eday Aigne,fray asway
ispatchedday onay isthay issionmay anday arriveday ithoutway ifficultyday atay ethay astlecay
ofay Erbstzay. Althoughay Ancefray anday Ermanygay ereway atay ar,way ittlelay Erbstzay adhay
eclaredday itselfay eutralnay. Aay Enchfray officeray ightmay ereforethay isitvay ethay
Incepray inay erfectpay afety,say otectedpray ybay itsay eutralitynay. Eday Aignefray
ingeredlay onay atay Erbst,zay ilewhay ethay eeksway assedpay ybay inay easantplay ocialsay
onversecay. Ethay Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay otewray etterslay otay erhay aughter,day
ichwhay evernay eachedray eirthay estinationday utbay onveyedcay otay Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray allay atthay ehay eedednay otay owknay.

Uddenlysay ethay ittlelay idylay ecamebay aay olcanovay. Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway
otnay easedplay otay avehay aay Enchfray officeray arryingtay atay Erbstzay. Ehay entsay
aay etachmentday ofay oldierssay otay arrestay ethay angerstray anday emoveray imhay otay
Ussianpray oilsay erewhay ehay ouldcay ebay operlypray ourt-martialedcay. Utbay ethay
Arquismay argueday ishay asecay anday esentedpray ishay idesay osay ellway atthay ethay
Ussianpray oldierssay etiredray ithoutway imhay. Ethay offendeday Enchman,fray aideday ybay
ethay oolishfay Incepray ofay Erbstzay anday ethay illstay oremay oolishfay othermay ofay ethay
Ince,pray entsay anay indignantay otestpray otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray. Afteray all,ay
Erbstzay asway eutral,nay anday ethay Ussianspray oughtay eallyray otay apologize.ay

Ederick’sfray answeray asway ompt:pray aay uadronsqay ofay artilleryay appeareday eforebay
ethay olday aygray allsway ofay Erbstzay. Eitheray eday Aignefray ouldway omecay outay oray ethay
allsway ouldway ogay ownday. Ethay Arquismay ecidedday otay ivegay imselfhay up,ay anday ethay
Ussianspray ooktay imhay uietlyqay away.ay Utbay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay anday erhay
onsay adhay ushedpay ethay issueay ootay arfay anday Ederickfray asway otnay oinggay otay etlay
emthay offay ootay easily.ay Ehay imposeday aay enaltypay ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ucatsday
anday ethay upplysay ofay oragefay enoughay orfay aay egimentray. Itay asway aay evastatingday
enalty;pay itay ipedway emthay out.ay Inay esperationday ethay Incesspray anday erhay onsay
edflay ethay ituationsay anday abandoneday ethay incipalitypray otay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay.
Inay eirthay astehay eythay eftlay ehindbay emthay ethay youngay ifeway ofay ethay Incepray. Oray
idday eshay erhapspay eclineday otay ogay ithway em?thay Erhapspay eshay oughtthay eshay adhay
othingnay otay oselay ybay emainingray ithway ethay Ussianpray occupation.ay Oweverhay
isthay aymay avehay een,bay eshay idday otnay onglay urvivesay ethay ightflay ofay ethay others.ay
Ithinway esslay anthay aay year,ay eshay iedday ofay aay okestray ofay aralysispay. Itay eganbay otay
ooklay asay ifay ethay ousehay ofay Erbstzay asway oomedday otay extinction.ay

Inay ethay eantime,may ethay eeingflay othermay anday onsay entway irstfay otay Amburghay.
Omfray Amburghay Itzfray epartedday otay enlistay inay ethay Austrianay armyay anday ightfay
Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray ilewhay ishay othermay entway onay otay Arispay. Eshay elievedbay
atthay ethay Enchfray overnmentgay ouldway elcomeway erhay ithway openay armsay afteray ethay
eatgray acrificesay atthay eshay adhay ademay orfay atthay ountrycay. Utbay ethay Enchfray
overnmentgay ackedlay appreciation.ay Eythay ownay ewknay asay uchmay aboutay Ohannajay
Elisabethay asay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ewknay enwhay eshay amecay ackbay omfray Ussiaray
ithway Ardefeld’smay ismissalday inay erhay Atelaine__chay. Ethay Incesspray ovedlay
intrigueay utbay eshay asway oomedday otay ailfay inay it;ay erhay ojectspray alwaysay urnedtay
againstay er,hay asay ifay eshay iedtray otay ackcray aay ipwhay ootay onglay orfay erhay engthstray
anday asway aughtcay inay ethay itebay ofay itsay uelcray aperingtay end.ay

Ethay Enchfray overnmentgay ademay ineffectualay attemptsay otay elayday ethay ogresspray
ofay ethay Incesspray asay eshay astenedhay owardtay Arispay. Eythay entsay aay astlay
esperateday essagemay otay arrestay erhay atay Ussels,bray utbay Ohannajay Elisabethay asway
onay ethay astlay aplay ofay erhay ourneyjay otay Arispay eforebay ethay essagemay arrived.ay
Erethay asway aay ertaincay athospay inay ethay etterlay ichwhay Erni,bay ethay oreignfay
inister,may otewray otay ethay Enchfray esidentray atay Etersburgpay. E“Thay Incesspray
ofay Erbstzay astenedhay osay atthay ethay etterlay ichwhay explaineday ethay ecessitynay
ofay ostponingpay erhay arrivalay inay Ancefray idday otnay eachray Usselsbray untilay eshay
asway alreadyay inay Alenciennes,vay omfray ichwhay oneay ouldcay otnay eventpray erhay omfray
omingcay onay otay Aris.”pay Ernibay ishedway ethay Empressay otay understanday atthay ehay
adhay otnay onnivedcay atay ethay Incess’spray ightflay otay Ancefray.

Elisabethay asway uriousfay ithway ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay. Ethay other’smay
ehaviorbay oincidedcay ithway ethay aughter’sday eddlesomenessmay inay ethay Apraxinay
usinessbay. Ethay ullfay athwray ofay ethay Empressay ellfay uponay ethay other’smay
ivolousfray ead;hay eshay omptlypray ithdrewway ethay ady’slay ensionpay. Ethay Incess,pray
owhay etendedpray otay observeay anay incognitoay inay Arispay asay Ountesscay ofay
Oldenburg,ay etsay upay anay establishmentay anday ungedplay intoay iterarylay anday ourtcay
ocietysay. Uddenlysay eshay oundfay erselfhay utcay offay ithoutway aay ousay. Erhay etterslay
otay ethay Empressay areay itiablepay. Asay erhay editorscray essedpray erhay arderhay anday
arder,hay eshay ultipliedmay erhay etitionspay. Ethay Empressay ondescendedcay otay ebay
ositivelypay indictivevay. Eshay entsay aay essagemay otay ethay ankruptbay omanway at,thay
afteray irstfay ayingpay erhay ebts,day eshay oughtay otay eavelay Arispay. Isthay ilencedsay
ethay oorpay omanway atay astlay.

Isthay asway inay ethay autumnay ofay 1759,ay anday ethay Incesspray asway alreadyay illay ofay
opsydray. Eshay assedpay ethay interway inay edbay attendeday ybay ysiciansphay. Erhay
etterslay otay Ussiaray easedcay otay etitionpay orfay oney;may eshay eemedsay otay ealizeray
atthay Elisabethay asway inexorable.ay Ethay Andgray Uchess,day owhay idday otnay owknay ofay
erhay other’smay inancialfay istress,day entsay erhay aay esentpray ofay omesay eatay anday
ubarbrhay. Utbay ethay Incesspray iedday eforebay isthay ittlelay iftgay arrived.ay Itay asway
onlyay ithway ethay eatestgray effortay atthay Atherinecay anday Ivanay Uvalov,shay omwhay
eshay inallyfay ersuadedpay otay elphay er,hay ouldcay induceay ethay Empressay otay aypay ethay
ebtsday ofay ethay eceasedday Incesspray. Elisabethay asway illingway ethay Incess’spray
ersonalpay effectsay ouldshay ebay oldsay atay ublicpay auction.ay Itay asway ardhay evenay orfay
ethay avorite,fay Ivanay Uvalov,shay otay ersuadepay erhay otay avesay erhay inswoman’skay
emorymay omfray isthay isgraceday. Owardtay Ohannajay Elisabethay eshay adhay alwaysay
eenbay evengefulray.


8ay

Ethay Empressay idday otnay onglay outlastay erhay enemy.ay Orfay anymay yearsay eshay adhay
eallyray eenbay anay invalid.ay Eshay adhay ecretlysay importeday aay amousfay Enchfray
ysicianphay owhay aidsay atthay eshay ufferedsay omfray ystericalhay Apors”“vay anday
onvulsionscay. Elisabeth’say ersonalpay ysicianphay asway aay Eek,gray Ondoidi,kay owhay
atay irstfay efusedray otay onsultcay ithway ethay oreignfay ecialistspay. Afteray uchmay
iplomatizingday onay ethay artpay ofay ethay Enchfray anday Ussianray overnments,gay ethay
ivalsray atay astlay onsentedcay otay eetmay. Itay urnedtay outay atthay eythay agreeday inay
eirthay iagnosisday ofay elancholiamay anday ysteria,hay anday osay eythay ookshay andshay
overay ethay oorpay Empressay owhay ontinuedcay otay etgay onay etterbay. Othingnay oremay
efiniteday anthay isthay asway ethay Empressay estinedday otay ieday of.ay Owingay otay ethay
onvulsionscay otay ichwhay eshay asway ubject,say erhay eathday eemedsay everalsay imestay
imminent;ay utbay enthay eshay ouldway uddenlysay ullpay erselfhay ogethertay anday eathday
ouldway ecederay otay aay espectfulray istanceday. Erhay illnessay aggeddray onay ikelay
ethay Evensay Years’ay Arway anday ethay outcomeay asway asay unpredictable.ay Omfray ethay
eginningbay ofay ethay yearay 1761,ay owever,hay erhay onditioncay atentlypay ewgray orseway.
Uringday ethay ummersay eshay ellfay intoay onvulsionscay ichwhay ausedcay erhay otay oselay
onsciousnesscay orfay everalsay ourshay atay aay imetay. Onay Istmaschray Ay,day 1761,ay eshay
ied,day atay ethay ageay ofay ifty-twofay. Erhay anspay ofay ifelay asway utbay ightlyslay esslay
anthay atthay ofay erhay alltay urbulenttay ather,fay Eterpay ethay Eat,gray owhay iedday atay
ifty-threefay.

Erethay ereway eethray eoplepay owhay adhay awaiteday erhay eathday ithway aryingvay
egreesday ofay impatience.ay Otay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ethay ewsnay asway annamay inay
ethay ilderness;way itay ademay imhay atay astlay ictorvay inay ethay Evensay Years’ay Arway.
Otay Andgray Ukeday Eter,pay itay asway ethay eleaseray ofay allay ishay eams;dray asay Arczay ofay
Ussia,ray ehay ouldcay ownay ollowfay ishay illusionsay ereverwhay eythay edlay im,hay evenay
otay ethay astlay imitslay ofay estructionday. Otay Andgray Uchessday Atherine,cay itay asway
otnay altogetheray opportune.ay Eethray yearsay eforebay eshay adhay eenbay oremay eageray
orfay Elisabeth’say eathday anthay eshay asway enwhay ethay Empressay atay astlay ademay ayway
orfay erhay. Atherinecay asway atay isthay imetay egnantpray ithway erhay irdthay ildchay anday
oremay anthay everay atay oddsay ithway ethay Andgray Uke,day erhay usbandhay. Erhay ewnay overlay
asway Egorygray Orlov,ay aay andsomehay youngay aptaincay ofay artillery.ay

Ilewhay Eterpay elebratedcay ishay accessionay otay ethay onethray ithway ethay usualay
eremonies,cay eshay ithdrewway erselfhay iscreetlyday omfray ethay ublicpay azegay. Eshay
apeddray erselfhay inay eavyhay ackblay anday aidpay erhay ailyday omagehay otay ethay orpsecay
ofay ethay Empress,ay eelingknay orfay ourshay esidebay ethay arcophagussay. Accordingay otay
ustomcay ethay odybay aylay exposeday otay ublicpay iewvay orfay ixsay eeksway. Inay ethay ifthfay
eek,way ithway erhay ownay andshay anday ithoutway aay uiver,qay eshay acedplay aay oldengay
owncray onay ethay eadhay ofay isthay alodorousmay object.ay Itay asway erhay inalfay actay ofay
obeisanceay otay ethay Empressay owhay ecededpray erhay.
