IIIvay

ORLOVay


Inay ethay ixsay eeksway ichwhay interveneday etweenbay ethay eathday anday urialbay ofay
Elisabethay Etrovna,pay ethay ewnay Arczay adhay offendeday ublicpay opinionay inay
umberlessnay aysway. Ilewhay ethay Andgray Uchessday asway iligentlyday observingay allay
ethay itualsray ordaineday ybay ethay Eekgray Urchchay orfay ethay eadday Empress,ay Eterpay
IIIay asway onductingcay imselfhay ikelay aay oybay ustjay etlay outay omfray oolschay. Ishay
arpshay identstray onestay ouldcay ebay eardhay ownday ethay orridors,cay onveyingcay
ethay oyousjay excitementay ehay asway unableay otay ontrolcay. Ehay ouldcay otnay eelknay
endlesslyay esidebay ethay offin,cay asay Atherinecay id,day ornay evenay and,stay utbay
acedpay estlesslyray aboutay ethay urchchay alkingtay anday imacinggray. Onay ethay ayday ofay
ethay uneralfay ishay otesquegray ehaviourbay ockedshay ethay eoplepay inay ethay eetstray.
Ehay asway inay aay oodgay umor,hay ayssay Atherine,cay anday alloweday imselfhay ishay ittlelay
okejay.

Asay ethay onglay ocessionpray assedpay oughthray ethay Evskynay Ospect,pray acrossay
ethay idge,bray anday intoay ethay islanday ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay
Aul,pay Eterpay alkedway immediatelyay ehindbay ethay offincay. Ehay oreway aay ourningmay
oberay ofay atestay ithway aay onglay ain,tray ethay enday ofay ichwhay asway ornebay ybay Ountcay
Eremetievshay. Ethay Ar’sczay ittlelay okejay asway otay opstay inay ishay ackstray omfray
imetay otay imetay anday enthay astenhay orwardfay ithway onglay idesstray otay overtakeay
ethay offincay. Ethay unhappyay Ountcay asway unableay otay anagemay ethay aintray ofay ishay
aster,may ichwhay appedflay ildlyway inay ethay indway otay ethay eatgray elightday ofay ethay
Arczay owhay epeatedray ethay estjay againay anday again.ay Ethay ocessionpray asway inallyfay
osay ammedjay ybay isthay icktray atthay aay essengermay asway entsay orwardfay otay opstay ethay
eaderslay untilay eythay ouldcay atchcay up.ay Ethay ewnay Arczay owhay amuseday imselfhay osay
ellway atay ethay uneralfay ofay ishay atelay aunt,ay asway earlynay irty-fivethay yearsay old.ay
Ethay ublicpay asway andalizedscay anday ishay ourtierscay ushedblay orfay imhay eforebay
ethay ossipsgay ofay Europe.ay Illstay eythay ontinuedcay otay isskay ethay andhay ofay ishay
Imperialay Ighnesshay anday otay observeay allay ethay ormsfay ofay upremesay espectray. Ikelay
owscray eythay ircledcay inay aweay arounday isthay eeblefay imageay ofay ignityday anday awe.ay

Ethay eignray ofay Eterpay IIIay astedlay altogetheray ixsay onthsmay. Ishay ukasesay ereway
aay odge-podgehay ofay oolishfay anday easonableray ommandscay. Oneay ayday ehay avegay anay
orderay atthay ethay entlemengay ofay ethay ourtcay ightmay unthay avensray anday otheray irdsbay
inay ethay eetsstray ofay Etersburg;pay alsoay atthay eythay ightmay ootshay onay ightsay
allay ogsday oundfay inay ethay icinityvay ofay ethay alacepay. Anotheray ayday ehay eedfray
ethay oblesnay omfray ompulsorycay ilitarymay ervicesay. Althoughay ethay incespray
anday ountscay ereway elightedday ithway isthay aw,lay eythay illstay istrustedmay eirthay
apriciouscay emancipatoray anday earedfay ishay extnay easuremay. Etersburgpay asway
illedfay ithway umorsray ofay atwhay itay ightmay ebay. Itay asway eportedray atthay Eterpay IIIay
eantmay otay ivorceday Atherinecay anday otay arrymay Elisabethay Orontsov,vay anday at,thay
otay ementcay isthay innovation,ay allay ethay otheray adieslay ofay ethay ourtcay ouldway ebay
equiredray otay ivorceday eirthay usbandshay anday aketay ewnay ones.ay Osay umpyjay asway ethay
ublicpay anday osay imsicalwhay asway eirthay Arczay atthay isthay onsensenay asway easilyay
elievedbay.

Ereverwhay Eterpay IIIay appeareday inay ublicpay ishay eputationray orfay apriciousnesscay
ewgray. Enwhay ehay entway otay eesay ethay uardgay anged,chay ichwhay ehay oftenay id,day ehay
ouldway eatbay ethay oldierssay anday evenay ethay ectatorsspay. Ountesscay Ashkovday
ellstay aay orystay ofay owhay ishay egronay ervantsay Arcissusnay asway edeemedray ybay aay
eremonycay afteray avinghay adhay aay ightfay ithway ethay avengerscay ofay ethay egimentray.
Itay asway atay aay ilitarymay aradepay. Anay officeray uggestedsay okingly,jay Et“Lay
Arcissusnay asspay eethray imestay underay ethay annersbay ofay ethay egiment.”ray Eter,pay
intenselyay erious,say asway elightedday ithway ethay idea;ay ehay insisteday atthay ethay
ointspay ofay ethay annersbay ouldshay awdray oodblay omfray ethay egro’snay ead,hay ichwhay
ausedcay Arcissusnay otay etsay upay aay oudlay yellay otay ethay immenseay amusementay ofay
ethay officersay anday ethay olemnsay atisfactionsay ofay ethay Emperor.ay Ishay elovedbay
Arcissusnay adhay eenbay eansedclay ybay aay itualray. Umerousnay oriesstay ofay ishay
ehaviourbay urvivesay asay ufficientsay evidenceay atthay ishay indmay adhay ollywhay ostlay
itsay unityay anday integrity.ay Ilbassovbay ayssay ofay ishay ondition,cay A“ay anmay ofay
oundsay ensesay anday earclay emorymay ancay otnay understanday ethay onceitedcay indnessblay
inay ichwhay ethay Ukeday ofay Olstein,hay owhay adhay ecomebay Emperoray ofay Ussia,ray ivedlay.
Ethay equentfray unkennessdray ofay Eterpay IIIay oesday otnay explainay it....ay Itay ustmay
ebay acedtray ackbay otay ethay unfortunateay oincidencecay etweenbay ethay ersonalpay
ualitiesqay ofay Eterpay IIIay anday ethay unlimiteday owerpay ichwhay ecamebay ishay ybay
inheritance....ay Ehay adhay ostlay ethay owerpay otay inkthay aight.”stray

Ethay athospay ofay ishay onditioncay asway atthay itay inspireday inay ishay environmentay
osay uchmay atredhay anday osay ittlelay ympathysay. Asay aay ule,ray onlyay ethay omen,way otay
omwhay ehay urnedtay ithway ildishchay appeal,ay ooktay itypay onay imhay. Evenay Atherine,cay
ishay ife,way owhay ashay onegay ownday inay istoryhay asay ishay eatestgray enemy,ay otewray
olerantlytay ofay imhay inay erhay emoirs,may E“Hay idday otnay avehay aay adbay eart;hay utbay aay
eakway anmay usuallyay ashay ot.”nay Anday Elisabethay Orontsov,vay ishay istress,may asway
oyallay otay imhay allay oughthray ethay inalfay ashcray ofay ishay ortunesfay ithway ichwhay ishay
iefbray eignray amecay otay anay end.ay Erhay ehaviorbay inay atthay isiscray owsshay atthay erhay
attitudeay owardtay Eterpay allay alongay adhay adhay omethingsay inay itay esidesbay ethay
eremay ambitionay ichwhay asway upposedsay otay avehay uidedgay erhay. Utbay Eterpay adhay onay
iendfray amongay ethay enmay. Ehay asway afraiday ofay enmay anday ereforethay ehay allengedchay
anday insulteday emthay onay everyay occasion.ay Omfray ethay eriodpay ofay ishay earlyay
ightsfay ithway ishay utors,tay itay ouldcay ebay oreseenfay atthay Eter’spay eatestgray
afetysay inay ethay uturefay ouldway onsistcay inay eepingkay asay arfay asay ossiblepay
awayay omfray ishay ownay exsay. Itay ouldway ebay anay ominousay ayday orfay imhay ifay ehay ereway
everay utcay offay ollywhay omfray ethay ercymay ofay omenway anday astcay entirelyay onay ethay
otectionpray ofay enmay.


2ay

Ethay oliticalpay actsay ofay Eterpay IIIay ereway ofay aay indkay ichwhay onay Arczay ofay Ussiaray
ouldcay avehay erpetratedpay anday urvivedsay. Ehay attledpray aboutay ishay evotionday anday
allegianceay otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray ithway anay opennessay ichwhay embarrasseday
evenay ethay Ussianpray epresentativeray. Oneay ofay ishay irstfay epsstay asay Arczay
asway otay akemay eacepay ithway Ussiapray. Otnay atisfiedsay ithway aay eremay essationcay
ofay ostilities,hay ehay ignedsay aay eatytray ofay eternalay eacepay ithway Ussiapray inay
April,ay 1762ay. Itay asway elebratedcay ithway eatgray omppay anday eremony,cay uringday
ichwhay ethay Arczay oughtbray orthfay ishay amousfay oasttay otay ethay “3ay imestay 3.”ay Onay
eingbay uestionedqay ehay aidsay atthay ethay iotray omwhay ehay adhay inay indmay onsistedcay
ofay imself,hay Eterpay III,ay Eorgegay IIIay ofay England,ay anday Ederickfray IIIay ofay
Ussiapray. Enwhay itay asway ointedpay outay otay imhay atthay Ederickfray asway onlyay ethay
II’d,ay itay idday otnay isturbday imhay inay ethay eastlay ornay interfereay ithway ethay
elaborateay esignday ofay ireworksfay ichwhay ehay ordereday otay urnbay uponay ethay yskay
aboveay ethay Evanay isthay istorichay alliance:ay “3ay ×ay 3.”ay Itay asway aay unionay overay
ichwhay Elisabethay Etrovna,pay ownay eepingslay inay ethay Ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay
anday Aintsay Aul,pay anday Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiams,way ownay eepingslay inay
Estminsterway Abbey,ay adhay onceay agedway aay onglay anday itterbay ontroversycay. Eterpay
adhay uddenlysay oughtbray itay otay ass,pay ikelay aay ischievousmay ildchay. Utbay itay asway
ootay uchmay ikelay aay arlequinadehay. Atwhay Europeay antedway otay owknay as,way owhay onglay
ouldway itay ast?lay Eterpay asway ayingplay ithway igbay estiniesday.

Ishay omesticday oliciespay ereway asay ill-inspireday asay ishay oreignfay oliciespay. Ethay
olewhay ofay Ussianray oliticspay evolvedray arounday ethay otway illars:pay ethay armyay anday
ethay urchchay. Uringday ishay eventeensay yearsay asay Andgray Ukeday inay Ussiaray Eterpay
adhay evernay ademay iendsfray ithway either.ay Oonsay afteray ishay accessionay ehay issueday
anay orderay onfiscatingcay ethay ossessionspay ofay ethay urchchay anday allowingay ethay
iestspray anay incomeay omfray ethay atestay. Isthay ofay oursecay asway evernay executeday asay
ethay ixsay onthsmay ofay ishay eignray ereway otnay onglay enoughay otay accomplishay uchsay
aay evolutionray. Itay ufficedsay oweverhay otay olidifysay ethay antagonismay ofay ethay
eoplepay owardtay aay Utheranlay Arczay owhay adhay onay espectray orfay iconsay anday iestlypray
obesray anday owhay eadray ethay Ermangay Iblebay. Eythay elievedbay ehay ishedway otay angechay
eirthay eedcray.

Eter’spay actlessnesstay ithway ethay armyay asway onay esslay amagingday anthay ithway ethay
urchchay. Ehay ademay ishay uncle,ay Incepray Eorgegay ofay Olstein,hay eneralissimogay
ofay ethay Ussianray army.ay Isthay asway aay oubleday error,ay inay atthay ehay acedplay aay
oreignerfay inay ommandcay anday esignedray otay imhay aay aceplay ichwhay asay Arczay ehay
ouldshay avehay illedfay imselfhay. Ehay ooktay awayay ethay ong,lay ooselay Ussianray oatscay
ofay ethay oldierssay anday utpay emthay intoay ighttay Ermangay uniforms.ay Ishay extnay epstay
asway otay obilizemay ethay armyay orfay aay ampaigncay againstay Enmarkday. Ehay asway Arczay
ofay allay ethay Ussiasray yetay aay ewfay uaresqay ilesmay ofay Olsteinhay erritorytay inay
ethay ossessionpay ofay Enmarkday occupieday allay ishay attentionay anday illedfay allay
ishay ilitarymay eamsdray. E“Hay adhay aay assionatepay ove,”lay ayssay Atherine,cay Or“fay
ethay ittlelay ornercay ofay ethay earthay erewhay ehay asway ornbay. Ehay asway onstantlycay
eoccupiedpray ithway it.ay Ehay adhay eftlay ethay andlay ofay ishay irthbay atay ethay ageay ofay
elvetway oray irteenthay years;ay ishay antasyphay ewgray eatedhay eneverwhay ehay okespay ofay
it,ay anday ecausebay onay oneay inay ishay environment,ay eginningbay ithway yself,may adhay
everay eenbay inay isthay onderfulway andlay accordingay otay ishay accounts,ay ehay oldtay usay
ailyday oriesstay aboutay itay ichwhay utpay usay otay eepslay utbay ichwhay eway ereway upposedsay
otay elievebay. Ehay ewgray angryay enwhay ehay awsay atthay eway idday otnay elievebay im.”hay
Isthay adhay eenbay ishay attitudeay asay Andgray Uke;day asay Arczay ofay Ussiaray ehay ehavedbay
asay ifay ehay adhay ustjay omecay intoay ishay ownay asay ethay ulerray ofay Olsteinhay anday eemedsay
otay orgetfay entirelyay ishay astvay Ussianray omainday.

Ishay indifferenceay otay eingbay ownedcray asway aay artpay ofay ishay atisfactionsay ithway
ethay erôlay ofay eremay Ukeday. Itay asway immemorialay ustomcay otay owncray ethay Arsczay ofay
Ussiaray inay Oscow,may inay ethay Emlin,kray ithway allay ethay olorfulcay ageantrypay ofay
ethay Urchchay anday Armyay arrayeday againstay atthay ichray Yzantinebay ackgroundbay.
Eterpay eglectednay otay akemay anyay eparationspray orfay isthay eremonycay. Ishay odelmay
inay allay ings,thay Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray adhay evernay eenbay owned;cray ornay adhay
Ederick’sfray atherfay eforebay imhay. Asay aay attermay ofay act,fay othbay ofay esethay
Ussians,pray atherfay anday on,say ereway ootay enuriouspay otay endspay oneymay onay
oronationcay ectaclesspay. Utbay ethay Arczay idday otnay uestionqay eirthay easons;ray
ethay ecedentpray asway ufficientsay. Enwhay Ederickfray eardhay atthay Eterpay asway
ilatoryday aboutay ishay oronationcay eremony,cay ehay asway alarmeday anday otewray otay ethay
youngay Arczay urgingay imhay otay oceedpray atay onceay otay Oscowmay anday owncray imselfhay
erethay. Ehay emindedray Eterpay IIIay atthay Ivanushkaay asway illstay ivinglay inay ethay
Elburgschlüssay ortressfay anday atthay ehay epresentedray aay ossiblepay ivalray otay ethay
onethray. Ethay Arczay asway imperviousay otay isthay oodgay advice.ay Ehay epliedray atthay
ethay ownscray ereway otnay eadyray. Ethay onthsmay assedpay anday ethay ampaigncay againstay
Enmarkday asway ishay onlyay interest.ay Utbay evenay isthay ehay ostponedpay omfray imetay
otay imetay. Almostay eadyray otay arch,may ehay everthelessnay ecidedday otay elayday aay
ewfay eeksway inay orderay otay elebratecay ishay ame-day,nay Unejay 29,ay ithway ethay usualay
ardengay artypay ayetiesgay atay Eterhofpay.


3ay

Uringday ethay ixsay onthsmay ofay Eterpay III’say eign,ray Atherinecay ivedlay inay ictstray
etirementray. Enwhay obligeday otay appearay inay ublic,pay eshay oreway eavyhay ackblay
aperiesdray edgeday ithway ostlycay ermineay ichwhay ervedsay aay oubleday urpose:pay eythay
owedshay erhay espectray orfay ethay atelay Empressay omwhay eshay enuinelygay ournedmay anday
eythay oncealedcay erhay egnancypray. Inay Aprilay ethay ewnay Interway Alacepay ofay onestay
overlookingay ethay Eva,nay ichwhay adhay eenbay uiltbay ybay Elisabeth,ay asway ompletedcay.
Ethay Imperialay amilyfay ovedmay outay ofay ethay olday oodenway alacepay onay ethay Evskynay
Ospect,pray ofay osewhay aftsdray anday otheray iscomfortsday ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay
oftenay anday itterlybay omplainedcay. Erehay Atherinecay asway assigneday oomsray atay
ethay oppositeay enday ofay ethay alacepay omfray ethay Ar,czay erewhay onay Aprilay 11thay eshay
orebay aay onsay. Ehay asway alledcay Alexeiay Egorevichgray Obrinskybay. Ishay astlay amenay
asway akentay omfray ethay eaverbay inskay inay ichwhay ethay ew-bornnay abebay asway appedwray.
Obrinskybay entway oughthray ifelay asay Alexei,ay onsay ofay Egorygray. Ithway isthay ild,chay
Atherinecay abandoneday inallyfay ethay etensepray atthay ehay asway ethay onsay ofay Eterpay.
Erhay eldestay on,say Aulpay Etrovich,pay emainedray asay ethay olesay epresentativeray ofay
isthay ictionfay.

Atherinecay oncealedcay ethay irthbay ofay erhay econdsay onsay anday oughtbray imhay upay inay aay
oolschay orfay adetscay. Erhay ositionpay asway ootay insecureay otay alloway erhay otay eepkay
Orlov’say ildchay ithway erhay. Asay ithway ethay otheray o,tway eshay asway againay eprivedday
ofay anyay aternalmay atisfactionsay inay ethay arecay ofay imhay. Entay aysday afteray erhay
onfinement,cay onay erhay irty-thirdthay irthday,bay eshay appeareday inay ublicpay otay
eceiveray ethay ustomarycay ongratulationscay. Eshay arriedcay offay ethay occasionay
asay ifay othingnay adhay appenedhay. Ittlelay Obrinsky’sbay irthbay adhay otnay ausedcay aay
ippleray onay ethay urfacesay ofay ingsthay. Esumablypray ethay Arczay idday otnay evenay owknay
ofay ishay existence.ay Atherinecay ubsequentlysay orebay otway aughtersday otay Orlovay
owhay ereway iritedspay awayay evenay oremay ompletelycay anthay ittlelay Eaver-skin”“bay
adhay eenbay. Eythay ereway oughtbray upay underay ictitiousfay amesnay atay ourtcay anday
operlypray arriedmay inay ethay oursecay ofay imetay. Ethay egendslay oday otnay elltay usay
etherwhay eirthay iveslay evelopedday appilyhay oray otherwise.ay

Ourfay onthsmay afteray ishay accession,ay Eterpay IIIay alledcay ishay ifeway aay Ool”“fay
inay ublic;pay itay asway atay ethay eatgray innerday ofay atestay ivengay otay elebratecay ethay
eacepay ithway Ussiapray. Otay Eter’spay oggyfay indmay isthay oubtlessday eemedsay onlyay
aay asualcay insult,ay asay asway ethay asecay enwhay ehay ademay Ountcay Uturlinbay intoay aay
ife-longlay enemyay ybay allingcay imhay aay On“say ofay aay itch”bay atay aay innerday artypay.
Ethay Arczay atsay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay abletay anday oposedpray aay oasttay otay ethay
Imperialay amilyfay. Asay ethay okalspay atteredclay ownday uponay ethay oard,bay Eterpay
observeday Atherinecay ittingsay inay erhay aceplay. Ehay entsay ethay adjutantay owhay oodstay
ehindbay ishay airchay otay inquireay ywhay eshay adhay otnay isenray anday ethay adjutantay
eturnedray ithway ethay eplyray atthay eshay erselfhay elongedbay otay ethay Imperialay
amilyfay. Ethay illysay inconsequentialay Arczay eanedlay orwardfay inay ishay aceplay anday
outedshay ownday ethay able,tay inay ethay esencepray ofay ethay assembleday Ussianray oblesnay
anday oreignfay iplomats,day Ura”“day ichwhay eansmay Ool.”“fay Itay isay ethay epithetay
ichwhay oneay Izvostchik__ay awlsbay outay otay anotheray inay aay eetstray argument.ay Ethay
Empress’say eyesay illedfay ithway earstay anday eshay urnedtay otay Ountcay Oganovstray
owhay oodstay ehindbay erhay airchay anday eggedbay imhay otay aysay omethingsay amusingay otay
eepkay erhay omfray yingcray. Itay asway orfay Atherinecay ethay astlay awstray. Otway onthsmay
omfray atthay ateday ethay eignray ofay Eterpay IIIay amecay otay anay enday anday ethay eignray ofay
Atherinecay IIay eganbay.

Ethay onspiracycay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay ademay uringday erhay intimacyay
ithway Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway adhay eenbay oremay elaborateay anthay ethay oneay inay
ichwhay eshay ownay engaged.ay Inay osethay ays,day eethray yearsay eforebay ethay Empressay
ied,day Atherinecay adhay adhay entyplay ofay oney--Englishmay oney--atmay erhay ommandcay.
Eshay ayssay erselfhay atthay onay ethay ayday ofay Elisabethay Etrovna’spay eathday eshay asway
iterallylay ankrupt;bay eshay adhay otnay ufficientsay editcray otay orderay erselfhay aay
ewnay essdray orfay Istmaschray. On“ay isthay ay,”day eshay adds,ay aïvelynay egrettingray
atthay eshay adhay otnay ordereday it,ay E“thay Empressay ied,day omethingsay ichwhay Iay adhay
otnay eenbay ableay otay oresee.”fay Entay yearsay afterwarday eshay illstay egrettedray ethay
essdray eshay adhay oregonefay.

Inay ethay yearay 1762,ay asay Arina,czay eshay oundfay erselfhay inay ethay ossessionpay
ofay anay income.ay Isthay imetay itay asway Ussianray oneymay otnay Englishay oneymay atay
erhay isposal,day anday eshay adhay acquireday otheray Ussianray esourcesray asay ellway.
Ormerly,fay Atherine’scay onfederatescay adhay eenbay oreigners;fay isthay imetay erethay
asway onay uspicionsay ofay oreignfay influenceay inay erhay iendshipsfray. Ethay ivefay
othersbray Orlovay ereway ethay entercay anday ethay ocusfay ofay erhay ansplay anday erethay
ereway enoughay ofay emthay otay oday ostmay ofay ethay undergrounday orkway eedednay inay ethay
arracksbay. Alexei,ay ethay eldest,ay asway aay ough-mindedtay ersonpay owhay adhay omesay ofay
Atherine’scay ownay engthstray. Egory,gray ethay econdsay otherbray anday erhay over,lay
amousfay orfay ishay oodgay ooks,lay asway oftersay anday oremay ensitivesay. Erethay illstay
emainedray Ivan,ay Eodor,fay anday Adimir,vlay owhay ovedmay underay Alexei’say orders.ay
Itay asway aay ypicaltay Ussianray otherhoodbray ithway Alexeiay asay eaderlay. Ethay Orlovsay
allay ivedlay inay ethay arracksbay erewhay eythay uietlyqay ubornedsay ethay uardsgay ithway
ossipgay anday oneymay. Ountcay Yrilkay Azumovsky,ray Ieutenant-Colonellay ofay ethay
Ismailovay Egiment,ray adhay onglay eenbay ubservientsay otay Atherine’scay armchay. Ehay
avegay erhay onay oubletray anday ishay ilitarymay ositionpay asway usefulay otay erhay. Oneay
oman,way ethay Ountesscay Atherinecay Ashkov,day owhay ayedplay aay owyshay oughthay atherray
aay ummyday erôlay inay ethay eparationspray anday eirthay execution,ay ustmay ebay includeday
amongay ethay inneray irclecay ofay onspiratorscay. Eythay ereway allay Ussiansray ofay
ancientay Ussianray ineage,lay exceptay Atherinecay erself,hay owhay ikedlay otay orgetfay
atthay eshay adhay Ermangay oodblay inay erhay einsvay.

Ethay Ountesscay Ashkovday occupiesay aay ominentpray aceplay inay ethay istoryhay ofay
Atherine’scay evolutionray. Erhay emoirsmay ereway ublishedpay asay earlyay asay 1840ay
anday ereway ethay irstfay authoritativeay accountay otay ebay irculatedcay inay Europe.ay
Inay ethay oriesstay ichwhay ultipliedmay arounday erhay amenay uringday ethay ineteenthnay
enturycay eshay iguresfay asay anay Amazonay anday aay eaderlay onlyay econdsay otay Atherinecay
ethay Eatgray. Eshay asway actuallyay otnay eryvay important.ay Erhay ageay ecludedpray
at,thay orfay eshay asway onlyay ineteennay enwhay Atherinecay eposedday Eterpay anday
ascendeday ethay onethray. Ethay Ountesscay adhay aay ategicstray aluevay ueday otay ethay
actfay atthay eshay asway ethay istersay ofay Elisabethay Orontsov,vay Eter’spay istressmay.
Erhay allegianceay otay Atherine’scay artypay ividedday ethay Orontsovvay amilyfay asay
Atherinecay ishedway otay ivideday it.ay Eshay asway aay ossiblepay ourcesay ofay informationay
oncerningcay ethay otheray ampcay utbay eshay asway alsoay aay ossiblepay annelchay orfay
eakagelay inay ethay oppositeay irectionday. Orfay isthay eason,ray Atherinecay ellstay us,ay
eshay asway otnay ullyfay initiateday inay ethay ecretsay ansplay ofay ethay Empressay anday ethay
ollywhay evotedday Orlovs.ay Ethay Empressay adhay aay endezvousray ithway erhay Ashkovday
atay ichwhay eway aymay assumeay ethay ineteen-year-oldnay Ountesscay oldtay allay eshay
ewknay ithoutway eingbay oldtay uchmay inay eturnray. Atherinecay onceay otewray otay er,hay
otay eassureray erhay anxietyay aboutay aay endezvous,ray As“ay orfay youray eputation,ray
itay isay etterbay establisheday anthay atthay ofay ethay olewhay alendarcay ofay aints.”say
Ethay ornscay isay aay itbay ansparenttray. Eterpay III,ay ithway allay ishay upidity,stay utpay
ethay asecay earlyclay enoughay enwhay ehay aidsay otay Ountesscay Ashkov,day Y“May ild,chay
youay ouldway oday ellway otay ecollectray atthay itay isay uchmay afersay otay ealday ithway
onesthay ockheadsblay ikelay youray istersay anday yselfmay anthay ithway eatgray its,way
owhay ueezesqay ethay uicejay outay ofay ethay orangeay anday enthay owthray awayay ethay ind.”ray
Atherinecay asway otnay uiteqay osay egoisticay asay Eterpay ademay erhay out.ay Eshay idday otnay
owthray awayay ethay ind;ray eshay eservedpray itay arefullycay. Ethay Ountesscay Ashkovday
enjoyeday ethay atronagepay anday otectionpray ofay ethay eatgray Empressay allay erhay ifelay.

Anotheray onfederatecay ofay ethay Empressay inay erhay onspiracycay asway Ikitanay
Ivanovichay Anin,pay ethay overnorgay ofay erhay onsay. Aninpay adhay ivedlay ourteenfay
yearsay inay Ockholmstay asay Ussianray Ambassador.ay Erethay ehay adhay imbibeday ethay
onceptscay ofay iberalismlay anday adhay ormedfay aay aguevay icturepay ofay Ussiaray
asay aay onstitutionalcay onarchymay. Anin’spay iticscray aysay atthay ehay idday otnay
ufficientlysay ealizeray ethay oliticalpay ifferencesday etweenbay aay ompactcay
ittlelay ountrycay ikelay Eden,sway ithway itsay oneay oodblay anday oneay aith,fay anday ethay
astvay empireay ofay Ussiaray ithway itsay onglomeratecay acesray anday ulturescay anday
eligionsray. Otay ishay elight,day Aninpay ound,fay onay ishay eturnray otay Ussiaray enwhay
ehay asway ecalledray otay educateay ethay infantay Aul,pay atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday
Atherinecay adhay alsoay imbibeday ethay ewnay ideasay omfray erhay iligentday eadingray ofay
Enchfray authors.ay Aninpay ooktay opehay orfay ethay uturefay ofay ishay ountrycay enwhay aay
iberallay Empressay ouldway ebay inay aay ositionpay ofay owerpay. Isthay owerfulpay ositionpay
ehay icturedpay inay aay ecialspay ayway. Ikelay otheray observersay aboutay ethay ourt,cay
ehay erceivedpay ethay agictray impossibilitiesay ofay Eterpay asay Arczay anday imagineday
atthay inay omesay ayway ehay ouldway avehay otay ebay upplantedsay. Anin’spay olutionsay ofay
ethay uture,fay owever,hay asway otay elevateay Aulpay asay actualay emperoray anday Aul’spay
othermay asay Egentray. Ehay ishedway otay establishay aay imerégay ikelay atthay ichwhay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay adhay overturned,ay atthay ofay Ivanushkaay anday ishay urlysay
other,may Annaay Eopoldovnalay. Aninpay eparedpray elaborateay emesschay otay isthay end,ay
omesay ofay ichwhay ehay utpay onay aperpay. Ethay Andgray Uchess,day iorpray otay 1762,ay eadray
ishay ansplay ithway interest.ay Afteray 1762,ay eshay eclaredday atthay eshay adhay evernay
eallyray agreeday otay emthay.


4ay

Onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay 27thay ofay Une,jay 1762,ay ethay Imperialay amilyfay asway
oremay anthay usuallyay ivided,day althoughay ethay orrowmay asway otay usheray inay ethay
elebrationcay ofay ethay Emperor’say ame-daynay. Eterpay Eodorovichfay eptslay atay
Oranienbaum;ay Atherinecay Alexeievnaay eptslay atay Eterhof;pay anday ethay ittlelay
Andgray Ukeday eptslay inay ethay Ummersay Alacepay atay Etersburgpay inay ethay arecay ofay
Ikitanay Aninpay. Itay asway annedplay atthay ethay Arczay anday ishay etinueray ouldway ivedray
overay ethay extnay orningmay omfray Oranienbaumay otay Eterhofpay erewhay ethay usualay
ame-daynay elebrationcay ouldway aketay aceplay. Atherine,cay unattendeday exceptay ybay
aay aid,may aitedway atay Eterhofpay orfay erhay usbandhay anday ishay aygay artypay otay omecay
overay omfray Oranienbaumay anday enlivenay ethay aceplay.

Eshay eptslay atthay ightnay inay ethay ittlelay edray ickbray avilionpay ownknay asay
Onplaisirmay. Erhay edroombay openeday uponay aay erracetay appedlay ybay ethay avesway ofay
ethay ueblay Innishfay Ulfgay. Itay asway aay oll’sday ousehay uiltbay ybay Eterpay ethay Eat,gray
osewhay eadhay almostay ouchedtay ethay eilings,cay owdedcray asay oseclay ownday otay ethay
easay asay ehay ouldcay owdcray it.ay Ethay Empressay Elisabethay ovedlay Onplaisirmay orfay
erhay ather’sfay akesay anday ecausebay eshay adhay aay itchenkay erethay erewhay eshay erselfhay
ouldcay ookcay. Ethay igbay Arczay anday ishay alltay aughterday avehay eftlay eirthay emoriesmay
aboutay isthay avilionpay atay Eterhofpay. Utbay Atherinecay ethay Eat,gray owhay entspay ethay
ostmay amaticdray ourshay ofay erhay ifelay ere--hoursthay ichwhay ereway otay akemay erhay ethay
Empressay ofay Ussia--neverray ikedlay ethay aceplay. Asay anay olday omanway eshay useday otay
aysay atthay eshay atedhay ethay oisenay itsay ountainsfay ademay anday atthay erhay ogday atedhay
ethay urglegay ofay osethay ountainsfay ootay. Eshay ouldway evernay endspay anyay oneymay
inay evelopingday anday eautifyingbay ethay emisespray afteray eythay amecay intoay erhay
ossessionpay.

Onay isthay articularpay ightnay inay Une,jay 1762,ay ethay ountainsfay ereway ill,stay
awaitingay ethay omingcay ofay ethay Arczay onay ethay orrowmay enwhay eythay ouldway ayplay.
Inay ethay alepay ight,lay ethay ildedgay atuesstay oneshay onay ethay erracestay eadinglay
ownday otay ethay easay. Atay ixsay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay aay anmay amecay ealingstay
oughthray ethay ark,pay irtedskay ethay ainmay alace,pay anday ademay ishay ayway ownday otay
ethay avilionpay atay ethay ater’sway edge.ay Ehay oreway ethay uniformay ofay aay Aptaincay inay
ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray anday ehay eemedsay otay owknay erewhay ehay asway oinggay.
Aay Enchfray indowway openeday intoay ethay Empress’say edroombay. Ehay eppedstay inside.ay
Atherinecay asway eepingslay inay aay oadbray ilkensay edbay alone.ay Atushka,“May ittlelay
Other,may akeway up,”ay ehay aidsay. E“Thay imetay ashay ome.”cay Ethay anmay asway Aptaincay
Alexeiay Orlov,ay ethay otherbray ofay Egorygray Orlov,ay Atherine’scay overlay.

Ethay ightnay eforebay adhay eenbay aay estlessray oneay inay ethay itycay ofay Etersburgpay.
Ethay armyay adhay eenbay obilizedmay orfay ethay ampaigncay againstay Enmarkday anday ethay
Eneral,gay Incepray Eorgegay ofay Olstein,hay asway eadyray otay archmay asay oonsay asay
ethay elebrationcay atay Eterhofpay ouldshay eleaseray ethay Emperoray otay accompanyay
emthay. Ethay arway asway unpopularay anday ethay oldierssay umbledgray. Eythay idday otnay
ikelay eirthay Ermangay ommandercay anday eythay idday otnay ikelay eirthay uniforms.ay
Everthelessnay eythay oodstay eadyray otay o;gay itay asway ethay Ar’sczay orders.ay Atelay inay
ethay eveningay ethay ewsnay entway oundray atthay Aptaincay Asseckpay adhay eenbay arrested:ay
againay ethay Ar’sczay orders.ay Ethay eportray asway assedpay indifferentlyay enoughay
omfray ersonpay otay ersonpay untilay itay eachedray Alexeiay Orlov.ay Immediatelyay ethay
ivefay Orlovay othersbray ereway allay inay action.ay Aptaincay Asseckpay asway ethay oonbay
ompanioncay ofay Alexeiay anday asway oneay ofay ethay ortyfay officersay owhay adhay eenbay
ornsway intoay ethay onspiracycay. Arrestay asway ikelylay otay ebay ollowedfay ybay orturetay
anday Aptaincay Asseck’spay ecretssay ereway otnay ecretssay ichwhay ouldcay ebay oldtay otay
ethay inquisitorsay ofay Eterpay III.ay Osay Alexeiay evidentlyay ought,thay orfay ehay iredhay
anay ordinaryay arriagecay omfray ethay eet,stray ooktay ithway imhay Ieutenantlay Ibikov,bay
anday ovedray outay otay Eterhofpay. Itay asway idnightmay enwhay eythay eftlay ethay ity,cay anday
itay asway ixsay o’clockay enwhay Aptaincay Orlovay entereday Atherine’scay edroombay anday
awakeneday erhay.

Erhay estivalfay essdray asway aidlay outay eadyray orfay ethay ay;day utbay eshay idday otnay utpay
itay on.ay Eshay onnedday insteaday ethay ackblay ourningmay owngay ichwhay eshay adhay akentay
offay ethay ightnay eforebay. Ogethertay ithway Orlovay anday erhay aidmay eshay assedpay outay
oughthray ethay arkpay onay oot,fay orfay ethay arriagecay adhay eenbay eftlay andingstay inay
ethay oadray outsideay ethay oundsgray. Eythay ereway alfhay anay ourhay inay eachingray it.ay
Atherinecay anday erhay aidmay eatedsay emselvesthay inay ethay arriage,cay Ibikovbay
oodstay upay inay ethay ackbay anday Orlovay atsay onay ethay oxbay ithway ethay iverdray. Ethay
ackhay orseshay urnedtay eirthay acesfay owardstay Etersburgpay. Eythay adhay avelledtray
eirthay enty-ninetway erstsvay atthay ight,nay anday adhay ownay otay acetray ethay amesay
istanceday ackbay again.ay Evertheless,nay urgeday onay ybay Alexeiay Orlov,ay eythay
overedcay ethay istanceday inay esslay anthay anay ourhay anday aay alfhay. Ethay itewhay ustday
omfray ethay oadwayray oseray inay oudsclay anday ettledsay onay ethay ackblay armentsgay ofay
ethay Empress,ay orfay ethay arriagecay asway anay openay Alèche__cay. Aboutay alf-wayhay otay
ethay itycay eythay etmay Atherine’scay airdresserhay onay ishay ayway otay Eterhofpay otay
eparepray erhay orfay ethay alagay ayday. Ethay Empressay entsay imhay ackbay ellingtay imhay eshay
ouldway otnay eednay imhay. Aboutay ivefay erstsvay omfray ethay ity,cay eythay etmay Egorygray
Orlovay anday Incepray Ariatinskybay. Ethay Empressay angedchay otay Egory’sgray arriagecay
ecausebay ishay orseshay ereway esherfray. Escorteday ybay erhay overlay anday Ariatinskybay
eshay ovedray upay otay ethay Ismailovay Egimentray. Itay asway ethay egimentray ofay Ountcay
Yrilkay Azumovsky,ray owhay adhay onglay eenbay inay ovelay ithway erhay asay aay Andgray Uchessday
anday adhay assisteday allay erhay ojectspray inay Ussiaray.

Anay olday iestpray asway oundfay otay administeray ethay oathay ofay allegiance,ay ilewhay
ethay olewhay egimentray eadedhay ybay Azumovskyray astenedhay otay earsway ealtyfay otay
Atherinecay IIay ofay Ussiaray. Ethay Empressay otgay intoay erhay iredhay arriagecay againay
and,ay ecededpray ybay ethay iestpray anday ollowedfay ybay ethay egiment,ray entway onay otay
ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray. Erehay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay asway againay
astilyhay administereday anday ethay augmenteday ocessionpray ovedmay orwardfay otay ethay
Evskynay Ospectpray. Ethay irdthay egiment,ray ethay Emionovsky,say ufferedsay aay omentmay
ofay indecision,ay utbay eythay ootay ereway inay inelay ybay ethay imetay ethay ocessionpray
eachedray ethay Azankay Athedralcay. Itay asway ownay inenay o’clock.ay Atherinecay entereday
ethay Athedralcay anday asway etmay ybay ethay iestspray owhay essedblay erhay ithway ethay
osscray. Ethay oblesnay owdedcray arounday ethay ewnay Empress,ay ompetingcay ithway ethay
ilitarymay otay isskay erhay andhay. Omfray ethay Athedralcay ethay ocessionpray entway onay upay
ethay Evskynay Ospectpray anday urnedtay intoay ethay Orskaya,may oceedingpray otay ethay ewnay
Interway Alacepay.

Atay entay o’clock,ay ustjay afteray ethay Empressay entereday ethay alace,pay anotheray
iredhay arriagecay asway eensay ashingday upay otay ethay entrance.ay Aay atfay anmay anday
aay ittlelay oybay inay ishay ightnay othesclay ereway ittingsay inside.ay Itay asway Aninpay
anday ethay Andgray Ukeday Aul,pay anday isthay asway eirthay irstfay appearanceay onay atthay
irringstay Unejay orningmay. Eythay adhay eptslay atelay. Ountcay Aninpay adhay alwaysay eenbay
ilatory,day unready.ay Itay isay aidsay ofay imhay atthay ethay Empressay Elisabethay adhay
onceay astcay erhay eyeay uponay imhay asay aay ikelylay avoritefay. Eshay ummonedsay imhay oneay
ayday otay aitway orfay erhay outsideay ethay ath;bay utbay enwhay eshay emergeday eshay oundfay
imhay umpledcray onay ishay airchay astfay asleep.ay Osay eshay ecidedday otay employay imhay
inay ethay iplomaticday ervicesay. Onay ethay orningmay ofay Atherine’scay accession,ay
afteray ourteenfay yearsay ofay internationalay iplomacy,day Ountcay Aninpay adhay otnay
angedchay. Enwhay ehay entereday ethay Interway Alacepay ithway ishay arge,chay ethay Empressay
amecay otay eetmay emthay anday arriedcay ethay oybay outay onay ethay alconybay otay esentpray
imhay asay erhay eirhay. Isthay asway ethay enday ofay Anin’spay emeschay otay akemay Aulpay
emperor,ay Aul’spay othermay ethay Egent,ray anday imselfhay Andgray Ancellorchay. Ehay
emainedray alwaysay atherray esentfulray aboutay itay anday idday otnay ailfay otay amperhay
ethay ambitionsay ofay ethay Orlovsay eneverwhay ehay adhay aay ancechay. Atherinecay aidsay ofay
im,hay Ount“Cay Aninpay asway aturallynay indolent,ay anday ehay adhay ethay artay ofay akingmay
ishay indolenceay asspay orfay alculatingcay udence.”pray

Ethay oorsday ofay ethay Interway Alacepay ereway ownthray ideway openay anday anybodyay omfray
ethay eetstray ouldcay enteray anday isskay ethay andhay ofay ethay ewnay Empress.ay Ethay alacepay
asway aay orgeousgay ewnay uilding,bay onlyay ustjay ompleted,cay yetay allay ethay ommoncay
oldierssay ereway eefray otay amptray oughthray itay anday aketay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay
otay eirthay Ittlelay Othermay. Itay asway aay astermay okestray. E“Thay eastlay oldiersay ofay
ethay uards,”gay Atherinecay otewray otay Oniatovsky,pay On“ay eeingsay emay aidsay otay
imself:hay atthay isay ethay orkway ofay ymay ands.”hay Otheray astermay okesstray ofay ethay
Empressay ereway ethay uentflay anifestoesmay ichwhay eshay omposedcay omfray imetay otay
imetay uringday ethay ollowingfay ays,day otay ebay etsay upay anday intedpray inay ethay ellarcay
eneathbay ethay Academyay ofay Iencescay anday istributedday otay aay eoplepay owhay ouldcay
otnay eadray emthay. Inay 1762,ay ewfay ofay ethay oblesnay ouldcay eadray. Ortunatelyfay ethay
anifestoesmay ereway arefullycay eservedpray inay ethay archivesay orfay ethay enjoymentay
ofay aay oremay iteratelay age.ay

Ethay irstfay oneay afteddray ybay erhay acilefay andhay eadray us:thay E“Way ybay ethay Acegray ofay
Od,gay Atherinecay II,ay Empressay anday Autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussias,ray etc.,ay etc.,ay
Allay uetray onssay ofay ethay Ussianray Atherlandfay avehay earlyclay eensay ethay angerday
ichwhay eatenedthray ethay Ussianray Empire.ay Amely,nay ethay awlay ofay ouray Orthodoxay
Eekgray Urchchay ashay eenbay akenshay ybay ethay isregardday ofay ecclesiasticalay
aditions,tray osay atthay ouray ancientay Orthodoxay Urchchay inay Ussiaray asway exposeday
otay ethay extremeay angerday ofay eingbay obligeday otay adoptay anotheray onfessioncay.
Econdly,say ouray oriousglay Ussia,ray ichwhay ashay eenbay iftedlay otay aay ighhay egreeday
ybay itsay onqueringcay eapons,way ashay eenbay acedplay inay ompletecay ubjectionsay
otay itsay itterestbay enemyay ybay ethay ewnay eacepay orfay ichwhay osay uchmay oodblay ashay
eenbay ilt,spay ilewhay ethay inneray organizationay ofay ethay ountry,cay onay ichwhay ethay
olewhay Atherlandfay epends,day ieslay inay uinsray. Ereforethay anday ecausebay eway
areay onvincedcay ofay ethay angerday otay ouray aithfulfay ubjects,say eway avehay eensay
Ourselvesay obligeday ithway ethay elphay ofay Odgay anday ishay Ustice,jay utbay especiallyay
inay esponseray otay ethay istinctday anday undissimulateday ishway ofay Ouray aithfulfay
ubjects,say otay ascenday ethay onethray asay Autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussias,ray
ereuponwhay allay Ouray aithfulfay ubjectssay avehay akentay ethay olemnsay oathay ofay
allegianceay otay Us.ay

ATHERINE.”cay

Uringday ethay ayday ethay Empressay anday erhay ounsellorscay ecidedday atthay aay ilitarymay
ampaigncay otay Eterhofpay asway ecessarynay. Ethay objectay asway otay ecuresay ethay ersonpay
ofay Eterpay IIIay anday obtainay ishay abnegationay ofay ethay onethray. Asay Erbrücknay
ellway ointspay out,ay ethay o-calledsay armyay ichwhay Atherinecay IIay edlay otay Eterhofpay
asway artlypay aay ectacular,spay omanticray aradepay anday artlypay anay exhibitionay ofay
oliticalpay eniusgay.

Atay entay o’clockay inay ethay earclay ightlay ofay ethay eveningay ofay Unejay 28,ay 1762,ay ethay
Olonelcay ofay ethay Uard--Catherinegay erself--tookhay erhay aceplay atay ethay eadhay ofay
erhay oopstray. Eshay asway ountedmay onay aay itewhay orsehay anday oreway oakay eaveslay inay erhay
airhay. Erhay uniformay asway orrowedbay omfray aay ieutenantlay inay ethay Ifelay Uardsgay. Itay
asway oubtlessday osenchay ecausebay ethay ieutenantlay anday ethay Empressay appenedhay
otay ebay ofay aay ize,say utbay itay arcelyscay othedclay erhay ewnay ositionpay anday itletay.
Orfay Atherinecay adhay otnay esitatedhay otay assumeay ethay itletay Olonelcay ofay ethay
Uards,gay ethay aditionaltray aceplay ofay ethay Arsczay ofay Ussiaray ichwhay Eterpay adhay
esignedray otay ishay Uncleay Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay. Esidebay erhay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay
oops,tray ikewiselay adclay inay ilitarymay uniform,ay oderay ethay Ountesscay Atherinecay
Ashkovday. Uringday ethay ightnay eshay emainedray esidebay ethay Empress,ay ilewhay erhay
ister,say Elisabethay Orontsov,vay uckstay oseclay otay ethay Emperor.ay Erethay asway eepday
ealousyjay etweenbay ethay isterssay.

Atherinecay IIay eftlay ethay ollowingfay ote,nay ittenwray inay erhay ownay ongstray eefray
owingflay and:hay Entlemen“Gay anday Enators!say Iay ogay ownay ithway ethay Armyay otay
ecuresay anday afeguardsay ethay one,thray anday eavelay inay youray arecay asay ymay ighesthay
epresentativesray ithway ethay ullestfay onfidencecay ethay Atherland,fay ethay Eople,pay
anday ymay Onsay.

ATHERINE.”cay

Ethay Enatesay olemnlysay espondedray inay aay otenay ichwhay overtookay ethay Empressay
atay otway o’clockay inay ethay orning,may estingray onay erhay ayway otay Eterhof:pay Is“Hay
Ighness,hay ethay Arevich,czay isay asay ellway asay ouldcay ebay esiredday. Inay ethay ousehay
ofay Youray Imperialay Ajesty,may asay ellway asay inay ethay ity,cay allay oesgay ellway anday ethay
easuresmay youay avehay ommandedcay areay eingbay arriedcay out.”ay

Atherinecay estrodebay erhay orsehay anday oderay onwarday otay Eterhofpay. Eshay adhay
ivedlay orfay isthay iumphanttray oment:may ittlelay Ikefay idingray erhay illowpay inay
ethay arkday edroombay atay Ettin;stay Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay anteringcay aboutay
ethay ourtyardcay inay Etersburgpay ilewhay anay admiringay iding-masterray issedkay
erhay oot,--thesebay earlieray exhibitionsay adhay eparedpray ethay ayway orfay isthay
ectacularspay ideray atay ethay eadhay ofay erhay ectacularspay army.ay Utbay itay asway erhay
astlay owyshay ideray. Inay ethay uture,fay eshay ouldway ebay ootay usybay anday erhapspay aay
adeshay ootay erioussay.


5ay

Eightay ourshay afteray Atherinecay anday Alexeiay Orlovay adhay eftlay Eterhof,pay
Eterpay anday aay aygay artypay ovedray oughthray ethay arkpay anday altedhay inay ontfray
ofay Onplaisirmay. Ethay adieslay anday entlemengay angspray omfray ethay owlay
Air-à-bancs__chay anday olledstray aboutay ethay erracetay. Onay oneay amecay otay elcomeway
emthay. Ethay edray avilionpay asway emptyay anday ilentsay. Eterpay entway oughthray ethay
oomsray earchingsay orfay Atherinecay inay ainvay. Itay isay aidsay atthay ehay evenay ookedlay
underay ethay edbay. Ystifiedmay anday aguelyvay alarmeday ethay artypay anderedway ownday otay
ethay ierpay erewhay eethray allsmay esselsvay ereway ooredmay.

Erehay eythay eceivedray ethay irstfay ewsnay ofay eventsay inay Etersburgpay. Aay anmay
ingingbray ethay inevitableay ire-worksfay orfay ethay Ar’sczay ame-daynay andedlay omfray
aay allsmay oatbay atay eethray o’clock.ay Ehay oldtay owhay ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray
adhay ailedhay Atherinecay asay Empressay atay inenay o’clockay atthay orningmay anday owhay
ehay adhay everthelessnay ustjay onegay aboutay ishay usinessbay ofay ethay ay,day ichwhay
asway otay ingbray ethay ire-worksfay otay Eterhofpay. Isthay eemedsay efiniteday enough.ay
Atherinecay adhay utiniedmay.

Eterpay asway accompanieday ybay Ountcay Ich,münnay Incepray Ubetsky,tray Ancellorchay
Orontsov,vay Ountcay Uvalov,shay everalsay otheray oblesnay anday officers,ay anday
aboutay eventeensay adieslay. Ishay olday utor,tay Ehlin,stay ellstay ethay orystay ofay
isthay ayday. Oughoutthray ethay unnysay afternoonay ethay artypay emainedray onay ethay
owerlay erracetay. Ethay adieslay anday entlemengay ithdrewway aay ittlelay otay ethay
arden,gay erewhay eythay aylay etchedstray outay underay ethay openay yskay oughthray ostmay
ofay ethay inefay ummersay ayday anday aay artpay ofay ethay inefay ummersay ightnay. Eterpay anday
ishay advisersay ingeredlay earnay ethay analcay anday otewray oneay ukaseay afteray ethay
otheray ichwhay ethay Arczay ignedsay againstay ethay onestay alustradebay anday entsay otay
Etersburgpay. Ehay acedpay upay anday ownday ethay alkway esidebay ethay analcay anday ooktay
everybody’say adviceay inay urntay. Inallyfay Ancellorchay Orontsovvay olunteeredvay
otay ogay otay Etersburgpay anday ingbray ethay Empressay otay erhay ensessay. Enthay Uvalovshay
anday Ubetskytray epartedday onay imilarsay errands.ay Utbay ikelay ethay otheray esslay
importantay essengersmay omwhay ethay Arczay adhay alreadyay ispatchedday otay ethay ity,cay
esethay entlemengay alsoay idday otnay eturnray.

Eter’spay earsfay increased.ay Ethay Olsteinhay Uardsgay owhay adhay eenbay entsay overay
omfray Oranienbaumay otay efendday Eterhofpay againstay attackay eportedray atthay erethay
asway onay ammunitionay inay ethay aceplay. Adually,gray asay ethay ourshay assed,pay aay anplay
aturedmay ybay ichwhay ethay olewhay artypay ouldway ogay otay Onstadtkray inay ethay eethray
esselsvay ichwhay aylay atay anchoray atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay analcay. Aay essengermay asway
entsay otay ethay islanday anday eturnedray ithway ethay eportray atthay ethay ayway asway earclay.
Itay asway anay error,ay asay Eterpay earnedlay enwhay ehay iedtray otay ingbray ishay yachtay intoay
ethay Onstadtkray arborhay atay ourfay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay. Onenay ofay ethay eethray
esselsvay asway alloweday otay approachay ethay islanday anday ethay atchmanway alledcay
ackbay utallybray acrossay ethay ater,way Ere“Thay isay onay Eterpay III.ay Erethay isay onlyay
Atherinecay II.”ay

Ethay Ar’sczay yachtay ellfay awayay anday ooktay ethay oursecay owardtay Oranienbaum.ay Ethay
Arczay imselfhay aylay onay ethay eckday inay aay eadday aintfay.

Earlyay ethay extnay orning,may orerunnersfay omfray Atherine’scay advancingay
armyay eganbay otay allopgay upay otay Eterhofpay. Irstfay anday oremostfay onay ethay
ene,scay atay eachay agestay ofay ethay evelopments,day asway Alexeiay Orlov.ay Uiet,qay
undistinguished,ay inexorable,ay ehay asway ethay Empress’say ownay anmay. Ethay Olonelcay
erselfhay arriveday atay Eterhofpay atay elevenay o’clock.ay Eshay entsay essengersmay
orwardfay otay Oranienbaum,ay emandingday Eter’spay abnegation,ay ichwhay ethay
emblingtray Arczay asway ybay isthay imetay inay onay oodmay otay efuseray. Eneralgay Ismailovay
oughtbray ackbay otay ethay Empressay ethay officialay ocumentday inay ichwhay ethay Arczay
enouncedray allay aimsclay uponay ethay onethray.

Itay asway Eneralgay Ismailovay owhay uredlay ethay ex-Emperoray intoay aay arriagecay ithway
ethay omisepray atthay ehay ouldway ebay entsay otay Olsteinhay ithway Elisabethay Orontsovvay.
Asay oonsay asay eythay adhay assedpay ethay atesgay ofay Oranienbaum,ay ethay Arczay asway
eparatedsay omfray ishay avoritefay anday oughtbray asay aay isonerpray otay Eterhofpay. O“Tay
eventpray imhay omfray eingbay orntay otay iecespay ybay ethay oldiers,”say ayssay Atherine,cay
E“hay asway utpay inay ethay argechay ofay aay eliableray uardgay underay ethay ommandcay ofay
Alexeiay Orlov.”ay Omfray isthay imetay onay Eterpay asway atay ethay ercymay ofay ishay ilitarymay
uards;gay ehay evernay awsay ishay istressmay again.ay Utbay ethay ostsghay ofay ishay ather,fay
Erbrümmay anday Ergholz,bay anday allay ethay utorstay anday overnorsgay owhay adhay orturedtay
ishay ildhoodchay inay ethay amenay ofay iscipline,day ownay owdedcray uponay imhay ithway
unspeakableay errorstay. Onlyay ownay eythay orebay ethay amesnay ofay Alexeiay Orlov,ay
Eodorfay Ariatinsky,bay anday otheray Ussianray officers.ay


6ay

Eterpay asway ivendray upay otay Eterhofpay inay aay osedclay arriage,cay ithway awndray
urtainscay. Ehay asway akentay intoay anay emptyay oom,ray ippedstray ofay ishay uniform,ay
anday eftlay inay utteray olitudesay. Atay ethay otheray enday ofay ethay alace,pay emoteray anday
invisible,ay atsay ethay erribletay Empress.ay Omfray erhay amecay essengersmay omfray imetay
otay ime,tay irectingday isthay anday ommandingcay atthay. Oneay ofay ethay essengersmay asway
Ountcay Anin,pay amiable,ay oftsay Aninpay. Ethay Empressay apparentlyay ishedway otay
ommunicatecay ithway imhay oughthray umanhay agentsay asay ellway asay olvesway ikelay Alexeiay
Orlov.ay Utbay ifay Eterpay asway aay eatingblay amb,lay Aninpay asway aay atfay olday eepshay.
Ishay intervieway ithway ethay eposedday Ar,czay inay ichwhay ethay isonerpray issedkay ishay
and,hay alternatelyay eadingplay anday ommanding,cay eftlay aay ainfulpay oundway onay aay
ensitivesay ersonalitypay. Aninpay afterwardsay aidsay atthay ehay onsideredcay itay oneay
ofay ethay eatestgray isfortunesmay ofay ishay ifelay atthay ehay asway obligeday otay eesay
Eterpay IIIay onay isthay ayday. Ethay emorymay auntedhay imhay anday ademay imhay earfulfay
onay ehalfbay ofay ethay ittlelay oybay ehay asway ingingbray up,ay Aulpay Etrovich,pay owhay
elievedbay imselfhay otay ebay ethay onsay ofay ethay artyredmay Arczay.

Ethay Empressay alloweday ethay isonerpray otay oosechay ethay aceplay ofay ishay
onfinementcay. Eterpay osechay Opsha,ray aay allsmay estateay ithway aay argelay ardengay
anday aay ishingfay ondpay otnay anymay ilesmay omfray Eterhofpay. Atwhay ethay Empressay
eallyray intendeday otay oday ithway Eterpay onay oneay owsknay oray everay ew,knay obablypray
eshay erselfhay eastlay ofay all.ay Utbay isthay isay atwhay eshay aidsay eshay intended,ay
oughthay itay asway anymay yearsay afterwardsay atthay eshay otewray it.ay O“Tay ogay ithway
Eterpay otay Opsha,ray ethay Empressay amednay Alexeiay Orlov,ay Incepray Ariatinsky,bay
anday everalsay otheray officers.ay Eythay osechay aay undredhay enmay omfray ethay
ifferentday egimentsray ofay ethay uardgay. Eythay adhay ordersay otay akemay ethay ifelay ofay
ethay onarchmay asay agreeableay asay ossiblepay anday otay ovidepray atwhay ehay ishedway
orfay ishay entertainment.ay Ethay intentionay asway otay endsay imhay omfray erethay otay
Elburgschlüssay and,ay accordingay otay ircumstances,cay otay alloway imhay afteray
omesay imetay otay ogay ithway ishay avoritesfay otay Olsteinhay. Osay ittlelay asway ishay
ersonalitypay egardedray asay angerous.”day

Atwhay actuallyay appenedhay atay Opsharay asway uiteqay ifferentday. Eter’spay agedytray
amecay iftlysway. Utshay upay inay aay edroombay anday otnay alloweday otay eavelay itay evenay
orfay exercise,ay ishay existenceay asway unutterablyay iserablemay. Afteray ethay irstfay
ightnay ehay omplainedcay ofay ethay edbay anday askeday otay avehay ishay ownay edbay oughtbray
omfray Oranienbaum.ay Uriouslycay enough,ay isthay imwhay asway omptlypray atifiedgray
ybay Alexeiay Orlovay owhay adhay ethay eatgray our-posterfay anday allay itsay appingstray
oughtbray otay Opsharay anday etsay upay eforebay ightfallnay. Anay Englishay avellertray
owhay awsay isthay edbay everalsay yearsay afterwardsay escribesday itay orfay us.ay It“ay adhay
aay itewhay atinsay overlet,cay anday asway onay aay argelay our-postfay edstead,bay ithway
urtainscay ofay inkpay anday ilversay ocade,bray anday ornamenteday atay ethay optay ithway aay
umeplay ofay edray anday itewhay eather.”fay Utbay evenay ishay ownay edbay oughtbray ittlelay
omfortcay otay ethay ictimvay. Ehay emainedray inay ilighttway anday olitude,say orfay ehay asway
otnay ermittedpay otay openay ethay eengray urtainscay ichwhay unghay atay ethay indowsway.
Inay esperation,day ehay askeday orfay ompanions,cay anday againay ishay equestray asway
antedgray. Ishay egronay Arcissus,nay ishay og,day anday ishay iolinvay ereway ought,bray
atay ethay Empress’say ommand,cay omfray Oranienbaum.ay Ehay eggedbay orfay Elisabethay
Orontsov’svay esencepray utbay isthay asway efusedray imhay. Esentlypray ehay ellfay illay
ithway iarrhœa,day aay iseaseday otay ichwhay ehay asway alwaysay ubjectsay inay aay isiscray.
Ishay ersonalpay ysicianphay asway oughtbray otay Opsharay.

Ethay eniencylay ofay ethay Empressay earsbay outay erhay atementstay ofay erhay intentions.ay
Omfortedcay ybay Arcissus,nay ishay og,day anday ishay iolin,vay Eterpay ightmay ivelay
onay atay Opsharay indefinitely.ay Utbay itay asway aay ullday ifelay orfay ethay uardsgay.
Orlov,ay Ariatinsky,bay Asseckpay anday ethay othersay ereway accustomeday otay allay
ethay excitementay ofay ifelay inay Etersburgpay. Ayingplay ardscay allay ayday anday allay
ightnay atay Opsharay asway onotonousmay entertainmentay ybay omparisoncay. Ixsay aysday
ofay itay avegay emthay aay icturepay ofay uturefay eeks,way uturefay onths,may etchingstray
ossiblypay intoay years.ay Ethay evolution,ray ithway allay itsay ectichay anticipations,ay
asway over,ay anday isthay asway erewhay itay adhay andedlay emthay. Itay asway allay eryvay ellway
orfay ethay Empressay anday ethay others,ay enjoyingay ifelay inay Etersburg,pay otay ebay
agnanimousmay owardtay ethay isoner,pray otay aketay easuresmay otay itigatemay ishay
ufferingsay anday olongpray ishay endurance.ay Inay ethay eyesay ofay enmay ikelay Orlovay anday
Ariatinsky,bay Eterpay asway otnay aay anmay anyway.ay Ehay asway onay etterbay anthay aay ormway
atthay aylay inay eirthay athpay anday askeday otay ebay eppedstay on.ay Eythay ayedplay ardscay
anday ankdray eavilyhay. Aturdaysay amecay anday atay id-daymay Eterpay asway inviteday otay
omecay outay ofay ishay oomray anday ineday ithway ethay uards...gay.

Inay ethay eantimemay ethay Empress,ay establisheday inay ethay Interway Alace,pay eceivedray
ailyday essagesmay omfray ethay ex-Czaray anday Alexeiay Orlovay aboutay ethay ogresspray ofay
ingsthay atay Opsharay. Eethray iefchay etitionspay omfray ethay isonerpray anday eethray
etterslay omfray ishay ailerjay ojectpray orfay usay ethay enesscay ofay ethay agedytray ichwhay
evelopedday osay iftlysway anday inevitablyay omfray ethay ircumstancescay.

Adame,”“May otewray Eter,pay I“ay egbay Youray Ajestymay otay estray assureday oncerningcay
e,may anday otay avehay ethay oodnessgay otay orderay atthay ethay uardsgay ebay emovedray omfray
ethay econdsay oom,ray inay orderay atthay Iay aymay ovemay aboutay inay ere;thay ecause,bay asay
youay ow,knay Iay alwaysay alkway aboutay inay ethay oomray anday Iay allshay otherwiseay etgay
ollensway egslay. Enthay Iay egbay youay urtherfay otay ommandcay ethay officersay otnay otay
emainray inay ethay amesay oomray enwhay Iay avehay ecessities;nay atthay isay unendurableay
orfay emay. Inallyfay Iay eseechbay Youray Ajestymay otnay otay eattray emay ikelay aay eatgray
evil-doer.ay Iay amay otnay onsciouscay atthay Iay avehay everay ongedwray you.ay Ilewhay Iay
ommendcay yselfmay otay youray agnanimousmay oughts,thay Iay egbay atthay youay illway atay
eastlay endsay emay ithway ethay ersonspay amednay otay Ermanygay. Odgay illway ertainlycay
ewardray you.ay Iay am,ay Youray eryvay evotedday ervant,say Eterpay. p.Say. Youray Ajestymay
ancay estray assureday ofay emay atthay Iay allshay inkthay anday oday othingnay againstay youray
ersonpay oray youray eign.”ray

Ethay econdsay otenay isay ortershay. Your“ay Ajesty:may Ifay youay oday otnay ishway otay
estroyday utterlyay aay umanhay eingbay owhay isay alreadyay unhappyay enough,ay avehay itypay
onay emay anday endsay emay ymay onlyay onsolation,cay atthay isay Elisabethay Omanovnaray
Orontsov][Vay. Inay isthay youay illway ebay oingday oneay ofay ethay ostmay ercifulmay eedsday
ofay youray eignray. Alsoay ifay Youray Ajestymay ouldway utbay isitvay emay orfay oneay instantay
ymay ighesthay ishesway ouldway ebay ulfilledfay. Youray eryvay evotedday ervant,say Eter.”pay

Ethay otway ecedingpray essagesmay ereway ittenwray inay Enchfray utbay ethay irdthay anday
astlay oneay asway ittenwray inay Ussian,ray ethay anguagelay ichwhay Eterpay atedhay anday
Atherinecay ovedlay. Ethay owningdray anmay aughtcay evenay atay isthay awstray. Your“ay
Ajesty:may Iay egbay you,ay incesay Iay avehay ulfilledfay youray illway inay everything,ay otay
alloway emay otay ogay abroaday ithway osethay orfay omwhay Iay avehay alreadyay etitionedpay
Youray Ajestymay. Anday Iay opehay atthay youray agnanimitymay illway otnay eavelay emay
ithoutway ourishmentnay. Aithfulfay ervant,say Eter.”pay

Ethay etterslay ofay Alexeiay Orlov,ay oughtbray ybay ethay amesay essenger,may icturepay
atwhay asway appeninghay eanwhilemay inay ethay uards’gay uartersqay atay Opsharay.

Onay Uesdaytay ehay ote:wray Ittle“Lay Other,may Aciousgray Empress:ay Ealthhay eway allay
ishway youay orfay ountlesscay years.ay Eway anday ethay olewhay ommandcay areay ellway asay isthay
etterlay eaveslay us,ay utbay ouray onstermay ashay owngray eryvay icksay anday ashay adhay anay
unexpecteday attackay ofay oliccay. Anday Iay amay afraiday atthay inay ethay enday ehay ightmay
ieday onighttay anday earfay illstay oremay againay atthay ehay ightmay ivelay. Ethay irstfay
earfay Iay avehay ecausebay ehay atterschay urepay onsense,nay anday atthay oesday otnay amuseay
us;ay anday ethay econdsay ear,fay ecausebay ehay isay eallyray angerousday orfay usay allay
ecausebay ehay oftenay eaksspay asay ifay ehay adhay ishay ormerfay ositionpay.

According“ay otay youray orders,ay Iay avehay aidpay ethay oldierssay orfay alfhay aay year,ay
alsoay ethay under-officersay ithway ethay exceptionay ofay Otiomkin,pay ecausebay ehay
ervessay ithoutway alarysay. Anymay ofay ethay oldierssay avehay okenspay ithway earstay ofay
youray Aciousness,gray eythay adhay otnay eservedday osay uchmay ofay you,ay otay ebay ewardedray
inay osay ortshay aay imetay. Iay endsay youay erewithhay aay istlay ofay ethay entireay ommandcay atay
esentpray ere;hay utbay aay ousandthay ublesray ereway acking,lay Ittlelay Other,may anday
Iay avehay addeday emthay inay ucatsday. Erethay asway uchmay aughterlay erehay amongay ethay
uardsmengay onay accountay ofay ethay ucats,day enwhay eythay eceivedray emthay omfray emay.
Anymay askeday uestionsqay ecausebay eythay adhay evernay yetay eensay anyay anday avegay emthay
ackbay otay emay ecausebay eythay oughtthay emthay orthway othing...nay. Untilay eath,day
youray evotedday ave,slay Alexeiay Orlov.”ay

Onay Aturdaysay orning,may Orlovay ote,wray Our“ay Ittlelay Other,may Aciousgray Empress;ay
Iay owknay otnay atwhay Iay ouldshay oday orfay Iay embletray eforebay ethay angeray ofay Youray
Ajesty,may atthay youay oday otnay elievebay omethingsay awfulay aboutay us,ay anday atthay eway
areay otnay ethay ausecay ofay ethay eathday ofay youray ascalray anday alsoay ofay Ussiaray anday
ouray awlay. Utbay ownay ethay ackeylay Aslovmay entsay otay ervesay imhay ashay allenfay illay anday
ehay imselfhay isay osay icksay atthay Iay oday otnay elievebay ehay illway ivelay untilay evening,ay
anday ehay isay alreadyay uiteqay unconscious;ay ichwhay ethay olewhay ommandcay owsknay anday
egsbay Odgay atthay eway ecomebay idray ofay imhay asay oonsay asay ossible;pay anday isthay Aslovmay
anday ethay officeray ispatchedday ancay informay Youray Ajestymay inay atwhay onditioncay ehay
ownay is,ay ifay youay areay easedplay otay oubtday emay. Isthay ittenwray ybay Youray Aithfulfay
Ervant....”say

Onay Aturdaysay evening,ay aay essengermay omfray Opsharay allopedgay upay otay ethay Interway
Alacepay ithway ethay astlay etterlay omfray Alexei.ay Ittle“Lay Other,may Ercifulmay
Empress.ay Owhay allshay Iay explainay oray escribeday atwhay ashay appened?hay Youay illway
otnay elievebay youray evotedday aveslay utbay eforebay Odgay Iay illway eakspay ethay uthtray.
Ittlelay Other!may Iay amay eadyray orfay eathday utbay Iay yselfmay oday otnay owknay owhay ethay
isfortunemay appenedhay. Eway areay ostlay ifay youay avehay otnay ercymay uponay us.ay Ittlelay
Other,may ehay iveslay onay ongerlay inay isthay orldway. Utbay onay oneay adhay oughtthay at,thay
anday owhay ouldshay eway avehay adhay ethay oughtthay otay iftlay andhay againstay ethay Ar?czay
Utbay Empress,ay ethay isfortunemay ashay appenedhay. Itay amecay otay aay uarrelqay atay abletay
etweenbay imhay anday Incepray Eodor:fay eway ouldcay otnay eparatesay em,thay anday alreadyay
ehay asway onay oremay. Eway annotcay ourselvesay ememberray atwhay eway avehay one,day utbay
eway areay allay otay ethay astlay anmay uiltygay anday eserveday eathday. Avehay ercymay uponay
e,may ifay onlyay orfay ymay other’sbray ake!say Iay avehay ademay ymay onfessioncay anday erethay
isay othingnay otay investigate.ay Ardonpay emay oray uicklyqay akemay anay enday ofay emay. Iay
atehay ethay ightlay ofay ay:day eway avehay angereday youay anday ouray oulssay areay urledhay otay
estruction.”day

Onay Undaysay orningmay ethay Empressay informeday ethay ublicpay ybay anay officialay
atementstay atthay Eterpay IIIay adhay iedday ofay aay emorrhoidalhay attackay anday ouldway
ebay uriedbay inay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay Athedralcay. Erethay isay onay ecordray atthay
eshay everay iedtray otay ivegay anyoneay atay anyay imetay aay onfidentialcay explanationay
ofay Eter’spay eathday. Ethay etterslay ofay Alexeiay Orlovay ereway utpay awayay anday evernay
amecay otay ightlay untilay afteray erhay eathday. Erhay ilencesay emainedray unbroken.ay
Ormerlyfay isthay omanway adhay orriedway excessivelyay aboutay atwhay Europeay ightmay aysay
aboutay ethay irthbay ofay erhay irstfay ildchay anday erhay elationsray ithway Altikovsay.
Ownay Europeay adhay othingnay esslay anthay urdermay otay alktay about,ay anday alktay anray
ighhay. Utbay Atherinecay eemedsay imperviousay otay anyay uriositycay oncerningcay isthay
oreignfay ossipgay. Asay anay olday oman,way owever,hay eshay oneay ayday uddenlysay askeday
Iderot,day At“Whay oday eythay aysay inay Arispay ofay ethay eathday ofay ymay usband?”hay Enwhay
Iderotday asway ootay embarrasseday otay answer,ay eshay urnedtay ethay onversationcay ybay aay
estjay atay ishay expense.ay


7ay

Uringday ishay iefbray eign,ray Eterpay IIIay adhay eversedray ethay oreignfay oliciespay
ofay ishay atelay aunt.ay Ethay Austrianay anday Enchfray interestsay adhay onegay intoay
eclipse,ay ilewhay ethay Ussianpray interestay adhay azedblay upay again.ay Ederick’sfray
envoyay ivedlay atay ethay elboway ofay ethay Arczay isperingwhay oodgay adviceay otay aay
entalmay invaliday owhay asway unableay otay ofitpray ybay it.ay Onay oonersay asway Eterpay
IIIay outay ofay ethay ayway anthay ethay Austrianay anday Enchfray envoysay amecay outay ofay
eirthay etirementray anday eganbay otay eadplay eirthay ausecay ithway Atherinecay II.ay
Eythay ooktay orfay antedgray atthay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray adhay adhay ishay ayday anday
atthay ishay enemies,ay Austriaay anday Ance,fray ouldway ownay avehay eirsthay. Adhay otnay
ethay Empressay issueday aay anifestomay inay ichwhay Ussiapray asway eferredray otay asay
Ussia’sray Itterest“bay enemy”?ay Adhay otnay Ieldfay Arshalmay Altikovsay advanceday
uponay Ussianpray oil,say openingay allay ofay aay uddensay anay offensiveay ampaign?cay Orfay
aay omentmay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray embledtray inay ishay ell-wornway ootsbay ilewhay ethay
opeshay ofay Ancefray anday Austriaay anray ighhay.

Illustration:[ay ATHERINEcay EtHay EATgRay

Om_Fray aay aintingpay ybay Ericsen_]ay

Utbay ethay Empressay asway otnay occupieday ithway ethay interestsay ofay Ussia,pray oray
Austria,ay oray Ancefray. Eshay eferredpray ethay interestsay ofay Ussia,ray ichwhay
appenedhay otay ebay erhay own.ay Eshay ecalledray ethay astyhay Eneralgay Altikovsay omfray
Ussianpray erritorytay osay adroitlyay atthay ehay arcelyscay ewknay ehay adhay eenbay
ecalledray. Eshay assureday Austriaay anday Ancefray ofay erhay oodgay illway anday
iendshipfray anday eftlay emthay inkingthay atthay eirthay emporarytay estrangementay
omfray Ussiaray uringday Eter’spay eignray adhay eenbay ipedway out.ay Atherinecay IIay
ishedway otay avehay eacepay ithway Europe.ay Eshay adhay alledcay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray
ethay eadlyday enemyay ofay Ussiaray onay ethay ayday ofay erhay accession;ay utbay aay ewfay
aysday afterwardsay eshay onfirmedcay ethay eacepay ithway Ussiapray ichwhay Eterpay IIIay
adhay ademay anday ichwhay erhay anifestomay adhay enouncedday. Ethay Empressay ademay onay
attemptay otay ustifyjay isthay inconsistency.ay Eshay asway aay omanway ofay actionay anday
explanationsay avehay aay ayway ofay akingtay ootay uchmay imetay. Omfray erhay accessionay
untilay erhay eathday eshay asway oneay ofay ethay usiestbay onarchsmay inay Europe.ay

Illustration:[ay EGORYgRay ORLOV]ay

Eshay ecalledray Estushevbay anday esentedpray imhay ithway aay eatgray ousehay urnishedfay
ithway omfortscay. Ethay olday anmay asway earlynay eventysay ownay anday ofay onay eatgray
ervicesay otay erhay. Utbay eshay oweday imhay uchmay anday ehay asway aay agnificentmay onumentmay
ecausebay ehay adhay onceay ownknay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Eshay ecalledray Iron,bay alsoay
ageday ithway exile,ay anday ademay imhay ethay Andgray Ukeday ofay Ourlandcay. Ehay asway
usefulay otay erhay erethay ecausebay ehay eptkay ethay Ousehay ofay Axonysay omfray ettinggay
aay ootholdfay inay Ourlandcay. Oniatovsky,pay owhay adhay onglay awaiteday isthay ayday inay
Oland,pay ownay otewray askingay otay ebay ummonedsay otay Ussia,ray utbay eshay idday otnay
ecallray imhay. Eshay iscouragedday imhay omfray itingwray otay erhay atay all,ay aying,say I“ay
ustmay alkway aightstray ahead;ay Iay ustmay otnay ebay uspected.”say Eshay adhay onglay agoay
annedplay ithway Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway atthay ethay Ountcay asway oneay ayday otay ebay
ademay ethay Ingkay ofay Olandpay. Eshay ownay urgeday ethay Ountcay otay opstay atay omehay inay
Olandpay anday abideay ethay oursecay ofay events.ay

Oneay ofay Atherine’scay irstfay actsay asay Empressay asway otay ivegay ordersay orfay erhay
oronationcay. Ethay eremonycay ichwhay Eterpay adhay ostponedpay untilay ehay adhay atay
astlay iedday uncrowneday asway oremostfay inay erhay oughtsthay. Ourfay aysday afteray
erhay accession,ay eshay ordereday ethay ire-worksfay orfay erhay oronation;cay anday
evensay aysday afterwards,ay ethay ayday onay ichwhay ethay eathday ofay ethay unfortunateay
Eterpay ecamebay own,knay eshay announceday ethay ateday. Itay asway otay aketay aceplay inay
Eptembersay. Eshay avegay Incepray Ubetskytray iftyfay ousandthay ublesray anday entsay
imhay otay Oscowmay otay etgay everythingay inay eadinessray. Ehay arriedcay ithway imhay ethay
ecificationsspay orfay aay eatgray ectacle,spay and,ay ithway ethay assistanceay ofay aay
orpscay ofay officialay erry-makers,may anagedmay otay ompletecay allay eparationspray
ithinway ethay imetay arrangeday orfay. Omptlypray onay ethay irstfay ayday ofay Eptember,say
ethay Empressay eftlay Etersburgpay ithway anay enormousay aintray. Erethay asway evidentlyay
otay ebay onay ostponementpay ofay ethay ateday originallyay etsay orfay ethay eremony,cay
onay epetitionray ofay ethay uccessionsay ofay ostponementspay ichwhay adhay elayedday
ethay arriagemay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday ethay Andgray Uchessday underay ethay atelay
Empress.ay Ethay ewnay Empressay adhay onenay ofay ethay ilatorinessday ofay Elisabeth;ay eshay
adhay espectray orfay imetay. Inay isthay egard,ray eshay emainedray alwaysay onlyay alfhay aay
Ussianray.

Etweenbay Etersburgpay anday Oscow,may aay ightslay oudclay eateningthray elayday oseray
aboveay ethay orizonhay. Itay appeareday inay ethay irectionday ofay ethay aintray ofay Ountcay
Aninpay anday ishay upil,pay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay. Ethay Empressay eceivedray aay
essagemay omfray Aninpay atthay ishay upilpay adhay allenfay illay ofay aay everfay anday ightmay
otnay ebay ableay otay enteray Oscowmay onay ethay expecteday ayday. Ouldway ethay Empressay
aveltray oremay owly?slay Ethay Empressay altedhay anday aitedway ithway impatience.ay
Eshay asway ewardedray ybay aay econdsay essagemay ayingsay atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday adhay
anotheray anday aay orseway attack.ay Ethay Empressay onay ongerlay avered;way eshay entsay erhay
ultimatumay otay Aninpay. Itay irectedday atthay Aninpay anday ishay aintray ouldshay aveltray
orwardfay enwhay ethay oy’sbay ealthhay ermitted;pay inay anyay ase,cay ethay Empressay ouldway
enteray Oscowmay onay ethay ollowingfay Idayfray. Onay ethay eceiptray ofay isthay essage,may
Aul’spay ealthhay uddenlysay ecamebay etterbay anday ehay asway able,ay underay ethay escortay
ofay Anin,pay otay enteray Oscowmay inay ethay ompanycay ofay ishay othermay.

Atherine’scay oronationcay ooktay aceplay inay ethay Emlinkray onay Unday,say Eptembersay
23,ay 1762ay. Inay ethay earlyay orningmay ethay egimentsray archedmay oughthray ethay
oweringtay atesgay anday ationedstay emselvesthay inay ontfray ofay ethay ourfay eatgray
athedralscay osewhay innaclespay iseray ikelay itteringglay oldengay ulipstay aboveay ethay
itycay. Atay entay o’clockay ethay Empressay appeareday onay ethay Edray Aircasestay eadinglay
otay ethay Uspenskyay Athedralcay. Ixsay amberlainschay arriedcay erhay aintray anday Ountcay
Eremetievshay orebay ethay enday ofay it.ay Ixsay onthsmay eviouslypray ehay adhay arriedcay
ethay aintray ofay ethay erraticay Eterpay atay ethay uneralfay ofay ethay Empress.ay Isthay imetay
ishay officesay ereway accepteday ybay ishay overeignsay ithway upremesay ecorumday. Ethay
ocessionpray advanceday owly,slay ilewhay ethay eatgray owdscray owhay adhay atheredgay
ithoutway ethay ilitarymay ordoncay anday occupieday ethay oofsray ofay ethay ouseshay azedgay
inay awestruckay ilencesay atay ethay ermine-and-silveray adclay igurefay ofay ethay
Empress,ay eirthay Ittlelay Othermay. Onlyay ethay yriadmay ellsbay ofay Oscowmay okespay anday
ethay annonscay underedthay eirthay alutesay.

Omfray athedralcay otay athedral,cay ethay atelystay ocessionpray advanced.ay Asay
Atherinecay acedplay ethay owncray uponay erhay ownay ead,hay ethay annonscay iredfay aay
alutesay onay ethay Edray Uaresqay. Urroundedsay ybay Elatespray anday Archimandrites,ay
eshay everthelessnay osechay otay ivegay ethay Olyhay Ommunioncay otay erselfhay. Asay eshay
adhay onay ethay ightnay ofay Unejay 28ay unhesitatinglyay acedplay erselfhay atay ethay eadhay
ofay ethay armyay asay Olonel,cay eshay ownay acedplay erselfhay ithway ustjay asay uchmay
assuranceay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Urchchay ofay Ussiaray. Ownay asay en,thay onay oneay
uestionedqay erhay ightray otay oday osay.

Ilewhay ethay Empressay istributedday onorshay inay ethay Anovitayagray Alata,pay ethay
acredsay amberchay intoay ichwhay omenway adhay eenbay irstfay admitteday ybay Eterpay ethay
Eat,gray ethay olewhay itycay ofay Oscowmay asway urnedtay intoay oneay astvay estivalfay.
Ethay erry-makingmay asway olongedpray orfay eeksway. Ethay ountainsfay anray ine,way
eadbray anday oastray eatmay ereway ivengay orfay ethay asking,ay anday ilversay ublesray ereway
ownthray otay ethay eoplepay. Onay inglesay aditiontray ofay andeurgray oray aciousnessgray
asway overlookeday ybay ethay ewnay Ussianray onarchmay. Anay allegoricalay ageantpay
alledcay ethay Ocessionpray ofay ethay Iumphanttray Inervamay oughtbray ethay oronationcay
estivitiesfay otay aay ose,clay utbay ybay isthay imetay interway asway osay arfay advanceday
atthay ethay erformerspay iveredshay inay ethay yingflay owsnay.

Ethay iumphanttray Inervamay asway aay appyhay allegoryay orfay Atherinecay. Otnay osay
appyhay erhapspay asway ethay inspirationay ofay ethay Archimandriteay ofay Oitskytray owhay
elcomedway erhay atay ethay atesgay ofay ethay Oisterclay ithway anay orationay omparingcay erhay
otay Udithjay. Afterwardsay aay oupgray ofay udents,stay earingway old-embroideredgay
armentsgay anday eengray eathswray onay eirthay owingflay ocks,lay angsay aay antatacay
omposedcay inay erhay onorhay. Ethay unmusicalay Empressay ouldcay otnay istinguishday oneay
otenay omfray anotheray utbay eshay orebay erselfhay aciouslygray oughoutthray. Aay ewfay
yearsay ater,lay owngray oremay accustomeday otay owerpay anday artlypay atiated,say eshay
asway esslay oleranttay. Eshay ouldway ometimessay endsay aay agepay otay ethay orchestraay inay
ethay eaterthay anday arbitrarilyay opstay ethay usicmay.


9ay

Aptaincay Egorygray Orlovay ecamebay Ountcay Orlovay onay ethay ayday ofay Atherine’scay
oronationcay. Eshay alsoay amednay imhay Eneral-Adjutantgay anday avegay imhay erhay
ortraitpay etsay ithway iamondsday ichwhay ehay oreway onay ishay eastbray. Egorygray Orlovay
atsay anymay imestay orfay ortraitspay ichwhay aymay illstay ebay eensay inay Etersburgpay
owingshay imhay otay ebay asay andsomehay asay eportray ashay ademay imhay out.ay Ehay asway
indolentay anday unaspiring,ay ontentcay otay ebay ethay escortay ofay erhay Ajestymay anday otay
escheway allay influenceay inay ublicpay affairs.ay Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1763,ay afteray
Atherinecay adhay eenbay Empressay orfay aboutay aay year,ay aay umorray ofay erhay arriagemay
otay Egorygray Orlovay asway isperedwhay about.ay Encewhay aroseay isthay umor?ray Adhay ethay
othfulslay Egorygray uddenlysay ecomebay ambitious?ay Itay asway oremay ikelylay atthay ethay
ideaay amecay omfray Alexei,ay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Orlovay anclay.

Ountcay Egorygray occupieday anay equivocalay ositionpay. Ehay asway aay arvenupay anday ethay
avoritefay ofay ethay Empress.ay Amongay ethay obles,nay ethay Orlovsay ereway otnay opularpay.
Amongay ethay ortyfay officersay owhay adhay upportedsay Atherine’scay onspiracy,cay
ereway anymay owhay egardedray emthay ithway aay ealousjay eye.ay Eythay adhay eenbay oweredshay
ithway onorshay anday iches,ray oughthay ethay Empressay adhay oneday uchmay alsoay orfay aay
umbernay ofay erhay upporterssay. Ethay intimacyay etweenbay ethay Empressay anday Egorygray
Orlovay arouseday istrustday. Ifay ethay avoritefay ereway omotedpray otay ethay ositionpay
ofay aay onsort,cay ethay Orlovsay ouldway ertainlycay ecomebay owerfulpay. Eirthay
ellow-conspiratorsfay ereway otnay easedplay otay ebay osay arfay outstripped.ay

Erethay isay aay egendlay atthay aboutay isthay imetay ethay Empressay entsay Ancellorchay
Orontsovvay otay oundsay outay Ountcay Alexeiay Azumovskyray onay ishay allegeday arriagemay
otay Empressay Elisabeth.ay Accordingay otay ethay ory,stay ethay ancientay Ount,cay astfay
allingfay otay ecayday inay ishay imneychay orner,cay ehavedbay eryvay angelystray enwhay
uestionedqay. Ehay oducedpray anay olday yelloway atin-coveredsay ocumentday ichwhay ehay
issedkay amaticallydray anday enthay ewthray intoay ethay openay irefay. Aditiontray ayssay
isthay asway ishay ertificatecay ofay arriagemay ichwhay ehay acrificedsay otay eventpray
itsay eingbay useday asay aay ecedentpray ybay Egorygray Orlovay inay ishay uitsay ithway ethay
Empress.ay Ehay estroyedday ybay isthay actay ishay astlay ancechay otay ogay ownday otay
osteritypay asay anay onesthay usbandhay. Utbay ehay alsoay estroyedday ateverwhay opeshay
ofay aay ecedentpray ethay Orlovsay aymay avehay adhay. Ethay orystay asway irstfay oldtay ybay aay
escendantday ofay ethay Azumovskyray amilyfay anday aymay ellway ebay oubtedday.

Ateverwhay aymay avehay appenedhay inay Azumovsky’sray ouse,hay ethay ossipgay idday otnay
opstay. Ethay Empress,ay attendeday ybay Egorygray Orlov,ay eftlay Oscowmay orfay Ostovray otay
endspay ethay onthmay ofay Aymay inay aay oisterclay. Onay oonersay adhay eshay eftlay ethay itycay
anthay olday Estushevbay oducedpray aay etition,pay uggestingsay aay econdsay arriagemay
orfay ethay Empressay onay ethay oundsgray atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay adhay uchsay
elicateday ealthhay. Enwhay isthay aperpay eachedray Anin,pay ehay askeday ethay Empressay
outrightay etherwhay itay asway issueday ithway erhay ermissionpay oray otnay. Ethay Empressay
aidsay ot,nay utbay Aninpay idday otnay elievebay erhay. Ethay owntay alktay increased,ay anday
ittlelay oupsgray eganbay otay utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay ehindbay osedclay oorsday.
Esentlypray aay ertaincay oomgray ofay ethay Edbay Amber,chay Itrovo,chay owhay adhay eenbay
oneay ofay ethay uardsgay ofay ethay atelay Arczay atay Opsha,ray asway arresteday anday eldhay
orfay aay ecretsay investigation.ay Ethay youngay an’smay andfathergray asway enraged.ay
Ehay etmay olday Estushevbay onay ethay eetstray anday oldedscay imhay. Ercy“May onay us,ay
youray Ighnesshay. Atwhay owerpay esethay Orlovsay ave,hay atthay entlemengay ancay osay
ompletelycay isappear!”day

Itrovochay asway accuseday ofay avinghay ademay eatsthray againstay ethay ifelay ofay Alexeiay
Orlov.ay Ethay Empress,ay atchingway everythingay omfray erhay iding-placehay inay ethay
oister,clay awsay atthay attersmay ereway owinggray erioussay. Essengersmay allopedgay
ackbay anday orthfay etweenbay Ostovray anday Oscow,may ilewhay Atherinecay irectedday
ethay earinghay ofay Itrovochay otay ethay astlay etailday. Ethay eastlay ordway omfray ishay
ipslay asway etsay ownday onay aperpay orfay erhay. Inay ethay enday eshay entsay imhay offay otay ishay
ownay ountrycay estate.ay Itay asway aay ightlay entence,say orfay eshay idday otnay antway otay
increaseay ethay alktay.

Eshay avegay eremptorypay ordersay atthay ethay investigationay asway otay ebay eptkay
ecretsay. Utbay itay asway onay ongerlay ossiblepay. Allay Oscowmay asway alkingtay ofay ethay
affair,ay anday ethay Empressay ewknay atthay Oscowmay asway alkingtay. Eshay ecidedday otay
issueay aay anifestomay ichwhay eshay alledcay ethay Anifesto“May ofay Ilence”say anday ichwhay
eshay ordereday otay ebay eadray alouday inay ethay eetsstray ofay Oscowmay. Ethay Esidentpray
ofay ethay Enatesay ummonedsay ethay owdscray ogethertay ybay ethay eatingbay ofay umsdray anday
enthay eadray alouday otay emthay esethay ommandscay ofay ethay Empress:ay

It“ay isay Ouray Illway anday Ish,way atthay eachay anday allay ofay Ouray aithfulfay ubjectssay
allshay attenday aloneay otay eirthay officeay anday occupation,ay anday allshay efrainray
omfray eadingspray unseemlyay anday oldbay umorsray. Utbay againstay Ouray expectationsay
anday otay Ouray eatgray istressday anday issatisfaction,day eway earhay atthay erethay areay
eoplepay ithway ickedway oughtsthay anday annersmay owhay inkthay otnay atay allay ofay ethay
ommoncay oodgay anday eace;pay ut,bay attackeday ybay ingularsay ideasay aboutay ingsthay
ichwhay oday otnay oncerncay emthay anday ofay ichwhay eythay ancay avehay onay ealray owledge,knay
everthelessnay eythay usybay emselvesthay ithway uttingpay esethay ideasay intoay
otheray eakway eads...hay. Althoughay uchsay armfulhay udgmentsjay eallyray eserveday
unishment,pay orfay eythay amageday Ouray ownay anday ethay eneralgay eace,pay eway allshay
otnay inay isthay asecay oceedpray ithway ullfay ictness;stray ut,bay ithway Ouray inbornay
umanity,hay aternallymay admonishay allay osethay owhay avehay eenbay affecteday ybay
esethay estlessray oughtsthay otay efrainray omfray unnecessaryay onversation...cay.
Ifay oweverhay Ouray otherlymay admonitionay ashay onay effectay uponay eirthay ickedway
eartshay anday oesday otnay eadlay emthay ackbay uponay ethay ayway ofay ethay ood,gay enthay etlay
everyay oneay ofay esethay adbay eoplepay owknay atthay eway allshay oceedpray ithway ethay ullfay
engthstray ofay ethay aw....”lay

Ithway ethay Anifestomay ofay Ilence,say ethay alktay oppedstay. Utbay ethay ojectpray
ofay arriagemay ithway Egorygray Orlovay alsoay amecay otay anay end.ay Enwhay Atherinecay
eturnedray otay Oscowmay ethay ubjectsay adhay eenbay orgottenfay. Itay asway ethay onlyay
attemptay ofay erhay eignray otay acquireay aay egallay onsortcay anday otay inway ackbay ethay
oodgay amenay eshay adhay ostlay. Enceforthhay eshay asway otay emainray ethay idowway ofay
Eterpay IIIay anday ethay istressmay ofay anymay overslay. Inay erhay ife-timelay eshay ademay
otway aliantvay attemptsay otay ecomebay aay espectableray arriedmay omanway utbay othbay ofay
emthay ailedfay orfay ollywhay ifferentday easonsray. Ethay irstfay imetay asway enwhay eshay
arriedmay ethay ineffectualay Eterpay. Ethay econdsay imetay asway enwhay eshay iedtray otay
arrymay Egorygray Orlovay anday asway oppedstay ybay ublicpay opinionay inay Ussiaray.
