IXay

ATHERINEcay EtHay EATgRay


Inay 1762,ay Etersburgpay asway illstay aay oodenway itycay. Ethay ourtcay itselfay adhay onlyay
ustjay emovedray omfray ethay aftydray oodenway alacepay onay ethay Evskynay otay ethay eatgray
onestay alacepay onay ethay Evanay. Ethay ouseshay ereway implesay oray ultiplemay ucturesstray
ofay uaredsqay ogslay ofay ethay ypetay illstay eensay inay Ussianray illagesvay. Ellarscay anday
asementsbay ereway unknown.ay Otay ethay ubstantialsay Ermangay indmay ofay ethay Empress,ay
ethay uperficialsay andeurgray ofay erhay apitalcay asway anay objectay ofay ecretsay
erisionday. Eifenheim’s“Gray ouse,”hay inay ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay orn,bay adhay eenbay
etterbay uiltbay. Eshay otewray aay ersevay aboutay ethay ousehay atthay Ackjay uiltbay ithoutway
anyay airwaystay ecausebay ethay airwaystay adhay eenbay orgottenfay.

Ethay ompositioncay illustratesay atwhay ethay Empressay oftenay aidsay ofay erself,hay
anday eryvay uly,tray atthay eshay asway onay oetpay. Utbay itay eryvay ellway expressesay atwhay
eshay oughtthay ofay Ussianray uildingbay inay erhay imetay. Eshay alledcay erhay oggerelday aay
Anson__Chay.

Ean“Jay itbâtay uneay aison,may
Uiqay an’ay inay imeray inay aison:ray
Iverl’hay onay yay ejèlay outtay oide,ray
l’étéay enay alay endray ointpay oide;fray
Ilay yay oubliaay escalier,l’ay
Uispay elay itbâtay enay espalier.”ay

Enwhay aay irefay okebray outay inay ethay ity,cay itay asway aay oriousglay ectaclespay. Uringday
ethay irstfay interway ofay erhay eign,ray ethay Empressay atchedway omfray erhay indowway
otway undredhay anday ortyfay oodenway ouseshay oinggay upay inay amesflay. Asay ethay arksspay
ascendeday omfray ethay oaringray ogslay againstay ethay acknessblay ofay ethay interway
y,skay eshay atchedway ethay isasterday ithway ixedmay eelings,fay orfay eshay yearneday
otay ebuildray atthay uarterqay ofay ethay itycay anyhow.ay Ithinway eethray yearsay itay
asway actuallyay ebuiltray ofay ickbray. Everalsay eatgray iresfay evastatedday ethay
itycay uringday ethay earlyay artpay ofay erhay eignray anday ethay Empressay estoredray ethay
avagedray ectionssay ithway ickbray anday uccostay ashedway inkpay anday eengray ybay Italianay
architects.ay Irstfay aisedray ybay Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday evelopedday ybay Atherinecay
ethay Eat,gray Etersburgpay asway anday emainsray orfay allay imetay aay ollywhay un-Russianay
ity,cay aay ittingfay onumentmay otay esethay otway ulersray owhay oinedjay Europeay anday
Ussiaray ogethertay.

Oughthay Atherinecay ethay Econdsay idedpray erselfhay onay eingbay aay Ussianray eshay
erishedchay aay ivatepray ornscay orfay uchmay atthay asway eciouspray otay ethay Ussiansray.
Erhay onesthay opinionay ofay Oscow,may etsay ownday inay erhay ournal,jay owsshay isthay.
At“ay atthay imetay [1750],ay evenay oremay anthay ow,nay itay asway inay eneralgay eryvay
ardhay orfay ethay obilitynay otay eavelay Oscow,may ethay itycay ichwhay eythay allay osay
oved,lay erewhay azinesslay anday indolenceay areay eirthay iefchay occupation.ay Eythay
ouldway adlyglay endspay eirthay olewhay iveslay ere,thay ivingdray aboutay inay aay ichlyray
ildedgay arriagecay ehindbay ixsay ansspay ofay orses,hay aay ymbolsay ofay ethay alsefay
ideaay ofay uxurylay ichwhay eignsray erethay anday oncealscay omfray ethay eyesay ofay ethay
assesmay ethay ovenlinessslay ofay ethay aster,may ethay ompletecay isorganizationday
ofay ishay ouseholdhay anday ishay annermay ofay ifelay. Itay isay onay arityray otay eesay aay
endidlysplay ownedgay adylay inay aay onderfulway arriagecay ithway ixsay eanlay anday
abbilyshay arnessedhay orseshay ivedray outay omfray aay eatgray ourtyardcay eapedhay ithway
irtday anday ashtray. Erhay unkemptay ackeyslay inay ettypray iverylay isgraceday erhay ybay
eirthay oorishbay ehaviorbay. Enerallygay eaking,spay othbay enmay anday omenway owgray
oftsay inay isthay eatgray ity:cay eythay eesay anday acticepray onlyay etchedness,wray
ichwhay eaveslay ethay ostmay undoubteday eniusgay otay erishpay anday ecayday. Ecausebay
eythay ollowfay eirthay umorshay anday eirthay ims,whay eythay evadeay allay awslay anday
executeay emthay adlybay. Ethay onsequencecay isay atthay eythay evernay earnlay otay
ommandcay atay allay oray atthay eythay ecomebay yrants...tay. Esidesbay isthay erethay
asway evernay aay eoplepay owhay adhay oremay objectsay ofay anaticismfay eforebay eirthay
eyes,ay uchsay asay onder-workingway aintssay atay everyay ep;stay urches,chay arsons,pay
oisters,clay ayingpray others,bray ascals,ray ieves,thay uselessay ervantssay inay
eirthay ouses--andhay uchsay ouses!hay Atwhay irtday inay osethay ouses,hay ichwhay occupyay
olewhay ieldsfay anday avehay udholesmay orfay ourtyardscay. Inay eneralgay everyay ersonpay
ofay ashionfay inay ethay itycay occupiesay otnay aay ousehay utbay aay allsmay arm.”fay Ethay
Empressay omplainedcay atthay ifay eshay entsay orfay aay ersonpay inay Oscow,may eshay adhay otay
aitway untilay ethay extnay ayday orfay erhay answer.ay Ethay Uscovitesmay adhay imetay. Ethay
Uscovitesmay ereway Ussiansray.

Althoughay Atherinecay asway eefray inay erhay iticismcray ofay ethay Oscowmay obles,nay erhay
ownay ourtcay atay Etersburgpay asway ustjay asay extravagantay anday ostentatiousay oughthay
ossiblypay oremay orderlyay anday eanlyclay ithalway. Othbay entlemengay anday adieslay
oreway ewelsjay anday iamondsday. Egorygray Orlov,ay atay ethay eighthay ofay ishay ortunes,fay
adhay aay uitsay ofay othesclay ichwhay ostcay aay illionmay ublesray anday ichwhay asway ewedsay
allay overay ithway iamondsday. Orlov’say extravaganceay asway ildmay omparedcay ithway
atthay ofay ishay uccessor,say Otiomkin,pay owhay asway earlyclay obligeday otay outshineay
ethay achievementsay ofay ishay edecessorpray. Istorianshay avehay estimateday atwhay
ethay Empressay entspay onay ethay othesclay anday upkeepay ofay erhay everalsay avoritesfay
anday owhay uchmay eshay urnedtay overay otay emthay inay ethay ormfay ofay estatesay anday
otheray aluablevay oodsgay anday avehay oundfay ethay otaltay ockingshay. Inay isthay eshay
eemssay otay avehay utbay ontinuedcay ethay aditiontray ofay Elisabethay owhay avegay ethay
Anitchkovay Alacepay otay Azumovskyray anday aay andfulhay ofay ationalnay onopoliesmay
otay ethay Uvalovsshay. Allay ethay oblesnay aboutay ethay ourtcay adhay inheriteday avishlay
andardsstay omfray Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday ethay avoritesfay ofay ethay Empressay ouldcay
otnay ossiblypay ebay outshoneay ybay Eremetievshay anday Oganovstray owhay ereway ountscay
anday ichray enmay ybay inheritance.ay Atherine’scay avoritesfay ereway arvenus;pay eythay
oweday everyay opeckcay otay erhay. Eshay alwaysay awsay otay atthay. Ethay Empressay erselfhay
asway aay arvenu;pay utbay ethay oblesnay ofay Oscowmay ereway otnay. Inay ethay alacespay erethay
ithway eirthay irymay ourtyardscay eltdway ethay ancientay oodblay ofay Ussiaray. Ilewhay ethay
Empressay iticizedcray eirthay irtday anday ostentation,ay eshay ewknay atthay omfray ethay
ointpay ofay iewvay ofay Oscowmay eshay erselfhay asway aay arvenupay anday erhay avoritesfay
ereway utbay eaturescray ofay yesterday.ay


2ay

Upay otay ethay imetay ofay Atherinecay ethay Econd,say ethay Arsczay ofay Ussiaray adhay eenbay
addresseday ybay ethay Europeanay ourtscay asay Your“ay Ajesty.”may Asay oonsay asay ethay
Empressay asway ownedcray atay Oscow,may eshay otifiednay ethay overeignssay ofay Europeay
atthay eshay expecteday inay ethay uturefay otay ebay addresseday asay Your“ay Imperialay
Ajesty.”may Erhay equestray asway antedgray exceptay inay Ance,fray ichwhay adhay ethay
onsciousnesscay ofay eingbay ethay ostmay ivilizedcay ountrycay inay ethay orldway anday asway
oundbay otay egardray Ussiaray asay aay avagesay interloper.ay Ancefray ouldway adlyglay
avehay ushedpay ethay ig,bay unwieldy,ay irtyday aoschay ownknay asay Ussiaray ackbay intoay
ethay armsay ofay Asia.ay Ethay Enchfray aintainedmay atthay Ar”“Czay idday otnay eanmay ethay
amesay asay Emperor”“ay atay all.ay Utbay Atherinecay aidsay ethay otway itlestay ereway
exactlyay ethay ame,say anday insisteday atthay Is“Hay Ostmay Istianchray Ajesty”may ofay
Ancefray ouldshay alwaysay addressay erhay asay Er“Hay Imperialay Ajesty”may ofay Ussiaray.
Atay astlay ethay Enchfray inister,may Oiseul,chay agreed.ay Enthay ehay entsay officialay
ommunicationscay otay Ussiaray inay ichwhay ethay ordway Imperial”“ay idday otnay appear.ay
Atherinecay efusedray otay eadray emthay oray otay ecognizeray anay envoyay owhay arriedcay
aperspay addresseday erelymay otay Er“Hay Ajesty.”may Ushedpay intoay aay orner,cay
Oiseulchay inallyfay eclaredday atthay Imperial“ay Ajesty”may asway impureay Ench,fray aay
orruptioncay ofay ethay acredsay anguagelay ichwhay ethay Enchfray Academyay existeday otay
otectpray. Ethay argumentay etweenbay Ersaillesvay anday Etersburgpay unspay itselfay outay
orfay years.ay

Ikelay aay oodgay anday aithfulfay ife,way Adamemay eday Oiseulchay oinedjay inay ethay uarrelqay
anday entway aboutay allingcay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray aay Onster.”“may Itay asway
isthay adylay owhay ovokedpray omfray Oltairevay ishay amousfay ordsway inay efenseday ofay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. I“ay aymay oastbay otay youay atthay Iay andstay atherray inay ethay
oodgay acesgray ofay ethay Empress;ay Iay amay erhay ightknay owardtay anday againstay all.ay
Iay owknay ellway atthay eshay isay eproachedray orfay everalsay iflestray owardstay erhay
usbandhay. Osethay areay amilyfay attersmay inay ichwhay Iay oday otnay ixmay. Oreovermay itay
isay alsoay ellway ifay oneay ashay aay ongwray otay akemay oodgay. Enthay itay ecomesbay one’say
irstfay interestay otay akemay eatgray effortsay otay inway orfay oneselfay ethay espectray anday
admirationay ofay ethay ublicpay. Ertainlycay erhay eadfuldray usbandhay ouldway otnay avehay
accomplisheday oneay ofay ethay ingsthay ichwhay ymay Atherinecay accomplishesay everyay
ay.”day

Atherinecay ethay Econdsay asway erhay ownay oreignfay inistermay. Ethay enmay omwhay eshay
acedplay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Ollegecay ofay Oreignfay Affairsay ereway ollowersfay
otnay eaderslay. Enwhay eshay ascendeday ethay one,thray eshay ewknay oremay aboutay ethay
internationalay elationsray ofay Europeay anthay eshay idday aboutay ethay internalay
affairsay ofay Ussiaray. Eshay asway otay earnlay aboutay Ussiaray afteray eshay ecamebay itsay
Empress.ay Inay 1762,ay ethay alignmentay ofay ethay Europeanay ationsnay adhay eenbay
ownthray intoay ighhay eliefray ybay ethay arlikeway activitiesay ofay Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray. Internationalay oblemspray ereway erfectlypay amiliarfay otay erhay. Erhay
opinionay asway ormedfay anday eshay asway eadyray otay aketay action.ay Atherinecay adhay
eenbay inspireday ybay Achiavelli’smay Ince,”“Pray ichwhay eshay adhay eadray uringday ethay
Oniatovskypay eriodpay enwhay eshay adhay intriguesay orfay owerpay ithway Irsay Arleschay
Anburyhay Illiamsway orfay anay ally.ay

Inay ishay onumentalmay orkway onay Atherinecay ethay Eat,gray Ilbassovbay evotesday aay
apterchay otay aay etailedday accountay ofay ethay eadingray ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday
uringday ethay yearsay ofay erhay irtualvay imprisonmentay ybay ethay Empressay Elisabeth,ay
anday emphasizesay ethay influenceay ichwhay erhay avoritefay authorsay adhay onay erhay
ubsequentsay areercay asay Empress.ay Ilbassovbay oundfay onay erhay abletay Oltaire,vay
Ontesquieu,may Acitus,tay Oyle;bay inay ort,shay aay ollectioncay ofay eefray inkersthay
owhay ightmay ebay expecteday otay ormfay ethay indmay ofay aay uturefay iberallay onarchmay.
Atherinecay eadray allay ofay ese,thay utbay eshay alsoay eadray Achiavelli,may osewhay amenay
isay otnay entionedmay ybay Ilbassovbay inay ishay arefullycay eparedpray apterchay onay erhay
eadingray. Inay oneay ofay erhay etterslay otay Evalierchay Illiams,way eshay uotesqay aay
aximmay ofay Achiavellimay otay ethay effectay atthay aay anmay isay arelyray asay ickedway asay ehay
oughtay otay ebay. Illiamsway asway aay ittlelay ockedshay apparently,ay orfay ehay eplied,ray
At“Whay Iay aysay is,ay ankthay Od,gay ethay ickedway arelyray avehay ethay ouragecay ichwhay
eythay oughtay otay avehay otay executeay eirthay ickedness.”way Otay ichwhay Atherinecay
epliedray oolly,cay O“Say uchmay ethay etter,bay ifay elay onbay Ieuday ashay urtailedcay ethay
ouragecay ofay ethay ickedway orfay ethay executionay ofay eirthay ickedness.”way

Ethay oreignfay olicypay ofay isthay Empressay asway uniformlyay aggressive.ay Inay erhay
omesticday olicies,pay erhay intentionsay ereway atay eastlay iberal,lay utbay allay erhay
ealingsday ithway oreignfay ationsnay ereway astuteay anday edatorypray. Ethay ailtray
ofay Achiavellimay asway overay all.ay Eshay orkedway orfay ethay expansionay ofay Ussiaray
anday oastedbay asay anay olday omanway ofay ethay umbernay ofay uaresqay ilesmay ichwhay
eshay adhay addeday otay erhay erritorytay. Ussiaray asway aay arvenupay anday eshay asway aay
arvenu;pay eirthay ausecay asway one.ay Europeay ouldshay ebay astonished,ay anday itay asway
astonished.ay Itay espondedray ybay allingcay erhay ethay Emiramissay anday Essalinamay
ofay ethay Orthnay anday Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. Inay esethay igh-soundinghay itles,tay
eshay exulteday anday erhay ersonalitypay ettledsay intoay emthay asay erhay odybay ettledsay
omfortablycay intoay itsay ermineay oberay.


3ay

Enwhay ethay uiresqay allsfay eirhay otay ideway ancestralay acres,ay ishay irstfay oughtthay
isay orfay ishay oundariesbay anday ishay encesfay. Osay itay asway ithway Atherinecay enwhay eshay
ellfay eirhay otay Ussiaray. Ourlandcay asway entrusteday otay Iron,bay ethay ecrepitday olday
Ukeday uledray ybay ishay aughtersday anday evotedday otay Atherinecay. Usthay ethay Empressay
ecuredsay isthay oundarybay ellway anday ouldcay enceforthhay ismissday itay afelysay omfray
erhay indmay. Eshay extnay onsideredcay erhay ownay orderbay ovincespray anday oundfay emthay
ootay estlessray orfay erhay astetay. Ittlelay Ussia,ray Ivonia,lay anday Inlandfay eedednay
otay ebay abilizedstay anday eshay otewray otay Iazemskyvay ecommendingray eatmenttray otay
atthay end.ay Ese“Thay ovinces,pray ikelay atthay ofay Olensk,smay ustmay ebay induceday inay
ethay entlestgay annermay otay Ussifyray emselves,thay osay atthay eythay onay ongerlay ooklay
arounday emthay ikelay olvesway inay ethay orest.”fay

Otay Olandpay eshay avegay erhay ownay ersonalpay attention.ay Atherine’scay amenay aysplay
aay eatgray erôlay inay ethay istoryhay ofay atthay ountrycay asay oneay ofay ethay originatorsay
ofay ethay istoricalhay ootinglay artypay ownknay asay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay. Eethray
onarchsmay aredshay ethay ooty:bay Atherinecay ofay Ussia,ray Ederickfray ofay Ussia,pray
anday Ariamay Eresathay ofay Austria.ay Ariamay Eresathay isay ethay onlyay oneay ofay ethay
eethray owhay ashay evernay eenbay accuseday ofay inventingay ethay idea.ay Incesay Atherinecay
erselfhay exonerateday ethay Austrianay Empressay inay aay etterlay ichwhay eshay otewray otay
Immgray inay 1770,ay Ariamay Eresa’sthay acklay ofay esponsibilityray orfay ethay imecray
inay Olandpay eemssay ufficientlysay established.ay As“ay arfay asay ethay earday orthyway
Adylay Ayerfulpray isay oncerned,”cay otewray ethay Ussianray Empress,ay I“ay ancay aysay
othingnay oremay anthay atthay eshay ufferssay omfray everesay attacksay ofay ovetousnesscay
anday imperiousness.ay Otay eepway isay aay ignsay ofay epentance,ray utbay incesay eshay
alwaysay oldshay astfay otay atwhay eshay ashay anday uiteqay orgetsfay atthay otnay otay oday aay
ingthay againay isay ethay estbay indkay ofay epentance,ray erethay ustmay ebay omethingsay
ubbornstay inay erhay osombay. Iay earfay itay ustmay ebay ethay originalay insay ofay Adamay ichwhay
aysplay isthay azycray omedycay. Utbay atwhay oesday oneay askay oremay omfray uchsay aay oman?way
Ifay eshay isay aithfulfay otay erhay usband,hay eshay ashay allay ethay irtuesvay anday eedsnay
othingnay ore.”may Ariamay Eresa’sthay etaliationray asway otay eakspay ofay ethay Empressay
ofay Ussiaray asay Ette“cay emme”fay anday alktay aboutay erhay openlyay asay aay ooselay omanway.
Otwithstandingnay isthay exchangeay ofay ersonalpay insults,ay eythay oöperatedcay
illinglyway inay ethay eizuresay ofay Olishpay erritorytay.

Ethay exactay artpay ayedplay ybay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray inay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay
ashay evernay eenbay osay earlyclay established.ay Itay isay anay embarrassingay episodeay
orfay ethay Ussianpray istorianhay otay explain.ay Otay assert,ay asay Erschlözay oes,day
atthay Ederickfray onlyay aduallygray anday eluctantlyray onsentedcay isay anay attemptay
otay itewashwhay ethay erohay inay aay ayway ichwhay akesmay imhay ightlyslay unheroic.ay Otay
ascribeay ethay initiativeay otay ethay Ussianray Empressay isay otay aceplay ethay eatgray
Ederickfray inay aay econdarysay ositionpay ichwhay isay inconsistentay ithway ethay
invincibleay ontfray ehay ashay alwaysay esentedpray otay istoryhay. Everthelessnay ethay
actualay idea,ay atthay is,ay ethay executionay ofay ethay ideaay eemssay otay avehay occurreday
irstfay ofay allay otay Atherinecay. Ethay expectationay ofay ethay isasterday adhay onglay
existeday inay Oland,pay ichwhay adhay eenbay orewarnedfay aay enturycay eforebay ybay oneay ofay
itsay Ings,kay Anjay Asimir,cay owhay aidsay atthay oneay ayday ethay ingthay ouldway appenhay
ustjay asay itay actuallyay idday appenhay. Ethay ismembermentday ofay Olandpay adhay eenbay
eensay asay aay ossibilitypay ybay allay ethay internationalay oliticianspay ofay Europeay
orfay oremay anthay aay enturycay eforebay itay ecamebay aay efiniteday icturepay inay ethay indmay
ofay Atherinecay ethay Econdsay. Eshay aloneay adhay ethay energizingay imageay atthay eadslay
otay action,ay anday asway undoubtedlyay esponsibleray orfay ethay irstfay Artitionpay ofay
Oland,pay althoughay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray aredshay ethay uiltgay orfay ethay econdsay
anday irdthay artitionspay ichwhay ollowedfay ogicallylay onay ethay irstfay.

Ethay epsstay ybay ichwhay Atherinecay amecay otay isthay ecisionday areay otnay ifficultday
otay acetray. Oonsay afteray erhay accessionay otay ethay Ussianray one,thray ethay Ingkay ofay
Olandpay aylay ownday otay ieday. Afteray aay eriessay ofay alsefay alarms,ay ehay actuallyay
idday ieday inay Eptember,say 1763ay. Ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray anday ethay Empressay ofay
Ussia,ray owhay adhay eenbay isledmay osay oftenay ybay alsefay eports,ray ereway othbay upsetay
ybay ethay eventay enwhay itay inallyfay occurred.ay Ederickfray angspray upay omfray ethay
abletay ithway ethay emark,ray I“ay atehay osethay eoplepay owhay alwaysay oday ingsthay atay
ethay ongwray ime.”tay Atherinecay alsoay angspray omfray erhay airchay enwhay ethay ewsnay
ame,cay alvanizedgay orfay action.ay Eshay adhay opedhay orfay itay osay onglay. Erhay onglay
eferredday ansplay otay akemay Anislasstay Oniatovskypay Ingkay ofay Olandpay equiredray
instantay attention.ay Eshay adhay alreadyay instructeday erhay Ambassador,ay Ountcay
Ayserling,kay oncerningcay ishay utiesday inay ethay esentpray isiscray. Ehay adhay inay actfay
eenbay electedsay orfay ethay ostpay ithway isthay eventay inay iewvay. I“ay amay endingsay Ountcay
Ayserlingkay ithoutway elayday asay Ambassadoray otay Oland,”pay eshay adhay ittenwray otay
Oniatovsky,pay In“ay orderay otay akemay youay Ingkay afteray ethay eathday ofay Augustay III.ay
Ifay ymay Ambassadoray isay otnay uccessfulsay inay akingmay youay Ing,kay enthay Iay esireday
atthay Adamay Artoriskyczay allshay ecomebay Ing.”kay

Adamay Artoriskyczay asway ethay uncleay ofay Anislas,stay aay epresentativeray ofay ethay
amesay amily,fay anday asway alsoay evotedday otay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray. Atherinecay
asway illingway otay alloway Olandpay aay econdsay oicechay omfray isthay amilyfay. Isthay
idday otnay ean,may owever,hay atthay eshay ovestray anyay esslay efficientlyay anday
eterminedlyday otay aceplay ethay andsomehay Anislasstay uponay ethay onethray. Eshay oldtay
Ayserlingkay atthay ifay ehay ouldcay otnay anagemay itay orfay esslay otay endspay asay uchmay asay
aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray onay ethay election.ay Ornay idday eshay utpay erhay aithfay
inay ethay influenceay ofay oneymay alone.ay Ussianray egimentsray ereway archedmay intoay
Olandpay otay ampcay ominouslyay earnay ethay electoralay onvocationcay. Ethay Empressay
ished,way owever,hay otay avoiday oodshedblay. Eshay eferredpray otay enlistay ethay aiday
anday influenceay ofay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay inay orderay atthay Olandpay ightmay eelfay itsay
easternay anday esternway eighborsnay osingclay inay uponay itsay existenceay ikelay aay
entlegay utbay inevitableay isevay.

Atherinecay avegay esentspray uiteqay unblushingly.ay Onay oonersay asway ethay
Olishpay Ingkay eadday anthay ourierscay ithway essagesmay anday iftsgay eganbay otay
enlivenay ethay oadray omfray Etersburgpay otay Erlinbay. Owingknay Ederickfray orfay aay
Einschmecker_,_Fay Atherinecay entsay imhay elonsmay omfray Astrakhanay anday apesgray
omfray ethay Imeacray. Ederickfray allantlygay eplied,ray Ere“Thay isay aay eatgray
istanceday etweenbay atermelonsway omfray Astrakhanay anday ethay electoralay assemblyay
ofay ethay Olishpay ovinces,pray utbay youay owknay owhay otay omprehendcay allay inay ethay
eresphay ofay youray activity.ay Ethay amesay andhay ichwhay esentspray atermelonsway
istributesday ownscray anday eservespray ethay eacepay inay Europe,ay orfay ichwhay Iay
anday allay owhay areay interesteday inay ethay affairsay ofay Olandpay allshay eternallyay
essblay you.”ay Atherine’scay iftsgay ontinuedcay. Ussianray aviarcay anday erletstay
ereway ollowedfay ybay Ussianray urs,fay ackblay oxfay anday artenmay. Anday inally,fay enwhay
Ederickfray expresseday anay interestay inay ethay omedariesdray osay ommonlycay useday
ybay ethay easantspay inay Ussia,ray ethay Empressay adhay otway ofay ethay estbay animalsay otay
ebay oundfay inay Ukrainiaay entsay ithway erhay omplimentscay otay ethay astermay ofay Anssay
Oucisay. Asay ethay irstfay atermelonsway adhay eenbay eraldshay ofay Oniatovskypay asay
Ing,kay ethay omedariesdray ereway arbingershay ofay ethay irstfay artitionpay ofay Olandpay.

Otnay ollywhay unlikeay ethay atelay Arczay ofay Ussia,ray Oniatovskypay asway ademay Ingkay
againstay ishay illway. Atherine,cay ethay Ing-maker,kay orcedfay isthay unwelcomeay
istinctionday uponay imhay. Ehay elievedbay anday anymay othersay elievedbay ithway imhay
atthay Atherinecay intended,ay afteray akingmay imhay ulerray ofay Oland,pay otay arrymay
imhay anday annexay ishay ountrycay otay erhay own.ay Ethay Ortepfay ofay Urkeytay asway oneay ofay
osethay owhay uspectedsay isthay otay ebay ethay anplay ofay ethay Ussianray Empressay anday
owhay accordinglyay etsay aboutay otay efeatday it.ay Ehay opposeday ethay electionay ofay
Anislasstay onay ethay oundgray atthay ehay asway otnay arriedmay. Oniatovsky’spay amily,fay
ethay Artoriskys,czay awsay ethay ogiclay ofay ethay Orte’spfay objectionay anday urgeday
ethay Ount,cay owhay adhay ertainlycay eachedray aay arriageablemay age,ay otay oosechay aay
uitablesay onsortcay. Utbay Oniatovskypay ubbornlystay efusedray otay aketay ethay atalfay
epstay. Ethay utmostay atthay ehay ouldway onsentcay otay o,day anday isthay asway onlyay afteray
anay emphaticay essagemay adhay arriveday omfray Atherinecay atay Etersburg,pay asway otay
ignsay anay undertakingay atthay ehay ouldway atay eastlay evernay arrymay anyay utbay aay Omanray
Atholiccay. Isthay omisepray uietedqay ethay Urkishtay oppositionay anday ethay electionay
asway alloweday otay oceedpray. Itay ooktay aceplay ybay immemorialay ustomcay inay ethay
openay ieldfay ybay aay otevay ofay oicesvay. Itay asway aay inefay ayday anday erethay asway onay
isorderday. Oniatovskypay otewray inay ishay ournal,jay E“Thay electionay asway erfectlypay
unanimousay anday osay anquiltray atthay anymay adieslay ereway outay onay ethay electoralay
ield.”fay Ehay ecame,bay atay ethay ageay ofay irty-two,thay Ingkay Anislasstay Augustay ofay
Olandpay.

Ethay ountrycay adhay indicatedvay itsay erishedchay epublicanray ystemsay anday
enthroneday anay electeday Ingkay. Ethay ourtscay ofay Europeay astenedhay otay endsay
acknowledgmentsay anday ongratulationscay. Ethay astlay ountrycay otay ebay eardhay omfray
asway Ussiaray. Asay oonsay asay Atherinecay adhay otgay erhay Ingkay electeday ithway erhay
ilitarymay icketspay anday erhay undredhay ousandthay ucats,day eshay ostlay allay interestay
inay ethay Olishpay ituationsay anday eftlay ethay Inistermay ofay Oreignfay Affairs,ay Ountcay
Anin,pay otay endsay ethay owersflay. E“Thay ingthay eemssay incredible,”ay otewray ethay
Ussianpray Ambassadoray otay ishay aster,may Evertheless“nay Iay assureay Youray Ajestymay
atthay isthay isay osay. Ethay otificationnay ofay Oniatovskypay aylay unanswereday orfay
ixsay eeksway onay Anin’spay ell-knownway ork-table.”way Isthay eemedsay amazingay otay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray otay omwhay omptnesspray anday ystemsay ereway etichesfay. Otay
Atherinecay uchsay ingsthay ereway onveniencescay.

Atthay Oniatovsky,pay aay ingkay inay itespay ofay imself,hay evernay oroughlythay enjoyeday
ishay eignray isay onlyay otay ebay expected.ay Ishay ountrycay asway orntay ybay internalay
issensions,day oliticalpay anday eligiousray. Ethay ewnay Ingkay asway aay anmay owhay
adhay eenbay ulliedbay allay ishay ife,lay irstfay ybay ishay othermay anday enthay ybay ishay
istress;may inay ort,shay aay anmay ofay armchay utbay onay orcefay. Erethay asway othingnay
ithinway imhay ithway ichwhay otay opecay ithway ethay urbulenttay onditionscay ofay ishay
ealmray. Atherinecay adhay aay eniusgay orfay econcilingray atwhay eemedsay otay ebay
opposites;ay utbay ethay Olishpay Ing,kay owhay adhay unray awayay omfray ishay othermay otay
ishay istressmay anday adhay enthay unray awayay omfray ishay istressmay otay ishay othermay
again,ay ouldcay otnay oldhay otway antagonisticay interestsay inay ishay indmay atay ethay
amesay imetay. Olandpay asway aay auldroncay ofay onflicts:cay istrictday ithway istrict,day
atusstay ithway atus,stay eligionray ithway eligionray. Underay Oniatovsky,pay ethay olday
amiliarfay eudsfay azedblay igherhay anday igherhay. Ishay ealthhay ufferedsay anday ehay
asway iserablemay. Afteray eethray yearsay ofay uchsay evastatingday esponsibility,ray
ehay otewray otay ishay Ambassadoray inay Ussia,ray E“Thay astlay ordersay ivengay ybay
Incepray Epninray E[thay Ussianray Eneral]gay otay introduceay egislationlay orfay ethay
issidentsday Eek[Gray Atholics]cay isay aay ealray underboltthay orfay ethay ountrycay anday
orfay emay ersonallypay. Ifay itay isay illstay umanlyhay ossible,pay ytray otay akemay ethay
Empressay eesay atthay ethay owncray ichwhay eshay ocuredpray emay illway ecomebay orfay emay aay
irtshay ofay Essusnay. Iay allshay ebay urntbay aliveay anday ymay enday illway ebay ightful.”fray

Usthay ethay Ingkay ailedway onay ishay omfortlesscay one,thray aay entlegay ousemay
emblingtray underay eethray atchfulway airspay ofay eyesay elongingbay otay eethray ofay ethay
ostmay eedygray onarchsmay ofay ethay enturycay. Erhapspay itay ouldway ebay oremay accurateay
otay aysay atthay ethay eethray atchfulway airspay ofay eyesay ereway ainedtray uponay eachay
otheray anday atthay eythay atherray overlookeday asay egligiblenay ethay ictimvay oweringcay
atay ethay entercay ofay ethay agestay. Ariamay Eresa,thay ethay Austrianay idowway owhay evernay
aidlay asideay erhay eeds;way Ederickfray ethay Econd,say ethay abbyshay achelorbay owhay
oreway atchespay onay ishay othes;clay anday Atherinecay ethay Econd,say ethay arvenupay
overeignsay owhay aintedpay erhay ace--thefay onjunctioncay ofay esethay eethray archay
aggressorsay odedbay onay oodgay orfay Oland,pay eakenedway asay eshay asway ybay incessantay
omesticday emorstray. Yetay ethay atastrophecay ichwhay adhay eenbay atheringgay orfay
yearsay anday ichwhay asway inherentay inay ethay ircumstances,cay asway ecipitatedpray atay
astlay asay ifay ybay anay accident.ay

Inay ethay autumnay ofay 1770,ay Atherinecay entertaineday aay istinguishedday oreignfay
uestgay. Ehay asway aay ortshay anmay ithway aay iffstay ompouspay arriagecay anday aay ilentsay
inexpressiveay emeanorday. Ehay adhay omecay otay Etersburgpay atherray eluctantlyray
atay ethay equestray ofay ishay otherbray owhay eltfay atthay anyay invitationay omfray ethay
Empressay ofay Ussiaray ouldshay ebay accepteday anday exploited.ay Erethay asway onay
owingknay atwhay ightmay ebay iddenhay ehindbay ethay advancesay ofay isthay omanway. Ethay
iff,stay ilentsay uestgay omwhay eshay entertaineday isthay autumnay asway Incepray Enryhay
ofay Ussia,pray ethay otherbray ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Incepray Enryhay asway almostay
asay unsociableay asay ishay otherbray utbay ehay adhay aay arpshay eyeay anday ensitivesay
erceptionspay. Ehay asway ideallyay ualifiedqay otay iffsnay arounday ethay ood-pileway ofay
ethay Ussianray onarchmay.

Atherine,cay owhay evernay ostlay anay opportunityay ofay isplayingday allay erhay ichesray
eforebay isthay amily,fay entertaineday Incepray Enryhay egallyray. Eshay installeday
imhay anday ishay etinueray inay aay alacepay acingfay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onastery,may
anay edificeay osay ugehay anday agnificentmay atthay itay asway aterlay onvertedcay omfray
aay esidenceray intoay aay oolschay orfay imperialay agespay. Ethay odest,may unassumingay
Enryhay ovedmay aboutay ithway onsiderablecay iscomfortday inay ethay ichray anday olorfulcay
ettingsay ichwhay ethay ospitablehay Empressay ovidedpray orfay imhay. Ishay appearancesay
ereway unctualpay anday eticulousmay utbay itay asway impossibleay orfay anyoneay otay ooklay
atay imhay anday ancyfay atthay ehay enjoyeday ethay allsbay anday asqueradesmay ichwhay ereway
ivengay orfay ishay entertainment.ay Ethay Ussiansray idday otnay ikelay imhay anday ademay
unfay ofay ishay olemnitysay anday oldnesscay. Ithway ethay Empress,ay owever,hay ehay otgay
onay extremelyay ellway. Eirthay onversationscay ereway arriedcay onay atay eatgray engthlay
anday anay intellectualay ympathysay evelopedday etweenbay emthay ichwhay edlay otay aay onglay
anday interestingay orrespondencecay. Incepray Enry’shay etterslay otay ethay Empressay
oday otnay ontaincay ethay over-straineday atteryflay ithway ichwhay ishay other,bray
Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray alwaysay addresseday erhay. Erethay isay evidenceay inay eirthay
etterslay otay owshay atthay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray asway oneay ofay ethay eoplepay ofay
erhay ownay enerationgay owhay understooday isthay omanway erfectlypay. Inay erhay olday
age,ay eshay urnedtay againstay imhay iolently,vay utbay ehay erishedchay onay esentmentray
againstay erhay. Ehay espectedray Atherinecay incerely,say anday asway evernay afraiday ofay
erhay asay ethay eatgray Ederickfray alwaysay as,way otnay ecausebay eshay asway anay Empressay
utbay ecausebay eshay asway aay omanway.

Incepray Enryhay eppedstay edatelysay oughthray allay ethay orgeousgay estivitiesfay ofay
aay Ussianray Istmaschray anday Ewnay Yearay inay Etersburgpay. Ethay Interway Alacepay adhay
evernay eenbay osay aygay atay isthay easonsay incesay Atherinecay adhay ecomebay Empress,ay
orfay ethay isitvay ofay ethay Ussianpray Incepray adhay ovidedpray anay excuseay otay outdoay
anythingay eshay adhay everay oneday eforebay. Inay Anuary,jay ustjay aboutay ethay imetay enwhay
ingsthay eganbay otay uietqay ownday aay it,bay aay isturbingday umorray amecay overay ethay
owssnay omfray Oscowmay. Itay asway aidsay atthay Ariamay Eresathay adhay entsay Austrianay
oopstray acrossay ethay orderbay otay occupyay aay ittlelay iece,pay aay eryvay ittlelay iecepay
ofay Olandpay. Ethay Austrianay onarchmay adhay eadyray erhay excuseay utbay ethay Ussianray
onarchmay idday otnay inkthay ellway ofay it.ay Eithernay ofay esethay augustay adieslay everay
avegay ethay otheray ethay enefitbay ofay ethay oubtday inay anyay ituationsay. Atherinecay
oppeddray isthay asualcay emarkray inay ethay esencepray ofay Incepray Enry:hay It“ay eemssay
atthay inay isthay Oland,pay oneay ashay onlyay otay oopstay anday elphay one’say elf.”say Incepray
Enryhay egardedray erhay ordsway asay aay ignificantsay essagemay orfay ishay otherbray
otay omwhay ehay eportedray em,thay adding,ay Although“ay isthay asway onlyay aay ancechay
easantry,play itay isay ertaincay atthay itay asway otnay aidsay orfay othingnay anday Iay oday otnay
oubtday atthay itay illway ebay eryvay ossiblepay orfay youay otay ofitpray ybay isthay occasion.”ay

Anday osay eganbay ethay eethray amousfay Artitionspay ofay Olandpay. Inay ethay irstfay
artition,pay Olandpay ostlay ourfay ousandthay uaresqay ilesmay anday ethay eethray
artitionerspay eltfay equallyay ellway eatedtray. Entytway yearsay ater,lay ethay econdsay
artitionpay ooktay aceplay inay ichwhay ethay Ussianray Empressay ofitedpray immenselyay
oremay anthay erhay artnerspay inay ethay ootinglay. Olandpay aisedray upay ationalnay
eroes,hay iefchay ofay omwhay asway ethay omanticray Osciuszko,kay owhay amecay otay erhay
efenceday. Utbay eirthay exploitsay onlyay ervedsay asay anay excuseay orfay ethay irdthay
invasion,ay ichwhay educedray Olandpay otay aay eremay emnant,ray anday inallyfay anday
utterlyay eprivedday Oniatovskypay ofay ishay onethray.

Orfay aay imetay ethay ex-Kingay ivedlay inay Olandpay underay ethay otectionpray ofay Ussiaray
anday aterlay ehay entway ackbay otay Etersburgpay erewhay ehay oundfay asylumay untilay ishay
eathday. Ehay outliveday ybay everalsay yearsay ethay istressmay ofay ishay youth,ay owhay adhay
irstfay ivengay imhay aay onethray anday enthay akentay itay awayay again.ay Oniatovskypay
asway onay erohay utbay ehay asway aay oodgay ealday ofay aay ilosopher;phay ehay accepteday ishay
eclineday anday allfay ithoutway anyay eatgray esturesgay ofay agedytray. Ehay adhay evernay
antedway otay ebay Ingkay anyhow.ay Ishay arstay entway ownday inay eacefulpay obscurity,ay
ilewhay ethay ationalnay erohay Osciuszkokay impersonateday orfay ethay orldway ethay
agedytray ofay Olandpay. Othbay ofay emthay ereway upportedsay ybay ensionspay omfray ethay
Ussianray overnmentgay. Atherine’scay estimateay ofay ethay ex-Kingay ofay Olandpay isay
illustrateday ybay aay egendlay ichwhay isay elievedbay evenay otay isthay ayday. Ethay orystay
oesgay atthay eshay oughtbray ishay ostlay onethray omfray Olandpay anday useday itay orfay aay
ater-closetway inay erhay apartmentay atay Arskoeczay Elosay.


4ay

Inay ethay eighteenthay entury,cay Ussiaray ooktay erhay ensuscay everyay entytway years.ay
Itay asway anay autocraticay evisionray arriedcay onay inay aay ipshodslay ayway underay
ilitarymay orders.ay Enwhay Atherinecay ascendeday ethay onethray itay asway imetay orfay
uchsay aay ensuscay otay ebay akentay. Ethay ewnay Empressay asway impatientay orfay ethay
esults;ray eshay antedway otay owknay owhay anymay oulssay eshay adhay anday owhay uchmay ofay ethay
earth’say urfacesay eshay owned,ay orfay itay asway inay uchsay ersonalpay ermstay asay esethay
atthay eshay icturedpay erhay ossessionspay.

Eturningray omfray Oscowmay inay Une,jay 1763,ay ustjay afteray ethay iascofay ofay erhay anplay
otay arrymay Orlov,ay eshay urnedtay erhay attentionay otay ethay ensuscay. Ethay Enatesay
asway eparingpray otay ogay aheaday accordingay otay ecedentpray. Althoughay Astorpay
Agnerway adhay eenbay aay ecialistspay inay eography,gay ishay upilpay ethay Empressay asway
everthelessnay eryvay aguevay aboutay Ussiaray. Eshay asway obligeday otay askay ethay
Enatorssay otay elltay erhay owhay anymay itiescay erethay ereway inay erhay ingdomkay anday
iscoveredday otay erhay orrorhay atthay otnay oneay ofay emthay ewknay. Ithoutway aay oment’smay
esitationhay eshay ooktay ivefay ublesray omfray erhay ocketpay anday entsay aay essengermay
ostpay astehay otay ethay Academyay ofay Iencescay ichwhay adhay ublishedpay anay atlasay ofay
Ussiaray otay ebay adhay orfay isthay icepray. Ethay Empressay esentedpray ethay atlasay otay ethay
Enatesay ithway erhay omplimentscay.

Ethay iscussionday ofay ethay ensuscay oceededpray. Atherinecay earnedlay atthay itay asway
ustomarilycay akentay ybay ilitarymay oopstray anday ostcay almostay aay illionmay ubles,ray
anday atthay itay invariablyay entsay ethay easantpay opulationpay intoay aay anicpay. Eythay
evadeday ethay istslay ybay idinghay inay ampssway anday orestsfay anday eeingflay acrossay ethay
orderbay intoay Olandpay. Ethay onsequencecay asway atthay ials,tray investigations,ay
anday unishmentspay ollowedfay inay ethay akeway ofay everyay ensuscay inay uchsay umbersnay
atthay ethay Enatorssay eadeddray otay undertakeay ethay objay atay all.ay Adlysay eythay
ookshay eirthay ewiggedbay eadshay anday eploredday ethay ecessitynay ofay ausingcay osay
uchmay ommotioncay amongay ethay error-strickentay eoplepay. Eythay ademay eechesspay
oneay afteray ethay otheray ithoutway offeringay anyay uggestionsay asay otay owhay esethay
egrettableray onsequencescay ouldcay ebay eventedpray. Ethay attentiveay Empressay
istenedlay untilay eshay asway iredtay anday ethay iscussionday inallyfay amecay otay aay eadday
end.ay Enthay eshay askeday aay ewfay uestionsqay.

Y“Whay avehay uchsay aay umbernay ofay oopstray anday ilepay upay esethay eavyhay ostscay orfay
ethay easury?tray Isay erethay onay otheray ay?”way Eshay asway oldtay atthay erethay asway onay
otheray ay;way itay adhay alwaysay eenbay oneday osay. Ut“Bay isthay anplay eemssay etterbay otay
e,”may eshay ersistedpay. Ublish“Pay oughoutthray ethay Empireay atthay everyay aceplay
allshay endsay aay istlay ofay itsay oulssay otay itsay ancellery,chay ethay ancellerieschay
otay ethay overnments,gay anday ethay overnmentsgay otay ethay Enate.”say Ourfay Enatorssay
okespay upay atay onceay otay elltay erhay atthay itay asway impossible.ay Ethay eoplepay ouldway
otnay eportray emselvesthay oluntarilyvay anday aay owshay ofay ilitarymay orcefay asway
ereforethay ecessarynay. Ethay Empressay ursuedpay erhay anplay. Offer“ay otay allay osethay
owhay avehay otnay yetay egisteredray eedomfray omfray unishmentpay anday orderay ethay ocallay
authoritiesay otay acceptay ethay ormerfay evadersay uponay ethay esentpray ist.”lay Ethay
elderlyay Incepray Akovskyshay angspray otay ishay eetfay. At“Thay isay otnay ustice,”jay ehay
outedshay. E“Thay uiltygay allshay ebay andledhay exactlyay ikelay ethay innocent!ay Iay avehay
alwaysay arefullycay eportedray omfray ymay istrictday anday onay oneay ashay eenbay omitted.ay
Utbay oeverwhay ashay enjoyeday ethay advantageay ofay omissionsay illway ownay andstay ustjay
erewhay Iay o!”day Utbay oneay ofay ethay youngeray Enatorssay adhay otgay ethay Empress’say ideaay
anday amecay otay erhay upportsay osay andsomelyhay atthay ethay anplay asway adopteday anday
arriedcay intoay execution.ay Enceforth,hay ethay Empress’say ethodmay asway alwaysay
ollowed,fay ithway ethay esultray atthay igrationsmay otay Olandpay anday outlawryay inay ethay
oodsway anday ampssway ichwhay onceay ollowedfay everyay ensuscay aduallygray isappearedday
altogether.ay

Atherinecay eftlay aay emorandummay ofay ethay orstway internalay anglestay ichwhay eshay
adhay otay undoay atay ethay eginningbay ofay erhay eignray. Ethay armyay adhay eenbay unpaiday
orfay anymay onthsmay. Ethay axestay ofay ethay Empireay adhay eenbay ortgagedmay ybay ethay
enatesay. Erethay asway aay arcityscay ofay urrency;cay onlyay aay illionmay oldgay ublesray
ereway inay irculationcay inay ethay olewhay empire.ay Ethay Empressay Elisabethay adhay
andedhay overay earlynay everyay anchbray ofay usinessbay anday allay ethay inesmay ofay ethay
ountrycay otay onopolists,may iefchay ofay omwhay ereway ethay Uvalovsshay. Atay ethay imetay
ofay Atherine’scay accession,ay ethay easantspay owhay orkedway inay ethay inesmay ereway inay
evoltray. Ethay Empressay egardedray esethay onopoliesmay ithway eatgray isfavorday anday
ethay ebelliousray easantspay ithway evenay eatergray isfavorday. Ikelay ethay Ermangay
Ausfrau__Hay atthay eshay as,way eshay enjoyeday ethay ieldingway ofay aay ewnay oombray anday
ofay ivinggay ethay ountrycay aay ealray ingspray eaningclay. Ybay ookhay oray ook,cray eshay
anagedmay otay aypay ethay army;ay eshay estoredray ethay axingtay owerpay otay ethay axtay
officers;ay eshay eformedray ethay urrencycay anday introduceday aperpay oneymay intoay
ommoncay use;ay eshay abolisheday atay oneay okestray allay onopoliesmay anday ollowedfay ethay
exampleay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray inay encouragingay ivatepray usinessbay enterprise.ay
Inally,fay eshay entsay erhay olonelscay anday erhay annonscay ownday otay ethay inesmay erewhay
ikesstray adhay okenbray outay uringday ethay eignray ofay ethay atelay Arczay anday ombardedbay
ethay ikersstray osay oroughlythay atthay eythay ereway adglay otay eeksay afetysay inay
ethay inesmay again.ay Ellway atisfiedsay ithway allay esethay eanings,clay eshay ipedway
erhay andshay onay erhay apronay anday atsay ownday otay erhay ilksay embroidery.ay Eshay asway
orkingway onay aay orgeousgay obe,ray ithway itchesstay asay elicateday anday erfectpay asay
ethay Inesechay ancay akemay em,thay otay ebay esentedpray otay ethay Archimandriteay ofay ethay
Oitskytray onasterymay.


5ay

Atherinecay ooktay onsiderablecay interestay inay ethay atusstay ofay erhay exsay anday
uestionsqay ofay oralitymay. Eshay onceay aidsay atthay eshay idday otnay owknay oray
understanday omenway. Eshay otewray otay Adamemay Elke,bjay Om“Fray ymay ifteenthfay otay
ymay irty-thirdthay year,ay Iay evernay eallyray adhay ethay opportunityay otay onversecay
ithway omen;way Iay onlyay adhay andmaidenshay aboutay emay. Enwhay Iay ishedway otay eakspay
ithway anyone,ay Iay adhay otay ogay intoay anotheray oomray erewhay erethay ereway onlyay enmay.
Osay itay isay ueday artlypay otay abithay anday artlypay otay ymay astetay atthay ashay eenbay osay
ormedfay atthay Iay eallyray understanday onlyay owhay otay arrycay onay aay onversationcay
ithway ethay atter.”lay Itay isay uetray atthay eshay adhay ewfay omenway iendsfray. Ethay
Incesspray Ashkovday owhay adhay iddenray esidebay erhay onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay Eterhofpay
ampaigncay asway evernay eallyray inay erhay onfidencecay. Eshay asway aay aylay igurefay. Inay
olday age,ay ethay Empressay ecamebay oremay anday oremay ependentday onay ethay iendshipfray
ofay Ountesscay Ucebray anday Ountesscay Otassovpray. Utbay erhay intimacies,ay emotionalay
anday intellectual,ay ofay ichwhay erethay ereway any,may ereway intimaciesay ithway enmay.
Eshay alwaysay adhay aay eefray anday ovialjay ayway ithway emthay.

Ethay Empressay initiateday omesay eformsray orfay erhay exsay ichwhay oreshadowedfay
ypicaltay aspectsay ofay ethay omanway oblem--apray oblempray ichwhay asway otnay eallyray
ornbay untilay ethay extnay enturycay. Omfray isthay ointpay ofay iew,vay eryvay ignificantsay
areay ethay epsstay ichwhay eshay ooktay. Ostitutionpray asway aay ell-developedway adetray
inay ethay Etersburgpay ofay osethay aysday. Inay oneay uarterqay ofay ethay itycay irlsgay ofay
ethay owntay ereway especiallyay umerous,nay anday enerealvay iseaseday ourishedflay
amongay emthay. Itay asway aay aladymay inay ichwhay ethay Empressay ooktay aay astvay interest.ay
Etherwhay eshay erselfhay adhay adhay anay unfortunateay experienceay oray etherwhay eshay
erelymay ememberedray atthay Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay ematurelypray arriedcay
offay ybay it,ay ethay Empressay asway orriblyhay afraiday ofay isthay ontagioncay. Aay
ell-authenticatedway orystay ashay itay atthay eachay ofay erhay overslay asway equiredray otay
ubmitsay otay aay ysicalphay examinationay ybay erhay Englishay ysician,phay Ogersonray.
Ornay idday erhay interestay opstay entirelyay ithway erselfhay. Eshay uiltbay aay inefay
ospitalhay orfay ethay uffererssay omfray isthay infection,ay ofay ichwhay Ajormay Assonmay
ays:say One“ay ospital,hay owever,hay oundedfay ybay Atherinecay eservesday otay ebay
entionedmay asay aay aracteristicchay establishment.ay Itay isay estinedday orfay
ethay eceptionray ofay iftyfay adieslay infecteday ithway aay ertaincay iseaseday. Onay
uestionqay isay askeday eitheray asay otay ethay amenay oray ethay ualityqay ofay osethay owhay
esentpray emselves,thay anday eythay areay eatedtray ithway equalay are,cay espect,ray anday
iscretionday. Isthay astlay ordway isay evenay arkedmay onay ethay inenlay appointeday orfay
eirthay use.”ay

Anotheray institutionay illstay emainingray asay aay onumentmay otay Atherine’scay eignray
asway ethay eatgray Oundlingfay Ospitalhay ichwhay eshay uiltbay onay ethay anksbay ofay ethay
Oscowmay. Yinglay againstay ethay iver,ray itay andsstay outay asay oneay ofay ethay ostmay
ominentpray eaturesfay ofay ethay itycay extnay otay ethay Emlinkray. Itsay aditiontray ashay
otnay aded,fay asay itay illstay ouseshay ethay aternitymay elfareway orkway ofay Oscowmay. Ethay
Empressay ademay itay originallyay aay omehay orfay oundlingsfay anday annedplay itay orfay ethay
iscouragementday ofay infanticide.ay Erhay institutionay ashay ethay amenay ofay eingbay
ethay irstfay ofay itsay indkay ichwhay angspray upay inay Europe;ay atay anyay ate,ray itay asway
ethay ostmay amousfay anday ervedsay asay aay odelmay orfay anymay ichwhay amecay afterwards.ay
Otnay allay ofay Atherine’scay ubjectssay ereway easedplay ithway erhay innovation.ay Aay
itizencay amednay Olinsmay otewray aay etterlay otay expressay ishay iscontentday. Ehay
eproachedray erhay orfay esethay oundlingfay omeshay ichwhay onlyay ervedsay orfay ethay
encouragementay ofay immorality.ay Ice,vay ehay aid,say ouldway owshay itselfay oremay
openlyay anday amelesslyshay asay aay esult;ray oremay anday oremay illegitimateay
ildrenchay ouldway ebay ornbay. Omfray isthay itay aymay ebay eensay atthay ethay Uritanpay idealay
ofay ethay epressionray ofay icevay idday otnay acklay epresentationray evenay inay Ussiaray inay
ethay eighteenthay enturycay.

Ethay Empress’say effortsay otay educateay erhay exsay etmay ithway oremay approval.ay Aay
oisterclay ownknay asay ethay Olnysmay Onventcay anday oundedfay ybay Elisabethay Etrovnapay
asway akentay overay ybay Atherinecay anday onvertedcay intoay aay oolschay orfay youngay
adieslay. Eshay avegay erhay ersonalpay attentionay otay isthay experimentay ichwhay asway
ethay idepray ofay erhay earthay. Eshay otewray otay Oltaire,vay You“ay ow,knay orfay othingnay
escapesay you,ay atthay ivefay undredhay youngay adieslay areay eingbay educateday inay aay
ousehay ichwhay asway ormerlyfay esignedday orfay eethray undredhay idesbray ofay eavenhay.
Esethay youngay adieslay Iay onfesscay arfay urpasssay ouray expectations.ay Eythay akemay
astonishingay ogresspray anday everyay oneay admitsay atthay eythay areay asay ovablelay asay
eythay areay owledgeableknay. Eirthay onductcay isay ustlyjay egardedray asay amelessblay
ithoutway avinghay atay ethay amesay imetay ethay ictstray anday ernstay annermay ofay ethay
oisterclay. Orfay ethay astlay otway intersway eythay avehay egunbay otay ayplay omediescay anday
agedies,tray anday eythay avehay oneday etterbay ithway emthay anthay osethay owhay akemay aay
ofessionpray ofay acting.”ay

Oudpray asay eshay isay ofay esethay ivefay undredhay aultlessfay amsels,day erethay isay oneay
oblempray ichwhay oublestray erhay. Allay ethay Enchfray aysplay includingay Oltaire’svay
own,ay ichwhay eshay ancay indfay orfay ethay oolschay urntay onay ethay emethay ofay ovelay. Atwhay
isay otay ebay oneday aboutay it?ay Eshay asksay Oltaire’svay advice.ay Atherinecay eelsfay
atthay erhay irls’gay attentionay ouldshay otnay ebay alledcay osay earlyay otay ethay ubjectsay.
Oltairevay agreesay anday elpfullyhay uggestssay atthay asay arfay asay ishay ownay aysplay
areay oncernedcay ethay attermay ancay ebay emediedray. Entay ineslay erehay anday elvetway
ineslay ere,thay otay ebay obliginglyay electedsay ybay ethay author,ay ancay ebay ickenstray
outay ithoutway amageday otay ethay ompositioncay anday allay ethay oprietiespray illway ebay
atisfiedsay.

Inay aay allantgay entence,say ehay efersray otay ethay Olnysmay amselsday asay Amazons.ay
Ethay Empressay ejectsray isthay itletay irmly,fay informingay imhay atthay eythay areay
otnay intendeday otay ecomebay Amazonsay atay allay utbay onesthay ivesway anday othersmay.
Itay appears,ay owever,hay atthay isthay admirableay institutionay adhay overlookeday
ethay oblempray ofay owriesday. Afteray elvetway yearsay ofay arefulcay ultivation,cay ethay
youngay adieslay emergeday asay aragonspay ofay irtuevay utbay entirelyay ennilesspay anday
omelesshay. Anymay ofay emthay ecamebay overnessesgay. Othersay illstay ereway aredsnay ybay
ethay officersay ofay ethay uardsgay osewhay arracksbay adjoineday ethay onventcay. Ey“Thay
atchedway everyay ermtay ofay ismissal,”day ayssay Ajormay Asson,may O“tay ensnareay ethay
ettiestpray. Itay ouldway ebay oremay acticalpray otay ave,say outay ofay ethay immenseay ostcay
ofay eirthay education,ay aay ufficientsay umsay otay ortionpay emthay oray atay eastlay otay
eepkay emthay illtay eythay ereway ovidedpray or.”fay Ethay Empressay apparentlyay idday otnay
oreseefay isthay ifficultyday. Asay ennilesspay Incesspray Ikefay ofay Anhaltay eshay adhay
omecay otay Ussiaray anday adhay otgay aay usbandhay ithoutway aay owryday. Ethay Olnysmay youngay
adieslay ightmay oday ethay amesay.


6ay

Althoughay Atherinecay idday otnay esitatehay otay ollowfay elf-interestsay inay oreignfay
elations,ray eshay ooktay anay idealisticay iewvay ofay erhay omesticday oblemspray. Eshay
urnedtay omfray Achiavellimay otay Ontesquieumay. Enwhay eshay oughtthay ofay Ourlandcay
anday Olandpay eshay icturedpay erselfhay asay aay eneralgay onay orseback;hay enwhay eshay
oughtthay ofay Ussiaray eshay icturedpay erselfhay asay ethay Ittlelay Other,may Atushkamay.
Eshay anday Ussiaray ereway uniteday againstay ethay estray ofay ethay orldway.

Ethay Empressay ishedway otay akemay erhay eoplepay appyhay ithoutway akingmay erselfhay
unhappy.ay Ussiaray adhay espotic,day onflicting,cay aoticchay awslay. Erethay asway aay
intedpray odecay ichwhay adhay eenbay andedhay ownday omfray Arczay Alexeiay Ichaelovich,may
ethay atherfay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Utbay ieflychay ethay eoplepay ereway uledray ybay
ukases,ay ofay ichwhay Atherine’scay Anifestomay ofay Ilencesay isay aay oodgay example.ay
Otnay always,ay owever,hay idday ethay Ussiansray obeyay osay omptlypray asay eythay adhay oneday
inay isthay articularpay instance.ay Itay asway ommonlycay aidsay ofay ethay easantspay enwhay
omesay orderay adhay otnay eenbay obeyed,ay Ey“Thay areay aitingway orfay ethay irdthay ukase.”ay
Uringday ethay eignray ofay Elisabethay Etrovna,pay ethay Enatesay adhay iscussedday ethay
eednay ofay odifyingcay ethay awslay utbay ostponementspay adhay ensueday anday othingnay adhay
eenbay accomplished.ay Onay ethay esholdthray ofay erhay eign,ray Atherinecay asway etmay ybay
isthay eednay. Itay asway aay asktay ademay otay erhay andhay.

Eshay ooktay ethay ancientay odecay ofay Arczay Alexeiay inay oneay andhay anday Ontesquieu’smay
Iritspay ofay Awslay inay ethay other.ay Erethay eemedsay otay ebay onay ayway ofay econcilingray
ethay o;tway osay eshay ecidedday atthay eshay adhay etterbay eaveclay otay Ontesquieumay
altogether.ay Eshay orkedway eethray ourshay everyay ayday orfay oremay anthay eethray yearsay
anday oducedpray aay ickthay olumevay. Erethay asway utbay ittlelay originalay oughtthay inay
itay asay ostmay ofay itay adhay eenbay adapteday omfray erhay ilosopherphay anday uidegay. Itay
asway ublishedpay underay ethay itletay Instruction“ay ofay Erhay Imperialay Ajestymay
Atherinecay ethay Econdsay orfay ethay Ommissioncay argedchay ithway eparingpray aay
ojectpray ofay aay ewnay odecay ofay aws.”lay Itay asway oremay ieflybray ownknay inay Ussianray asay
ethay Akaznay.

Eshay orkedway ecretly,say owingshay erhay ookbay otay onay oneay utbay Aninpay anday Orlov.ay
Ountcay Aninpay asway elightedday. Ethay Empressay asway atay astlay engageday onay aay anplay
inay ichwhay ehay ouldcay ole-heartedlywhay are,shay atthay ofay uttingpay oliticalpay anday
ocialsay idealsay onay aperpay. Ethay Ountcay iedcray out,ay ilewhay ishay ugehay erukepay
oppedflay otay oneay idesay inay ishay excitement,ay Ese“Thay areay inciplespray ichwhay illway
astcay ownday alls!”way Ethay andsomehay Egory,gray ounginglay ithway ishay eetfay up,ay
oughtthay ethay iterarylay effortsay ofay ishay Empressay ouldway urelysay adday otay erhay
alreadyay iningshay aurelslay. Ehay ishedway otay aketay ethay agespay ichwhay eshay eadray otay
imhay anday owshay emthay arounday otay ethay olewhay ourtcay. Utbay Atushkamay orbadefay imhay
otay oday isthay.

Inay ethay ummersay ofay 1767ay ethay orkway asway atay astlay inishedfay. Inay Ecemberday
Atherinecay adhay entsay outay aay ukaseay orderingay ethay electionay ofay elegatesday orfay
aay egislativelay ommissioncay. Uringday ethay ing,spray aay imetay ofay eatgray oodsflay
anday eshetsfray inay Ussia,ray ethay electionsay adhay akentay aceplay. Erethay adhay eenbay
uchmay oaninggray anday otestingpray omfray istrictsday afflicteday ybay eavyhay ains,ray
asay ethay ollensway eamsstray ademay aveltray ifficultday anday angerous,day utbay ethay ewnay
Empressay ignoreday allay excusesay orfay elayday anday omehowsay oray otheray ethay eamsstray
ereway ordedfay. Inay earlyay ummer,say ethay elegatesday eganbay otay arriveay inay Oscow,may
inay ibitkas,kay onay orseback,hay onay ootfay. Eythay epresentedray ities,cay istricts,day
ocialsay asses,clay eligions,ray acesray. Erethay ereway Ussianray oblesnay earingway
aces,lay iamonds,day anday elvetsvay ademay upay inay ethay atestlay Arispay ashion;fay erethay
ereway erchantsmay anday ilitarymay en;may erethay ereway aay ewfay easantspay inay ocks;smay
erethay ereway Artarstay anday Ashkirsbay. Overay aay ousandthay elegatesday assembled.ay

Iorpray otay ethay onvention,cay ethay Empressay equesteredsay erselfhay inay ethay
Olomenskoekay Alacepay otnay arfay omfray Oscowmay. Erehay eshay atheredgay arounday
erhay ariousvay inkingthay ersons,pay asay eshay alledcay em,thay anday askeday emthay otay
iticizecray erhay anuscriptmay. Otay eetmay eirthay onflictingcay objections,ay eshay
ossedcray outay osay uchmay atthay onlyay alfhay ofay ethay Instructionay asway eftlay.
Ollectingcay ethay emnantray ofay erhay abors,lay eshay entsay itay otay ethay inter,pray anday
enthay adhay itay eadray eforebay ethay egislativelay onventioncay. Asay anymay ofay ethay
elegatesday ouldcay otnay ead,ray itay asway ecessarynay atthay ethay Instructionay ouldshay
ebay eadray alouday equentlyfray anday ullyfay. Atay irstfay ethay elegatesday oseray inay aay
odybay atay ethay irstfay oundsay ofay Erhay Ajesty’smay ords;way utbay ethay ocumentday asway
eadray ootay oftenay anday ootay engthilylay. Inallyfay eythay ustjay emainedray ittingsay
oray illedmay arounday accordingay otay eirthay ustomcay. Omesay Englishay isitorsvay owhay
attendeday ethay onventioncay alledcay itay aay iotray. Etherwhay ethay eetingmay asway
eallyray asay umultuoustay asay ethay Englishay Arliamentpay ancay ebay onay occasionay isay
oubtfulday. Utbay ethay Ussianray elegatesday oreway osay anymay ay,gay imitivepray olors,cay
itay obablypray eemedsay otay Anglo-Saxonay observersay asay ifay eythay expresseday
excitementay anday avagerysay inay everyay ayway.

Ethay egislativelay ommissioncay aggeddray onay aay yearay anday aay alfhay. Ethay irstfay
essionssay ooktay aceplay inay ethay Emlinkray utbay iftedshay otay Etersburgpay enwhay
ethay Empressay eturnedray otay erhay orthernnay esidenceray. Ethay ommissioncay ikelay
everythingay elseay inay Ussiaray accommodateday easilyay otay aay omadicnay ifelay. Inay
Atherine’scay ay,day ethay ourt,cay ichwhay avelledtray ontinuallycay ackbay anday orthfay
etweenbay Etersburgpay anday Oscow,may ooktay eirthay urniturefay ithway em,thay orfay
urniturefay asway arcescay anday eciouspray. Otay ivegay aay anmay Euble__may omfray Ancefray
asway oneay ofay ethay estbay aysway ofay ibingbray imhay. Isthay asway oneay ofay ethay essonslay
atthay Atherinecay adhay earnedlay omfray ethay Empressay Elisabeth.ay

Enwhay ethay Empressay etsay orthfay orfay Etersburgpay inay Ecember,day 1767,ay eshay adhay
oremay eoplepay anday oremay urniturefay anthay usualay inay erhay aintray. Oneay ousandthay
elegatesday ereway eptsway orthwardnay inay yingflay eighsslay anday ereway eassembledray
inay ethay Interway Alacepay afteray ethay Istmaschray estivitiesfay adhay eenbay ulyday
elebratedcay. Inay Etersburgpay asay inay ethay Emlin,kray ethay Empressay eptkay erselfhay
odestlymay inay ethay ackgroundbay. Eshay atsay inay aay oxbay ehindbay aay awndray urtaincay anday
eftlay ethay ommissioncay entirelyay inay ethay andshay ofay aay esidiumpray omposedcay ofay
Iazemsky,vay Ibikov,bay anday Uvalovshay. Erhay Eneral-Adjutant,gay Egorygray Orlov,ay
asway ominentpray onay ethay oorflay anday onay oneay occasionay okespay upay eloquentlyay
inay efenseday ofay aay easantpay owhay adhay eenbay alledcay Azy“lay anday ubborn”stay ybay aay
oblemannay. Ethay Empressay asway otnay officiallyay esentpray. Eshay entsay essagesmay
omfray erhay oxbay otay ethay esidiumpray utbay idday otnay appearay onay ethay oorflay. Isthay
ademay itay ossiblepay orfay ethay onventioncay otay awdray upay ormalfay addressesay otay
ethay authoray ofay ethay Instructionay anday orfay erhay otay eplyray inay itingwray otay
emthay. Inay oneay ofay esethay addressesay eshay asway esignatedday orfay ethay irstfay imetay
asay Atherine“Cay ethay Eat.”gray Eshay odestlymay epliedray atthay ethay itletay asway
oneay ichwhay eshay adhay otnay yetay earned.ay Illstay ethay itletay ungclay anday eshay asway
otay enjoyay itay orfay anymay onglay yearsay asay eshay asway otnay yetay ortyfay enwhay ethay
ommissioncay onay awslay estowedbay itay uponay erhay.

Ethay Instructionay aboundsay inay emocraticday ideas.ay Itay oesgay osay arfay asay otay
advocateay ethay adualgray abolitionay ofay erfdomsay inay Ussiaray ybay allowingay ethay
erfssay otay ownay opertypray anday otay urchasepay eirthay ownay eedomfray. Utbay ethay
Ussianray oblesnay ereway otnay inay avorfay ofay ethay eformray. Ostmay ofay ethay anplay asway
ickenstray outay ybay erhay ounsellorscay eforebay ethay Instructionay everay entway otay
intpray anday ethay emainderray asway eliminateday ybay eechesspay inay ethay onventioncay.
Ethay Empressay abandoneday allay opagandapray orfay ethay abolitionay ofay erfdomsay orfay
ethay estray ofay erhay ifelay anday onsoledcay erhay onsciencecay ybay abusingay ethay Ussianray
oblesnay inay erhay emoirsmay. At“Whay adhay Iay otnay otay uffersay omfray ethay oicevay ofay anay
irrationalay anday uelcray ublicpay opinionay enwhay isthay uestionqay asway onsideredcay
inay ethay egislativelay ommissioncay. Ethay obmay ofay obles,nay osewhay umbernay asway
uchmay eatergray anthay Iay adhay everay upposedsay ecausebay Iay adhay udgedjay emthay ootay
uchmay ybay ethay eoplepay owhay ailyday urroundedsay e,may eganbay otay uspectsay atthay esethay
iscussionsday ightmay ingbray aboutay anay improvementay inay ethay ositionpay ofay ethay
easants...pay. Iay elievebay atthay erethay ereway otnay entytway umanhay eingsbay owhay
eflectedray onay ethay ubjectsay atay atthay imetay ithway umanity,hay eallyray ikelay umanhay
eings!”bay


7ay

Atherine’scay ampaigncay againstay allpoxsmay inay Ussiaray onway eatgray amefay orfay erhay
inay Europe.ay Itay ustmay ebay admitteday atthay erhay epstay ooktay ouragecay inay osethay
aysday. Ethay evalencepray ofay ethay iseaseday asway uchsay atthay everybodyay elievedbay
atthay everybodyay adhay otay avehay it.ay Orfay instance,ay ethay ourtcay okespay ofay ethay
Andgray Uke’sday uncertainay ancechay ofay ifelay ecausebay ehay Ad“hay otnay yetay adhay ethay
allpox.”smay Ethay oyalray amilyfay adhay onay oremay otectionpray anthay ethay oorestpay
easantpay. Ethay iancéfay ofay Empressay Elisabethay adhay eenbay arriedcay offay ybay
allpoxsmay onay ethay eveay ofay ishay arriagemay anday Eterpay ethay Econdsay adhay iedday inay
earlyay youthay ofay ethay amesay iseaseday. Omfray ethay imetay ofay Atherine’scay arrivalay
inay Ussiaray eshay asway onstantlycay ursuedpay ybay ethay earfay ofay ethay estpay anday everyay
imetay eshay ellfay illay eshay oughtthay itay adhay overtakenay erhay.

Eshay adhay eardhay ofay accinationvay inay England.ay Erhay admirationay orfay Englishay
institutionsay adhay eenbay encourageday ybay erhay iendshipfray ithway Irsay Arleschay
Anburyhay Illiamsway anday ethay influenceay ofay Oltairevay. Ethay acticalpray Englishay
adhay importeday accinationvay omfray ethay Orient,ay anday anay English-woman,ay Adylay
Arymay Ortleyway Ontagu,may adhay etsay aay avebray exampleay ybay allowingay erselfhay anday
erhay onsay otay ebay inoculated.ay Onay ethay otheray and,hay erethay ereway anymay oicesvay
aisedray againstay it.ay Ethay ysiciansphay ofay ethay Orbonnesay iscountenancedday
accinationvay anday isregardedday ethay experienceay ofay Englanday ithway ethay
acticepray. Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway intenselyay afraiday ofay itay anday otewray
otay Atherinecay otay urgeay erhay onglystray otnay otay aketay ethay iskray. Eshay epliedray
atthay eshay adhay alwaysay earedfay ethay allpoxsmay anday ishedway oremay anthay anythingay
elseay otay ebay eedfray ofay erhay enslavementay otay isthay earfay. I“ay amay osay uckstray ybay aay
ituationsay osay unworthyay atthay Iay egardray itay asay aay eaknessway otnay otay escapeay omfray
it.”ay

Eshay entereday intoay orrespondencecay ithway anay Englishay urgeon,say dray. Omasthay
Imsdale,day owhay asway adventurousay enoughay otay acceptay erhay invitationay otay
omecay otay Ussiaray. Ehay adhay ublishedpay aay orkway onay inoculationay anday isthay adhay
attracteday ethay Empress’say attention;ay eshay adhay alwaysay eenbay aay eatgray importeray
anday eaderray ofay oreignfay ooksbay. Ethay amousfay dray. Imsdaleday arresteday erhay
attention,ay eoccupiedpray asay eshay asway atay allay imestay ithway erhay anxietyay aboutay
allpoxsmay.

Ehay arriveday atay ethay ourtcay ofay Etersburgpay inay Ecember,day 1768ay. Ehay asway
eceivedray asay allay oreignfay uestsgay ereway eceivedray ithway ocialsay entertainmentsay
ichwhay ethay orthyway octorday ubsequentlysay escribedday inay ullfay inay ishay actstray
onay inoculationay inay Ussiaray. Ethay Empressay adhay eenbay arnedway againstay ethay
experimentay anday erhay earsfay ereway iferay. Althoughay eshay adhay entsay orfay Imsdaleday
otay accinatevay er,hay eshay illstay ontinuedcay otay iscussday ethay attermay opray anday
oncay. Atay astlay eshay utpay anay enday otay erhay earsfay ybay orderingay ethay ysicianphay otay
accinatevay erhay ecretlysay oneay ayday. Ethay esttay ucceededsay apitallycay. Ethay ostghay
ofay isthay earfay asway aid,lay evernay otay alkway again.ay

Ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay asway ownay accinatedvay anday Egorygray Orlov.ay Onay ethay econdsay
ayday afteray ethay operation,ay Orlovay adhay onegay untinghay. Isthay asway ewsnay otay endsay
otay Europe,ay illstay emblingtray atay ethay arebay oughtthay ofay accinationvay. Ethay
Empressay otewray ethay orystay otay Oltaire,vay ustingtray imhay otay eadspray itay inay ethay
operpray uartersqay. Allay atay onceay eshay asway ashameday atthay eshay adhay everay eenbay
osay imoroustay asay otay earfay accinationvay. Afteray all,ay everyay eetstray urchinay inay
Englanday adhay asay uchmay ouragecay asay at!thay Eshay urgeday inoculationay uponay ourtcay
irclescay inay Etersburgpay anday ethay aristocraticay Ussiansray uddenlysay ecamebay
eryvay oldbay. dray. Imsdaleday asway eptkay usybay ithway impatientay applicants.ay A“ay ewfay
eeksway ago,”ay aidsay Atherine,cay Obody“nay ouldway earhay ofay inoculation;ay utbay ownay
obodynay ancay aitway otay ebay accinatedvay. Itay ashay ecomebay ethay ashion.”fay

Ethay amaticdray exampleay ofay ethay Empressay idday ot,nay alas!ay utpay anay enday otay
allpoxsmay inay Ussiaray. Itay eantmay onlyay atthay ethay eir-apparenthay ofay ethay onethray
asway ownay immuneay anday ethay ynastyday asway otay isthay extentay assured.ay Itay eantmay
atthay aay ewfay ousandthay oblesnay anday eirthay amiliesfay ereway immune.ay Utbay ethay
astvay opulationpay ofay Ussiaray asway onay etterbay offay anthay ifay ethay elebratedcay
Imsdaleday adhay evernay isitedvay eirthay ountrycay. Erhapspay ethay eatestgray
ontributioncay ofay ishay isitvay adhay eenbay otay iminishday uperstitionsay amongay ethay
eastlay uperstitioussay elementay ofay ethay opulationpay. Ethay ostmay uperstitioussay
element,ay ethay easants,pay adhay evernay eardhay ofay Imsdaleday oray accinationvay. Enwhay
ethay allpoxsmay ame,cay eythay illstay edflay otay ethay Irgin,vay osewhay onder-workingway
ortraitspay unghay inay everyay apelchay. Enwhay ethay atientpay asway ootay illay otay ogay anday
ethay amilyfay ouldcay afforday otay aypay orfay it,ay ethay onder-workingway imageay ofay Ouray
Adylay ouldway ebay orrowedbay omfray ethay urchchay anday arriedcay otay ethay ufferer’ssay
edsidebay. Is,thay owever,hay asway areray. Usuallyay ethay icksay oneay asway ornebay intoay
ethay urchchay ybay ethay embersmay ofay ethay amilyfay anday aidlay atay ethay eetfay ofay ethay
Irginvay osewhay itypay eythay implored.ay

Osay itay asway inay ethay itycay ofay Oscowmay inay ethay autumnay ofay 1771ay. Orfay onthsmay ethay
agueplay adhay agedray anday avagedray ethay owntay. Ethay Empressay adhay entsay allay ethay
ysiciansphay eshay ouldcay ommandeer,cay ichwhay eantmay aay eatgray anymay. Oughthay
eshay ofessedpray otay atehay ysicians,phay eshay alwaysay eptkay aay argelay etinueray onay
allcay. Ethay ickenstray itycay asway unusuallyay ellway akentay arecay ofay uringday isthay
epidemic.ay Atherinecay adhay openeday ospitalshay orfay ethay ictimsvay ofay ethay agueplay.
Allay esethay innovationsay ailedfay otay inway ethay onfidencecay ofay ethay error-shakentay
opulationpay owhay adhay omehowsay otgay ethay ideaay atthay ethay ysiciansphay anday eirthay
ospitalshay adhay oughtbray ethay estpay otay Oscowmay. Eythay edflay omfray ethay edicalmay
enmay anday atheredgay atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay iconsay ithway eirthay invalids.ay Ethay
Irginvay atay ethay Arvarskyvay Ategay ecamebay oremay opularpay anthay ethay others,ay anday
ethay erribletay estilencepay aylay assedmay atay erhay eetfay ayday anday ightnay. Eshay
ecamebay ethay orstway entercay ofay ontagioncay inay ethay entireay ity,cay istributingday
ethay estpay otay undredshay ofay ewnay ictimsvay everyay ayday.

Ethay ysiciansphay ereway atay eirthay its’way end.ay Eythay aredday otnay aketay anyay adicalray
epsstay otay eventpray ethay ightenedfray eoplepay omfray oingday atwhay eythay easedplay.
Ethay ishopbay ofay Oscow,may Atherfay Ambrosius,ay asway anay enlighteneday anmay owhay
awsay atthay ethay ysiciansphay ereway elplesshay. Elyingray onay ishay authorityay asay aay
iest,pray ehay esolvedray otay adoptay aay esperateday emedyray. Ehay adhay ethay Arvarskyvay
Irginvay emovedray underay overcay ofay ightnay anday iddenhay away.ay Enwhay ethay ilgrimspay
arriveday inay ethay earlyay awn,day Ouray Adylay adhay anishedvay. Ethay anaceapay asway one,gay
anday Eathday oweredglay inay erhay acantvay ichenay. Atherfay Ambrosiusay elievedbay atthay
ethay authorityay ofay ethay Urchchay asway enoughay otay akemay esethay ear-drivenfay
umanhay eingsbay ubmitsay. Eythay ereway ishay ildrenchay owhay adhay alwaysay obeyed.ay Ehay
oughtthay at,thay asay oonsay asay eythay ewknay atthay ethay oodgay atherfay adhay oneday it,ay
eythay ouldway isperseday otay eirthay omeshay anday ethay agueplay otspay ouldway ebay ipedway
out.ay Utbay insteaday ofay ispersing,day eythay ereway uddenlysay eldedway intoay aay ob,may
aay owling,gray eatening,thray eeping,cray ood-thirstyblay ackpay. Asay ethay enacingmay
ingthay eganbay otay ove,may Ambrosiusay edflay omfray ishay omehay intoay ethay Emlin,kray anday
ooktay efugeray inay ethay Onskoyday Onasterymay. Onay ownday intoay ethay ellarcay ehay ed,flay
idinghay imselfhay inay ethay arkestday ornercay ehay ouldcay indfay. Ethay obmay amecay afteray
imhay anday invadeday ishay acredsay etreatray. Eythay oundfay imhay inay ethay arknessday anday
oretay imhay imblay omfray imblay.

Enwhay ethay Empressay eceivedray aay eportray ofay ethay agedy,tray eshay ealizedray atthay
ethay opulationpay ofay Oscowmay asway outay ofay andhay. Ethay agueplay agedray on.ay Ilewhay
ethay ictimsvay ultiplied,may ethay ospitalshay oodstay empty.ay Iotsray ereway addeday otay
allpoxsmay untilay itay eemedsay asay ifay ethay olday Uscovitemay itycay ustmay oonsay erishpay
underay itsay urdenbay ofay afflictions.ay Ethay Empressay adhay utbay oneay esourceray
eftlay anday atthay asway aay ilitarymay occupation.ay Eshay entsay Egorygray Orlovay ithway
aay egimentray otay aketay argechay ofay ethay owntay. Egorygray adhay eenbay accinatedvay
ybay Imsdaleday eethray yearsay efore,bay anday ethay actfay atthay ehay elievedbay
imselfhay immuneay avegay imhay extraordinaryay ouragecay anday effectivenessay onay
isthay occasion.ay Itay ustmay ebay admitteday atthay Orlovay asway otnay istinguishedday
ordinarilyay orfay ouragecay anday initiative.ay Ishay ecordray inay uttingpay ownday ethay
allpoxsmay inay Oscowmay isay exceptional.ay Orfay onceay ehay eemedsay otay aketay aay eaflay
omfray ethay ookbay ofay ishay otherbray Alexei.ay Ehay ulliedbay ethay opulacepay intoay
ompletecay ubmission,say osay atthay ethay yingday ouldcay atay eastlay ieday uietlyqay
undisturbeday ybay obsmay anday iotsray. Ehay askeday ethay ysiciansphay atwhay eythay
antedway otay avehay oneday anday agooneddray ethay eoplepay intoay actualay obedience.ay
Aay ertaincay Ermangay octorday isay aidsay otay avehay urnishedfay ethay anitarysay ideasay
ichwhay Egorygray Orlovay utpay intoay executionay anday ichwhay inallyfay elpedhay otay ipeway
outay ethay agueplay. Ateverwhay ethay ientificscay anmay aymay avehay ontributed,cay ethay
eroichay eatfay ofay Egorygray Orlovay isay unquestionable.ay Orfay onceay ehay ehavedbay
ikelay aay earlessfay anmay anday eservedday ishay istress’smay encomiums.ay

Ethay Empressay asway almostay iddygay ithway elightday. Eshay asway onay ongerlay obligeday
otay inventay easonsray orfay aisingpray erhay avoritefay inay erhay orrespondencecay.
Eshay otewray otay Incepray Enry,hay E“Thay aladymay atay Oscowmay ashay eenbay educedray
otay aay ifthfay ofay atwhay itay as,way anksthay otay ethay arecay anday intelligenceay ofay
Ountcay Orlov.ay Ehay as,hay esides,bay understooday owhay otay ubduesay ethay anaticalfay
iritspay otay obedience,ay otnay onlyay inay ethay attermay ofay iracles,may utbay ehay idday
otnay evenay ermitpay ethay eoplepay otay enteray ethay Urchchay otay earhay ass,may ecausebay
ouray urcheschay areay all;smay and,ay incesay everybodyay emainedray anding,stay ethay
essurepray atthay existsay ouldcay increaseay ethay infection.ay Uringday ethay ervicesay
ethay eoplepay ereway ademay otay emainray outsideay ethay urches--anchay orderay ichwhay
eythay ollowedfay otay ethay etterlay. Anotheray alutarysay egulationray arriedcay outay
espiteday ethay igots,bay asway ethay ohibitionpray againstay uryingbay inay ethay urcheschay
anday ethay emeteriescay ofay ethay itycay. Ethay Ountcay ademay ishay ownay ousehay intoay aay
ospital,hay ooktay oneay ofay inemay orfay ishay ownay use;ay afteray ichwhay everyay uarterqay
ofay ethay itycay ovidedpray one.”ay

Ethay Empressay eapedhay onorshay uponay erhay erohay enwhay ehay eturnedray otay Etersburgpay
inay Ecemberday. Eshay uiltbay aay iumphaltray archay inay ethay arkpay ofay Arskoeczay Elosay
ithway ethay inscription,ay O“Tay imhay owhay avedsay Oscowmay omfray ethay ague.”play Aay
edalmay asway uckstray otay ommemoratecay ishay avery,bray onay ichwhay Orlov’say ortraitpay
anday atthay ofay Urtiuscay ereway united.ay Ussia“Ray alsoay ashay uchsay ons,”say eadray ethay
inscription.ay


8ay

Ethay avorite’sfay arstay asway otay etsay inay oryglay. Enwhay ehay ubduedsay ethay Oscowmay
ague,play ehay adhay eenbay ivinglay ithway ishay Empressay orfay aay eriodpay ofay entay years.ay
Ethay enday ofay ethay yclecay adhay omecay. Atwhay adhay onegay ongwray etweenbay esethay otway
owhay adhay eenbay ikelay arriedmay eoplepay orfay osay onglay anday owhay adhay adhay eethray
ildrenchay ogether?tay Erethay areay oriesstay ofay Orlov’say infidelitiesay anday
Atherinecay ayssay atthay ehay iredtay ofay erhay. Apparentlyay eshay incerelysay elievedbay
afterwardsay atthay Egorygray esertedday er,hay althoughay itay asway onlyay ithway ethay
eatestgray ifficultyday atthay eshay ovedray ethay andsomehay uardsmangay omfray erhay
idesay. Eshay idday otnay esitatehay otay employay orcefay enwhay orcefay ecamebay ecessarynay.

Inay ethay eantime,may eforebay anday afteray Oscow,may Orlovay adhay ayedplay ishay artpay inay
ethay Urkishtay arsway oughthay itay asway ybay onay eansmay asay allantgay asay ishay Oscowmay
exploits.ay Ethay Empressay editedcray imhay ithway eatergray achievementsay inay ethay
Outhsay anthay othersay idday. Inay ethay ummersay afteray ethay allpox,smay eshay entsay imhay
otay ethay Ongresscay ofay Okshanifay asay erhay elegateday inay ethay eacepay egotiationsnay.
Erehay ehay aggeredsway aboutay inay aay iamond-studdedday ostumecay anday offendeday ethay
Urkstay ybay ishay igh-handedhay attitudeay osay atthay ethay egotiationsnay amecay otay
othingnay. Oriesstay aboutay Orlov’say onductcay atay isthay imetay uggestsay atthay ehay asway
aay anmay ofay idiosyncrasies.ay Afteray ethay attlebay ofay Esmetchay ehay oldtay Atherinecay
ithway aay uddershay atthay ethay aterway inay ethay arborhay asway oloredcay edray ithway ethay
oodblay ofay ethay Urkstay owhay adhay erishedpay. Otway yearsay ater,lay ishay iamondsday anday
ishay oliticalpay indiscretionsay atay Okshanifay indicateay atthay antasyphay asway
owinggray onay imhay. Ehay asway ometimessay ootay imidtay anday ometimessay ootay oldbay.

Esentlypray ehay asway ungedplay aightstray omfray ethay oudsclay otay ethay uttermostay
epthsday ybay aay isconcertingday iecepay ofay ewsnay. Ethay Empressay adhay akentay aay
ewnay overlay inay ishay absence.ay Aay youngay anmay amednay Assilchikovvay adhay eenbay
installeday inay Orlov’say apartments.ay Akingtay Enchfray eavelay ofay ishay oliticalpay
anday ilitarymay esponsibilities,ray Egorygray Orlovay artedstay atay onceay orfay
Etersburgpay. Otnay anymay erstsvay omfray ethay itycay ehay asway oppedstay ybay ethay ostmay
ironicalay ircumstancecay onceivablecay. Ethay Empressay adhay imhay uarantinedqay
inay ishay ownay alacepay atay Atchinagay. Erethay asway allpoxsmay inay ethay Outh,say eshay
aid,say anday ehay ustmay otnay ingbray itay otay Etersburgpay. Eshay adhay orgottenfay atthay
Orlovay asway immune.ay Eshay utshay imhay upay orfay ourfay eeks,way underay ilitarymay
uardsgay. Eshay alsoay utpay oubleday ockslay anday ilitarymay ostspay atay ethay oorsday ofay
ethay apartmentay occupieday ybay youngay Assilchikovvay. Allay ethay ilewhay eshay otewray
eassuringray otherlymay etterslay otay Orlovay anday entsay imhay eanclay ockssay anday
irtsshay. Eshay oweredshay imhay ithway ifts;gay anotheray alace,pay aay ousandthay oremay
erfs,say ethay itletay ofay Incepray ontributedcay otay ethay eaningway ocesspray. Atay astlay
itay asway uccessfulsay. Orlovay amecay otay Etersburgpay anday esentedpray imselfhay atay
ethay Empress’say eceptions,ray ookinglay onay ilewhay ishay ivalray erformedpay ethay
unctionsfay ichwhay ehay aloneay adhay erformedpay everay incesay Atherinecay adhay ecomebay
Empressay ofay Ussiaray. Ehay evenay overdiday ishay art,pay akingmay aay omradecay ofay
Assilchikovvay anday oinggay aboutay ithway imhay everywhere.ay

Egorygray Orlovay asway ownay astpay ortyfay yearsay ofay age.ay Utcay adriftay atay isthay age,ay
ethay exileay idday otnay owknay erewhay otay urntay. Atay irstfay ehay omfortedcay imselfhay
ithway omenway ofay ethay eets,stray owingshay imselfhay inay eirthay ocietysay inay ethay
icinityvay ofay ethay Alacepay. Ehay entway abroaday anday oastedbay anday uanderedsqay ikelay
ethay ashbucklersway atthay ehay asway. Ehay amecay omehay again;ay unghay orfay aay ortshay
imetay inay uspensesay anday inactionay anday enthay arriedmay ishay irstfay ousin,cay aay
irlgay ofay ineteennay arfay onegay inay uberculosistay. Ethay Enatesay issueday aay ukaseay
ommandingcay emthay otay eparate,say asay irstfay ousinscay ereway otnay alloweday otay arrymay
ybay ethay Ussianray Urchchay. Ethay Empressay ewknay exactlyay atwhay uchsay ukasesay ereway
orth;way eshay adhay erselfhay arriedmay aay ousincay enwhay eshay amecay otay Ussiaray. Asay
eadhay ofay ethay Urch,chay eshay issueday aay ispensationday otay Egorygray Orlovay anday ishay
idebray anday avegay emthay erhay essingblay. Eythay entway awayay otay Europeay erewhay eythay
anderedway omfray ecialistspay otay ecialist,spay yingtray otay indfay omesay oneay owhay
ouldcay estoreray ethay youngay ife’sway ealthhay. Utbay eadilystay eshay adedfay. Onglay
eforebay eshay ied,day Orlovay adhay eenbay eclaredday insane.ay

Orriblehay oriesstay areay oldtay ofay ishay astlay ays:day atthay ehay asway onstantlycay

Ethay iddle-agedmay Empressay ewgray enormouslyay outstay. Omesay ofay ethay othesclay

erhay ateplay.

Ethay ovelay elationshipsray ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ormfay ethay ostmay ascinatingfay
aspectay ofay erhay ifelay anday aracterchay. Orfay earlynay otway undredhay yearsay eshay ashay

Osteritypay owsknay erhay asay aay ooselay omanway.

Eshay ovedlay otay icturepay erselfhay inay eavenhay onversingcay ithway Onfuciuscay anday

eastlay adowshay ofay aay oubt,day avehay eenbay extremelyay appyhay anday elightedday. Atthay
osteritypay ouldshay inkthay ofay erhay asay aay emininefay Onday Uanjay ouldway ebay exactlyay
otay erhay astetay. Eshay oughtthay ofay erselfhay asay aay emininefay Onday Uan;jay or,ay

atthay utbay orfay ishay atalfay owesspray asay aay Onday Uanjay ehay ouldway avehay ucceededsay inay

Ethay umbernay ofay erhay overslay asway afteray allay onlyay irteenthay ifay eway ountcay erhay
usbandhay. Eythay ereway openlyay acknowledgeday anday onay egitimatelay onsortcay ouldcay
avehay enjoyeday aay ighterbray owglay ofay ublicitypay. Ethay Empressay idday otnay indulgeay
inay ecretsay Endezvous__ray oray episodicay affairs.ay Uringday ethay eriodpay enwhay eshay
asway eakingbray awayay omfray erhay en-years’tay unionay ithway Orlov,ay erethay ereway

urprisingsay anthay ethay ormalityfay ithway ichwhay eshay urroundedsay erhay avoritesfay
