amecay afterwardsay enwhay Atherinecay anday erhay elvetway overslay adhay onegay ethay ayway
ofay allay eshflay.

Ethay Empressay as,way inay isthay aspectay ofay erhay ifelay asay ellway asay others,ay aay omanway
ofay ewfay explanations.ay Utbay eshay otewray aay ortsay ofay apologiaay orfay erhay exsay ifelay
anday eftlay itay asay aay egacylay otay istory,hay insertingay itay inay ethay emoirsmay ichwhay
eshay otewray orfay ublicationpay. I“ay asway eryvay affectionate,”ay eshay aid,say And“ay
iftedgay ithway anay appearanceay ichwhay asway eryvay attractive.ay Iay easedplay atay ethay
irstfay ance,glay ithoutway employingay anyay artsay oray ainspay otay atthay end.ay Iay asway
eryvay ympatheticsay anday ossessedpay atherray aay asculinemay anthay aay emininefay
emperamenttay. Asay Iay avehay alreadyay aid,say Iay easedplay ethay enmay. Ethay irstfay alfhay
ofay ethay emptationtay asway erethay anday ethay econdsay ollowedfay ethay irstfay accordingay
otay umanhay ature;nay orfay otay empttay anday ebay emptedtay areay eryvay oseclay otay eachay
other.ay Anday ifay aay ongstray eelingfay isay addeday otay is,thay oweverhay onglystray ethay
inciplespray ofay oralitymay aymay ebay imbeddeday inay ethay ind,may oneay oesgay artherfay
anthay oneay ouldway ish;way and,ay evenay untilay ownay Iay oday otnay owknay owhay atthay isay
otay ebay eventedpray. Inay isthay ase,cay erhapspay absenceay ightmay ingbray aid;ay utbay
erethay areay ases,cay ituationssay inay ife,lay anday ircumstancescay ichwhay akemay
absenceay impossible.ay Owhay ancay oneay inay ethay idstmay ofay ourtcay ifelay eeflay away,ay
emoveray oneself,ay urntay aside?ay Atthay ouldway atay onceay attractay attentionay anday
ausecay alktay. Yes,ay ifay oneay annotcay emoveray oneself,ay othingnay isay arderhay inay ymay
opinionay anthay otnay otay yielday otay atthay ichwhay allures.ay Allay atthay isay aidsay otay
ethay ontrarycay isay ypocrisyhay anday ignoranceay ofay ethay umanhay earthay. Oneay oesday
otnay oldhay one’say earthay inay one’say and,hay anday itay oesday otnay obeyay ethay ommandscay
ofay eason.”ray

Isthay asway aay inceresay effortay onay ethay artpay ofay aay ixty-year-oldsay Empressay otay
ebay uthfultray anday andidcay aboutay erhay astpay. Asideay omfray ertaincay obviousay
isrepresentations,may uchsay asay ayingsay atthay eshay adhay anay attractiveay
appearanceay oughthay eshay idday otnay elievebay itay erself,hay eshay oughtthay atthay
eshay asway eakingspay ethay uthtray. Utbay oneay isay uckstray ybay ethay extraordinaryay
eaknessway ofay erhay efenseday. Aay omanway owhay ashay adhay elvetway overslay anday ashay
earnedlay onay oremay omfray ifelay anthay otay efendday erselfhay onay oralisticmay oundsgray
owsshay atthay eshay ashay emainedray unteachableay otay ethay astlay. Erhay explanationay
ofay erhay onductcay ightmay uitablysay ebay ivengay ybay aay irlgay ofay ifteenfay. Atherinecay
onceay aidsay ofay Iderotday atthay inay omesay espectsray ehay asway aay undredhay yearsay olday
anday inay othersay ehay asway onay oremay anthay entay. Itay asway aay iseway emarkray anday ouldcay
ebay equallyay ellway applieday otay erselfhay. Enwhay eshay iestray otay explainay ethay
irregularitiesay ofay erhay exsay ifelay ybay ayingsay atthay emptationtay ashay eenbay ootay
ongstray orfay erhay otay esistray eshay eaksspay asay ethay upilpay ofay Astorpay Agnerway. Itay
owsshay atthay erhay onductcay asway illstay ustjay asay uchmay ofay aay ysterymay otay erselfhay
asay itay asway otay anybodyay else.ay Eshay adhay earnedlay oweverhay oneay ingthay ichwhay
Astorpay Agnerway anday ethay ationalistsray ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay adhay otnay
aughttay er,hay anday atthay isay atthay ethay earthay oesday otnay obeyay ethay ommandscay ofay
easonray.

Oweverhay impulsiveay ethay Empressay aymay avehay eenbay inay ethay initialay agestay ofay aay
ovelay affair,ay eshay asway ockinglyshay ationalray inay ethay ayway atthay eshay evelopedday
it.ay Ikelay Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray eshay adhay aay errortay ofay enerealvay iseaseday utbay
eshay adhay aay esslay asceticay ethodmay ofay otectingpray erselfhay. Eshay equiredray ethay
opefulhay andidatecay otay ubmitsay imselfhay otay aay edicalmay examinationay atay ethay
andshay ofay dray. Ogerson,ray erhay Otchscay ysicianphay. Ehay asway enthay utpay oughthray
aay indkay ofay ordealay oray apprenticeshipay ybay Ountesscay Ucebray oray Incesspray
Otassovpray owhay ereway ownknay orfay eirthay unctionfay asay Es“lay eprouveuses.”ay Ifay
esethay experienceday adieslay ecommendedray ethay youngay anmay orfay ishay office,ay ehay
asway installeday inay ethay elegantay apartmentsay eparedpray orfay ishay eceptionray. Inay
ethay awerdray ofay ishay essing-tabledray ehay oundfay ethay enerousgay alarysay allotteday
otay ethay Empress’say Adjutantay Eneral,gay anday enthay eganbay orfay imhay aay ifelay ofay ethay
ostmay appallingay egularityray.

Atay entay o’clockay everyay orning,may ehay alledcay onay ethay Empress,ay anday atay entay
everyay eveningay ehay escorteday erhay otay erhay ivatepray amberschay. Enwhay eshay ovedray
out,ay ehay atsay esidebay er,hay anday onay allay occasionsay oodstay eadyray otay offeray ishay
arm.ay Ehay asway edicatedday otay ishay utiesday anday ivedlay inay ompletecay etirementray.
Afteray Egorygray Orlov,ay onenay ofay Atherine’scay overslay asway alloweday otay akemay
isitsvay oray eceiveray emthay. Onay Ultansay ouldcay avehay eenbay oremay arbitraryay ithway
ishay aremhay anthay Atherinecay ithway erhay avoritesfay. Eshay avishedlay esentspray anday
onorshay uponay em;thay erhay extravaganceay owardtay emthay ewknay onay oundsbay. Ethay
Englishay Ambassadoray Arris,hay owhay adhay aay alenttay orfay atistics,stay estimateday
atthay eshay entspay $190,000,000ay inay ashcay onay ethay enmay eshay eptkay. Ethay amountay
eemssay aggeringstay evenay orfay ouray ayday. Yetay itay asway otnay enough,ay ithway allay ethay
otheray erquisitespay added,ay otay olongpray ethay ondagebay ofay ethay ictimvay oremay
anthay otway oray eethray yearsay onay ethay average.ay Afteray Egorygray Orlov,ay eythay allay
escapeday inay oneay ayway oray anotheray atay ethay enday ofay aay eriodpay ofay aboutay isthay
urationday.

Assilchikov,vay ithway omwhay eshay arriedcay onay ethay ostmay erfunctorypay affairay eshay
everay ad,hay escribesday ishay ifelay ithway ethay Empressay us:thay I“ay asway othingnay oremay

uestsgay oray otay ogay out.ay Ifay Iay ademay aay equestray orfay anyoneay else,ay Iay eceivedray onay
answer.ay Ifay Iay okespay orfay yself,may itay asway ethay amesay. Enwhay Iay ishedway otay avehay
ethay orderay ofay Aintsay Anne,ay Iay okespay otay ethay Empressay aboutay it.ay Ethay extnay ayday
Iay oundfay aay irtythay ousandthay ubleray anknotebay inay ymay ocketpay. Inay isthay ay,way
eythay alwaysay oppedstay ymay outhmay anday entsay emay otay ymay oom.”ray

Itay ustmay ebay aidsay atthay Assilchikov’svay ourtshipcay asway obablypray ethay oorestpay
erformancepay ivengay ybay anyay ofay Atherine’scay overslay. Ethay onlyay oneay ofay

imarilypray otay elphay erhay eanway ethay Ountcay. Otnay atthay ethay Empressay asway awareay
atthay eshay asway ushingpay Orlovay outay ofay ishay armway estnay intoay aay oldcay ardhay orldway.
Onay ethay ontrary,cay eshay adhay otgay ethay ideaay atthay Orlovay intendeday otay esertday
erhay anday eshay idday otnay eanmay otay ebay eftlay inay ethay urchlay. Eshay alsoay oughtthay

Uriks,ray anday asway itterlybay isappointedday enwhay ethay affairay ovedpray oldcay. Erhay
omplaintscay ofay eirthay elationshipray ereway ullyfay asay ismalday asay ishay anday erhay

appearsay atthay Otiomkinpay adhay eardhay oriesstay aboutay ishay edecessors,pray ichwhay
owsshay atthay ossipgay adhay alreadyay egunbay otay exaggerateay ethay umbernay ofay ethay
Empress’say overslay. Otay eassureray im,hay ethay Empressay otewray aay iefbray onfessioncay
inay ichwhay eshay oldtay imhay allay ethay actsfay aboutay erhay eviouspray elationshipsray.

Ethay Empress’say istlay eginsbay ithway Ergeisay Altikovsay anday ellstay owhay eshay
accepteday imhay onay ethay adviceay ofay Adamemay Oglokovchay anday owhay Adamemay Oglokovchay

Ama.”may Isthay uddensay eepingpay outay ofay Ergei’ssay amamay omfray ehindbay ethay enesscay
ofay Atherine’scay ifelay akesmay aay ividvay impression.ay Ethay adylay asway alreadyay anay
invalid,ay itay eems,say owhay ulledpay ethay ingsstray ofay istory,hay ustjay onceay anday
ilently,say anday iedday.

Ethay extnay overlay amednay inay Atherine’scay onfessioncay isay ethay Ingkay ofay Olandpay.
E“Hay asway amiable,”ay ayssay ishay istress,may And“ay asway ovedlay omfray 1755ay otay 1761ay.

Incepray Egorygray Egorevich,gray otay omwhay ell-meaningway eoplepay alledcay ymay

omfray itay ethay implesay onclusioncay atthay ithway isthay owledgeknay Iay ouldcay onay

otay akemay outay ofay esperationday aay oicechay ybay ancechay Assilchikov)(Vay. Uringday
isthay ime,tay yesay untilay isthay onth,may Iay avehay ettedfray oremay anthay Iay ancay aysay
anday evernay oremay anthay enwhay othersay ereway atisfiedsay. Everyay expressionay ofay

angryay anday eftlay emay inay eacepay. Utbay ishay endernesstay orcedfay emay otay eep.”way

Ethay onfessioncay endsay orfay ethay imetay eingbay ithway Egorygray Otiomkin,pay ethay
overlay otay omwhay itay isay addresseday anday ofay omwhay eshay egsbay orgivenessfay orfay

ee,thray onlyay elievebay ethay uthtray. Odgay owsknay atthay Iay ooktay emthay otnay outay ofay

ithoutway ove...lay. Utbay Iay itewray youay atthay eedlesslynay orfay accordinglyay youay
illway ovelay oray illway otnay ishway otay ogay awayay otay ethay army,ay outay ofay earfay atthay
Iay ouldcay orgetfay you.ay Utbay eallyray Iay oday otnay elievebay atthay Iay ouldcay ebay osay
oolishfay. Ifay youay ouldway attachay emay otay yourselfay orever,fay enthay owshay emay asay

uth.”tray


3ay

Otiomkinpay ustmay avehay understooday ishay ady’slay ishway anday atisfiedsay itay inay ishay
ay,way orfay Atherinecay ovedlay imhay ifteenfay years.ay Eshay adhay ovedlay erhay irstfay
Egorygray entay yearsay eforebay eshay astcay imhay off;ay erhay econdsay Egorygray eldhay
irstfay aceplay inay erhay affectionsay orfay aay ongerlay eriodpay. Eshay adhay aay egreeday ofay
aithfulnessfay ithway ichwhay eshay ashay evernay eenbay editedcray. Otnay atthay Otiomkinpay
ingeredlay inay ethay eremtay allay isthay imetay. Asay officialay avoritefay anday ublicpay
escortay ehay astedlay onlyay otway years.ay Ehay asway ootay estlessray orfay aptivitycay anday
ehay ouldcay otnay earbay otay ebay aredstay at,ay aay artpay ichwhay ethay andsomehay Orlovay adhay
ayedplay otay erfectionpay. Aay uriouscay arrangementay asway eachedray etweenbay ethay
anderingway avoritefay anday ethay Empress.ay Otiomkinpay entway awayay otay Ovgorod,nay
otay ethay Urkishtay ars,way otay ethay Imea;cray ehay asway ivendray itherhay anday itherthay
acrossay ethay endlessay ainsplay ofay Ussiaray ybay ishay avingcray estlessray iritspay.
Ethay Empress,ay eftlay alone,ay omethingsay atthay eshay ouldcay otnay ear,bay ooktay oneay
overlay afteray ethay otheray inay ishay aceplay. Utbay alwaysay Otiomkinpay eturnedray anday
ompelledcay erhay otay isposeday ofay emthay. Atay aay ordway omfray im,hay eshay urnedtay emthay
out.ay

Accordingay otay ethay egend,lay Otiomkinpay ecamebay aay ortsay ofay andererpay otay ishay
adylay anday ethay entlemengay omwhay ehay osechay orfay erhay urvivedsay asay onglay asay eythay
emainedray inay ishay oodgay acesgray. Atwhay eallyray appenedhay asway atthay ethay Empressay
osechay eachay ewnay overlay orfay erselfhay anday ertainlycay ithway ethay opehay atthay ehay
ouldway eesay erhay oughthray. Ut,bay afteray aay yearay oray o,tway ethay unmanageableay
Otiomkinpay ouldway uddenlysay arriveay onay ethay enescay anday urntay ethay ascalray out.ay
Ishay appearanceay ouldway ebay ecededpray ybay eateningthray etterslay aboutay atwhay ehay
asway oinggay otay oday. Orfay instance,ay ethay igbay ondblay Yermalovay atsay uneasilyay inay
ishay armchairay oneay ayday ecausebay Otiomkinpay adhay ittenwray erhay atthay ehay asway
omingcay otay Etersburgpay otay endsay At“thay itewhay igger”nay away.ay Otiomkinpay amecay
anday ethay itewhay iggernay entway. Atherinecay urnedtay erhay attentionay otay arkday
overslay anday osechay otway ofay em,thay Amonovmay anday Ubovzay.

Amonovmay ovedpray otay ebay oneay ofay erhay ewfay istakesmay. Ehay asway aay ormalnay anmay owhay
ellfay inay ovelay ithway oneay ofay ethay adieslay ofay ethay ourtcay ofay ishay ownay ageay anday
arriedmay erhay. Itay asway ethay onlyay imetay atthay erhay Ajestymay asway everay actuallyay
esertedday ybay oneay ofay erhay overs,lay unlessay Altikovsay aymay ebay aidsay otay avehay
oneday o,say anday itay asway aay atteringshay experience.ay Eshay osechay anotheray arkday
an,may Atoplay Ubov,zay anday iedtray otay aingay orfay imhay ethay approvalay ofay ethay
absenteeay Otiomkinpay. Ethay ittlelay ackblay oy,bay eshay ote,wray asway earninglay ast,fay
entsay ishay ovelay otay Apa,pay anday osay on.ay Utbay Otiomkinpay otewray ackbay atthay ehay asway
eturningray otay Etersburgpay O“tay avehay aay oothtay out,”ay ichwhay adhay anay ominousay
ayplay onay Ubov’szay ame,nay ichwhay eansmay Ooth.”“tay Ethay onflictcay overay Ubov’szay
emovalray oughtbray otay anay enday ethay elationray etweenbay Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay
ichwhay adhay astedlay orfay ifteenfay years.ay Otiomkinpay asway otnay ableay otay endsay isthay
ivalray away.ay

Ethay overslay owhay ollowedfay Otiomkinpay ereway Avadovsky,zay Oritch,zay Orsakov,kay
Anskoy,lay Yermalov,ay Amonov,may anday inallyfay Ubovzay. Exceptay orfay Anskoy,lay owhay
ied,day anday Amonov,may owhay arried,may Otiomkinpay adhay arbitrarilyay ismissedday allay
ofay emthay oray elievedbay atthay ehay adhay osay ismissedday emthay. Enwhay ehay ouldcay onay
ongerlay oday atthay ehay ealizedray atthay ishay adylay adhay iscardedday imhay orfay oodgay. Ehay
ecame,bay asay Egorygray Orlovay adhay ecomebay ifteenfay yearsay efore,bay anay exileay omfray
ethay armway estnay atthay adhay elteredshay imhay orfay osay ong,lay and,ay ikelay Egorygray
Orlov,ay ehay ouldcay otnay urvivesay ishay anishmentbay.

Otiomkinpay adhay aay ascinatingfay ersonalitypay. Ehay asway otnay ikablelay utbay ehay
eizedsay ethay imaginationay anday apturedcay ethay attention.ay Egendlay ashay icturedpay
imhay asay aay eatgray Ussianray utebray owhay ankdray eavilyhay anday oresway outrageously.ay
Oubtlesslyday ehay ore,sway asay everyay Ussianray earssway asay aturallynay asay ehay
eathesbray. Utbay ehay asway otnay aay unkarddray anday ehay asway otnay aay utebray. Ehay asway
aay ightened,fray imidtay are,hay ithway aay ertaincay eativecray eniusgay ichwhay amecay
oughthray erehay anday erethay ithoutway everay evelopingday eryvay arfay inay anyay
irectionday. Ehay ouldcay ebay aay ealray oetpay onay occasion,ay althoughay ehay isay ownknay
asay ethay authoray ofay onlyay oneay ong,say anday alsoay aay ealray eneralgay onay occasion,ay
althoughay ehay embledtray atay ethay oundsay ofay unsgay. Ethay ostmay ontradictorycay
ingsthay avehay eenbay aidsay aboutay imhay ecausebay ethay ostmay ontradictorycay ingsthay
ereway uetray aboutay imhay.

Ehay adhay ethay all,tay ell-builtway igurefay ichwhay Atherinecay equiredray ofay erhay
overslay utbay otherwiseay ishay appearanceay asway otnay epossessingpray. Ehay adhay
ostlay anay eyeay anday itay isay aracteristicchay ofay Otiomkin’spay eticenceray atthay
obodynay ewknay enwhay oray owhay ethay accidentay adhay appenedhay. Otiomkinpay imselfhay
evernay okespay ofay itay utbay ishay eelingsfay onay ethay ubjectsay aymay ebay imagineday
omfray ethay actfay atthay enwhay aay one-eyeday anmay asway entsay otay imhay oneay ayday ithway
aay essage,may Otiomkinpay uckstray imhay ownday. Ariousvay oriesstay areay oldtay aboutay
ethay osslay ofay ishay eye.ay Alexeiay Orlovay isay aidsay otay avehay utpay itay outay inay aay
ugglestray overay aay amegay ofay illiardsbay. Anotheray orystay oldtay isay atthay Otiomkinpay
imselfhay estroyedday itay ecausebay itay adhay aay emish,blay obablypray aay uintsqay.
Itay isay oubtfulday etherwhay Atherinecay erselfhay ewknay ethay uetray ausecay ofay ethay
accident.ay Inay itingwray aboutay Otiomkin,pay eshay assedpay overay ishay andicaphay
asay ifay itay idday otnay exist.ay Anday yetay eshay ademay oneay indirectay eferenceray inay
erhay emoirsmay. Inay eakingspay ofay ethay ignoranceay ofay ethay Ussianray ourt,cay eshay
emarkedray atthay evenay anay ordinarilyay intelligentay ersonpay atay isthay ourtcay asway
ikelay aay one-eyeday anmay amongay ethay indblay. Anotheray eculiaritypay ofay Otiomkin’spay
ichwhay eshay assedpay overay inay ilencesay asway aay ervousnay erkingjay ofay ishay ace,fay aay
indkay ofay acialfay Ic__tay ichwhay eshay adhay onceay etestedday inay Ountcay Uvalovshay.
Oneay ait,tray owever,hay eshay idday eferray otay ometimessay inay aay estingjay onetay anday
atthay asway ethay ayway ehay onstantlycay awedgnay ishay inger-nailsfay. Ethay estray ofay ishay
eculiaritiespay eshay assedpay overay inay ilencesay.

Otiomkinpay asway ynical,cay orose,may anday ilent;say aay istful,way orturedtay eaturecray
owhay asway obligeday otay akemay eoplepay afraiday ofay imhay inay orderay otay oncealcay ishay
imiditytay owardtay others.ay Eythay alledcay imhay Yclops”“Cay anday ishay imposingay
igurefay idday otnay eliebay ethay eferenceray otay ethay one-eyeday iantgay. Erhapspay ethay
originalay Yclopscay alsoay asway asay ensitivesay anday earfulfay atay ethay orecay asay asway
ethay awe-inspiringay Otiomkinpay. Egendlay ashay ademay aay eatgray ealday ofay ethay iddlemay
yllablesay ofay ishay ame,nay Iom,”“tay ichwhay eansmay ark,day anday ashay ervedsay otay
accentuateay ethay omanticray icturepay ofay Otiomkinpay asay aay illainvay anday aay erohay.

Ikelay Azumovskyray owhay adhay eenbay ethay avoritefay anday ethay eputedray usbandhay ofay
Empressay Elisabeth,ay Otiomkinpay asway aay Outherner,say aay Ukrainian.ay Ethay enmay
ofay ishay amilyfay adhay ollowedfay eitheray aay ilitarymay oray aay oisteredclay ifelay.
Ishay atherfay asway anay obscureay aptaincay anday anay uncle,ay owhay adhay isenray otay ethay
ankray ofay olonel,cay etiredray omfray ethay armyay otay enteray aay onasterymay. Egorygray
Otiomkinpay eversedray ishay uncle’say oursecay. Ehay irstfay ecamebay aay onkmay oray almostay
ecamebay one,ay avinghay entspay everalsay yearsay inay eparationpray avellingtray omfray
oneay onasterymay otay ethay other.ay Ehay asway ellway ersedvay inay ethay eologythay ofay
ethay Eekgray Urchchay anday asway extremelyay uperstitioussay. Ishay orthodoxyay asway
anotheray aspectay ofay erhay overlay ichwhay Atherine,cay owhay idedpray erselfhay onay
eingbay aay ee-thinker,fray idday otnay ikelay otay expose.ay Uringday ethay irstfay yearay
atthay eshay ivedlay ithway im,hay eythay ademay aay ilgrimagepay oughthray ethay olday Ussianray
oistersclay ogethertay. Itay appenedhay atthay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray asway ueday otay
aypay aay isitvay otay Atherinecay uringday esethay onths,may utbay eshay otewray askingay imhay
otay ostponepay ishay isitvay untilay ethay ollowingfay year.ay Usuallyay eshay ikedlay otay
avehay oreignfay uestsgay accompanyay erhay onay erhay avels,tray utbay isthay imetay eshay idday
otnay ishway otay ombinecay ethay Otestantpray incepray anday ethay Eekgray eologianthay inay
oneay eligiousray ilgrimagepay.

Upay otay ethay ageay ofay irty-five,thay enwhay ehay ecamebay ethay avoritefay ofay ethay
Empress,ay Otiomkinpay eemssay otay avehay adhay onay ovelay affairsay anday onay ideaay ofay
arriagemay. Ehay asway eeplyday attacheday otay ishay ister,say om,whay ithway erhay ivefay
aughters,day Atherinecay eptkay aboutay ethay ourtcay. Ithway oneay ofay ishay ieces,nay
Ountesscay Anicky,bray Otiomkinpay asway especiallyay intimate.ay Afteray ehay eftlay
ethay Empress,ay isthay iecenay accompanieday imhay everywhere.ay Itay asway asay if,ay ikelay
Atherine,cay ehay asway orbidlymay afraiday ofay eingbay eftlay alone,ay anday Ashinkasay
Anickybray asway obligeday otay ebay alwaysay ithway imhay. Oneay ofay ethay andalsscay aboutay
Eneralgay Otiomkinpay asway at,thay insteaday ofay allopinggay overay ethay attlefieldbay
onay aay arway orsehay ikelay Eneralgay Uvarov,say ehay usuallyay appeareday ivingdray alongay
inay aay ibitkakay ithway Ashinkasay atay ishay idesay. Inay isthay ate,stay evertheless,nay
ehay anagedmay otay overcay aay eatgray ealday ofay ound,gray orfay ewfay Ussiansray avelledtray
artherfay oray oremay iftlysway anthay idday Eneralgay Otiomkinpay. Anday alwaysay ishay
evotedday iecenay asway earnay atay andhay. Owhay Ashinkasay oundfay imetay otay arrymay
anday avehay ildren,chay asay eshay id,day isay ardhay otay explain.ay Itay ashay eenbay aidsay
atthay erhay elationsray ithway erhay uncleay ereway otnay aboveay eproachray. Ifay itay asway
uetray atthay aay ysicalphay intimacyay existed,ay erethay ouldway avehay eenbay othingnay
ockingshay inay ethay ircumstancescay otay ethay Ussianray Empressay owhay adhay onceay
ontemplatedcay arriagemay ithway erhay Uncleay Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay anday okespay inay
aterlay ifelay almostay egretfullyray ofay ethay unfulfilleday engagement.ay

Otiomkinpay adhay eenbay oneay ofay ethay originalay onspiratorscay owhay adhay elpedhay otay
akemay Atherinecay ethay Empress.ay Ehay adhay iddenray otay Eterhofpay inay erhay aintray
onay atthay itewhay ightnay inay 1762ay enwhay eshay eizedsay ethay Arczay anday imprisoneday
imhay. Ehay adhay eenbay oneay ofay ethay uardsmengay eftlay inay argechay ofay ethay ex-Czaray
atay Opsha,ray anday ehay adhay eenbay esentpray atay Eter’spay eathday. Alexeiay Orlov’say
etterlay absolvesay imhay omfray allay esponsibilityray orfay ethay urdermay. Ethay orstway
atthay ancay ebay aidsay ofay imhay inay isthay onnectioncay isay atthay ithway anymay others,ay
owhay ereway ikewiselay otnay amed,blay ehay alsoay asway esentpray. Ethay Empressay idday
otnay orgetfay imhay uringday ethay extnay entay years,ay orfay eshay urtheredfay ishay areercay
ybay endingsay imhay ithway aay etterlay otay Eneralgay Azumovsky,ray owhay employeday imhay
inay ethay Urkishtay arsway. Ishay icturepay aylay ormantday inay erhay indmay oughthray
allay isthay imetay untilay itay eganbay otay aketay onay anay increaseday ividnessvay ybay
omparisoncay ithway ethay actualay esencepray ofay aay Assilchikovvay osewhay aressescay
ademay erhay eepway. Ethay oriesstay ofay Otiomkin’spay ooingway ivegay imhay editcray orfay anay
amountay ofay initiativeay ichwhay ehay idday otnay avehay. Inay Atherine’scay onfession,cay
addresseday otay Otiomkin,pay eshay ayssay atthay eshay eliberatelyday ecalledray imhay otay
Etersburg,pay ereaswhay ethay urrentcay orystay ellstay owhay Otiomkinpay emedschay otay ebay
entsay otay ethay Ittlelay Othermay ithway aay aintingpay anday aay essagemay anday owhay enwhay ehay
otgay erethay ehay impetuouslyay ooedway erhay. Ethay econdsay orystay isay ethay oneay ichwhay
ethay Empressay ouldway avehay uchmay eferredpray otay avehay usay elievebay adhay erhay ownay
atementsstay ofay atwhay ooktay aceplay otnay eakenedway itsay edibilitycray.

En“Thay amecay aay ertaincay ero,”hay eshay otewray. Is“Thay erohay as,way oughthray ishay
ervicessay anday ishay enduringay enderness,tay osay onderfulway atthay asay oonsay asay
eoplepay eardhay ofay ishay arrivalay eythay eganbay otay aysay atthay ehay oughtay otay emainray
erehay. Eythay idday otnay owknay ofay oursecay atthay eway adhay ummonedsay imhay ecretlysay
ybay aay etter,lay utbay ithway ethay ecretsay intentionay afteray ishay arrivalay otnay otay
oceedpray uiteqay indlyblay utbay otay investigateay etherwhay atthay inclinationay
existeday ofay ichwhay Ucebray adhay okenspay anday ichwhay anymay adhay onglay uspected;say
atthay is,ay ethay indkay ofay inclinationay ichwhay Iay ishedway atthay ehay ouldshay ave.”hay

Itay isay otnay ifficultday otay icturepay ethay impulsiveay Atherinecay ittingsay ownday
otay erhay iting-tablewray oneay inefay orningmay otay enpay ethay etterlay ichwhay oughtbray
Otiomkinpay otay Etersburgpay asay astfay asay aay ibitkakay ouldcay arrycay imhay. Ethay imageay
ofay ethay ark,day orosemay an,may itingbay ishay ailsnay anday oweringglay atay ethay orld,way
ichwhay adhay eptslay osay onglay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay ool,pay adhay atay astlay isenray otay
ethay urfacesay anday ownay oatedflay erethay ithway aay arpshay ommandingcay ividnessvay.
Otiomkin’spay imetay adhay omecay. Ethay Empressay atsay ownday anday addresseday otay ethay
erohay osewhay imageay ummonedsay erhay ethay etterlay ichwhay asway otay ebay ethay akingmay ofay
ishay ortunefay. Ehay amecay otay Etersburgpay anday orfay otway yearsay ehay emainedray inay
oseclay attendanceay onay ethay Empress.ay Ehay ayedplay ishay artpay inay ethay Ermitagehay
atheringsgay inay ishay ownay eculiarpay ayway. Ehay asway aay entriloquistvay anday ouldcay
imitateay otay erfectionpay ethay oicesvay ofay ariousvay animals.ay Ehay ouldcay eproduceray
ithway uncannyay accuracyay ethay oicevay ofay Atherinecay erselfhay utteringay omesay
aracteristicchay emarkray. Isthay icktray ugelyhay elightedday ethay Empressay owhay adhay
alsoay aay iftgay orfay imicrymay. Inay eturn,ray eshay ouldway aterwaulcay aay uetday ithway ethay
Incesspray Ashkovday o,whay ikelay ethay Empress,ay asway unableay otay arrycay aay unetay.

Illustration:[ay ATHERINEcay EtHay EATgRay

Ainted_Pay ybay Ericsenay orfay Aronbay Imsdale_]day

Otiomkinpay asway aay emi-Tartarsay inay ishay abitshay. Ovenlyslay anday indolent,ay
ehay ouldway ielay onay ishay ouchcay orfay aysday adclay onlyay inay aay alatkhay. Inay ethay
amesay informalay abithay ehay ouldway isitvay ethay Empress,ay otay ethay orrorhay ofay ethay
Europeansay anday ethay astonishmentay evenay ofay ethay Ussiansray. Otiomkinpay anciedfay
imselfhay inay isthay informalay ostume,cay overay anday eyondbay ethay actfay atthay ethay
azylay undressay uitedsay ethay inertiaay ofay ishay emperamenttay. Ethay ooselay alatkhay
asway otnay unlikeay ethay onasticmay oberay ichwhay ehay adhay onceay annedplay otay earway anday
ichwhay ownay anday en,thay enwhay ingsthay entway ongwray etweenbay imselfhay anday ishay
imperialay istress,may ehay oughtthay ofay uttingpay onay again.ay Ehay asway iendlyfray ithway
allay iests,pray ithway omwhay ehay entspay uchmay ime,tay ot,nay itay appears,ay osay uchmay inay
eologicalthay iscussion,day oughthay ehay isay aidsay otay avehay excelleday inay is,thay asay
inay ard-playingcay anday ettingbay. Ishay evotionday otay ethay Urchchay isay eensay inay
ethay ayway atthay ehay ouldcay andstay otionlessmay anday ecorousday allay ayday ilewhay assmay
asway eingbay aidsay. Ehay asway otnay ysicallyphay ootay azylay orfay isthay effortay althoughay
otherwiseay osay indolentay atthay ethay ormalitiesfay ofay Ussianray ourtcay ifelay ereway
ootay arduousay orfay imhay.

Illustration:[ay ATHERINEcay EtHay EATgRay

Om_Fray aay aintingpay ybay Oslin_]ray

Anymay indictivevay outréay ortraitspay ofay Atherine’scay overlay avehay eenbay awndray
orfay osteritypay. Ostmay ofay emthay ereway oducedpray ybay Enchfray iterswray owhay ouldcay
otnay understanday aay anmay o,whay otwithstandingnay allay ethay ichesray atthay ishay
istressmay acedplay atay ishay isposal,day eferredpray otay ivelay asay aay Yzantinebay enwhay
ehay ightmay avehay ivedlay asay aay Arisianpay. Otay ethay ophisticatedsay Enchfray owhay
eftlay ostmay ofay ethay ittenwray accountsay ofay Ussiaray inay ethay eighteenthay entury,cay
Otiomkinpay asway arcelyscay aay Ussian;ray ehay asway almostay anay Asiatic.ay Ethay igbay
one-eyeday anmay owhay awledspray onay aay ouchcay allay ayday inay aay ightbray essing-gown,dray
ayingplay ithway aay andfulhay ofay unsetay ewelsjay oray isteninglay otay Utarch’splay Iveslay
ichwhay omesay oneay eadray aloud,ay asway aay angestray eaturecray owhay adhay eliberatelyday
urnedtay ishay ackbay onay ethay ivilizationcay ofay Ouislay xVay anday Ancefray anday owhay
yearneday onlyay otay eviveray ethay ancientay oriesglay ofay Alexanderay ethay Eatgray anday
Onstantinoplecay.

Ethay eremay amenay ofay Alexanderay asway anay inspirationay otay Atherinecay anday
Otiomkin:pay itay adhay eenbay ethay amenay ofay Otiomkin’spay atherfay anday ecamebay ethay
amenay ofay Atherine’scay andsongray. Itay ymbolizedsay ethay agnificentmay eamdray
ichwhay uniteday emthay. Ogethertay eythay ouldway ogay otay Onstantinoplecay. Oneay ayday
Otiomkinpay urstbay orth,fay asay ehay awledspray onay ishay ouchcay anday istenedlay otay
Utarch’splay Ives,lay If“ay anyoneay ouldshay omecay odaytay anday elltay emay atthay Iay
ouldshay evernay ogay ither,thay Iay ouldway ootshay yselfmay oughthray ethay ead.”hay Inay aay
imilarsay ood,may oughthay esslay iolent,vay ethay atiricalsay Empressay eatened,thray inay
asecay ethay Edessway ombardedbay erhay outay ofay Etersburg,pay otay etsay upay erhay apitalcay
inay Onstantinoplecay. Ifay eshay idday otnay eviveray ethay Yzantinebay Empire,ay eshay
opedhay atthay Onsieurmay Alexander,ay erhay andson,gray ouldway oneay ayday eviveray itay inay
erhay eadstay. Uniteday inay eirthay everishfay eam,dray ethay Empressay anday erhay overlay
ovedray inay erfectpay unisonay owardtay eirthay ommoncay opehay. Ogethertay eythay ouldway
oneay ayday enteray Onstantinoplecay. Orfay anymay yearsay eythay assionatelypay elievedbay
it;ay anday enwhay eythay onay ongerlay elievedbay it,ay eythay iedday.


4ay

Otiomkin,pay aay uetray onsay ofay Ukrainia,ay asway aay oubadourtray. Ehay omposedcay aay ongsay
otay ishay adylay ichwhay ecamebay aay opularpay yriclay. As“ay oonsay asay Iay eheldbay ee,thay Iay
oughtthay ofay eethay alone;ay ythay ovelylay eyesay aptivatedcay e,may yetay Iay embledtray otay
aysay Iay ovedlay. Otay ee,thay ovelay ubjectssay everyay eart,hay anday enchainsay emthay ithway
ethay amesay arlandsgay. Ut,bay ahay eaven,hay atwhay aay ormenttay otay ovelay oneay otay omwhay
Iay areday otnay eclareday it!ay Oneay owhay ancay evernay ebay inemay. Uelcray ods,gay ywhay avehay
youay ivengay erhay uchsay arms?chay Or,ay ywhay idday youay exaltay erhay osay igh?hay Ywhay idday
youay estineday emay otay ovelay erhay anday erhay alone,ay erhay osewhay acredsay amenay illway
evernay asspay ymay ips,lay osewhay armingchay imageay illway evernay uitqay ymay eart.”hay

Atherine’scay urlishchay overlay asway otnay oorpay inay ancyfay. Ehay ouldcay offeray
ibutestray otay ishay adylay owingshay anay imaginationay ofay onay eanmay order.ay Asay ehay
omposedcay yricslay inay erhay onor,hay ehay ouldcay alsoay omposecay ageantspay anday otheray
exhibitionsay ofay eatgray eautybay anday impressiveness.ay Ethay amousfay ourneyjay otay
ethay Imeacray asway aay agnificentmay ocessionalpray. Otiomkin’spay arrangementay
ofay isthay iptray asway ethay orkway ofay aay oetpay anday aay amatistdray asay ellway asay atthay
ofay aay oliticianpay anday aay eneralgay. Itay employeday allay ishay alentstay atay once.ay
Ishay ontrivancecay ofay effectsay alongay ethay ayway ashay eenbay isunderstoodmay.
Encehay ethay egendlay ofay ethay Otiomkin“Pay illages,”vay ichwhay accordingay otay ishay
etractorsday ereway eremay aintedpay açadesfay overlookingay ethay Olgavay anday illedfay
ithway easantspay anday attlecay owhay adhay avelledtray onay ootfay anymay undredshay ofay
erstsvay inay orderay otay ompletecay ethay icturepay. Atthay istoryhay ouldshay avehay
amedblay insteaday ofay aisingpray Otiomkinpay orfay ishay artistryay owsshay owhay ittlelay
ishay issionmay inay ifelay anday ishay areshay inay Atherine’scay andiosegray emesschay avehay
eenbay understood.ay Othbay ofay emthay elievedbay atthay ethay oadray otay Onstantinoplecay
ouldway oneay ayday ebay inedlay ithway osperouspray illagesvay anday atthay ethay emporarytay
ettlementssay ownthray upay atay osay uchmay expenseay alongay ethay outeray ouldway atay onay
eatgray istanceday inay ethay uturefay ecomebay ermanentpay establishments.ay Onay oneay
asway eceivedday ybay ethay emonstrationday ofay osperity,pray unlessay erhapspay itay asway
Otiomkinpay imself,hay owhay alf-wayhay elievedbay inay ethay ectacularspay owthgray ofay
opulationpay induceday uddenlysay ybay ishay ownay imaginationay aideday ybay Atherine’scay
ublesray. Incepray eday Igne,lay owhay accompanieday ethay Empressay onay erhay Imeancray
ourney,jay iedtray otay orrectcay ethay orystay atay ethay outset.ay Ey“Thay avehay alreadyay
eadspray aay idiculousray eport,”ray ehay otewray otay Ance,fray At“thay illagesvay ofay
ardboardcay avehay eenbay istributedday alongay ouray outeray atay intervalsay ofay aay
undredhay eagues,lay atthay aintingspay ofay esselsvay anday annonscay anday avalrycay
ithoutway orseshay areay isplayed.”day Ethay Incepray ersistedpay inay ishay effortsay
otay endsay outay otay Europeay aay uetray escriptionday ofay ethay Imeancray ourney;jay utbay
ehay aredfay asay allay onesthay anday unpicturesqueay ournalistsjay areay estinedday otay
arefay. Eoplepay eferredpray otay elievebay inay Otiomkin’spay ardboardcay illagesvay anday
inay ethay erfidypay ofay eirthay ontrivercay owhay employeday inay eirthay onstructioncay
illionsmay ofay ethay Empress’say ownay ublesray inay orderay otay eceiveday ethay Empress.ay
Ethay orystay isay illstay oldtay otay owshay otay atwhay efariousnay epthsday Otiomkinpay asway
illingway otay escendday. Atwhay itay eallyray owsshay isay atthay ehay asway aay aringday artistay
owhay esignedday anday executeday andiosegray effects.ay

Ethay Empress’say olewhay Imeancray iptray asway aay eatricalthay enterpriseay ithway
Otiomkinpay asay author,ay oducer,pray anday actor.ay Itay ollowedfay oonsay afteray ethay
irthbay ofay erhay otway andsonsgray omwhay eshay atay irstfay annedplay otay aketay ithway erhay
oughthay eshay abandoneday ethay ideaay eforebay ethay artstay asway ademay. Ethay urposepay
ofay ethay ourneyjay asway ostensiblyay otay inspectay ethay orkway ofay Eneralgay Otiomkinpay
asay administratoray inay ethay Outhsay. Itsay actualay intentionay asway olitical,pay
otay econnoitreray ethay ayway otay ethay Orientay ilewhay ostilitieshay etweenbay ethay
Ussiansray anday ethay Urkstay ereway inay abeyance.ay Onay oneay understooday isthay indkay ofay
oliticalpay amegay etterbay anthay Otiomkinpay anday ishay istressmay. Ostentationay asway
ethay eathbray ofay eirthay ostrilsnay anday orfay onceay eythay adhay eirthay illfay ofay it.ay
Ethay Empressay anday erhay entourageay oceededpray ownday ethay Ieperdnay inay aay eetflay ofay
entytway oats,bay eachay ofay ichwhay asway amednay orfay omesay ibutarytray ofay ethay eamstray.
Atherine’scay ownay esselvay asway alledcay ethay Ieperdnay anday asway ittedfay outay ithway
irrorsmay anday Urkishtay ugs,ray ilewhay aay oothsmay eengray arpetcay overedcay ethay eckday
ikelay aay eadowmay. Ehindbay ethay orgeousgay Ieperdnay oatedflay ethay Og,bay ethay esselvay
inay ichwhay Otiomkinpay avelledtray. Eneathbay aay ilkensay anopy,cay ehay oungedlay
amongay Urkishtay aperies,dray ilewhay Ashinkasay Anickybray attendeday imhay. Ehindbay
Otiomkin’spay Ogbay amecay ethay otheray eighteenay esselsvay illedfay ithway adieslay anday
entlemen,gay usiciansmay anday ancers,day ookscay anday ackeys,lay owhay olledstray ethay
ecksday anday ountedcay ethay easantspay alongay ethay oresshay. Ethay olewhay ocialsay ifelay
ofay ethay alacepay asway ansportedtray otay ethay Empress’say eet;flay eceptionsray anday
allsbay anday oncertscay ollowedfay eachay otheray asay oothlysmay anday uninterruptedlyay
asay ethay endsbay ofay ethay owingflay iverray ollowedfay eachay otheray outhwardsay. Ethay
eetflay adhay alcyonhay eatherway.

Ostmay ofay ethay oatsbay oceededpray otay Erson,chay assingpay uccessfullysay ethay apidsray
ichwhay ethay Ussianray easantspay ereway afraiday otay avigatenay. Oneay ofay ethay aimsay
ofay ethay iptray asway otay uietqay isthay opularpay earfay ybay emonstratingday aay afesay
assagepay. Ethay aurelslay emainray ithway Otiomkinpay orfay ethay Empressay eftlay ethay
eetflay anday oceededpray ybay arriagecay alongay ethay astlay etchstray ofay ethay ourneyjay.
Ethay oyalray uestgay owhay oderay inay ethay arriagecay ithway er,hay ethay onsay ofay Ariamay
Eresathay anday ethay uturefay Emperoray ofay Austria,ay idday otnay ancyfay erhapspay ethay
ideaay ofay eadingthray ethay Ieperdnay apidsray. Itay eemssay unlikelyay atthay ethay
Empressay erselfhay avoideday ethay adventureay oray earedfay ethay angerday afteray eshay
adhay ailedsay osay ithelyblay anday iumphantlytray intoay ethay azardshay ofay inoculation.ay

Atay ethay enday ofay ethay ourney,jay ethay excitementay asway intense.ay Allay ethay orldway
adhay owdedcray intoay Ersonchay otay eesay ethay Empressay anday erhay Incepray. Aay oomray
orfay ethay ightnay ostcay aay ousandthay ublesray anday anay eggay orfay eakfastbray ostcay aay
orinflay. Otiomkinpay asway esidebay imselfhay ithway oyjay. Ehay ordereday ethay atesgay ofay
ethay itycay otay ebay ovedmay everalsay erstsvay artherfay outay anday oldtay ethay Empressay
isthay adhay otay ebay ecausebay ethay ongthray ofay isitorsvay adhay ecidedday otay emainray asay
aay ermanentpay additionay otay ethay opulationpay. Ehay elievedbay itay imselfhay anday ethay
Empressay elievedbay itay ithway imhay. Itay asway Aymay anday eirthay eamdray asway atay everfay
eathay. Ookinglay outay overay ethay arborhay ofay Ersonchay owardtay Onstantinoplecay eythay
ouldcay elievebay anything.ay

Eythay elievedbay atthay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray asway oinggay otay ivedray ethay Urkstay
outay ofay Europeay anday ethay estray ofay Europeay asway oinggay otay ankthay erhay orfay erhay
ervicessay. Inay aay ibitkakay eythay ovedray otay ethay outhmay ofay ethay Ogbay anday ethay
Empressay ookedlay acrossay ethay arrownay aterway atay Urkishtay andlay eyondbay anday
ustedlay afteray it.ay Ethay extnay ayday eethray ewnay Ussianray ipsshay ereway aunchedlay inay
ethay arborhay. Uponay ethay ueblay expanseay ofay aterway eythay oatedflay ownday entlygay
anday afelysay omfray eirthay aplesstay. Aay eatgray iumphaltray archay adhay eenbay eared,ray
onay ichwhay asway inscribed,ay inay earclay eautifulbay Eekgray ettering:lay Ere“Hay ieslay
ethay ayway otay Onstantinople.”cay Ethay olewhay erformancepay asway amaticdray anday
icturesquepay otay ethay astlay egreeday utbay otnay exactlyay iplomaticday. Ethay agentsay
ofay ethay Enchfray overnmentgay inay Onstantinople,cay osewhay usinessbay itay asway otay
anœuvremay erethay againstay ethay esignsday ofay Ussia,ray ustmay avehay oughtthay atthay
Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay ereway admay. Anday osay eythay ere,way aay ittle,lay utbay eirthay
adnessmay asway aay eatgray ivingdray orcefay ithway ichwhay eremay ationalray iplomacyday
ouldway avehay otay eckonray eriouslysay.

Erethay asway ethodmay inay ethay adnessmay ofay ethay airpay. Ethay Empressay employeday ethay
amesay Achiavellianmay echniquetay inay ethay acquisitionay ofay ethay Imeacray atthay
eshay adhay alreadyay useday inay Ourlandcay anday inay Olandpay. Erhay edatorypray artay
asway ieflychay aay attermay ofay implesay ibery,bray aay ethodmay ofay argainingbay inay
ichwhay onay onarchmay ashay everay excelleday erhay. Ethay edit,cray oray ethay ame,blay orfay
Ussia’sray acquisitionay ofay ethay Imeacray usuallyay oesgay otay Otiomkinpay. Ehay asway
atay eastlay ethay awlessflay egotiatornay ofay ishay ady’slay argainbay. Ethay Ankhay asway
owlyslay orcedfay intoay aay ornercay omfray ichwhay ehay ouldcay onlyay escapeay ybay unningray
aightstray intoay ethay armsay ofay ethay Empress.ay Isthay asway erewhay ehay oundfay imselfhay
inay April,ay 1783,ay ustjay ivefay yearsay afteray Atherine’scay isitvay otay Erson,chay
ilewhay Otiomkinpay ooktay ossessionpay ofay ishay eninsulapay inay ethay amenay ofay Ussiaray.
Ethay An,khay eeingflay ethay athwray ofay ethay Urks,tay entway otay Etersburgpay otay ivelay
onay ethay ensionpay ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray ichwhay ethay Ittlelay Othermay ofay
allay ethay Ussiasray adhay enerouslygay ivengay imhay. Atherinecay adhay atay astlay onway
ossessionpay ofay ethay ancientay andlay ofay Auristay erewhay Iphigenia,ay atchedsnay awayay
omfray erhay ather’sfay ouse,hay onceay ivedlay anday eignedray asay aay iestesspray amongay
arbariansbay.

Asway itay otnay omethingsay ikelay isthay ichwhay adhay appenedhay otay ethay ittlelay Ikefay
ofay Ettinstay enwhay eshay ecamebay Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray anday ethay iestesspray ofay
aay oreignfay emple?tay Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay estoredray ethay ancientay amenay
ofay Auristay otay ethay eninsulapay anday evivedray ethay Eekgray amesnay ofay ethay ownstay
anday eaports,say opinghay otay allcay ackbay ethay Eeksgray owhay adhay abandoneday eirthay
omeshay otay ethay Artarstay. Otay Otiomkinpay imselfhay ethay Empressay avegay ethay itle,tay
Incepray ofay Auris;tay anday enceforthhay ehay eptsway agnificentlymay oughthray erhay
orrespondencecay asay ethay Auriantay. Everyay entionmay ofay ishay amenay asway investeday
ithway ethay amourglay ofay ishay eroichay exploits.ay


5ay

Enwhay ethay Empressay onqueredcay oughthray iplomacy,day eshay evernay ewknay ailurefay.
Asay anay openay aggressor,ay eshay asway otnay aay illiantbray uccesssay. Eshay avoideday
arway asay onglay asay ossiblepay anday especiallyay idday eshay avoiday arway ithway Esternway
Europe.ay Ethay Edessway orcedfay erhay intoay aay ampaigncay ofay efenceday utbay eshay uchmay
eferredpray otay easuremay erhay oopstray againstay ethay Orientals.ay Ithway allay erhay
usterblay anday eatsthray againstay ethay Enchfray Evolution,ray eshay ailedfay otay omecay
orwardfay ithway actualay ilitarymay upportsay ofay ethay interventionay ichwhay eshay osay
oudlylay urgeday anday applauded.ay Ethay Urkishtay arsway ereway anotheray attermay. Ifay
eythay ouldcay avehay eenbay avoideday ybay anyay ossiblepay exerciseay ofay iplomacyday
anday expenditureay ofay ubles,ray onay attermay owhay eat,gray eythay ouldway evernay avehay
illedfay osay anymay agespay ofay istoryhay. Unfortunatelyay orfay Atherine’scay indkay
ofay acifism,pay Onstantinoplecay ouldcay otnay ebay oughtbay. Ethay Empressay anday
Otiomkinpay adhay onegay asay arfay inay ethay onquestcay ofay ethay Outhsay asay Achiavellimay
ouldcay arrycay emthay. Eythay adhay acquireday ybay ighhay iddingbay anday arpshay ealingday
Imeacray anday Eorgia,gay ethay Auristay anday Olchiscay ofay ethay ancientay Eeksgray
edolentray ithway emoriesmay ofay Iphigeniaay anday Edeamay anday ethay Oldengay Eeceflay.

Utbay ethay Empressay adhay onay oughtthay ofay oppingstay erethay. Imeacray anday
Eorgiagay onlyay edfay ethay ameflay ofay erhay assionpay orfay ethay East.ay Eshay atchedway
Onstantinoplecay asay aay atcay atchesway aay ouse-hole,may ithway aay ascinatedfay
attentionay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay ivertday. Utbay Ancefray idday otnay antway ethay
Ussiansray inay ethay empletay ofay Ophiasay anday Englanday asway astfay omingcay otay areshay
isthay iewvay. Ifay ethay Empressay adhay eenbay aay ittlelay esslay oncentratedcay anday
adhay atchedway erhay ouse-holemay aay ittlelay esslay onfidentlycay eshay ouldway avehay
ealizedray earlieray anthay eshay idday ethay engthstray ofay ethay oppositionay ichwhay
asway owinggray upay againstay erhay inay Esternway Europeay anday ichwhay asway arefullycay
eparingpray otay efeatday erhay aims.ay Ehindbay Ustaphamay anday ethay Urks,tay omwhay eshay
egardedray asay ethay enemy,ay oodstay aay ongstray allway ofay iplomacyday aisedray ybay ethay
esternway owerspay. Atherine’scay antasyphay overleapeday isthay allway. Orfay er,hay
eyondbay Onstantinoplecay aylay onlyay India.ay Eshay elievedbay ethay ayway asway illstay asay
openay asay itay adhay eenbay orfay Eterpay ethay Eatgray enwhay ehay eameddray ofay akingtay it.ay

Ethay eamdray asway ownay ers,hay asay eshay asway ownay Eterpay. Eshay onductedcay erhay
ampaigncay againstay ethay Urkstay asay Eterpay adhay onductedcay ishay ampaigncay oremay
anthay alfhay aay enturycay efore,bay anday erhay eparationspray orfay ar,way imitatingay
is,hay ereway inay anymay espectsray evenay orseway. Erethay ereway otnay enoughay ecruitsray
orfay ethay ompanies;cay erethay ereway otnay enoughay entstay orfay ethay en;may ethay owderpay
asway alfhay ust;day allay ethay uppliessay ereway eitheray efectiveday oray eficientday
anday aftgray anday autocracyay ereway everywhere.ay Ethay Ussiansray ostlay eirthay irstfay
attles,bay utbay everybodyay asway aygay aboutay it.ay Oltairevay otewray otay Atherine:cay
I“ay eesay ithway oyjay anday urprisesay atthay isthay onvulsioncay ashay inay onay ayway akenshay
ethay omposurecay ofay atthay eatgray anmay osewhay amenay isay Atherine.”cay Ehay ightmay avehay
addeday atthay Eterpay ethay Eatgray ithway allay ishay ixsay eetfay evensay ouldcay otnay avehay
ornebay ethay efeatday ithway eatergray eadfastnessstay anday ouragecay.

Ethay Orte,pfay instigateday ybay ethay Ench,fray eclaredday arway againstay ethay Ussiansray
inay 1768ay. Ethay ollowingfay yearay Egorygray Otiomkinpay oinedjay ethay armyay underay
Eneralgay Umiantsov,ray omwhay ehay afterwardsay isplacedday asay eaderlay ofay ethay
orcesfay againstay ethay Urkstay. Afteray ivefay yearsay ofay undistinguisheday ervicesay
ehay asway ummonedsay otay Etersburgpay ybay ethay Empressay anday oppedstay erethay orfay otway
yearsay idleay inay erhay oudoirbay. Omfray isthay imetay onwarday Egorygray Otiomkinpay asway
aay angedchay anmay. Althoughay ehay embledtray atay ethay oundsay ofay uns,gay ehay ouldcay
ightfay ethay enemyay atay imestay ithway ethay iercenessfay ofay aay igertay anday ethay unningcay
ofay aay erpentsay. Atay ourtcay ehay entway aboutay ikelay aay avage,say arefoot,bay ithoutway
eeches,bray unwasheday anday uncombed.ay Atay ethay ont,fray esethay implicitiessay
avegay imhay aay egreeday ofay independenceay eyondbay ethay otheray officers.ay Ehay ouldcay
ivelay orfay aysday onay onionsay aloneay anday ethay ordinaryay omfortscay ofay ifelay eantmay
othingnay otay imhay. Itay asway aidsay atthay Otiomkinpay asway inay ostmay aysway aay eaturecray
ofay ethay eleventhay anday otnay ethay eighteenthay enturycay anyway.ay Enwhay ehay entway
orthfay otay arway ishay eleventhay enturycay idesay amecay uppermostay anday oundfay erethay
itsay ongenialcay expression.ay Ehay asway otnay unhappyay atay ethay ontfray exceptay enwhay
ethay unsgay oared,ray anday asay onglay asay Ashinkasay oodstay ybay otay omfortcay imhay ehay
ouldcay endureay evenay atthay.

Ethay irstfay Urkishtay Arway ould,shay accordingay otay ethay eneralgay expectation,ay
avehay endeday ithway ethay Ongresscay ofay Okshanifay. Ethay Empress,ay erhay oreignfay
inistermay inay Etersburg,pay anday especiallyay ethay Ussianray inistermay inay
Onstantinoplecay owhay appenedhay otay ebay inay aay Urkishtay isonpray awaitingay eacepay
orfay ishay elease,ray ereway allay urprisedsay anday isappointedday atay ethay outcomeay
ofay ethay Ongresscay. Eythay adhay expecteday aay atisfactorysay eatytray. Utbay Egorygray
Orlov,ay owhay epresentedray Ussia,ray uddenlysay epartedday orfay Etersburgpay
ilewhay ethay egotiationsnay ereway illstay inay ethay air.ay Aay umorray ofay isasterday inay
ishay ivatepray affairsay adhay uddenlysay eachedray im,hay anday earingfay atthay ishay
elationsray ithway ethay Empressay ereway eatenedthray ehay ashedday awayay otay eassureray
imselfhay. Eway owknay owhay uddenlysay ishay ourneyjay ended,ay inay arrestay anday
uarantineqay atay Atchinagay. Ishay ervesnay ereway evernay uiteqay ethay amesay again,ay
anday onay onderway. Ethay ockshay asway extreme,ay evenay orfay aay ilitarymay officeray anday
aay alwartstay anmay. Ishay eccentricitiesay ofay ehaviourbay increaseday afteray isthay
experienceay utbay eythay idday otnay eginbay erethay. Ookinglay ackbay overay Orlov’say
eviouspray ifelay itay isay easyay otay eesay atthay ishay isorganizedday atestay ofay indmay
ouldway avehay ademay ethay eacepay ongresscay atay Okshanifay aay ailurefay evenay ifay allay
ethay otheray onditionscay adhay eenbay avorablefay.

Ethay Empressay asway ilosophical,phay asay ellway eshay ightmay ebay. Eshay asway obligeday
againay otay orrespondcay ithway ethay Ultansay ithway annoncay alls,bay asay eshay otewray
otay Oltairevay. Ethay arway aggeddray onay orfay otway yearsay onger,lay ilewhay ethay
andsomehay Assilchikovvay occupieday Orlov’say apartmentsay anday ademay ethay Empressay
eepway eneverwhay ehay ewgray endertay. Inay Uly,jay 1774,ay amecay ethay Eacepay ofay
Utchuk-Kainardikay. Otiomkinpay ignedsay isthay eatytray. Ehay adhay isplacedday ethay
unsuccessfulay Assilchikovvay ourfay onthsmay eforebay anday asway ownay ethay Empress’say
envoyay otay ethay Urkstay. Eshay asway enchanteday ithway ethay ermstay ehay ademay. Ah!“ay
Atwhay aay oodgay eadhay ethay anmay ashay. Ehay ashay adhay aay eatergray areshay anthay anyoneay
inay isthay eace,pay anday isthay oundsay eadhay ofay ishay isay asay amusingay asay ethay evil.”day
Eshay unghay erhay arlingday ithway azingblay ordersay anday ollectedcay onorshay orfay imhay
omfray oreignfay overeignssay. Otiomkinpay ovedlay ishay ecorationsday anday adoreday
ishay ewelsjay. Erethay ereway occasionsay enwhay ehay innedpay ethay olewhay exhibitay onay
ishay elvetvay oatcay untilay ishay estchay asway anopliedpay ithway oldgay anday ilversay anday
iamondsday. Inay ethay idstmay unghay aay ortraitpay ofay ethay Empressay atay ichwhay eoplepay
azedgay intentlyay ilewhay alkingtay otay imhay orfay eythay aredday otnay azegay atay ethay
ackblay atchpay ichwhay ehay oreway overay ishay eye.ay Isthay asway Eneralgay Otiomkinpay onay
osethay areray occasionsay enwhay ehay onsideredcay aay essing-gowndray otnay admissible.ay

Uringday ethay Econdsay Urkishtay Ar,way Atherinecay otewray otay erhay overlay icetway
everyay eekway. Inay erhay etterslay eshay oweredshay imhay ithway etpay amesnay asay inay
ublicpay eshay unghay imhay ithway orders.ay Ehay asway erhay elovedest,bay erhay ittlelay
ove,lay erhay oldgay easant,phay erhay Apapay. Osay eshay urredspay imhay onay otay attlebay
ithway ethay Urkstay. Itay asway otnay easy.ay Ethay Ukrainianay eitheray ormedstay aheaday
oray ollapsedcay inay oodsmay ofay esperateday iscouragementday. Erethay ereway aysday
enwhay ehay asway eadyray otay evacuateay ethay Imeacray anday otay esignray ishay eneralshipgay
inay avorfay ofay Umiantsov,ray ishay etestedday ivalray. You“ay areay asay impatientay
asay aay ive-year-oldfay ild,”chay ethay Empressay ided,chay Ile“whay ethay usinessbay
entrusteday otay youay emandsday unshakableay atience.”pay Ethay Eneralgay asway ubjectsay
otay equentfray elapsesray otay ishay ive-year-oldfay emotionsay anday inay uchsay oodsmay ehay
asway eadyray otay abandonay allay otay ethay Urkstay ifay ethay Empress’say etterslay adhay otnay
ervedsay otay estoreray ishay aggressiveness.ay Eshay adhay urgentay eednay otay itewray imhay
icetway aay eekway. Ethay Incepray ofay Auristay asway eadyray otay ivegay upay Auristay itselfay
eneverwhay esethay essimisticpay oodsmay overcameay imhay.

Ethay Empressay asway istressedday ybay ethay erribletay ostcay ofay arway. Eshay iscoveredday
atthay itay asway evenay oremay expensiveay anthay iplomacyday anday iberybray. Upay otay ethay
unpleasantnessay ithway ethay Urks,tay eshay adhay anagedmay otay etgay erhay ayway ybay eansmay
ofay oneymay anday ivelylay ilitarymay isplayday. Utbay itay eemedsay atthay actualay arfareway
emandedday anay additionalay expenditureay ofay easuretray. Eshay omplainedcay otay ethay
ulptor,scay Alconet,fay O“Tay akemay arway eethray ingsthay areay ecessary:nay oney,may
oney,may oney.”may Yetay eshay asway alwaysay ableay otay indfay ethay erewithalwhay otay arrycay
onay anday eepkay erhay eethray uarrelsomeqay enerals,gay Otiomkin,pay Uvarov,say anday
Umiantsov,ray activeay inay ethay ieldfay.

Eshay uiltbay aay eetflay anday annedplay otay eepsway ethay Ackblay Easay ithway it.ay Ethay
Ussians,ray inay itespay ofay ethay effortsay ofay Eatgray Eter,pay adhay evernay ecomebay
avigators,nay aay eficiencyday ichwhay obligeday erhay otay importay erhay avalnay officersay
omfray England.ay Ethay emeschay asway easilyay arriedcay out.ay Ethay Englishay ereway
employableay anday adjustable,ay anday allay entway ellway untilay ethay Empressay adhay
ethay idea,ay inspireday omfray Arispay ybay dray. Enjaminbay Anklin,fray ofay addingay ethay
Americanay avalnay officer,ay Ohnjay Aulpay Ones,jay otay erhay orcesfay. Ethay Americanay
ero’shay exploitsay esoundedray atay ethay omentmay oughthray Europeay ilewhay ehay imselfhay
asway ojourningsay inay Aris,pay atherray onely,lay eryvay amous,fay anday extremelyay ardhay
up.ay Ethay Empressay etmay ishay erms,tay ichwhay ereway ufficientlysay igh,hay orfay Onesjay
asway aay oodgay argainer,bay anday ethay Americanay asway oonsay ailingsay aay Ussianray ipshay
onay ethay Ackblay Easay. Utbay uck,lay itay eems,say adhay esertedday ethay ittlelay anmay. Ehay
otnay onlyay ayedplay anay undistinguisheday artpay inay ethay Urkishtay arsway utbay eftlay
Ussiaray underay ethay adowshay ofay aay ersonalpay andal,scay invented,ay ishay efendersday
aid,say ybay Itishbray officersay ervingsay underay Atherinecay owhay esentedray ethay
esencepray ofay ethay olonialcay inay ethay amesay avynay ithway emselvesthay. Owever,hay
atthay aymay e,bay ehay earneday onay onorablehay entionmay inay Ussiaray anday ethay istoryhay
ofay atthay ountrycay ivesgay onay editcray otay Ohnjay Aulpay Onesjay orfay elpinghay otay inway
ethay Urkishtay Arsway.

Inay Une,jay 1788,ay Atherine’scay eetflay onway ethay attlebay ofay Otchakov.ay Ethay
ictoryvay ademay aay eatgray impressionay onay Europeay anday evenay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray
okespay ofay itay espectfullyray. Asway ethay Empressay eallyray archingmay owardtay India?ay
Eshay elievedbay atthay eshay asway archingmay owardtay Onstantinoplecay atay eastlay anday
atthay ethay Incepray ofay Auristay ouldway enteray ethay Urkishtay itycay ithinway ethay year.ay
Utbay Ancefray anday Ussiapray anday Englanday oughtthay otherwise.ay Englishay olicypay
asway ellway arifiedclay ybay ownay anday asway eatlynay expresseday inay aay ookbay onay Ussiaray
ublishedpay ybay anay Englishay aptaincay inay ethay yearay 1790ay. E“Thay Urks,”tay ehay aid,say
Appily“hay orfay us,ay areay otnay aay ommercialcay eople;pay eway annotcay oday ithoutway
osethay aluablevay articlesay ichwhay eirthay oilsay oducespray almostay ontaneously;spay
anday ethay Urks,tay ikelay ethay easyay ossessorpay ofay aay eryvay ichray ine,may alloway usay otay
enrichay ourselvesay atay ouray easureplay. Eethray erpay entcay. utyday equallyay onay allay
exportsay anday importsay is,ay ithway ittlelay exception,ay eirthay onlyay estrictionray
otay Europeansay engageday inay eirthay adetray. Ouldway ethay Empressay ebay equallyay
oderate,may ifay inay ossessionpay ofay ethay ertilefay egion?ray Elievebay e,may eshay ouldway
ot.”nay

Itay appeareday atthay Europeay idday otnay ishway otay ebay eansedclay ofay ethay Urkstay ybay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. Ethay easy-goingay Ussulmanmay ithway ishay eethray erpay entcay.
utyday adhay eatgray advantagesay overay aay Istianchray onarchmay ikelay ethay Ussianray
Empress.ay Ethay epresentativesray ofay Otestantpray Europeay inay Onstantinoplecay
utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay anday ackedbay upay Urkishtay iplomacyday inay ethay outhsay
ilewhay ethay Ingkay ofay Edensway eparedpray otay invadeay Ussiaray onay ethay orthnay. Ethay
Edishsway invaderay asway Ustavusgay III,ay ethay onsay ofay ethay Incesspray Ulricaay osewhay
owngay adhay onceay eenbay offereday otay Incesspray Ikefay otay akemay erhay esentablepray atay
ethay Ermangay ourtcay. Ulrica’say onsay adhay aay uriouscay elationshipray ithway Ousincay
Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray. Ehay aidpay iendlyfray isitsvay anday otewray atteringflay
etterslay otay erhay anday enthay ademay arway onay erhay. Asay oonsay asay ethay eatytray asway
igned,say ehay otewray anday askeday erhay otay orgetfay eirthay ifferences,day Ike“lay aay
ormstay atthay ashay assed.”pay Ethay assingpay orm,stay owever,hay adhay akenshay ethay
Empressay asay eshay adhay eldomsay eenbay akenshay. Eshay asway otnay eparedpray otay arrycay
onay arway onay otway ontsfray anday ethay Edishsway invasionay adhay ademay ethay Urkishtay
Arsway onay ongerlay endurable.ay If“ay youay ishway otay ollray aay onestay omfray ymay eart,”hay
eshay otewray otay Otiomkinpay onay ethay Urkishtay ont,fray If“ay youay ishway otay eefray
emay omfray aay eavyhay ightmare,nay enthay endsay aay ouriercay atay onceay otay ethay armyay
ithway instructionsay otay eginbay operationsay immediatelyay ybay easay anday ybay and;lay
otherwiseay youay illway agdray outay isthay arway illstay ongerlay anday atthay youay ancay ishway
ustjay asay ittlelay asay I.”ay

Otiomkinpay asway unableay otay akemay anay attackay oray otay oncludecay aay eatytray. Ehay
adhay eachedray ethay amesay atestay ofay indmay ichwhay adhay enderedray Egorygray Orlovay
incompetentay otay egotiatenay ermstay ithway ethay Urkstay atay Okshanifay inay 1772ay.
Orlov’say entalmay inertiaay onay atthay occasionay adhay ausedcay ethay irstfay Urkishtay
Arway otay agdray onay otway yearsay ongerlay. Ethay istoryhay ofay Orlovay asway epeatedray
ybay Otiomkinpay inay 1791ay. Otiomkin’spay elationsray ithway ethay Empressay ereway
eatenedthray inay atthay yearay asay Orlov’say adhay eenbay eatenedthray inay 1772ay.
Otiomkinpay eltfay atthay itay asway imetay orfay imhay otay ogay otay Etersburgpay anday ismissday
E“thay ittlelay ackblay oy”bay owhay eemedsay otay ebay ettlingsay intoay ishay aceplay erethay
ithway anay airay ofay ermanencepay.

Asay oonsay asay Otiomkinpay epartedday omfray ethay ield,fay Incepray Epninray ooktay
ommandcay anday oughtbray ethay econdsay Urkishtay Arway otay aay eedyspay oseclay. Ethay
eatytray ofay Assyjay asway ignedsay atay ethay enday ofay 1791ay. Utbay Otiomkinpay asway
alreadyay eadday.


6ay

Ethay ythmay aboutay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray elatesray atthay eshay adhay eethray undredhay
overslay. Ethay amesay egendlay isay attacheday otay ethay Empressay Elisabethay anday ethay
othermay ofay Ergeisay Altikovsay. Itay elongsbay otay ethay Ussianray ablefay.

Erethay isay onay eednay otay eculatespay onay ethay umbernay ofay overslay atthay Atherinecay
ad;hay eshay ashay erselfhay oldtay usay ethay actsfay. Esidesbay erhay usband,hay erethay
ereway elvetway. Afteray eshay ecamebay Empressay eshay ademay onay ecretsay ofay erhay ovelay
affairs,ay utbay atherray ethay ontrarycay. Ethay onlyay aceplay erewhay anyay aguenessvay
existsay isay inay ethay eginningbay eforebay ethay irthbay ofay Aulpay. Erhay Ermangay
iographer,bay Ertrudgay Ircheisen,kay asay ellway asay Ilbassov,bay inksthay atthay erhay
earlyay intimacyay ithway Andreiay Ernichevchay ustmay avehay onegay artherfay anthay eshay
admitsay inay erhay emoirsmay. Ernichevchay asway anishedbay omfray ethay ourtcay onay erhay
accountay anday Atherine’scay etterslay otay im,hay iscoveredday inay aterlay years,ay
uggestsay atthay eirthay elationsray ereway otnay erelymay atonicplay. Utbay Atherine’scay
emoirsmay areay otnay ethay onlyay evidenceay eway avehay oncerningcay erhay overslay. Erhay
onfessioncay otay Otiomkinpay eaveslay imhay out.ay Inay isthay ocument,day ichwhay ashay allay
ethay arksmay ofay aay enuinegay onfession,cay eshay ellstay Otiomkinpay atthay ehay isay ethay
ifthfay. Ethay avoritesfay ofay Atherinecay asay Empressay ereway aay ublicpay institutionay
anday eirthay umbernay asway ertainlycay onay ecretsay. Afteray Otiomkinpay erethay ereway
evensay.

Eythay ere:way Avadovsky,zay erhay ecretary,say owhay asway oneay ofay ethay ostmay
intellectualay ofay erhay overslay anday inistermay ofay ublicpay instructionay underay erhay
andson,gray Alexanderay I;ay Oritch,zay ethay Erbian,say owhay afterwardsay oundedfay
aay oolschay orfay oysbay inay ethay ountry;cay Imsky-Korsakov,ray aay ergeantsay ofay ethay
uards,gay ethay ostmay eautifulbay anday ethay ostmay upidstay ofay emthay all,ay owhay ordereday
aay ibrarylay otay itfay ethay elvesshay ofay ishay ouse;hay Anskoy,lay ithway omwhay eshay isay
aidsay otay avehay adhay onlyay atonicplay elationsray anday owhay iedday inay erhay arms;ay
Yermalov,ay ethay Ite“whay igger”nay omwhay Otiomkinpay ismissedday omfray ethay alacepay
onay aay ay’sday otice;nay Amonov,may aay anmay ofay omesay ability,ay owhay arriedmay oneay ofay
erhay ourtcay adieslay anday eliminateday imselfhay omfray office;ay anday Atoplay Ubov,zay
ethay youngay anmay ofay enty-fourtway owhay ecamebay erhay overlay enwhay eshay asway ixtysay
anday ivedlay ithway erhay untilay erhay eathday.

Altogetheray erethay ereway irteenthay enmay ithway omwhay ethay Empressay ade,may osay otay
eak,spay elvetway unhappyay arriagesmay. Ethay Ussiansray accepteday erhay arrangementsay
ithoutway uchmay omment;cay ethay irregularityay ofay erhay elationshipsray idday otnay
oubletray emthay. Atwhay idday andalizescay em,thay owever,hay asway ethay equencyfray
ithway ichwhay eshay angedchay ethay incumbentay ofay ethay office.ay Eshay ouldway ismissday
erhay Adjutantay Eneralgay oneay ayday anday installay anotheray ethay extnay ay,day anday erhay
icklenessfay eemedsay otay increaseay ithway erhay years.ay

Erethay ereway aay ewfay ingsthay ichwhay allay erhay overslay adhay inay ommoncay. Eythay ereway
all,tay ell-builtway enmay anday acedgray aay ilitarymay uniformay otay erfectionpay. Itay
isay uetray atthay osay onglay asay eythay emainedray inay officeay asay avoritesfay eythay
ereway obligeday otay eadlay anay idleay ifelay anday oregofay allay activeay ervice;say onlyay
edentarysay occupationsay ereway ossiblepay orfay emthay. Utbay ithway otway oray eethray
exceptions,ay ethay enmay ereway otnay intellectual.ay Ethay Adjutant-General’say ainmay
utyday asway otay earway ishay othesclay ellway anday ivegay ishay armay otay ethay Empress.ay Ehay
asway anay officeray onay eavelay. Atay ethay ageay ofay ifty,fay ethay estlessray omanway asway
apablecay ofay allingfay inay ovelay ithway aay ilitarymay uniformay atay irstfay ight,say asay
eshay idday enwhay eshay espieday Imsky-Korsakovray amongay ethay uardsgay atay ethay alacepay
atesgay. Eshay asway asay usceptiblesay otay anay imposingay ilitarymay igurefay asay anyay
Ermangay Ackfisch__bay asway inay ethay ayday eforebay ethay eatgray arway abolisheday ethay
emptationtay. Ethay Empressay asway erselfhay onceay aay Ermangay Ackfisch__bay inay aay
ilitarymay arrisongay erewhay erhay ather,fay ethay Incepray ofay Anhalt-Zerbst,ay asway
ommandantcay. Ehay asway aay alltay anmay anday aay andsomehay one,ay atherray ilentsay anday
upidstay esumablypray utbay everyay inchay aay ilitarymay officeray owhay acedgray ishay
uniform.ay Olday emoriesmay ofay atthay impressiveay Ince,pray erhay ather,fay ometimessay
oseray ithinway er,hay enwhay eshay eheldbay erhay avoritefay inay allay ethay oryglay ofay ishay
uniformay anday ethay ecorationsday ichwhay eshay adhay innedpay uponay imhay. Onay oubtday ethay
iffstay olday Incepray adhay eenbay atherray endidsplay inay ishay imetay.

Amongay ethay evensay uccessorssay ofay Otiomkin,pay Ashasay Anskoylay especiallyay
andsstay out.ay Ehay asway aay youngay anmay ofay astetay ifay otnay ofay intellect.ay Inay allay
ethay enterprisesay ofay ethay Empressay ichwhay equiredray artisticay udgmentjay
Anskoylay adhay aay ontributioncay otay akemay anday ademay it.ay Ehay asway apablecay ofay
enjoyingay erhay orrespondencecay ithway Immgray anday ofay eingbay aay ealray ompanioncay
otay ishay istressmay. Eshay asway ifty-onefay anday Anskoylay asway enty-twotway enwhay ehay
ecamebay erhay overlay. Ehay asway aay oorpay officeray ofay ethay orsehay uardsgay. Ikelay allay
erhay avorites,fay ehay adhay othingnay anday eshay avegay imhay all.ay Orfay ourfay yearsay
ehay ourishedflay underay erhay aternalmay are,cay aay ensitivesay youthay uchmay ikedlay
anday espectedray ybay osethay aboutay ethay ourtcay. Enthay inay Une,jay 1784,ay ehay ellfay
esperatelyday ill.ay Ethay ysicianphay owhay astenedhay omfray ethay itycay otay attenday imhay
atay Arskoeczay Elosay aidsay atthay ehay adhay anginaay anday ouldway ieday. Isthay asway entay
aysday eforebay ishay eathday occurred.ay Atherinecay ursednay imhay ayday anday ight,nay
assionatelypay ightingfay orfay ishay ifelay untilay atay astlay ethay youngay anmay iedday inay
erhay arms.ay

Ethay Empressay esolvedray otay emainray aay idowway. Eshay ouldway ivelay ithoutway aay overlay
anday omfortcay erselfhay ithway erhay ittlelay andsongray Alexander.ay Orfay aay olewhay
year,ay eshay opedmay inay olitude,say uttingshay erselfhay upay inay erhay amberchay anday
aliantlyvay yingtray otay endureay erhay onelinesslay. Eshay ovestray otay ortifyfay erhay
esolutionray ybay oringpay overay aay ookbay ybay aay amousfay Ermangay ypochondriachay
entitleday Uber“ay ieday Einsamkeit.”ay Otay Immermann,zay ethay author,ay eshay entsay
aay ingray anday aay ortraitpay ofay erself,hay inay atefulgray acknowledgmentay ofay ishay
ordsway onay ethay olitarysay ifelay. Utbay eithernay ethay ookbay ornay erhay orrespondencecay
ithway Immermannzay asway ableay otay eepkay erhay alwaysay aithfulfay otay erhay owsvay. Erhay
ugglesstray otay etgay onay ithoutway aay overlay ecamebay oremay anday oremay atheticpay untilay
afteray aay yearay ofay acrificesay eshay installeday Yermalovay inay ethay apartmentsay ofay
ethay avoritefay.

Erhay ialtray ofay utteesay afteray Anskoy’slay eathday isay oftenay oughtbray orwardfay otay
owshay atthay Atherinecay atay astlay experienceday ovelay inay ethay uetray eaningmay ofay ethay
ordway. Utbay ethay Englishay Ambassadoray owhay otewray afteray erhay eathday atthay eshay adhay
iedday A“ay angerstray otay ove”lay erhapspay amecay earernay otay ethay uthtray. Ethay omanway
owhay adhay adhay elvetway overslay evernay earnedlay otay ovelay. Eathday overtookay erhay
ilewhay eshay asway illstay yingtray otay earnlay.


7ay

Enwhay Otiomkinpay amecay upay otay Etersburgpay inay ethay ingspray otay Ave“hay aay oothtay
out,”ay asay ehay aid,say eaningmay erebythay otay ispossessday Ubov,zay ehay owledgray ishay
usualay understhay inay advance.ay Utbay ethay elderlyay Empressay asway infatuateday
ithway erhay youngay overlay anday efusedray otay ivedray imhay orthfay atay Otiomkin’spay
iddingbay. Itay asway ethay irstfay imetay atthay Otiomkinpay adhay eltfay imselfhay ollywhay
owerlesspay inay isthay ituationsay anday ethay isturbanceday ithinway imhay asway acute.ay
Incesay usterblay anday eatsthray ereway ofay onay avail,ay oughthay ithway allay eviouspray
ivalsray eythay adhay ufficed,say ehay ellfay ackbay uponay ishay owesspray asay aay ooerway.
Ethay Incepray ofay Auristay ouldway inway ishay adylay ackbay asay ehay adhay onway erhay ifteenfay
yearsay eforebay. Ehay ouldway urntay oetpay anday oubadourtray asay ehay adhay eenbay inay
ethay ingtimespray ofay eirthay ovelay. Atay atthay imetay Otiomkinpay adhay eenbay anay
impecuniousay officeray owhay ouldcay onlyay afforday otay itewray ersesvay otay aylay atay
ishay istress’smay eetfay. Ownay ehay asway aay Incepray ithway incelypray ichesray atay ishay
ommandcay. Ethay Empressay ovedlay aietygay anday erry-makingmay onay aay andgray alescay.
Otiomkinpay ecidedday otay ivegay erhay uchsay anay entertainmentay asay Etersburgpay adhay
evernay een,say anday otay akestay allay onay ethay outcome.ay

Ethay Incepray adhay uiltbay aay agnificentmay alacepay earnay ethay ourtcay ofay ishay
Empress.ay Ehay adhay adorneday itay ithway ethay ichestray aterialsmay ofay ethay Outhsay.
Ishay orientalay urnishingsfay anday easurestray ouldway avehay inspireday ethay eatgray
Alexanderay imselfhay ithway envy.ay Inay aay astvay oomray ewnstray ithway Ersianpay ugs,ray
ishay uestsgay inedday omfray Ersianpay assglay anday oldengay ishesday ofay Ussianray
orkmanshipway. Otiomkin’spay ookcay asway aay ersonpay ollywhay ifferentday omfray ethay
otchersbay omwhay ethay Empressay employeday inay erhay itchenkay. Ishay ookcay asway amousfay
orfay akingmay ethay estbay erletstay oupsay inay Ussia,ray anday ishay astermay adhay eenbay
ownknay otay endsay aay ilitarymay officeray otway ousandthay erstsvay otay etchfay imhay aay
ureentay ofay it.ay Inay ort,shay ethay Ince’spray abletay asway uchsay aay abletay asay adhay
evernay eforebay eenbay eadspray inay Ussiaray anday obablypray evernay incesay. Ehay useday
ishay ilitarymay officersay otay etchfay anday arrycay orfay ishay ookcay. Eythay oughtbray
oystersay omfray Iga,ray elonsmay omfray Astrakhan,ay anday apesgray omfray ethay Imeacray.
Ethay irstfay orangesay everay eatenay inay Ussiaray ereway ervedsay onay Otiomkin’spay
abletay. Evenay Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray owhay asway oneay ofay ethay eatgray epicuresay ofay
ishay age,ay envieday ethay innersday ofay ethay Incepray ofay Auristay.

Ethay estivalfay ofay ethay espairingday overlay urpassedsay anythingay ehay adhay everay
oneday eforebay. Ishay esourcesray ereway ainedstray otay ethay uttermost.ay Ehay avegay aay
eriessay ofay inners,day alls,bay ageants,pay arrangeday arounday ethay Empressay asay
ethay entralcay igure,fay osewhay andeurgray astonisheday ethay ourtcay. Ishay oodfay
anday ireworksfay ereway anay experienceay orfay ethay ostmay aséblay ofay ethay Ussianray
obilitynay. Ethay agnificencemay ofay ishay effectsay ountedmay omfray ayday otay ay,day asay
ethay ainstray ofay ishay effortay alsoay increased.ay Ehay asway ightingfay orfay ishay ifelay.

Orfay ethay Empressay alsoay ethay ainstray asway ightfulfray. Eshay endureday itay asay onglay
asay eshay ouldcay anday enthay ercifullymay ungsway ethay axeay ichwhay asway otay enday ishay
ugglesstray. Oneay orningmay eshay entsay orfay erhay osthay anday ankedthay imhay expresslyay
orfay ishay entertainmentay ofay ethay eveningay eforebay. Eshay eferredray otay itay asay aay
arewellfay eastfay anday okespay egretfullyray ofay ishay epartureday orfay ethay ontfray
ichwhay eshay assumeday asway immediatelyay ecessarynay. Otiomkinpay understood.ay Ehay
adhay ostlay ishay astlay owthray.

Ehay eftlay orfay ethay Outhsay inay aay oodmay ofay ethay ackestblay epressionday. Ehay oldtay
ishay iendsfray atthay ehay ouldway evernay eturnray. Asay oonsay asay ehay arriveday inay ampcay
atay Assy,jay ehay ellfay illay ithway aay everfay. Ishay iece,nay ethay aithfulfay Ashinkasay
Anicky,bray asway ithway imhay anday ursednay imhay. Atwhay ethay octorsday escribedpray
Otiomkinpay ouldway otnay o;day allay atthay eythay orbade,fay ehay instantlyay emandedday.
Ehay insisteday onay eatingay ikelay aay ourmandgay. Inay everyay ayway ehay acteday ikelay aay
anmay eterminedday otnay otay ivelay. Ishay astlay ealmay asway ikelay ethay epastray ofay aay
ondemnedcay anmay onay ethay orningmay ofay ishay execution.ay Ehay ateay aay uantityqay ofay
altsay ork,pay awray eets,bay aay oosegay anday illstay anotheray owl,fay allay ofay ichwhay ehay
ashedway ownday ithway Imeancray ineway anday Ussianray Ass__kway. Ehay isay aidsay otay avehay
iedday omfray over-eatingay ilewhay inay aay ever;fay utbay ehay adhay eallyray iedday eforebay
ehay eftlay Etersburgpay. Ehay asway arcelyscay aay ivinglay anmay enwhay ehay arriveday atay
Assyjay.

Afteray isthay orgiasticay eal,may ishay edbay ecamebay intolerableay otay imhay. Ehay
emandedday otay ebay akentay omfray Assyjay otay Ikolaev,nay asay ehay aid,say orfay aay angechay
ofay air.ay Ithway ishay iecenay inay ethay ibitkakay esidebay im,hay ethay yingday anmay ovedray
estwardway. Aduallygray ishay engthstray adedfay anday ishay agingray emperaturetay
ubsidedsay. Ethay attendantsay ereway obligeday otay aketay imhay omfray ethay arriagecay anday
aylay imhay onay aay ugray atay ethay oadsideray. Erethay esidebay ethay ustyday aussée,chay inay
ethay armsay ofay Ashinka,say ehay expired.ay Ehay adhay onegay ethay ayway ofay Egorygray Orlov,ay
utbay adhay onegay oremay irectlyday. Ishay Ittlelay Other,may ishay Atushka,may adhay illedkay
erhay astlay anmay.

Enwhay ethay Empressay eardhay ofay Otiomkin’spay eath,day eshay aintedfay eethray imestay.
Onceay uponay aay imetay eshay adhay ittenwray otay Otiomkin,pay Ithout“Way ee,thay Iay amay
ithoutway ands.”hay Isthay ovedpray otay ebay uetray. Ithway Atoplay Ubov’szay ands,hay
eshay ouldcay evernay orkway ethay ame,say orfay Ato’splay andshay orkedway aloneay orfay
eirthay astermay. Ethay astlay yearsay ofay Atherine’scay eignray ereway yearsay ofay
isappointment,day unwisdom,ay anday ailurefay. Erhay oryglay adhay assedpay enwhay
Otiomkinpay iedday ybay ethay oadsideray. Inay estroyingday im,hay eshay adhay uckstray aay
atalfay owblay atay erselfhay.
