Ixay

ATHERINEcay ECOMESbay Aay ANDMOTHERgRay


Overay aay antelpiecemay inay ethay alacepay ofay Atchinagay angshay aay ortraitpay ofay Aulpay
Iay asay aay oybay ofay entay. Itay isay ethay onlyay oneay ofay ishay ortraitspay ichwhay earsbay aay
esemblanceray otay ishay othermay. Ofay allay ethay artistsay owhay aintedpay im,hay isthay oneay
aloneay eemssay otay avehay aughtcay anay aspectay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday ichwhay uggestssay
ethay Empress.ay Eetingflay itay ustmay avehay een,bay orfay Aulpay ewgray upay otay ebay
ikinglystray unlikeay ishay aternalmay arentpay. Ehay asway estinedday otay advertiseay ybay
ishay acefay anday igurefay otay allay ethay orldway ethay anonymousay aternitypay ichwhay adhay
oducedpray imhay.

Atherinecay asway annoyeday ybay Aul’spay appearanceay anday isposition,day inheriteday
asay eythay ereway omfray ishay ather’sfay amilyfay. Itay offendeday erhay atthay ehay ouldshay
urntay outay otay ebay osay ompletelycay aay Altikovsay. Atthay erhay onsay erivedday osay ittlelay
omfray erselfhay eemedsay aay erversitypay ofay ortunefay. Eshay eflectedray aay eatgray
ealday onay ethay ubjectsay. Y“May Od,”gay eshay urstbay outay inay oneay ofay erhay etterslay otay
Imm,gray Y“whay oday ildrenchay osay oftenay esembleray eirthay athersfay enwhay itay ouldway
ebay etterbay otay esembleray eirthay others?may Atthay isay otnay ommoncay ense;say ameday
Aturenay isay oftenay aay ockheadblay. Oneay ayday Iay allshay itewray aay issertationday
onay at,thay ichwhay Iay allshay edicateday otay you.”ay Eshay idday otnay itewray ethay
issertationday orfay Imm,gray althoughay issertationsday inay eneralgay ereway uchmay inay
erhay inelay. Eshay ippedday intoay ientificscay esearchray omfray imetay otay imetay ithway
impressiveay esultsray. Erhay ontributionscay otay omparativecay ilologyphay avehay
onway ecognitionray omfray olarsschay inay atthay ield;fay utbay erhay ontemplatedcay udystay
ofay inheritanceay ofay aracteristicschay asway evernay arriedcay out.ay Eshay evernay otgay
eyondbay osingpay ethay uestion,qay otay ich,whay owever,hay eshay epeatedlyray eturnedray
ithoutway everay ushingpay onwarday otay anyay indkay ofay eorythay. Eshay edbray ogsday anday
observeday atthay eythay owedshay ethay amesay endencytay asay umanhay eingsbay inay isthay
espectray. Itness“Way Irsay Omtay Anderson,”ay eshay aidsay ofay erhay avoritefay ound,hay
All“ay ishay amilyfay esemblesray imhay. Ethay amesay irit,spay ethay amesay aste,tay ethay
amesay igure,fay ethay amesay ysiognomy,phay ethay amesay endency.”tay Eshay asway uzzledpay
anday esentfulray.

Atherinecay asway estrangeday omfray erhay onsay Aulpay omfray ethay ayday ofay ishay irthbay.
Eprivedday ofay allay opportunityay otay expressay erhay aternalmay eelingsfay ybay ethay
Empress’say eft,thay eshay adhay onay actualay experienceay ofay otherhoodmay. Ainfulpay
associationsay usteredclay arounday ethay infancyay ofay isthay over-preciousay ildchay.
Atherinecay adhay eenbay esertedday ybay erhay irstfay overlay owhay openlyay eplacedray erhay
ybay unworthyay ivalsray. Eshay atedhay Altikov,say asay eshay afterwardsay earnedlay otnay
otay atehay anyay ofay erhay avoritesfay afteray eirthay affairay adhay unray itsay oursecay. Ethay
ildchay omwhay eshay awsay onceay aay eekway inay ishay ox-furfay adlecray emindedray erhay ofay
itterbay isillusionmentday. Asay ehay ewgray older,ay ishay uerulousqay isposition,day
ishay under-sizeday ature,stay ishay izenedway in,skay ishay aldness,bay anday ishay
uglyay osenay allay elpedhay otay akemay imhay eemsay alienay otay ishay othermay. Ehay asway aay
inging,cray icklysay oybay ofay omwhay itay asway ifficultday otay ebay oudpray. Eshay adhay
oducedpray imhay atay uchsay aay ostcay anday ehay epresentedray uchsay anay inferioray iumphtray
afteray all.ay Asay umanhay aterialmay ehay asway inay ethay amesay assclay asay Eterpay ethay
Ird,thay omfray ichwhay anymay istorianshay avehay argueday atthay Aulpay asway Eter’spay onsay
anday aay enuinegay escendantday ofay ethay Omanovsray.

Atherine’scay econdsay onsay anday erhay irstfay ildchay ybay Orlov,ay Incepray Obrinsky,bay
alsoay ailedfay otay inheritay ethay eniusgay ofay ishay othermay. Ehay asway oughtbray upay
underay ethay Empress’say upervisionsay ybay anay Italianay utor,tay Admiralay Ibas,ray anday
asay aay youngay anmay asway aay e’er-do-wellnay anday aay asterway. Ishay othermay entsay imhay
onay aay ourtay oughthray Europeay anday ethay aygay youngay Incepray ofay ethay Eaver-skinbay
eftlay aay ailtray ofay ebtsday ehindbay imhay inay itycay afteray itycay. Inallyfay ethay
exasperateday Empressay adhay imhay arresteday anday interneday inay Iga,ray afteray ichwhay
istoryhay owsknay imhay onay oremay. Ehay asway aay endthrift,spay ikelay othbay ishay arents,pay
utbay ehay adhay onenay ofay ethay entalmay anday oralmay andicapshay ofay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.
Afteray ishay ublicpay isgraceday inay Iga,ray ehay eturnedray otay Ussiaray anday edlay anay
unambitiousay anday uneventfulay ifelay. Ehay arriedmay anday eftlay escendantsday inay
omwhay istoryhay akestay onay interest.ay

Ethay iefchay artpay ichwhay Obrinskybay ayedplay inay ethay amadray ofay ishay other’smay ifelay
asway otay eightenhay ethay onflictcay ichwhay alwaysay existeday etweenbay Atherinecay
anday erhay irst-bornfay. Erethay asway aay omentmay inay ethay Empress’say ifelay enwhay
eshay oughtthay ofay arryingmay Egorygray Orlovay utbay asway uddenlysay eckedchay inay
erhay intentionsay ybay ethay enemiesay ofay ethay Orlovsay anday ethay oppositionay ofay
Aninpay. Ountcay Anin,pay owhay antedway omfray ethay irstfay otay akemay Aulpay emperor,ay
ecamebay uddenlysay energeticay enwhay ehay uspectedsay atthay ethay Empressay ishedway
otay egitimatizelay Obrinskybay. Evenay afteray ethay angerday ofay ethay arriagemay adhay
eenbay averted,ay isthay astardbay Incepray illstay overedhay eateninglythray inay ethay
ackground,bay ellway aredcay orfay ybay ethay Empress,ay ishay other,may aay ermanentpay
objectay ofay uspicionsay otay Ountcay Aninpay anday ofay earfay otay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.
Isthay oybay owhay embledtray orfay ishay ifelay ouldcay indfay onay eassuranceray inay ethay
existenceay ofay aay ivalray alf-brotherhay asay onglay asay ehay eptkay ishay ealthhay anday
ishay other’smay avorfay. Ethay youngay Obrinsky,bay ikelay everythingay elseay inay eirthay
environment,ay ontributedcay otay ethay estrangementay etweenbay Atherinecay anday erhay
eirhay.

Enwhay Atherinecay ecamebay Empress,ay oneay ofay erhay irstfay oncernscay asway otay ovidepray
orfay ethay educationay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay. Eshay electedsay onay esslay aay ersonpay
orfay ethay ostpay anthay Alembertd’ay. Utbay ethay Enchfray olarschay eclinedday erhay
invitation.ay Ethay Empressay ouldway otnay aketay onay orfay anay answer;ay eshay oopedstay otay
onquercay. I“ay owknay youay ootay ellway orfay aay oodgay an,”may eshay ote,wray O“tay ascribeay
youray efusalray otay anityvay. Iay owknay atthay ethay olesay otivemay ofay itay isay ethay esireday
orfay eacepay anday eisurelay otay ultivatecay etterslay anday ethay iendshipfray ofay
osethay omwhay youay esteem.ay Utbay atwhay isay erethay inay isthay objection?ay Omecay ithway
allay youray iendsfray. Iay omisepray othbay emthay anday youay everyay onveniencecay anday
advantageay atthay ependsday uponay e;may anday erhapspay youay illway indfay oremay ibertylay
anday easeay erehay anthay inay youray ativenay ountrycay. Youay efusedray ethay invitationay
ofay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussia,pray otwithstandingnay youray obligationsay otay imhay. Utbay
atthay Incepray ashay onay onsay. Iay admitay otay youay atthay Iay avehay ethay educationay ofay ymay
onsay osay uchmay atay eart,hay anday Iay inkthay youay osay ecessarynay otay it,ay atthay erhapspay
Iay esspray youay ithway ootay uchmay earnestness.ay Excuseay ymay indiscretionay orfay ethay
akesay ofay itsay occasion;ay anday ebay assureday atthay itay isay ymay esteemay orfay youay atthay
akesmay emay osay urgent.”ay

Isthay etitioningpay ofay Alembertd’ay oughtbray oneay ofay ethay arpestshay umiliationshay
ofay erhay ifelay. Alembertd’ay eadfastlystay efusedray. Ivatelypray ehay uttereday aay
arcasticsay emarkray ichwhay avelledtray arfay. Inay Ussia,ray ehay aid,say eoplepay iedday
ootay easilyay ofay olic,cay itay asway etterbay otay emainray inay Ancefray. Ethay Empressay
evernay orgavefay imhay isthay yslay eferenceray otay erhay anifestomay oncerningcay
Eter’spay untimelyay end.ay Aay ecadeday oray oremay afterwards,ay enwhay eshay asway
engageday inay ethay invasionay ofay Oland,pay aay oupgray ofay Enchfray ofessorspray ivinglay
erethay ellfay intoay erhay andshay anday ereway interneday atay Ievkay. Alembert,d’ay
ememberingray ishay olday estigepray ithway ethay Empress,ay attempteday otay ecuresay
eirthay eleaseray ybay endingsay aay ersonalpay etitionpay otay ethay Ussianray Empress,ay
utbay eshay urnedtay aay eafday earay otay ishay intercession.ay Ethay istressedday olarschay
atay astlay appealeday otay Oltairevay owhay ucceededsay inay ettinggay onlyay aay oldcay eplyray
omfray ethay Empress.ay Eshay aidsay atthay ethay Enchfray ofessorspray ereway oingday eryvay
ellway inay Ussiaray anday ouldway aystay erethay orfay ethay esentpray. Eshay implieday atthay
Alembert,d’ay owhay adhay oughtthay atthay eoplepay iedday ootay easilyay ofay oliccay inay
isthay arbarousbay and,lay ightmay ownay eesay orfay imselfhay owhay ellway eoplepay ouldcay
ivelay erethay. Ethay ofessorspray ereway eingbay aredcay orfay anday ouldway emainray
interneday untilay ethay Empressay oundfay eisurelay otay eleaseray emthay. Eirthay eriodpay
ofay internmentay asway obablypray otnay eatlygray olongedpray ybay Alembert’sd’ay appeal.ay

Enwhay ethay Empress’say effortsay otay importay igherhay educationay orfay erhay onsay
atteredshay onay isthay embarrassingay assagepay etweenbay erselfhay anday ethay Enchfray
encyclopædist,ay eshay avegay upay allay urtherfay attemptsay otay improveay onay Anin’spay
edagogypay. Erhay opinionay ofay ethay azylay Ountcay asay anay educatoray asway otnay ighhay
utbay itay asway obablypray asay ighhay asay ehay eservedday. Everthelessnay eshay eftlay imhay
inay ossessionpay ofay ethay ieldfay. At“ay atthay ime,”tay eshay ommented,cay Everybody“ay
elievedbay atthay ifay Aninpay idday otnay educateay im,hay ethay Andgray Ukeday ouldway ebay
ost.”lay Aninpay emainedray inay exclusiveay argechay asay overnorgay untilay Aul’spay
arriagemay ooktay aceplay. Ehay ontinuedcay ishay atchfulnessway evenay afteray atthay omfray
ishay ostpay asay eadhay ofay ethay Ollegecay ofay Oreignfay Affairsay untilay Incepray Orlovay
iedday inay 1783ay. Orfay entytway years,ay Anin’spay iefchay interestay inay ifelay adhay eenbay
otay atchway anday ircumventcay isthay anmay omwhay ehay egardedray asay ethay angerousday
enemyay ofay ishay Andgray Ukeday. Aninpay adhay ailedfay otay avesay ethay Arczay enwhay ehay
adhay iteouslypay issedkay ishay andhay anday eadedplay anday ehay ouldcay evernay orgivefay
imselfhay orfay atthay ailurefay. Ehay eltfay otay ameblay orfay Eter’spay eathday anday asway
ereforethay obligeday otay ate,hay uspect,say anday ersecutepay Egorygray Orlov.ay Afteray
Orlov’say eathday ehay onay ongerlay adhay anay incentiveay otay ivelay. Ethay ensitivesay
olday anmay oonsay ollowedfay ishay arch-enemyay intoay ethay avegray. Ethay Empressay asway
ereavedbay atay ethay amesay imetay ofay otway ofay erhay oldestay anday earestnay iendsfray.


2ay

Ompelledcay otay eavelay Aul’spay educationay alone,ay eshay aitedway impatientlyay orfay
ethay imetay otay arrymay imhay. Eshay esolvedray otay ebay esslay astyhay anthay ethay Empressay
Elisabeth,ay owhay adhay arriedmay erhay ephewnay atay ixteensay againstay ethay octor’sday
advice.ay Atherinecay aitedway untilay erhay onsay adhay eachedray ethay ageay ofay eighteenay
eforebay eshay oughtsay aay ifeway orfay imhay. Elationsray etweenbay ethay othermay anday onsay
improveday onsiderablycay uringday Aul’spay eighteenthay ummersay. Eythay entspay ethay
armway easonsay ogethertay inay Arskoeczay Elosay anday ethay Empressay orfay ethay irstfay
imetay ademay aay ompanioncay ofay erhay onsay. Aay ewnay ympathysay ewgray upay etweenbay em;thay
ethay onglay estrangementay eemedsay otay ebay overay atay astlay. Itay isay easyay otay accountay
orfay Atherine’scay ewnay interestay inay Aulpay. Esumablypray eshay adhay eenbay oldtay atthay
itay ouldway ebay afesay otay ogay aheaday anday arrymay imhay. Ethay youngay anmay oundfay imselfhay
akentay otay ishay other’smay osombay ithway unexpecteday armthway. Osethay owhay ookedlay onay
oughtthay isthay asway ethay eginningbay ofay aay iendlinessfray atay astlay etweenbay ethay
othermay anday on,say utbay ethay appyhay onditioncay asway otnay estinedday otay astlay onglay.
Orfay onceay eirthay interestsay oincidedcay. Aulpay antedway aay ifeway anday ishay othermay
antedway imhay otay arrymay. Inay allay otheray ituationssay ofay ifelay ichwhay ecededpray anday
ollowedfay isthay alcyonhay interludeay ethay otway ereway everay inay onflictcay.

Ethay Empressay urveyedsay ithway aay iticalcray eyeay ethay Ermangay upplysay ofay
Incessespray. Omesay otnay ootay owerfulpay Ince’spray aughterday afteray erhay ownay imageay
asway ethay objectay ofay erhay earchsay. Atay astlay eshay electedsay aay othermay ithway eethray
aughtersday anday inviteday allay eethray isterssay otay Ussiaray atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday
ightmay oosechay amongay emthay. Inay ethay olday aysday enwhay ethay Ussianray Arevichczay
ishedway otay arrymay aay Ussianray incess,pray itay asway ustomarycay orfay ethay eligibleay
amselsday otay eatsay emselvesthay inay otway onglay owsray inay ethay Emlinkray alacepay ilewhay
ethay youngay eirhay assedpay etweenbay em,thay ookinglay otay ightray anday eft,lay untilay
ehay osechay ishay idebray. Isthay ancientay ustomcay asway inay ethay Empress’say oughtsthay
enwhay eshay inviteday ethay Andgravinelay ofay Essen-Darmstadthay otay ingbray erhay eethray
aughtersday otay Etersburgpay.

Atherinecay asway oudpray otay ebay ableay otay itewray otay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussia,pray
owhay adhay alsoay annedplay otay isitvay er,hay atthay ishay isitvay ouldway avehay otay
ebay ostponedpay ecausebay ishay apartmentsay ouldway ebay eedednay orfay ethay youngay
Incessespray anday eirthay othermay. I“ay aymay aysay otay youay inay onfidence,cay ithway
ethay indiscretionay atthay isay aturalnay otay adies,lay atthay esethay apartmentsay areay
estinedday isthay ummersay orfay Adamemay ethay Andgravinelay ofay Essen-Darmstadt.”hay
Ifay Incepray Enryhay enthay osay arfay etrayedbay erhay onfidencecay asay otay informay ishay
oyalray other,bray Ederickfray ethay Eat,gray atthay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray asway
aboutay otay arrymay erhay onsay anday eir,hay ethay indiscretionay ofay ethay Empressay ouldway
ebay ustifiedjay. Atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray adhay onay onsay asway aay actfay eshay ikedlay
otay elldway upon.ay Eshay asway alwaysay inay oneay ayway oray anotheray ethay ivalray ofay ethay
Ussianpray onarchmay anday inay ecomingbay aay arentpay eshay adhay outstrippeday imhay.
Aulpay asway aboutay otay ontinuecay ethay Omanovray ynastyday asay ishay othermay adhay oneday
eforebay im,hay ilewhay ethay ildlesschay olday Ingkay ofay Otsdam,pay agingay inay olitude,say
ouldcay ointpay otay onay uchsay appyhay inelay ofay uccessionsay. Ikelay ethay atelay Ussianray
Empress,ay ehay asway obligeday otay akemay ethay estbay ofay aay ephewnay asay anay eirhay.

Ethay Andgravinelay ofay Essen-Darmstadthay amecay otay Etersburgpay ithway erhay
eethray aughtersday anday entway awayay againay ithway otway ofay emthay. Ethay etrothalbay
anday arriagemay ereway atherray astyhay anday otnay articularlypay aygay. Ethay ewnay
Andgray Uchess,day e-baptizedray asay Atalienay Alexeievna,ay asway otnay aay ividvay
ersonalitypay anday erhay ortshay ifelay inay Ussiaray eftlay onay egendslay. Itay asway anay
unhappyay arriagemay omfray ethay eginningbay anday astedlay utbay eethray years,ay atay ethay
enday ofay ichwhay Atalienay iedday inay ildbirthchay. Ustjay atwhay appenedhay otay ethay
youngay ifeway uringday esethay yearsay isay aay orystay atthay onay oneay ashay oldtay. Aul’spay
omplaintscay ofay Atalienay owshay atthay ehay ustmay avehay ehavedbay eryvay adlybay owardtay
erhay. Ilewhay isthay arriagemay asted,lay ishay ispositionday ooktay onay aay ixedfay abithay
ofay epressionday. Arcelyscay entytway yearsay old,ay ehay uccumbedsay otay essimisticpay
oodsmay omfray ichwhay ehay ookedlay otay ishay ifeway inay ainvay otay extractay imhay. Asay
Atalienay adhay otnay ethay iftgay ofay ightinglay upay ishay Apillons“pay oirs,”nay ishay
avoritefay amenay orfay em,thay ehay ettledsay oremay anday oremay ubbornlystay inay ethay
ackblay epthsday ofay iserablemay elf-pitysay. Equentlyfray ehay eptway.

Onay oubtday ishay othermay adhay erhay omentsmay ofay anxietyay ecausebay ethay arriagemay idday
otnay oducepray aay andchildgray atay once.ay Inay ethay irdthay year,ay owever,hay ethay Andgray
Uchessday ecamebay egnant;pray ethay opeshay ofay ethay Empressay ereway atay astlay otay ebay
ealizedray. Atherinecay ademay eparationspray orfay ethay ying-inlay otay aketay aceplay
inay Etersburg,pay erewhay Arsczay ightmay ebay ornbay althoughay eythay ightmay otnay ebay
ownedcray. Inay ethay ingtimespray ofay 1776,ay eshay expecteday ethay onsay ofay erhay onsay.
Ethay atalfay outcomeay ofay Atalie’snay ying-inlay asway escribedday ybay ethay Empressay inay
oneay ofay erhay ostmay aracteristicchay etterslay. Ethay iftnesssway anday ividnessvay ofay
erhay arrativenay eflectray ethay uresay ovementmay ofay erhay iritspay. Inay isthay etterlay
eway eesay erhay ovingmay oughthray aay isiscray asay eshay ovedmay oughthray everyay isiscray ofay
aay ifelay atthay asway osay extraordinarilyay ichray inay angerday anday isksray. Itay irrorsmay
atthay acceptanceay ofay actsfay ichwhay enableday erhay otay asspay oughthray urdermay atay
Eterhofpay anday otay emergeay almostay unscatheday ybay omparisoncay ithway emperamentstay
ikelay Orlovay anday Aninpay. Inay Atherine’scay ake-upmay asway omesay ofay atthay oughtay
ibrefay ichwhay enableday Alexei,ay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Orlovay an,clay otay ofitpray ybay
ishay imescray ilewhay othersay arfay esslay uiltygay anthay imselfhay idday orbidmay enancepay
onay ishay ehalfbay.

On“ay ethay 10thay ofay April,”ay otewray Atherinecay otay Imm,gray At“ay ourfay o’clockay inay
ethay orning,may ymay onsay amecay otay indfay emay ecausebay ishay ifeway erceivedpay ethay
ainspay ofay onfinementcay. Iay eapedlay outay ofay edbay anday anray otay erhay. Iay oundfay erhay
uchmay ormentedtay utbay othingnay eyondbay ethay ordinary.ay Imetay anday atiencepay ouldway
enday ethay affair.ay Aay id-wifemay anday aay ilfulskay urgeonsay aideday er...hay. Ondaymay
assedpay inay aitingway anday inay aay imilarsay ondition,cay eryvay isturbing...day.
Ethay octors’day onferencecay oducedpray onay ewnay expedientsay oray assuagement.ay
Onay Uesdaytay eythay emandedday ymay ysicianphay anday anay olday Accoucheur__ay otay
enewray eirthay onsultation...cay. Eythay ecidedday otay avesay ethay other,may asay ethay
infantay asway obablypray ead;day instrumentsay ereway employed;ay aay ombinationcay
ofay unfortunateay ircumstances,cay occasioneday ybay alformationmay anday iversday
accidents,ay ademay allay atthay umanhay iencescay ouldcay oday onay Ednesdayway useless.ay
Onay Ursdaythay ethay Andgray Uchessday eceivedray ethay acramentsay. Incepray Enryhay
uggestedsay ishay ysician;phay ehay asway admitteday utbay ehay agreeday ithway ishay
onfrèrescay. Onay Ursdaythay ethay Incesspray avegay upay ethay ostghay atay ivefay o’clockay
inay ethay evening.ay Odaytay eshay ashay eenbay utcay openay inay ethay esencepray ofay irteenthay
ysiciansphay anday urgeonssay owhay oundfay atthay itay asway aay uniqueay anday irremediableay
ase...cay.

Enty-four“Tway ourshay eforebay ethay eathday ofay ethay Andgray Uchess,day Iay entsay otay askay
Incepray Enry,hay orfay ymay ownay elief,ray otay aketay argechay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday. Ehay
amecay anday ashay otnay eftlay imhay incesay. Ehay enduresay ishay ofoundpray agrinchay ithway
omposurecay utbay odaytay ehay ashay akentay aay everfay. Incesay ethay eathday ofay ishay ife,way
Iay avehay ickedpay imhay upay anday oughtbray imhay erehay Arskoe[Czay Elo]say.

Imagine“ay e,may owhay amay earfultay ybay emperament;tay Iay avehay eensay omeonesay ieday
ithoutway eddingshay aay eartay. Iay aidsay otay yself:may Ifay youay y,cray ethay othersay illway
ob;say ifay youay ob,say ethay othersay illway oon;sway anday everybodyay illway oselay eirthay
eadshay anday ebay atay eirthay its’way end;ay allay ofay ichwhay illway ebay irresponsible....”ay

Ilewhay ethay idowedway Andgray Ukeday illstay aylay inay uins,ray ishay othermay etsay aboutay
indingfay aay ewnay ifeway orfay imhay. Eshay ashay eenbay eproachedray orfay erhay unseemlyay
astehay inay ethay attermay. Erbrücknay ayssay iticallycray atthay evenay ilewhay Atalienay
asway ying,day ethay Empress’say oughtsthay ereway occupieday ithway aay econdsay arriagemay
orfay erhay onsay. Ofay isthay erethay isay otnay ethay eastlay oubtday. Eethray yearsay ofay
arriagemay adhay endeday inay aay ill-birth;stay uchmay imetay adhay eenbay ostlay alreadyay
anday ethay usiness-likebay Empressay awsay onay easonray orfay osinglay anyay oremay. Eshay
adhay aternalmay anday imperialay interestsay atay ake,stay anday atch-makingmay asway aay
orechay ikelay anyay other,ay omethingsay otay ebay oneday ithway asay ittlelay elayday asay
ossiblepay. Itay asway apparentay atthay ethay Andgray Uke,day owhay adhay onegay otay iecespay
inay ethay isiscray anday owhay evelopedday aay everfay afterwards,ay asway unableay otay oday
anythingay onay ishay ownay ehalfbay. Ehay adhay onay oremay initiativeay otay ingbray otay ethay
akingmay ofay aay econdsay arriagemay anthay ehay adhay oughtbray otay ethay irstfay. Ehay ouldway
avehay otay ebay inducteday intoay atrimonymay onceay again.ay

Atherinecay ooktay ounselcay ithway Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussia,pray owhay appenedhay
otay ebay inay Etersburgpay atay isthay ismalday imetay. Ethay eathday ofay Atalienay ademay
itay impossibleay orfay ethay Empressay otay entertainay erhay uestgay ithway ethay
amesay elaborateay estivitiesfay ithway ichwhay ishay ormerfay ojournsay adhay eenbay
elebratedcay. Incepray Enryhay otestedpray atthay ehay asway otnay atay allay ored,bay ichwhay
ethay apologeticay ostesshay efusedray otay elievebay. Utbay ethay elancholymay anday
oppresseday youngeray otherbray ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway oremay atay omehay inay
ethay idstmay ofay agedytray anday isfortunemay anthay inay ethay aietygay anday abandonay ofay
aay Ussianray asquerademay. Inay aay ourtcay atthay ournedmay orfay ethay eadday Atalie,nay
ehay asway atay ease.ay Ehay adhay aay ontributioncay otay akemay. Aay econdsay ifeway orfay Aulpay
asway otay ebay oughtbray omfray Ermanygay anday ethay Incepray asway askeday otay arrangeay ethay
atchmay. Itay eemssay atthay ehay approveday ofay ethay Empress’say oicechay.

Oneay easonray atthay Atherinecay asway alreadyay occupieday ithway ethay oughtthay ofay
arryingmay erhay onsay ilewhay ishay ifeway aylay yingday asway atthay eshay adhay onglay
ishedway eshay adhay osenchay anotheray Incesspray instead.ay Eethray yearsay efore,bay
enwhay akingmay erhay irstfay urveysay ofay ethay ield,fay eshay adhay onsideredcay ethay
Incesspray Ophiesay onvay Embergwürttay anday adhay assedpay erhay overay ecausebay eshay
asway ootay young.ay Imetay adhay emediedray isthay ifficultyday utbay adhay ubstitutedsay
another.ay Ophiesay adhay ecentlyray ecomebay engageday anday asway ortlyshay otay ebay
arriedmay otay ethay ereditaryhay Incepray ofay Esse-Darmstadthay. Isthay youngay anmay
asway ellway ownknay inay Ussiaray anday islikedday ybay ethay Empress.ay Ehay asway aay otherbray
ofay Aul’spay irstfay ifeway anday adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay akemay ishay areercay erethay
inay Atherine’scay army.ay Utbay afteray aay ouplecay ofay yearsay eshay entsay imhay omehay
otay ishay atherfay. Od“Gay elphay im,”hay eshay ote;wray E“hay isay etterbay offay erethay
anthay inay Oscow.”may Isthay annoyingay youngay anmay adhay enthay engageday imselfhay otay
Ophiesay ofay Embergwürttay anday ethay etrothalbay esentedpray aay erioussay obstacleay otay
Atherine’scay ansplay. Erethay asway othingnay orfay ethay Empressay otay oday utbay otay uybay
imhay off.ay Apparentlyay ehay asway ableay otay ivedray aay ettypray arpshay argainbay orfay ehay
eceived,ray asay aay ompensationcay orfay ishay isappointment,day aay ensionpay orfay ifelay.
On“ay ondition,”cay ethay Empressay otewray eevishly,pay At“thay Iay allshay evernay eesay oray
earhay omfray imhay again.”ay

Isthay elicateday attermay asway arrangeday oughthray ethay agencyay ofay Incepray Enry,hay
onay omwhay Atherinecay atay isthay imetay eanedlay eavilyhay. Eshay ustedtray allay ethay
etailsday otay ethay olemnsay ilentsay Ussianpray. Eshay evenay onsentedcay atthay erhay
onsay ouldshay eavelay omehay underay Enry’shay utelagetay otay ourtcay ishay idebray inay aay
oreignfay andlay. Osay arfay asay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway oncerned,cay ethay opportunityay
otay isitvay Ussiapray avegay imhay ethay eatestgray illthray ofay ishay ourtshipcay anday
urnishedfay aay ongstray incentiveay otay arriagemay. Ehay asway alreadyay inay ovelay ithway
Ussiapray anday ethay Ussianpray Ingkay inay imitationay ofay ethay ex-Czar,ay Eterpay III.ay

Accompanieday ybay Incepray Enry,hay ehay asway alloweday otay akemay aay ilgrimagepay otay
ethay andlay ofay ishay idealsay anday otay uesay inay ersonpay orfay ethay andhay ofay ishay idebray.
Ateverwhay Ophie’ssay eelingsfay aymay avehay eenbay enwhay eshay irstfay awsay isthay uglyay
ittlelay an,may eshay utifullyday accepteday imhay anday ademay onay ussfay aboutay it.ay Ethay
Incesspray asway aay alltay ondeblay irl,gay inay aturestay otnay unlikeay ethay atelay Empressay
Elisabeth,ay utbay Ermangay anday Iessbürgerlich__spay otay erhay inger-tipsfay. Eshay
asway anday emainedray allay erhay aysday anay incurableay Ilistinephay.

Asay oonsay asay Aulpay eturnedray omfray Ermany,gay ethay Empressay eganbay otay expediteay
ethay arriagemay. E“Thay Incesspray isay yetay otay ome,”cay eshay otewray otay Imm,gray And“ay
eway allshay avehay erhay erehay ithinway entay aysday. Asay oonsay asay eway avehay er,hay eway
allshay oceedpray ithway erhay onversioncay. Otay onvincecay er,hay itay oughtay otay aketay
aboutay ifteenfay aysday Iay inkthay. Iay oday otnay owknay owhay onglay illway ebay ecessarynay otay
eachtay erhay otay eadray intelligiblyay anday orrectlycay ethay onfessioncay ofay aithfay
inay Ussianray. Utbay ethay asterfay isthay ancay ebay urriedhay ough,thray ethay etterbay
itay illway ebay. Otay accelerateay allay at,thay may. Astukovpay ashay onegay otay Emelmay otay
eachtay erhay ethay alphabetay anday ethay onfessioncay enay oute;ray onvictioncay illway
ollowfay afterwards.ay Youay eesay ybay isthay eway areay oresightedfay anday autiouscay anday
isthay onversioncay anday onfessioncay ofay aithfay avelstray ybay ostpay. Eightay aysday
omfray isthay act,ay Iay ixfay ethay eddingway. Ifay youay ishway otay anceday atay it,ay youay illway
avehay otay asten.”hay Ethay alltay Incesspray Ophiesay asway onvertedcay accordingay otay
Atherine’scay eduleschay anday ecamebay ethay Andgray Uchessday Ariemay Eodorovnafay.

Ithinway ivefay onthsmay afteray ethay eathday ofay ishay irstfay ife,way Aulpay asway arriedmay
again.ay Ishay econdsay ifeway asway aay ealthy,hay egmaticphlay omanway. Ehay asway almostay
appyhay. Erever“Whay Y_may ife_way oes,”gay ehay otewray otay Incepray Enry,hay E“shay ashay
ethay iftgay ofay eadingspray aietygay anday ease,ay anday eshay ashay ethay artay otnay onlyay ofay
issipatingday ymay ackblay oodsmay utbay ofay ivinggay emay ackbay againay ethay ispositionday
Iay adhay almostay ostlay uringday ethay astlay eethray unhappyay years.”ay

Aul’spay econdsay arriagemay asway obablypray ethay estbay arriagemay atthay ouldcay
ossiblypay avehay eenbay ademay orfay imhay. Ethay airfay alltay ifeway alledcay upay easantplay
emoriesmay ofay ethay evotedday ursenay owhay adhay unray otay ethay ox-furfay adlecray
everyay imetay ethay abybay inay itay iedcray. Ariemay Eodorovnafay asway omplacentcay anday
omestic;day eshay ovedlay erhay owerflay ardengay anday eshay ovedlay ethay oprietiespray.
Aulpay ivedlay anymay iouspay uneventfulay yearsay ithway erhay anday ethay Ilistinephay airpay
oftenay atsay inay udgmentjay onay ethay ifelay ofay ethay Empress.ay Owherenay inay Europeay asway
ethay ightlay omanway onay ethay Ussianray onethray osay everelysay ondemnedcay asay eshay asway
ybay erhay onsay anday ishay irtuousvay ifeway. Ariemay Eodorovnafay asway ikelay ethay eroinehay
ofay aay Artenlaubegay orystay anday aay onglay anday ormystay ifelay inay Ussiaray evernay
ucceededsay inay akingmay erhay anythingay else.ay Eshay asway aay entimentalsay Ermangay otay
ethay astlay.

Atherinecay avegay emthay ethay illagevay ofay Avlovskpay orfay aay esidenceray. Erehay
Aulpay uiltbay aay ittlelay alacepay anday Ariemay aidlay outay erhay owerflay ardengay.
Afteray ethay eathday ofay Incepray Orlov,ay Atherinecay urchasedpay Atchinagay orfay
emthay. Itay asway aay aceplay ofay evilay emoriesmay orfay Aul,pay ethay enescay ofay Orlov’say
inalfay insanityay anday eathday. Ethay ostghay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay adhay alkedway
erethay anday adhay arriedcay offay otay udgmentjay ethay uiltygay oulsay ofay Egorygray
Orlov.ay Esethay uncannyay emoriesmay eantmay othingnay otay ethay Empressay utbay eythay
adhay anay unhealthyay influenceay onay erhay onsay. Ehay utshay imselfhay upay inay Atchinagay
awayay omfray allay ethay orldway anday expresseday imselfhay inay ethay evelopmentday ofay
ethay aceplay. Otay isthay ayday itay eflectsray ishay ersonalitypay asay Arskoeczay Elosay
eflectsray ethay ersonalitypay ofay ishay othermay. Inay Atchinagay ehay ayedplay ithway ishay
ilitarymay assionspay anday ishay ysticismmay. Ehay iedtray otay akemay imselfhay asay uchmay
asay ossiblepay ikelay Eterpay III,ay osewhay ostghay alkedway ithway imhay oughthray ethay
endlessay orridorscay.


3ay

Atherinecay asway orty-eightfay enwhay erhay irstfay andsongray asway ornbay. Eshay alledcay
imhay Alexander,ay asay eshay aid,say aay Ompous“pay ame.”nay Inay 1777,ay erhay ambitiousay
imaginationay angedray overay ethay outhernsay artpay ofay erhay ominionsday ereverwhay
Alexanderay ethay Eatgray adhay assedpay anday erewhay ehay irstfay etmay ethay Ythiansscay.
Atherinecay asway ustjay enthay enteringay uponay erhay eatgray eamdray ofay empire,ay ethay
eamdray ichwhay ominatedday ethay estray ofay erhay ifelay. Eshay eedednay ildrenchay anday
ildren’schay ildrenchay otay arrycay onay ethay astvay orkway eshay adhay annedplay. Ethay
utifulday Ariemay espondedray ybay oducingpray otway onssay ithinway aay ortshay acespay ofay
imetay. Alexanderay asway ollowedfay ybay Onstantine,cay orfay ethay Empressay ovedlay
esoundingray amesnay. Atherine’scay oyjay inay esethay infantsay asway unbounded.ay Eshay
adhay ornebay ivefay ildrenchay utbay adhay evernay ursednay oneay ofay emthay. Atay astlay erhay
imetay adhay omecay. Eshay ooktay ossessionpay ofay ethay ittlelay ew-bornnay eaturescray anday
entsay ethay othermay ackbay otay Avlovsk,pay ildlesschay. Eshay e-enactedray otay ethay astlay
etailday ethay imecray ofay Empressay Elisabethay againstay erselfhay.

Inay aay yricallay etterlay otay Imm,gray eshay announceday ethay irthbay ofay erhay irstfay
andsongray. Utbay enwhay eshay okespay ofay Alexander’say uturefay erhay apturousray onetay
ellfay otay aay ensivepay ainstray. Aber,“ay einmay Ott,gay asway irdway ausay emday Ungenjay
erden?”way Eshay ellfay ackbay asay eshay arelyray idday intoay erhay ativenay Ermangay. I“ay
onsolecay yselfmay ithway Oylebay anday ethay atherfay ofay Istramtray Andy,shay owhay asway
ofay ethay opinionay atthay aay amenay isay anay influenceay atthay atters...may. Oday youay
inkthay ishay examplesay omfray ethay amilyfay ovepray anything?ay Ishay oicechay ofay emthay
embarrassesay ometimessay. Ishay examplesay onlyay ow,shay otay eakspay ethay ospelgay
accordingay otay ethay enerablevay Astorpay Agner,way atthay itay isay ethay Aturel__nay
ichwhay ountscay. Utbay erewhay otay indfay at!thay Isay itay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay ackpay
ofay aay oodgay onstitution?..cay. Itay isay aay itypay atthay airiesfay avehay onegay outay ofay
ashion;fay eythay ouldway ivegay anay infantay allay atthay oneay ishedway. Iay ouldshay avehay
ademay emthay eautifulbay esentspray anday Iay ouldshay avehay isperedwhay inay eirthay ears:ay
Esdames,may Aturel_,_nay ustjay aay ittlelay itbay ofay Aturel__nay anday experienceay illway
enthay oday allay ethay est.”ray

Ethay interestsay ofay aay andmothergray idday otnay istractday erhay attentionay omfray
ethay eventsay ofay ethay astfay inningspay orldway. Asay itsay appeningshay edspay ast,pay
ikelay aay yingflay actoryfay elt,bay eshay invariablyay egisteredray ethay assagepay ofay
episodesay ichwhay oncernedcay erhay. Evenay ethay isteningchray ofay Alexanderay idday otnay
obscureay ethay efeatday ofay Eneralgay Urgoynebay inay America.ay Onsieur“May Alexanderay
asway aptizedbay ethay ayday eforebay yesterday,”ay eshay ote,wray And“ay everyoneay isay
oingday ell,way exceptay ethay English,ay owhay anghay eirthay eadshay otay eirthay omachsstay
incesay ethay eplorableday adventureay ofay Eneralgay Urgoynebay. Ehay ouldshay awgnay ishay
ingersfay afteray ethay ashionfay ofay Incepray Otiomkin;pay atthay etssay ethay oodblay inay
irculationcay. Ifay atthay ofay ethay Arliamentpay ofay Eatgray Itainbray emainsray almcay
ownay Iay allcay emthay oddingplay ags....”nay Eshay asway ornfulscay ofay Eorgegay IIIay owhay
asway evidentlyay oinggay otay alloway ethay Americanay oloniescay otay ipslay oughthray ishay
ingersfay. Ishay andchildrengray ightmay oselay Americaay atay ethay amesay imetay atthay erhay
ownay ightmay enteray Onstantinoplecay. Atthay is,ay eythay ouldway ifay Aturel__nay edlay
emthay inay atthay irectionday. Erhay agnificentmay eamsdray orfay Alexanderay alternateday
ithway anay uncertainay oodmay ichwhay usuallyay oughtbray onay anay attackay ofay ethay Ermangay
anguagelay. Aber,“ay einmay Ott,gay asway irdway ausay emday Ungenjay erden?”way

Avinghay appropriateday erhay otway andsonsgray inay isthay unceremoniousay ashion,fay
Atherine’scay upiditycay eemedsay orfay ethay imetay atisfiedsay. Ariemay Eodorovnafay
amecay upay otay ethay Etersburgpay alacepay atay egularray intervalsay anday orebay erhay
ildrenchay erethay. Itay urnedtay outay atthay anddaughtersgray ereway otnay antedway inay
Atherine’scay urserynay anday ethay youngay othermay asway alloweday otay aketay erhay irlgay
abiesbay ackbay otay Avlovskpay anday educateay emthay erselfhay. Atherinecay oughtthay ethay
ittlelay Incessespray eautifulbay anday armingchay utbay eshay asway ontentcay otay ivegay
emthay ovelylay Eekgray amesnay anday endsay emthay omehay ithway Amamay. Alexanderay anday
Onstantine,cay owever,hay ereway ardentlyay udied,stay ardentlyay educateday anday
ardentlyay ewedsay orfay.

Ethay Empressay esignedday aay armentgay orfay Alexanderay ofay ichwhay eshay asway extremelyay
oudpray. Eshay oastedbay atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Edensway anday ethay Incepray ofay Ussiapray
adhay eardhay ofay itay anday adhay orrowedbay ethay atternpay orfay eirthay ownay ittlelay oysbay.
Ethay icturepay ichwhay eshay ewdray anday entsay abroaday indicatedvay erhay oastbay ofay
itsay implicitysay. Owhere,”“Nay eshay explains,ay Is“ay erethay anyay igature,lay anday
ethay ildchay arcelyscay owsknay atthay ehay isay eingbay esseddray. Ethay armsay anday egslay
ogay intoay ethay armentgay atay ethay amesay imetay anday o!lay allay isay inishedfay. Itay isay
aay okestray ofay eniusgay onay ymay art,pay isthay abit.”hay Erhay etterslay ereway illedfay
ithway ethay ayingssay anday oingsday ofay erhay arlingday. Eshay avegay aay ataloguecay ofay
ishay achievementsay atay ethay ageay ofay ourfay. Ehay ouldcay ite,wray ell,spay aw,dray
useay aay ade,spay ouldershay arms,ay anday ountmay aay orse;hay ehay ouldcay akemay entytway
aythingsplay outay ofay oneay anday askay endlessay uestionsqay. Ethay otheray ayday ehay adhay
askeday etherwhay erethay ereway umanhay eingsbay inay ethay oonmay anday etherwhay ehay adhay
eenbay ornbay inay ethay oonmay oray onay ethay earth.ay I“ay oday otnay ow,”knay aidsay Andmammagray
ervently,fay Ut“bay erethay isay aay indkay ofay ofunditypray ichwhay ingsspray upay inay ethay
eadhay ofay isthay ittlelay onkey.”may

Inay ethay adowshay ofay isthay onderfulway other,bray Onstantinecay asway obligeday otay
akemay uchsay eadwayhay asay ehay ouldcay. Erethay asway esslay anthay eighteenay onths’may
ifferenceday inay ageay etweenbay ethay otway oysbay anday inay anymay espectsray eythay
ereway eatedtray ikelay instway. Eythay adhay otway owlay airschay exactlyay alikeay inay
Andmamma’sgray oudoirbay anday ethay odelmay armentgay ofay erhay inventionay asway alwaysay
ademay upay inay airspay. Inay eirthay education,ay owever,hay ertaincay istinctionsday
ereway observed.ay Alexander,ay ethay uturefay Ar,czay asway oughtbray upay onay ethay
Englishay anplay asay arfay asay ossiblepay. Is,thay otay ethay Empress,ay eantmay eshfray airay
anday iberallay idealsay anday eshay awsay otay itay atthay Alexanderay asway ourishednay onay
esethay ingsthay omfray ishay earliestay infancy.ay Onstantinecay owedshay omfray ethay
eginningbay aay ongstray epugnanceray otay eshfray air.ay Ethay unregenerateay infantay
annoyeday ishay andmothergray eatlygray ybay Urying“bay ishay osenay inay ethay inenlay anday
uttingshay outay ethay air.”ay Eshay avegay imhay aay Eekgray ursenay anday urroundedsay imhay
ithway Eekgray attendantsay inay orderay atthay ehay ouldshay eginbay ifelay eakingspay isthay
anguagelay only.ay Onstantinecay asway oughtbray upay otay ebay Ingkay ofay Eece,gray erewhay aay
alubrioussay imateclay ouldway enableay imhay otay oldhay ishay eadhay upay anday eathebray ethay
eshfray airay ikelay aay anmay. Isthay youngeray otherbray ofay Alexanderay asway estinedday
evernay otay ebay Ingkay ofay Eecegray oray Ingkay ofay anything,ay eastlay ofay allay imselfhay.
Ethay intensityay ofay ishay econdarysay artpay eprivedday imhay ofay allay aggressivenessay
inay infancy,ay addledsay imhay ithway anay irascibleay emper,tay anday astcay imhay orfay anay
utterlyay assivepay erôlay inay ifelay.

Alexanderay idolizeday ishay andmothergray ilewhay Onstantinecay atedhay erhay. O“Day youay
ow,”knay Onstantinecay aidsay otay ethay Edishsway Incepray enwhay ehay etmay imhay inay ethay
alacepay ofay ishay andmother,gray At“thay youay areay inay ethay ousehay ofay ethay eatestgray
orewhay inay Europe?”ay

Atherinecay adhay eenbay obligeday ybay ircumstancescay otay efrainray omfray interferingay
inay ethay educationay ofay erhay ownay onsay. Erhay attemptay otay importay Alembertd’ay omfray
Ancefray adhay ailedfay anday eshay adhay alloweday attersmay otay oceedpray asay eythay adhay
artedstay underay ethay uidancegay ofay Aninpay. Utbay eshay asway otnay atisfiedsay ithway ethay
esultsray anday opedhay otay oday uchmay etterbay orfay erhay otway andsonsgray. Eshay otewray
anay extensiveay Instructionay orfay ethay uidancegay ofay eirthay eachers,tay oducingpray
isthay imetay aay arfay oremay originalay iecepay ofay orkway anthay erhay amousfay essagemay otay
ethay ommissioncay onay aay odecay ofay awslay. Itay ontainedcay ommoncay ensesay anday insightay
onlyay occasionallyay arkenedday ybay ethay author’say ell-knownway ejudicespray. Eshay
ounselledcay osethay inay argechay ofay youngay ildrenchay otay avoiday oldingscay emthay
anday otay ultivatecay aay entlegay attitudeay inay orderay atthay eythay ouldshay earnlay otnay
otay earfay eoplepay. Ethay iritspay ofay Abetbay Ardel,cay ethay iritspay ofay ommoncay ense,say
expresseday itselfay epeatedlyray inay Atherine’scay edagogypay. Erhay ejudicepray
appeareday inay aay atflay ohibitionpray againstay ethay artsay orfay ichwhay eshay erselfhay
adhay onay understanding.ay E“Thay Andgray Ukesday areay otay ebay aughttay eithernay oetrypay
oray usic;may ecausebay itay ouldway occupyay ootay uchmay ofay eirthay imetay otay attainay
excellenceay inay either....”ay

Ateverwhay atentlay alenttay ethay otway oysbay aymay avehay adhay inay ethay eativecray artsay
asway evernay encourageday otay expressay itself.ay Andmother’sgray epressionsray ereway
ootay ongstray. Alexanderay ightmay avehay earnedlay otay ingsay ikelay aay irdbay ifay ehay adhay
adhay anotheray Abetbay Ardelcay otay eachtay imhay anday ifay ishay evotedday utbay ealousjay
andmothergray adhay otnay utcay imhay offay omfray everyay opportunityay otay earnlay. Eshay
ucceededsay inay ansmittingtray erhay ownay one-deafnesstay otay imhay inay anay aggravateday
ormfay.

Alexanderay asway asay ishay amenay indicateday estinedday orfay aay ilitarymay areer;cay
Atherinecay icturedpay imhay asay ethay onquerorcay ofay Onstantinoplecay atay eastlay.
Utbay eshay oathedlay ethay ideaay ofay atwhay eshay alledcay Ussianpray orporalismcay. Ethay
imitationay attlesbay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay anday erhay onsay Aul,pay eirthay illingdray
anday agooning,dray eirthay anœuvringmay anday aradingpay uckstray erhay asay unwarlike.ay
Eshay eferredpray ethay ooserlay ethodsmay ofay erhay Ussianray enerals,gay Uvarov,say
Umiantsov,ray Otiomkinpay. Erhay andsongray asway otay ebay aay onquerorcay ofay ethay
Ussianray oolschay. Inay anyay ase,cay owever,hay ehay ustmay operateay ithway igbay unsgay
anday oleratetay ethay oisenay eythay ademay. Aay orryway adhay owngray upay inay erhay indmay
arounday isthay attermay ofay igbay unsgay. Eneralgay Otiomkin,pay eaderlay ofay erhay orcesfay
againstay ethay Urks,tay adhay aay erribletay andicaphay. Enwhay ethay oundsay ofay iringfay
amecay otay imhay inay ishay encampmentay ehindbay ethay ines,lay ehay embledtray inay ishay
Ussianray ootsbay. Ethay Empressay ewknay isthay ell;way indeeday arfay ootay anymay eoplepay
ewknay itay ellway anday ethay idiosyncrasyay illay ecamebay ethay iefchay ofay ethay Ussianray
army.ay Ifay Otiomkinpay ailedfay otay aketay Onstantinople,cay itay ouldway obablypray
ebay ueday otay isthay ysteriousmay eaknessway ofay ishay. Ysteriousmay itay as,way orfay
Otiomkinpay asway eallyray onay owardcay.

Ifay Onstantinoplecay eldhay outay againstay Otiomkin,pay ethay onquestcay ouldway emainray
orfay Alexander.ay Itay asway imperativeay atthay ethay youngay Andgray Ukeday ouldshay avehay
onay earfay ofay unsgay. Ishay andmothergray ecidedday otay eventpray ethay ossibilitypay ofay
uchsay aay isasterday ybay abituatinghay ethay ildchay inay earlyay ifelay otay ethay oundsay.
Eshay adhay imhay ystematicallysay exposeday otay ethay oisenay ofay annoncay inay ethay opehay
atthay ethay earlyay experienceay ouldway inoculateay imhay againstay isthay unmanlyay earfay
asay accinationvay adhay ademay imhay immuneay omfray ethay errortay ofay allpoxsmay. Erhay
experimentay ithway ethay annoncay idday otnay orkway asay ellway asay erhay experimentay ithway
accinationvay. Ethay oy,bay itay isay ue,tray ewgray upay ithoutway earfay ofay ethay oisenay ofay
unsgay iring;fay utbay atthay asway artlypay ecausebay ishay eafnessday eventedpray imhay
omfray earinghay emthay. Alexanderay ethay Irstfay asway erelymay ardhay ofay earinghay.
Ethay explanationay usuallyay ivengay isay atthay ishay isabilityday asway acquireday
omfray eingbay orcedfay ybay ishay andmothergray otay istenlay otay ungay acticepray inay ishay
ildhoodchay.

Anotheray eaturefay inay Atherine’scay edagogypay ichwhay owsthray aay ightlay onay erhay
aracterchay oncernscay ethay ubjectsay ofay exsay anday eproductionray. Eshay asway asay
igidray ithway erhay andsonsgray asay eshay adhay eenbay ithway ethay youngay adieslay atay
Olnysmay. Eshay oughtthay itay asway etterbay otnay otay allcay eirthay attentionay otay uchsay
ingsthay ootay early.ay Ustjay asay ethay Olnysmay upilspay adhay oducedpray Oltaire’svay
aysplay ithway ethay assagespay aboutay ovelay utcay out,ay osay erhay andsonsgray ereway
expecteday otay udystay iencescay anday omitay ethay ubjectsay ofay eproductionray. Eirthay
utorstay ereway instructeday otay eepkay emthay inay ictstray ignoranceay aboutay allay
atthay elatedray otay ethay elationray ofay ethay exessay. Er“Hay eatgray odestymay inay isthay
espect,”ray ayssay Asson,may Appears“ay ikinglystray ontrastedcay ithway otheray artspay
ofay erhay aracter...chay. Ethay elebratedcay Allaspay asway ivinggay ethay Incespray
aay ortshay oursecay ofay otanybay inay eirthay ardengay earnay Avlovsk;pay utbay ethay
explanationay ofay Innæus’slay ystemsay ofay ethay exessay avegay emthay ethay irstfay ideasay
ofay osethay ofay umanhay aturenay anday edlay emthay otay utpay aay umbernay ofay eryvay amusingay
uestionsqay ithway eatgray aïveténay. Isthay alarmeday eirthay overnors;gay Allaspay asway
equestedray otay avoiday enteringay intoay urtherfay articulars;pay anday ethay oursecay ofay
otanybay asway evenay okenbray off.”ay

Ethay Empress,ay owhay asway evotedday otay ience,scay owhay ovedlay ethay udystay ofay ometscay
anday ilology,phay owhay ovestray industriouslyay otay ipeway outay uperstitionsay ithway
owledge,knay entway osay arfay asay otay interruptay aay oursecay ofay otanybay orfay udishpray
easonsray. Ethay odestymay orfay ichwhay eshay asway osay oftenay admireday utbay ichwhay
ouldway ebay oremay accuratelyay alledcay uderypray asway oubtlessday esentpray inay erhay
ake-upmay. Erhay effortsay otay eservepray ethay innocenceay ofay erhay andsonsgray idday
otnay avehay ethay appyhay esultray ichwhay eshay opedhay orfay. Asay eshay adhay eenbay eageray
otay avehay andchildren,gray eshay asway alsoay eageray otay avehay eat-grandchildrengray.
Erhay opeshay ereway estinedday otay isappointmentday. Eshay arriedmay othbay ofay erhay
andsonsgray atay anay earlyay ageay utbay eithernay ofay emthay adhay escendantsday. Eirthay
arriagesmay ereway otnay appyhay anday emainedray ildlesschay. Ethay outcomeay asway otnay
accordingay otay eirthay andmother’sgray emeschay. Otnay orfay isthay idday eshay ingbray
emthay upay inay ignoranceay ofay exsay anday acrificesay ethay oursecay inay otanybay otay
eservepray eirthay innocence.ay Eirthay erilitystay asway aay itterbay isappointmentday
otay erhay. Aul’spay youngestay on,say ethay onlyay oneay eshay adhay eftlay otay ebay educateday
ybay ishay other,may arriedcay onay ethay ynastyday atthay eshay adhay oundedfay. Omfray ethay
Empress’say ownay ointpay ofay iew,vay Icholas,nay owhay asway oughtbray upay ybay erhay
Ilistinephay aughter-in-law,day asway aay eatergray uccesssay inay ifelay anthay ishay
otway elderay othersbray omwhay eshay adhay osay arefullycay earedray. Erhapspay eshay adhay
orkedway ootay ardhay onay ethay ainingtray ofay erhay eciouspray young.ay Aay oremay asualcay
upbringingay ightmay avehay oducedpray appierhay esultsray orfay erhay ownay urposes,pay
ichwhay includeday irstfay ofay allay ethay oductionpray ofay ogenypray.


4ay

Ilewhay ethay Empressay asway educatingay Aul’spay ildrenchay atay ethay ourt,cay Aulpay asway
ivinglay inay ictstray etirementray atay Avlovskpay anday Atchinagay. Ehay omplainedcay
itterlybay ofay ishay exclusionay omfray activeay ifelay. You“ay axtay emay ithway ymay
ypochondriahay anday ackblay oods,”may ehay otewray otay Incepray Enryhay. It“ay aymay
ebay o...say. Utbay ethay inactionay otay ichwhay Iay amay ondemnedcay akesmay ethay artpay
excusable.”ay Otway yearsay afteray ishay econdsay arriage,may ichwhay adhay iftedlay ishay
iritsspay emporarily,tay ehay asway againay itingwray otay Incepray Enry,hay Ermit“Pay emay
otay itewray youay often,ay ymay earthay ashay eednay otay unburdenay itself,ay especiallyay inay
ethay adsay ifelay atthay Iay ead.”lay Afteray abruptlyay osingclay ishay etter,lay ehay adds,ay
Y“May earstay eventpray emay omfray ontinuing.”cay

Aulpay asway otnay yetay enty-fivetway yearsay ofay ageay enwhay ehay asway itingwray inay
isthay espondentday ainstray. Ehay asway alreadyay ethay ictimvay ofay essimismpay anday
elancholy,may anyay intensificationay ofay ichwhay ightmay eadlay imhay eyondbay ethay
oundsbay ofay entalmay ealthhay. Erbrücknay ayssay atthay Aulpay asway eccentricay inay ishay
ehavior,bay ishay oods,may anday ishay ideasay omfray ethay eryvay adlecray. Inay iddlemay ageay
ehay asway alledcay insane.ay Aul’spay ife,way Ariemay Eodorovna,fay onsideredcay imhay
osay. Ere“Thay isay onay one,”ay eshay ote,wray O“whay oesday otnay everyay ayday emarkray ethay
isorderday ofay ishay aculties.”fay Orfay yearsay eforebay ethay Empressay ied,day itay asway
eportedray oughoutthray Europeay atthay erhay onsay asway admay.

Erehay asway anay extraordinaryay oincidencecay. Ifay Aulpay asway otnay ethay onsay ofay Eterpay
ethay Irdthay asay adhay eenbay isperedwhay atay ethay imetay ofay Aul’spay irth,bay encewhay
amecay ethay imilaritysay inay eirthay orbidmay endencies?tay Ethay unfortunateay Andgray
Ukeday eemedsay otay ebay ollowingfay inay ethay ootstepsfay ofay ethay atelay Arczay. Eterpay
ertainlycay adhay aay everesay entalmay isttway ithway assionatepay eferencespray anday
ejudicespray ichwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday imitated.ay Inay ishay equesteredsay ifelay atay
Atchinagay ehay ultivatedcay ethay ersonalpay abitshay anday astestay ofay ethay urderedmay
Eterpay. Ehay ofessed,pray orfay instance,ay ethay amesay artialitypay orfay Ederickfray
ethay Eatgray anday accomplisheday atwhay Eterpay adhay ongedlay orfay utbay adhay evernay
attained:ay ehay awsay ethay Ussianpray idolay inay ethay eshflay. Enwhay Aulpay anday ishay
ifeway ademay ethay andgray ourtay ofay Europeay inay 1781,ay eythay isitedvay Ederickfray
inay Erlinbay. Itay asway aay emorablemay eetingmay orfay everalsay easonsray. Ederickfray
ethay Eatgray orfay ethay irstfay imetay inay anymay yearsay adhay aay ewnay uitsay ade--newmay
oughoutthray. Itay asway aay eatgray oncessioncay omfray ethay Otsdampay ecluseray anday
iser,may anay eloquentay estimonialtay ofay espectray orfay ethay aintedpay adylay ofay
Etersburgpay owhay as,way incidentally,ay otnay osay iendlyfray owardtay Ussiapray asay eshay
onceay adhay eenbay. Ethay Ing’skay ewnay othesclay ereway ethay alktay ofay Erlinbay.

Asay aay opictay ofay onversation,cay eythay ereway onlyay upersededsay ybay ethay Amlethay
orystay. Aay ecialspay oductionpray ofay Amlethay adhay eenbay announceday inay ethay Andgray
Uke’sday onorhay utbay ethay irectorday ofay ethay eatrethay ithdrewway ethay iecepay atay ethay
astlay omentmay asay inappropriateay orfay ethay occasion.ay Ethay ublicpay asway agogay
ithway uriositycay anday ethay ensitivesay elf-pityingsay Aulpay ecamebay ethay ocusfay
ofay anay over-wroughtay anday over-acteday omanceray ofay ublicpay ympathysay. Orfay
everalsay aysday Aul’spay icturepay ofay ishay ownay agedytray unghay eforebay ethay Ermangay
ublic;pay Erlinbay awsay imhay asay aay Ussianray Amlethay osewhay atherfay adhay eenbay aay
artyrmay artlypay orfay ishay ovelay ofay Ussiapray. Allay isthay asway extremelyay adbay orfay
ethay elancholymay Andgray Uke,day orfay omwhay anyay icturesquepay enhancementay ofay ishay
isfortunesmay addeday anay elementay ofay angerday otay atthay alreadyay inherentay inay
ishay abitualhay oodingbray. Ethay omparisoncay ithway Amlethay asway atefulgray otay imhay
orfay everyay eason,ray utbay ostmay ofay allay orfay ethay easonray atthay Amlethay asway ishay
ather’sfay ownay onsay. Ifay ethay ublicpay identifieday Aulpay ithway Amlet,hay itay eantmay
atthay eythay accepteday imhay asay ethay onsay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay. Isthay aspectay ofay
ethay amadray epresentedray omethingsay atthay Aulpay asway obligeday otay elievebay. Otay
oubtday itay eantmay orfay imhay unendurableay uffering,say otay ebay escapeday atay everyay
ostcay.

Asay aay abybay inay ethay adle,cray Aulpay asway aay ensitivesay eature,cray artingstay anday
emblingtray atay everyay oundsay. Ehay asway evotedlyday ursednay ybay ethay Empressay
Elisabethay anday oppresseday ybay erhay ysteriahay. Afteray erhay eathday ehay asway
ependentday onay Anin,pay aay anmay owhay eameddray eamsdray anday ademay onay effortay otay
ealizeray emthay. Anin’spay utelagetay asway otnay aay oursecay inay ouragecay anday Aul’spay
ituationsay especiallyay equiredray it.ay Ehay asway onstantlycay inay earfay ofay eingbay
oisoned,pay inay earfay ofay eingbay oundfay outay orfay aay astard,bay inay earfay ofay osinglay
ishay aimclay otay ethay onethray ofay ethay Omanovsray. Ishay elationsray ithway ishay
othermay ereway alwaysay unsympatheticay anday afteray ishay econdsay arriagemay eythay
ecamebay unfriendly.ay Aulpay adhay onay interestay inay oliticspay anday ascribeday ishay
indifferenceay otay ethay elfishnesssay ofay ethay Empressay owhay ealouslyjay excludeday
imhay omfray anyay articipationpay inay affairsay ofay atestay. Utbay ehay asway arfay ootay yshay
anday impracticalay ybay emperamenttay otay engageay inay oliticspay inay anyay orm;fay otay
organize,ay otay ompromise,cay otay adjustay eansmay otay endsay ereway otnay ithinway ishay
apacitycay.

Ehay as,way onay ethay otheray and,hay ofoundlypray attracteday ybay ethay ysticalmay
ovementsmay ofay ishay age.ay Ybay isthay ethodmay ehay ecamebay onnectedcay ithway ethay
otestantpray eligionsray ofay Europe,ay anay allianceay ichwhay asway otnay onsistentcay
ithway ishay uturefay ositionpay asay eadhay ofay ethay Eekgray Urchchay. Itay illway ebay
ememberedray atthay Eterpay ethay Irdthay ouldcay evernay ollywhay abandonay ethay eligionray
ofay ishay ativenay Olsteinhay anday emainedray otay ethay enday ostilehay otay Ussianray
orthodoxy.ay Aulpay evelopedday ethay amesay endencytay otay allyay imselfhay ithway
angestray anday ebelliousray aithsfay. Ehay ecamebay aay Eemason,fray aay Artinist,may
anday aay Ightknay ofay Altamay. Ethay Eighteenthay Enturycay asway olificpray inay ysticmay
ultscay atay ethay amesay imetay atthay itay ooktay itsay aceplay inay istoryhay asay ethay ageay
ofay enlightenment.ay Asay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray asway identifieday ithway allay ethay
ovementsmay orfay enlightenment,ay erhay onsay asway identifieday ithway allay ethay ormsfay
ofay obscurantismay ichwhay ourishedflay idesay ybay idesay ithway ethay ewnay ationalismray.
Atherinecay asway ispleasedday ithway Aul’spay allianceay ithway ackblay agicmay anday
idedpray erselfhay onay eingbay eefray omfray anyay eaningslay owardtay uperstitionsay.
Enwhay eshay asway aay eryvay olday oman,way erhay atentlay edulitycray urstbay out;ay utbay
erhay apselay atay ethay eleventhay ourhay eednay otnay epriveday erhay ofay erhay ositionpay
asay oneay ofay ethay iningshay eaderslay ofay ethay ageay ofay easonray. Aulpay alwaysay
elongedbay inay ethay otheray amp,cay ethay ampcay ofay ethay edulous,cray ybay irtuevay ofay ishay
emperamenttay. Ehay ightmay avehay oundfay aay indkay ofay eacepay erethay ifay estinyday adhay
otnay alledcay imhay otay ayplay anay activeay artpay inay ifelay.

Afteray ehay ecamebay Arczay ishay orbidmay ideasay axedway anday edlay imhay intoay anymay
otesquegray anday extremeay acts.ay Ikelay Amlet,hay ehay oughtthay ishay irstfay utyday
asway otay avengeay ishay atherfay. Althoughay Eterpay adhay eenbay eadday orfay oremay anthay
irtythay years,ay ehay adhay ethay avegray opened,ay ethay orpsecay exposeday otay ublicpay
iew,vay anday anay impressiveay uneralfay acteday out.ay Ethay Arczay adhay eenbay uriedbay inay
ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onastery,may ilewhay allay ethay otheray Arsczay ofay Ussiaray
afteray Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay uriedbay inay ethay Ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay
anday Aintsay Aulpay. Anay elaborateay uneralfay ocessionpray ansportedtray ethay eadday
Eterpay omfray ishay olday otay ishay ewnay esting-placeray. Asay ethay arcophagussay asway
ornebay alongay ethay Evskynay Ospect,pray Alexeiay Orlovay ollowedfay immediatelyay
afteray asay iefchay ournermay. Isthay asway ethay owncray ofay Aul’spay evenge,ray otay exposeay
ethay urderermay otay ethay ondemnationcay ofay ethay orldway.

Egorygray Orlovay asway eadday utbay ortunatelyfay orfay Aul’spay admay amadray ishay otherbray
emainedray otay ayplay ethay inistersay erôlay ichwhay Aulpay adhay inventeday orfay imhay.
Atwhay ethay ageday Orlovay oughtthay ofay asay ehay udgedtray alongay ehindbay ethay orpsecay
ofay ethay anmay ehay adhay uckstray ownday irty-fourthay yearsay agoay isay attermay orfay
eculationspay. Omfray atwhay eway owknay ofay Alexei’say aracter,chay ehay asway obablypray
otnay occupieday ithway emorsefulray oughtsthay. Erhapspay ehay asway inkingthay ofay ethay
ongstray ish-soupfay ithway ichwhay ehay asway oinggay otay eviveray ishay eakway olday egslay
enwhay ethay Ar’sczay inefay uneralfay asway over.ay Erhapspay ehay asway inkingthay atthay
Aulpay asway asay admay asay Eterpay adhay een,bay anday onderingway atay ethay oincidencecay.

Ethay esemblanceray etweenbay ethay atefay ofay Atherine’scay usbandhay anday erhay onsay asway
arriedcay outay otay ethay end.ay Asay Emperor,ay Aul’spay orbidmay uspicionssay increaseday
anday ishay eprisalsray againstay osethay omwhay ehay uspectedsay arouseday earfay anday
atredhay onay everyay andhay. Ishay eaddray ofay ersecutionpay alledcay orthfay actualay
ersecutionpay erewhay onenay adhay ormerlyfay existed.ay Oonsay aay onspiracycay eganbay
otay aketay apeshay amongay ishay enemies,ay eadedhay ybay ethay Ubovzay others,bray Atoplay
anday Alerianvay. Ethay astlay apterchay ofay Eter’spay istoryhay asway epeatedray. Afteray
aay iefbray eignray ofay onlyay ourfay years,ay Aulpay asway urderedmay oneay ightnay ybay aay
andbay ofay onspiratorscay owhay aidsay atthay ehay asway aay angerousday unaticlay anday adhay
otay ebay utpay outay ofay ethay ayway. Erethay isay everyay easonray otay upposesay atthay ishay
onsay anday uccessor,say Alexanderay ethay Irst,fay asway awareay ofay ethay onspiracycay
againstay ishay ather’sfay ife,lay anday oremay efinitelyday awareay anthay Atherinecay
adhay eenbay enwhay Eterpay adhay eenbay assassinateday atay Opsharay. Oneay ofay ethay ingsthay
ichwhay Alexanderay adhay earnedlay omfray ishay extraordinaryay andmothergray asway otay
overlookay aay urdermay ichwhay ouldcay otnay ebay eventedpray anday akemay ethay estbay ofay ethay
onsequencescay. Inay othbay asescay ethay onsequencescay entitleday emthay otay ascenday
ethay onethray overay ethay eadday odybay ofay eirthay edecessorspray.


5ay

Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ovedlay otay itewray. Eshay oseray atay ixsay o’clockay everyay
orningmay anday occupieday erselfhay ithway iterarylay orkway uringday ethay eethray
ourshay oray osay ichwhay interveneday eforebay erhay Ussianray ervantssay eganbay otay
ubray eirthay eepyslay eyes.ay Eshay adhay Artanspay ethodsmay ofay awakeningay erselfhay.
Irstfay eshay ashedway erhay acefay anday earsay ithway ice;ay enthay eshay ankdray ivefay upscay
ofay ethay ongeststray offeecay everay ewedbray. Eshay atsay ownday esidebay erhay andlecay
ithway erhay enpay anday otewray inay aay argelay eefray owingflay and,hay instructions,ay
orrespondence,cay emoirs,may ables,fay istories,hay omediescay. Erhay outputay asway
oluminousvay. Eshay idday otnay aitway otay inishfay oneay iecepay eforebay eshay eganbay
another,ay anday ethay irstfay emainedray oreverfay unfinished.ay Everythingay eshay
otewray isay aay agmentfray. Eshay otewray erhay emoirsmay inay ethay 70’s,ay anday enthay
otewray emthay allay overay againay inay ethay 90’say. Eshay etsay ownday aay agmentfray
ofay autobiographyay orfay Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiams,way anotheray orfay
Oniatovsky,pay anday anotheray orfay Otiomkinpay. Eshay asway otnay eticulousmay asay otay
ethay indkay ofay aperpay anday uchsay ings,thay asay aymay ebay eensay omfray erhay otesnay inay
ethay Ussianray archivesay ichwhay areay ibbledscray iterallylay onay apsscray ofay aper,pay
anythingay ichwhay amecay otay andhay. Erhay indmay ookshay itselfay outay ooselylay inay ethay
acktray ofay aay iftlysway ovingmay enpay.

Ateverwhay eshay otewray asway oselyclay elatedray otay ethay affairsay ofay ethay ayday. Itay
asway addresseday otay omesay articularpay ersonpay oray asedbay onay omesay oncretecay
experience.ay Ethay evolutionay ofay erhay iterarylay expressionay ancay ebay oughlyray
acedtray ikelay is:thay uringday erhay irties,thay eshay otewray onay oliticalpay ubjectssay
anday attersmay ofay ate;stay uringday erhay orties,fay eshay otewray erhay emoirsmay anday
orrespondedcay ithway Oltairevay anday Imm;gray uringday erhay ifties,fay eshay otewray
allegories,ay onicles,chray anday omedies;cay anday inay erhay ixties,say eshay urnedtay otay
eminiscencesray again,ay oducingpray ethay ersionvay ofay erhay ifelay ichwhay eshay antedway
osteritypay otay eadray. Eshay ewgray esslay anday esslay abstractay asay ethay yearsay entway ybay.

Afteray ethay irthbay ofay erhay otway andsons,gray ethay Empressay adhay anay outburstay ofay
imaginativeay itingwray. Orfay everalsay yearsay eshay addresseday allay erhay itingswray
otay ethay ittlelay Andgray Ukesday. E“Thay Egendlay ofay ethay Arevichczay Or”chlay asway
ittenwray orfay Alexanderay enwhay ehay asway ivefay yearsay old.ay Erhay Ussianray istory,hay
ichwhay illsfay otway olumes,vay icturespay aay imitivepray ageay ithway appropriateay
implicitysay. Eshay oralizesmay arcelyscay atay all,ay orfay ethay iveslay ofay ethay Aziaknay
Elikivay oday otnay ointpay ethay ightray indkay ofay oralmay.

Atherine’scay ittlelay istorieshay areay aay arrativenay ofay onstantcay arsway etweenbay
ethay Ussiansray anday ethay Eeks;gray iftsway anday ividvay etchesskay ofay omadicnay
incespray anday argelay amiliesfay ofay othersbray arringway againstay eachay otheray orfay
aay eritagehay. Ethay orystay ofay Incesspray Olgaay owhay entway otay Onstantinoplecay anday
asway erethay aptizedbay isay oldtay enthusiasticallyay anday atay engthlay. Olgaay iedtray
otay onvertcay erhay onsay utbay ehay ouldway otnay ebay onvertedcay ecausebay ehay aidsay ethay
otheray enmay ouldway otnay ikelay it.ay Eshay adhay otay aitway untilay erhay andson,gray omwhay
eshay eared,ray ewgray otay anhoodmay eforebay eshay ouldcay akemay erhay influenceay eltfay.
Itay asway erhay andsongray owhay Istianizedchray Ussiaray.

Isthay egendlay asway eryvay opularpay ithway Atherinecay anday erhay andsongray Alexander.ay
Ithway erhay obes,glay ethay Empressay owedshay ethay ittlelay oybay owhay ethay ordeshay ofay
ethay Enghisgay Ankhay adhay assedpay acrossay ethay andslay ofay Ussiaray anday erewhay ethay
Ythiansscay adhay etmay ethay Eeksgray. Esethay essonslay ademay erhay intimacyay ithway
ittlelay Alexanderay ethay appiesthay ofay erhay ifelay. Eshay ollectedcay erhay itingswray
intoay aay o-calledsay Ibrarylay orfay ethay Andgray Ukesday. Otay ebay ure,say ethay ojectedpray
Ibrarylay asway evernay ompleted;cay ornay asway ethay istoryhay ofay Ussiaray oughtbray
ownday eyondbay ethay irteenththay enturycay. Osay arfay asay erhay Ussianray istoryhay asway
oncerned,cay itay asway aay itypay atthay ethay authoray eftlay onlyay aay agmentfray. Eshay adhay
aay iftgay orfay ivelylay ompactcay arrativenay anday ethay eaderray eelsfay aay istinctday
isappointmentday enwhay ethay orystay eaksbray offay uddenlysay eforebay ethay arrivalay ofay
ethay Artarstay.

Erhay aithfulnessfay otay istoryhay isay easyay otay explain.ay Ethay artistay adhay oundfay
aay ewnay ovelay. Eshay adhay uddenlysay iscoveredday omedycay. Ethay Empressay adhay akentay
otay itingwray aysplay inay ethay annermay ofay Olièremay. Anay anecdoteay oftenay oldtay otay
owshay ethay affectionay existingay etweenbay Alexanderay anday ishay andmothergray ellstay
owhay ethay oy,bay atay ethay ageay ofay eight,ay avegay aay erformancepay ofay aay ive-actfay
omedycay omposedcay ybay Atherinecay. Inay ethay eeperday ayerslay ofay erhay emorymay ethay
orksway ofay Olièremay adhay eenbay yinglay onglay unnoticed.ay Uddenlysay ethay atentlay
emoriesmay osay onglay eddedbay erethay inay orgetfulnessfay anday ilencesay eganbay otay
erminategay. Atay aboutay ethay amesay ageay ichwhay Onsieurmay Alexanderay adhay ownay
owngray otay e,bay Atherinecay adhay onceay edfay uponay ethay aysplay ofay Olièremay ecausebay
erhay overness,gay Abetbay Ardel,cay adhay ownknay emthay allay ybay earthay. Asay eshay atsay
eachingtay erhay eight-year-olday andson,gray ethay astestay anday interestsay ofay
atthay ageay inay erhay ownay ifelay eganbay otay irstay anday assertay emselvesthay ithinway
erhay. Atherinecay asway otnay ontentcay asay Abetbay adhay eenbay otay ivegay erhay upilpay
eady-maderay omediescay oweverhay asterlymay. Eshay eferredpray otay omposecay omediescay
erselfhay orfay Alexander.ay Omptlypray eshay ellfay otay orkway anday iftlysway ereway erhay
aysplay ompletedcay. Isthay imetay erethay ereway onay agments;fray ethay evitybray ofay ethay
oductpray asway exactlyay uitedsay otay erhay emperamenttay. Eshay otewray evensay iecespay
inay oneay year,ay anday enthay abandoneday ethay ieldfay altogether,ay erhapspay ecausebay
ethay Urkishtay Arsway ecamebay ootay engrossing.ay

Erhay omediescay allay ealday ithway oneay ubjectsay inay ethay amesay annermay. Eythay areay
atiressay onay ethay entimentalsay anday uperstitioussay aitstray ofay umanhay aturenay.
Erhay itlestay owshay owhay aithfullyfay eshay adhereday otay erhay emethay. Ethay Arlatan,chay
Ethay Upe,day Ethay Iberiansay Aman,shay Amilyfay Iscordday Oughthray Alsefay Uspicions,say
Onay Oodgay Ithoutway Evilay ereway ethay ostmay opularpay. Eirthay otsplay anday aracterschay
owshay atthay ethay authoray isay omethingsay ofay aay ychologistpsay anday aay oodgay ealday ofay
aay atiristsay. Itay isay oticeablenay atthay ethay eaknessesway ichwhay eshay especiallyay
atirizessay areay aracteristicchay ofay ethay ehaviorbay ofay erhay onsay Aulpay.

Atay ethay imetay enwhay Atherinecay otewray erhay omediescay erethay asway onay ongerlay anyay
etensepray ofay ympathysay etweenbay ethay othermay anday onsay. Ethay isintegrationday ofay
Aul’spay aracterchay adhay ogressedpray osay arfay atthay ehay adhay ithdrawnway imselfhay
omfray allay ethay orldway exceptay osethay omwhay ishay othermay alledcay arlatanschay anday
amansshay. Ethay Empressay identifieday erhay onsay ithway allay uperstitioussay olkfay
anday astigatedcay ethay olewhay ibetray inay erhay omediescay. Eshay arelyray entionedmay
Aulpay irectlyday inay erhay emoirsmay anday erhay orrespondencecay. Inay ethay intimateay
amilyfay istoryhay ichwhay illsfay erhay etterslay otay Imm,gray ishay amenay evernay
occurs.ay Erhay atredhay oundfay anay outletay inay erhay atiricalsay omediescay. Erehay
eshay indirectlyay exposeday ishay otoriousnay eaknessesway anday eldhay emthay upay otay
idiculeray. Eshay espisedday ishay aracterchay asay eshay espisedday ishay ookslay. Aulpay
esembledray ethay Almuckcay ypetay inay ysiquephay anday ountenancecay. Ortshay ofay
aturestay anday ub-nosedsnay asay ehay as,way ishay othermay ouldcay otnay ooklay atay imhay
ithoutway eingbay emindedray ofay ethay Altikovsay idesay ofay ishay eredityhay. Anyoneay owhay
eadsray oughthray erhay iterarylay orksway illway ebay uckstray ybay ethay umbernay ofay imestay
ethay Empressay efersray otay ethay astlyghay uglinessay ofay ethay Almuckcay ypetay. Eshay
ouldcay otnay etgay awayay omfray it.ay

Ethay omediescay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ereway egardedray asay aay eatgray
ontributioncay otay ethay ampaigncay againstay obscurantism.ay Eshay eppedstay
orthfay asay ethay Aintsay Eorgegay ofay enlightenmentay ikingstray ownday ethay agondray
ofay uperstitionsay. Erhay atiresay asway eveledlay againstay ethay Artinists,may
ethay Eemasons,fray anday ethay Alchemists;ay eshay atteredbay atay allay oupsgray anday
organizationsay atthay adhay aay ecretsay understandingay anday alkedtay ysteriouslymay
aboutay ethay oblemspray ofay ifelay anday eathday. Ortunatelyfay orfay erhay interest,ay
ichwhay adhay onay eatgray olerancetay orfay abstractions,ay aay esh-and-bloodflay
antagonistay asway aisedray upay otay imulatestay anday increaseay erhay energies.ay Ethay
amousfay Agliostrocay ecidedday otay akemay aay isitvay otay Etersburg,pay elievingbay atthay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ouldway avorfay ishay ultcay. Utbay ehay adhay eckonedray ithoutway
ishay Empress.ay Atherinecay asway evernay iredtay ofay abusingay im,hay othbay uringday
anday afteray ishay ojournsay inay Ussiaray. Enwhay ehay asway imprisoneday inay Ancefray inay
onnectioncay ithway ethay affairay ofay ethay iamondday ecklace,nay eshay exulteday inay
ethay ostmay unbecomingay annermay. Omesay ofay erhay ongeststray anday eastlay ady-likelay
anguagelay asway ouredpay outay onay ethay eadhay ofay ethay alentedtay agician,may om,whay ybay
ethay ay,way eshay adhay evernay evenay eensay. Otay Imm,gray eshay ote,wray I“ay avehay eadray
ethay emoirmay ofay Agliostrocay ichwhay youay avehay entsay emay anday ifay Iay adhay otnay eenbay
alreadyay ersuadedpay atthay ehay asway aay Enchfray arlatan,chay ishay emoirmay ouldway avehay
onvincedcay emay. Ehay isay aay ogueray anday ackguardblay anday ehay oughtay otay ebay anged.”hay

Eshay asway osay eatlygray interesteday inay isthay anmay atthay itay ustmay avehay ostcay erhay
aay eatgray effortay otay enyday imhay anay audienceay uringday ishay aystay inay Ussiaray. “May.
Agliostro,”cay eshay ote,wray Arrived“ay erehay atay aay eryvay avorablefay omentmay orfay
im,hay atay aay imetay enwhay anymay odgeslay ofay Eemasons,fray infatuateday ithway ethay
inciplespray ofay Edenborg,sway esiredday ithway allay eirthay owerpay otay eesay iritsspay.
Eythay ereforethay anray otay Agliostrocay owhay aidsay atthay ehay asway inay ossessionpay ofay
allay ethay ecretssay ofay Octorday Alk,fay intimateay iendfray ofay Ukeday Ichelieu,ray owhay
adhay onceay acrificedsay otay imhay inay ethay eryvay idstmay ofay Iennavay aay ackblay oat...gay.
may. Agliostrocay enthay oducedpray ishay arvellousmay ecretssay ofay ealinghay. Ehay
etendedpray otay awdray uick-silverqay omfray aay outygay ootfay anday asway aughtcay inay ethay
actay ofay ouringpay aay easpoonfultay ofay ercurymay intoay ethay aterway intoay ichwhay ehay
asway oinggay otay utpay ethay outygay ember...may.

Ater“Lay on,ay ackedray ybay ebts,day ehay ooktay efugeray inay ethay ellarcay ofay Onsieurmay
Yelaginay ..ay. erewhay ehay ankdray allay ethay ine,way ampagne,chay anday Englishay eerbay
atthay ehay ouldcay et...gay. Onsieurmay Yelagin,ay annoyeday ybay ishay otherbray atray inay
ethay ellarcay anday ybay ethay oughtthay ofay allay ethay ine,way anday eerbay ..ay. avegay imhay anay
olday Invalide__ay otay accompanyay imhay asay arfay asay Ilanmay. Isthay isay ethay istoryhay
ofay Agliostrocay inay ichwhay erethay isay othingnay exceptionallyay arvellousmay. Iay
avehay evernay eensay imhay earnay oray ar,--norfay avehay Iay adhay anyay emptationtay otay oday
o,say orfay Iay oday otnay ovelay arlatanschay. Iay assureay youay atthay Ogersonray inksthay ofay
Agliostrocay asay uchmay oray esslay anthay Oah’snay Ark.ay Incepray Orlov,ay ontrarycay otay
ishay ustom,cay ashay otnay ademay uchmay ofay Agliostrocay. Ehay akesmay unfay ofay imhay asay ofay
osethay owhay omfray eremay uriositycay unray otay eesay im,hay anday ehay ashay ontributedcay
utbay ittlelay otay angechay intoay ineway ethay aterway ofay ethay amelessshay artisanspay ofay
isthay oorpay evilday. Utbay incesay ethay oremay upidstay anday ignorantay ethay arlatanschay
areay ethay oremay impressionay eythay eatecray inay ethay eatgray ities,cay itay isay otay ebay
upposedsay atthay Agliostrocay illway ebay inay ishay elementay inay Aris....”pay

Omfray ethay ehemencevay ofay ethay Empress’say ondemnation,cay oneay uspectssay atthay eshay
idday otnay atestay aay actfay enwhay eshay eclaredday atthay eshay adhay onay emptationtay otay
eesay imhay. Anday eshay asway arfay omfray avinghay inishedfay ithway ethay ubjectsay. Otway ofay
erhay omedies,cay Ethay Iarlay anday Ethay Upe,day ereway asedbay onay Agliostro’scay isit,vay
anday Ethay Iberiansay Amanshay asway inspired,ay oughthay otnay avowedly,ay ybay ethay amesay
emethay. Everalsay ofay erhay aysplay ereway aay eatgray uccesssay enwhay oducedpray inay
Etersburg,pay anday Ethay Iarlay anday Ethay Upeday ooktay inay oremay anthay entytway ousandthay
oublesray. Ethay ublicpay asway itivatedtay ybay ethay Empress’say atiresay anday intrigueday
ybay ethay imelinesstay ofay erhay iterarylay attackay onay ethay ostmay otoriousnay
aracterchay inay Europe.ay

Onay oneay askeday ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay anday ishay onsort,cay ethay Artenlaubegay adylay
ofay Avlovsk,pay atwhay eythay oughtthay ofay ethay Empress’say amaticdray efforts.ay Onay
oneay askeday Aulpay anday Ariemay aboutay anything.ay Ethay Empressay overlookeday emthay
ompletelycay. Eneverwhay eshay eferredray otay erhay uccessor,say ethay eferenceray asway
otay erhay andsongray. Onsieur“May Alexanderay illway inishfay isthay anday at,”thay eshay
ouldway itewray. Ot“Nay inay ymay ime,tay utbay inay atthay ofay Onsieurmay Alexander.”ay Eshay
iedtray otay orgetfay ethay existenceay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.
