IIxay

EsHay OWSgRay OLDay


Upay otay ethay eathday ofay Otiomkin,pay ethay Empressay adhay eenbay associateday ithway olday
iends,fray owhay adhay aredshay ithway erhay ethay experiencesay ofay 1762ay. Orlovay anday
Otiomkinpay adhay othbay oodstay overay ethay armway odybay ofay Eter,pay abbedstay otay eathday
ybay Alexeiay anday Ariatinskybay. Althoughay eithernay ofay emthay adhay iftedlay aay andhay
againstay ethay Ar,czay eythay aredshay ithway erhay ethay emorymay ofay aay imecray ichwhay adhay
otay ebay ademay oodgay. Isthay asway otnay uchsay aay adbay ing,thay aidsay Oltaire,vay incesay
itay ademay ethay Empressay oneay ofay ethay estbay onarchsmay ofay ethay enturycay. Otay edeemray
erselfhay inay ethay eyesay ofay Europe,ay eshay asway obligeday otay accomplishay iraclesmay.
Inay aay esserlay egreeday ethay amesay obligationay estedray onay Orlovay anday Otiomkinpay.
Althoughay eythay ereway othbay elfishsay anday extravagant,ay eythay ereway oodgay
atriotspay anday idday eirthay utmostay orfay ethay oryglay ofay Ussiaray. Aay ysteriousmay
orcefay ustainedsay Egorygray Orlov,ay aay eryvay ordinaryay an,may oughthray aay eryvay
emarkableray areercay. Otiomkin,pay aay anmay ofay eatergray abilityay anthay Orlov,ay
asway orrespondinglycay oremay effectiveay anday oremay istinguishedday. Ethay oodymay
Ukrainianay ustmay avehay eenbay urprisedsay otay indfay imselfhay egardedray asay aay eatgray
Eneralgay anday aay eatgray atesmanstay anday otay ealizeray atthay atay imestay ehay actuallyay
asway allay atthay ehay asway upposedsay otay ebay.

Orfay earlynay irtythay years,ay ethay Empressay adhay adhay ethay ompanionshipcay ofay esethay
otway enmay. Afteray ethay eathday ofay Otiomkin,pay eshay asway orfay ethay irstfay imetay
alone.ay Allay atay onceay eshay ecamebay uncertain,ay inadequate,ay unsuccessful,ay
anday ethay ingloriousay yearsay ofay erhay eignray eganbay. Erhay aimclay otay ethay
itletay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ouldway avehay eenbay ongerstray adhay eshay iedday
ithway Otiomkinpay. Ethay astlay ecadeday ofay erhay ifelay iminishedday atthay aimclay
onsiderably,cay ichwhay ashay oftenay eenbay onstruedcay asay owingshay ethay engthstray ofay
Otiomkin’spay influenceay anday ethay importanceay ofay ishay ideas.ay Utbay Otiomkinpay
asway erelymay ethay affstay onay ichwhay eshay eanedlay anday ichwhay eshay adhay okenbray
ithoutway oreseeingfay ethay onsequencescay otay erselfhay.

Youngay Atoplay Ubovzay adhay onay ealizationray ofay ethay imecray atay Opsharay. Ishay
onsciencecay asway irginvay anday ishay youthay ademay imhay irresponsibleay anday elfishsay.
Ehay asway aay anmay ithoutway aay ast,pay ehay adhay othingnay otay akemay oodgay. Ortunefay adhay
uddenlysay ainedray easuretray uponay imhay outay ofay aay earclay yskay anday ehay accepteday
erhay ountybay ikelay aay ildchay owhay orgetsfay otay aysay Ank“thay you.”ay Ehay asway
arrogant,ay arbitrary,ay anday asping,gray anday ehay ecamebay uthlessray afteray ishay
iumphtray overay ethay edoubtableray Otiomkinpay. Ethay eathday ofay ishay ivalray eftlay imhay
invincibleay anday ehay ewknay it.ay

Ubovzay asway otnay implysay youthful;ay ehay asway youth.ay Ethay otway others,bray Atoplay
anday Alerian,vay ereway ustjay emergingay omfray ethay adolescentay eriodpay ichwhay ethay
Empress’say andsons,gray Alexanderay anday Onstantine,cay ereway ustjay entering.ay
Ethay ifferenceday inay ageay anday aturitymay etweenbay ethay otway airspay ofay othersbray
asway otnay eatgray. Ethay Empressay asway inay ovelay ithway Alexanderay utbay eshay adopteday
Atoplay Ubovzay insteaday anday eganbay astingcay aboutay orfay aay ifeway orfay Alexanderay
owhay adhay eachedray ethay ageay atay ichwhay eshay adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay ebay arriedmay.
Onsieur“May Alexander,”ay eshay adhay okenspay ofay omfray infancyay asay ifay ehay ereway aay
anmay anday Ubovzay eshay ownay eferredray otay alwaysay asay E“thay ild.”chay Atay ethay ageay ofay
ixty,say ethay Empressay adhay onay eyesay orfay anythingay utbay youth.ay Erhay overslay adhay
eenbay owinggray youngeray anday youngeray untilay allay ethay orldway expecteday erhay otay
enday erhay ifelay inay ethay armsay ofay aay oybay. Osay onsistentlycay adhay eshay oweredlay ethay
ageay ofay onsent,cay isthay eemedsay ethay onlyay ogicallay outcome.ay

Itay asway assumeday ybay osethay aboutay ethay ourtcay atthay onlyay iplingsstray eednay
applyay orfay ethay ostpay ofay avoritefay. Erethay asway aay omentmay enwhay itay eemedsay asay
ifay ethay eventeen-year-oldsay onsay ofay Incesspray Ashkovday ightmay eriouslysay
ompetecay. Ishay other,may owhay adhay iddenray esidebay ethay Empressay asay aay istersay
Amazonay onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay Eterhofpay ampaign,cay ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay
atthay ethay youngay Incepray adhay eenbay adviseday ybay Egorygray Orlovay otay ecomebay aay
uitorsay. Ethay Incesspray asway ockedshay enwhay eshay eardhay erhay onsay usthay emptedtay ybay
Atherine’scay ex-favorite.ay As“ay oonsay asay ehay asway one,”--shegay actfullytay entsay
youngay Ashkovday onay anay impromptuay errand,--“Iay expresseday ymay astonishmentay otay
Incepray Orlovay atthay ehay ouldcay eakspay inay uchsay aay annermay otay aay youngay anmay otnay
eventeensay yearsay ofay age,ay anday ompromisecay ethay onorhay anday ignityday ofay erhay
Ajestymay inay uchsay aay annermay. Asay otay avorites,fay Iay adebay imhay ecollectray atthay Iay
eithernay ewknay ornay acknowledgeday uchsay ersons,pay anday atthay isthay asway aay ubjectsay
ichwhay Iay ouldway otnay uffersay otay ebay enewedray inay ymay esence,pray uchmay esslay inay ethay
esencepray ofay ymay on,say omwhay Iay adhay oughtbray upay ithway entimentssay ofay ethay utmostay
enerationvay orfay ethay Empressay asay ishay overeignsay anday odmother,gay ever,nay asay Iay
usted,tray otay owknay anyay other.”ay

Ethay Incesspray everthelessnay etsay offay atay onceay orfay Etersburg,pay erewhay eshay
oonsay asway uresay otay ebay angerouslyday exposeday otay ethay armschay ofay ethay ageday irensay
onay ethay Ussianray onethray. Asay oonsay asay ethay Ashkovsday arrived,ay ethay other’smay
earsfay increased.ay E“Thay absurday umorsray atthay ymay onsay ouldway ebay ethay avoritefay
eganbay otay ebay enewed.”ray Oneay ayday ethay ephewnay ofay Incepray Otiomkinpay alledcay
atay erhay ousehay anday askeday otay eakspay ithway ethay youngay Ince,pray owhay asway out.ay
All“ay atthay youay areay oingday emay ethay onorhay otay ay,”say ethay Incesspray urstbay orthfay
ehemently,vay althoughay ethay essengermay adhay aidsay onay oremay anthay atthay Incepray
Otiomkinpay ishedway otay eesay erhay on,say Ould“cay evernay ebay eantmay orfay ymay ears.ay
Erhapspay itay ightmay ebay youray ommissioncay otay eakspay ithway Incepray Ashkovday. Asay
orfay yself,may ilstwhay Iay ovelay ethay Empressay anday areday otnay opposeay erhay ill,way Iay
avehay ootay uchmay elf-respectsay anday elf-esteemsay otay aketay artpay inay anyay affairay
ofay uchsay aay aturenay. Anday ifay atwhay youay areay easedplay otay intimateay ouldshay everay
occur,ay ethay onlyay useay Iay allshay akemay ofay ymay on’ssay influenceay illway ebay otay
obtainay eavelay ofay absenceay orfay omesay yearsay anday aay assportpay otay isitvay oreignfay
ountries.”cay

Erethay isay onay evidenceay exceptay ishay other’smay emoirsmay atthay ethay Empressay everay
eallyray onsideredcay youngay Ashkovday. Oonsay afteray ishay arrivalay inay Etersburg,pay
ehay asway ordereday awayay otay ishay egiment,ray aay atefay ichwhay evernay overtookay
youngay enmay omwhay ethay Empressay ishedway otay eesay aboutay erhay. Ethay opeshay ofay ishay
othermay ollapsedcay. Ethay Incepray entway awayay underay aay oudclay ofay ailure,fay
ikelay aay udentstay owhay adhay iedtray orfay ollegecay entranceay anday ailedfay inay ishay
examinations.ay Ithinway aay ewfay eeksway ehay etmay aay easantpay irlgay anday arriedmay erhay
uringday aay ausepay ofay ishay egimentray. Ethay estray ofay ishay orystay elatesray owhay ishay
othermay evernay ecognizedray ishay ife,way owhay ehay ivedlay apartay omfray er,hay anday owhay
ehay iedday early.ay Ehay adhay evernay eenbay aay appyhay incepray.

Youngay Ashkov’sday agedytray owsthray aay ightlay onay ethay Empress’say assionpay orfay
youngay enmay. Erethay ereway othersmay inay Ussiaray owhay ereway illingway otay offeray upay
eirthay onssay anday ofitpray ybay anay unsuitableay ove-relationshiplay ichwhay ouldcay
ebay ossedglay overay asay omanticray. Erethay ereway olderay enmay ikelay Orlovay owhay ereway
eadyray otay adviseay aay inefay youngay oldiersay otay ytray ishay ortunesfay ithway ethay
Empress.ay Allay ofay esethay ounsellorscay expecteday otay eceiveray inay omesay orm,fay
etherwhay inay assportspay anday undsfay orfay oreignfay aveltray oray otherwise,ay agesway
orfay eirthay ervicessay. Orfay ethay uckylay youngay anmay itay eantmay iches,ray onors,hay
itles,tay onsiderationcay. Ethay Empress’say enerositygay asway otorious--andnay eshay
ouldcay otnay ossiblypay ivelay onglay. Utbay aay onglay anday incelypray uturefay awaiteday
ethay youthfulay overlay owhay urvivedsay erhay.

Atoplay Ubovzay asway aay oicechay afteray erhay ownay earthay. Ethay Ild”“chay asway otnay
asay alltay asay ehay ightmay avehay eenbay utbay ehay asway arkday ikelay erhay irstfay over,lay
Altikov,say owhay adhay ookedlay Ike“lay aay yflay inay ethay ilk-pan”may anday owhay adhay ooedway
erhay atay irstfay osay ardently.ay Atoplay asway otnay iffidentday. Ehay adhay akentay ainspay
otay utpay imselfhay inay ethay Empress’say ayway. Ishay uncle,ay oneay ofay Atherine’scay
ield-marshals,fay adhay eenbay induceday otay akemay imhay ommandercay ofay ethay orsehay
uardsgay atay Arskoeczay Elosay anday ethay youngay officeray ostlay onay opportunityay ofay
acingplay imselfhay inay ethay oregroundfay eneverwhay ethay Empressay assedpay. Ubovzay
adhay eenbay onay ethay oundgray orfay omesay imetay eforebay Amonov’smay infidelityay asway
iscoveredday. Ethay ismissalday ofay Amonovmay asway ollowedfay instantaneouslyay ybay
ethay electionay ofay Ubovzay. Ethay Empressay entspay onlyay oneay ightnay alone.ay Ethay
extnay ayday Atoplay Ubovzay asway omotedpray otay ethay ostpay ofay Eneral-Adjutantgay anday
appeareday atay ethay Empress’say ightray andhay atay inner,day asay andsomehay aay ilitarymay
igurefay asay adhay everay adorneday ethay aceplay. Erethay asway uculencetray inay ethay etsay
ofay ethay youngay an’smay ead,hay oughthay ishay arkday eyesay oreway atthay eamydray ooklay
ichwhay ishay edecessorspray allay ethay ayway ackbay otay Incepray Istianchray Augustay ofay
Anhalt-Zerbstay adhay alwaysay ornway.

Erethay isay aay adition,tray otnay ellway established,ay atthay erhay elationshipray ithway
Ubovzay asway Atonicplay. Ifay isthay asway ue,tray ethay agingay Empressay ooktay oodgay
arecay atthay itay ouldshay otnay ebay ownknay. Eshay atedhay owinggray olday anday esistedray
otay ethay astlay ethay infirmitiesay ofay erhay advancingay years.ay Eshay etestedday
assesglay oughthay eshay asway obligeday otay useay emthay. Isthay asway ot,nay eshay oldtay erhay
ecretary,say ueday otay anyay ordinaryay ocesspray ofay ysicalphay ecayday utbay Ecause“bay
eshay adhay ornway erhay eyesay outay inay ethay ervicesay ofay ethay ate.”stay Ethay osslay ofay
erhay eethtay idday otnay orryway erhay earlynay osay uch,may ecausebay ethay infirmityay asway
osay universalay anday osay irremediable.ay Inay itespay ofay owder,pay igs,way anday eautybay
ots,spay ethay eethtay ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay adylay ereway atay ethay ercymay ofay
erhay years,ay anday ethay Empressay ithway erhay illionsmay ofay ublesray asway onay etterbay
offay anthay anyay easantpay andmothergray ofay erhay ealmray.

Orstway ofay all,ay eshay ostlay ethay useay ofay erhay egslay. Eythay ecamebay osay ollensway atthay
eshay ouldcay otnay ovemay aboutay onay em,thay anday asway obligeday otay itsay inay aay eeledwhay
airchay ilewhay eshay ooktay erhay airingay inay ethay olonnadecay ofay erhay Arskoeczay Elosay
alacepay. Otay eachray erhay elovedbay Englishay ardengay ichwhay aylay irectlyday elow,bay
eshay uiltbay ofay onestay anday odsay anay inclineday ayway ownday ichwhay erhay airchay ouldcay
ebay entlygay opelledpray untilay itay eachedray ethay ovegray ofay ivelay oaks.ay Osethay
embersmay ofay ethay obilitynay osewhay invitationsay eshay accepteday uiltbay imilarsay
approachesay otay eirthay alacespay inay orderay atthay ethay Empressay eednay imbclay onay
airsstay. Eaninglay onay ethay armay ofay erhay eplumed,bay eribbonedbay anday estarredbay
escort,ay ethay andsomehay Ato,play eshay ouldway oiltay owlyslay upay ethay inclineay ilewhay
erhay osthay oodstay owingbay otay awaitay erhay uccessfulsay arrival.ay Inay isthay ashionfay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ademay erhay astlay ublicpay appearances,ay otteringtay eforebay
ethay eyesay ofay allay eholdersbay ikelay aay ildchay earninglay otay aketay itsay irstfay epsstay.

Inay itespay ofay erhay ysicalphay andicaps,hay eshay ersistedpay inay actingay asay ifay eythay
idday otnay existay anday erhay owesspray asway amazing.ay Erhay ovelay ofay ocietysay emainedray
asay ongstray asay everay anday eshay asway alwaysay ethay ayestgay inay anyay ompanycay. Erhay
infirmitiesay ereway eatergray anthay osethay ichwhay adhay imprisoneday Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray inay ishay armchairay uringday ishay astlay years,ay anday adhay utshay imhay offay omfray
ethay orldway. Utbay unlikeay ethay Ussianpray Ing,kay omwhay eshay eridedday asay eingbay asay
Old“ay asay Erod,”hay eshay evernay ellfay intoay ethay entalmay igidityray ichwhay omescay
omfray osslay ofay ontactcay ithway ethay orldway. Erhay eactionaryray acts,ay ichwhay ereway
entifulplay enoughay inay ethay astlay ecadeday ofay erhay eign,ray ereway ueday otay omethingsay
otheray anthay ethay ardeninghay ofay ethay ocialsay arteriesay ichwhay ometimessay etssay inay
ithway ethay adventay ofay olday age.ay

Eshay ooktay otay ard-playingcay oremay assiduouslyay anthay ever,ay anday erhay assionpay
orfay onversationcay ewgray atherray esslay anthay inay ethay olday aysday enwhay eshay ouldway
alktay ithway Immgray anday Iderotday orfay evensay ourshay atay aay etchstray. Ethay angechay
aymay avehay eenbay ueday otay ethay actfay atthay eshay onay ongerlay adhay enmay ikelay Immgray anday
Iderotday aboutay erhay otay empttay erhay otay esethay onversationalcay orgies.ay Adamemay
Igéevay Ebrunlay asway inay Etersburgpay uringday ethay astlay yearsay ofay ethay Empress,ay
utbay Atherinecay evernay entspay evensay ourshay atay aay imetay onversingcay ithway anyay
omanway. Evenay afteray ixty,say eshay asway otnay educedray otay atthay. Erhay energyay
ufficedsay otay ethay eryvay astlay otay efendday erhay ominantday ikeslay anday islikesday.
Eshay adhay ufferedsay eatgray ysicalphay osseslay. Ethay useay ofay erhay egs,lay allay ofay erhay
eeth,tay anday alfhay ofay erhay eyesightay ereway one,gay yetay ethay igorvay anday irilityvay
ofay erhay ersonalitypay emainedray unimpaired.ay Onay ethay armay ofay aay andsomehay
youngay over,lay eshay ouldway azenbray itay outay otay ethay end.ay Eshay oreway imhay ikelay aay
ecorationday.

Erethay isay onay oubtday atthay Atherinecay asway afraiday ofay Ubov;zay atthay is,ay afraiday
ofay osinglay im,hay anday atthay eshay oiledspay imhay eadfullydray. Eshay oiledspay allay
ethay Ubovzay others,bray Ato,play Alerian,vay anday Icholasnay. Itay asway aay epetitionray
ofay erhay ituationsay ithway ethay Orlovay others,bray onlyay ethay Ubovzay amilyfay asway
oremay aspinggray. Egorygray Orlovay adhay umbledstay intoay ishay oodgay uck,lay osay otay
eak,spay utbay Atoplay Ubovzay adhay orkedway orfay is;hay esidesbay ehay asway youngeray anday
imestay adhay angedchay. Ehay ostlay onay opportunityay otay arnergay ethay ewardsray ofay ishay
enterpriseay orfay imselfhay anday ishay othersbray. Inay aay ortshay ime,tay eythay adhay
acquireday allay ethay onorshay anday ichesray orfay ichwhay ethay Orlovsay adhay aitedway entay
yearsay anday Otiomkinpay anday ishay otégéspray ifteenfay. Eedlessnay otay ay,say ethay
Ubovszay ereway extremelyay unpopular.ay Icholasnay asway arriedmay anday asway atherray
esslay ominentpray aboutay ethay ourtcay anthay Atoplay anday Alerian,vay owhay ereway ethay
entercay ofay itsay ocialsay anday oliticalpay ifelay. Eythay enjoyeday ethay onstantcay
ocietysay ofay ethay Empress.ay

Omfray ethay ointpay ofay iewvay ofay ethay elderay obility,nay Atoplay anday Alerianvay ereway
upstarts.ay Ethay inistersmay anday oreignfay iplomats,day owhay adhay otnay achieveday atay
aay inglesay ound,bay ereway obligeday otay andstay athay inay andhay asay esethay youngstersay
assedpay. Atherine’scay avoritesfay adhay alwaysay eenbay arvenuspay anday ethay oblesnay
adhay owngray accustomeday otay arebay eirthay eadshay otay Eneral-Adjutantsgay owhay adhay
onay ancestry.ay Utbay ethay Ubovszay ereway otnay erelymay unknown;ay eythay ereway ecklessray
youthsay ithoutway experienceay oray anyay otheray easuremay ofay ethay owerpay ichwhay asway
eirsthay. Erethay asway otnay evenay aay Otiomkinpay otay imtray eirthay aws,clay incesay ethay
Incepray ofay Auristay adhay eenbay aidlay awayay inay anay anonymousay outhernsay avegray
ecausebay Atoplay Ubovzay ouldway otnay alloway ethay Empressay otay uildbay aay orthyway ombtay
orfay imhay. Onay urvivorsay ofay ethay Empress’say ownay enerationgay adhay anyay influenceay
ithway erhay.

Ethay aracterchay ofay ethay Ittlelay Ermitage,hay inay ichwhay Atherinecay adhay alwaysay
eceivedray erhay intimates,ay adhay angedchay. Inay ethay aysday enwhay Egorygray Orlovay
adhay uttedstray aboutay ikelay anay apple-cheekeday Adonisay ithway ishay illiterateay
onversation,cay ethay Ermitagehay adhay allay eenbay oremay oray esslay ofay anay ageay anday
adhay olickedfray ikelay ildrenchay ogethertay. Ater,lay enwhay Egorygray Otiomkinpay adhay
oomedglay inay aay ornercay ilewhay ethay Empressay ayedplay ardscay ithway ear-markstay onay
erhay eekschay oray adhay erformedpay ishay entriloquistvay ickstray untilay erhay idessay
acheday ithway aughter,lay erethay adhay illstay eenbay aay indkay ofay armonyhay amongay emthay.
Utbay ethay oupgray ownay eatenedthray otay eakbray intoay otway artspay alongay aay inelay ofay
ocialsay eavageclay ichwhay eparatedsay ethay olday omfray ethay young.ay Asay ethay Empressay
adhay owngray older,ay ethay ostmay ominentpray enmay inay ethay Ermitagehay adhay owngray
younger.ay Ethay otway Ubovszay anday erhay andsonsgray ownay occupieday ethay oregroundfay
ilewhay allay ethay iddle-agedmay anday elderlyay avalierscay ereway elegatedray otay ethay
ackgroundbay. Onlyay Eolay Arishkinnay asway asay olday asay erself,hay Eolay owhay adhay onceay
eowedmay ikelay aay atcay otay allcay erhay orthfay otay aay endezvousray ithway Oniatovskypay
anday omwhay eshay adhay ippedwhay ithway ettlesnay onay ethay oneay occasionay inay allay ishay
ifelay enwhay ishay allegianceay adhay anderedway. Arishkinnay adhay onay influenceay ithway
erhay. Ehay asway erhay oldestay iendfray inay Ussia,ray ownay owngray asay atfay asay eshay anday
aringcay onay ongerlay otay ayplay ind-man’s-buffblay ichwhay adhay onceay eenbay eirthay
avoritefay amegay. Eshay ayedplay ardscay ithway imhay anday uarreledqay ithway imhay anday
ampoonedlay imhay inay ersevay. Enwhay ethay eveningay asway over,ay ethay Empressay otgay uponay
erhay eetfay ithway ifficulty,day anday eaninglay onay ethay armay ofay erhay ark-eyedday Atoplay
etiredray otay erhay edbay amberchay adjoining.ay Ethay Incesspray Alexandrina,ay owhay
asway ownay ourteenfay anday aay embermay ofay ethay Ermitage,hay asway aay itnessway ofay isthay
unconventionalay exitay ofay erhay andmothergray.

Aduallygray ethay Empress’say environmentay eganbay otay eelfay atthay ethay ionesslay asway
owinggray eakerway. Eythay onay ongerlay earedfay erhay awsclay asay ormerlyfay. Enwhay eythay
awsay erhay ookinglay anxiouslyay otay ethay arrogantay Atoplay orfay approval,ay eirthay
ouragecay otay iticizecray awoke.ay Erhay ependenceday avegay erhay away.ay Orfay ethay
irstfay imetay inay erhay eignray umorsray ofay isrespectday anday idiculeray ereway eardhay.
Onglay agoay enwhay eshay adhay oughtthay ofay arryingmay Egorygray Orlov,ay ethay ossipsgay inay
Oscowmay adhay utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay anday isperedwhay. Utbay eythay adhay oppedstay
uddenlysay enoughay enwhay ethay Empressay adhay entsay outay ithway aay ollray ofay umsdray
erhay amousfay Anifestomay ofay Ilencesay. Ethay onguestay ofay Oscowmay adhay easedcay otay
agway enwhay Ittlelay Othermay okespay onay atthay occasion.ay Owadaysnay eshay oosedlay onay
understhay anday ethay ossipsgay eganbay otay ensesay eirthay eedomfray.

Erhay everestsay itics,cray asay usual,ay ereway oundfay inay ethay Enchfray olonycay. Esethay
oreignersfay indulgeday emselvesthay inay ulgarvay estsjay atay ethay expenseay ofay ethay
Ussianray Empressay anday erhay ourtcay anday entway osay arfay asay otay etsay ownday eirthay
Abelaisianray effortsay onay aperpay. Atay aay Elfthtway Ightnay artypay eythay ampoonedlay
ethay Ittlelay Ermitagehay ithway aay eedomfray ichwhay oneay ightmay upposesay otay ebay
Ussianray ifay oneay idday otnay owknay atthay ethay omposerscay ofay ethay ocumentday ereway
Arisianpay. Oneay ybay oneay eythay atirizedsay ethay ourtiers,cay eginningbay ithway Ubovzay.

Ubov“Zay ashay evernay enderedray anyay ervicesay otay ethay atestay anday isay onay ongerlay
ofay ervicesay otay ethay Empress,ay incesay ethay Apphics,say Anickybray anday Otassovpray
executeay ethay unctionsfay ofay ishay office.ay Etlay aay ewfay emeticsay ebay ivengay im,hay otay
akemay imhay ingbray upay atwhay ehay ashay allowedsway.

Ince“Pray Ariatinsky,bay Arshalmay ofay ethay Ourt,cay allshay ebay appointeday Ackjay
Etchkay. Aay oremay entlegay odemay ofay uttingpay otay eathday anthay atthay ybay ethay outknay
isay otay ebay introduced;ay anday ehay allshay avehay ethay officeay ofay otheringsmay anday
anglingstray inay ecretsay osethay atthay areay otay ebay ispatched,day etherwhay itay ebay anay
emperoray oray ishay on;say itay isay expected,ay owever,hay atthay ehay oday otnay etlay emthay
ycray out,ay asay ehay idday aboutay irtythay yearsay ago.ay

Arshal“May Uvarovsay allshay avehay aay atentpay orfay ealingday asay aay utcherbay inay umanhay
esh;flay anday ethay armyay allshay ebay alloweday otay eedfay onay itay inay Oland,pay erewhay
othingnay utbay arcassescay areay eftlay.

A“ay ommitteecay ofay Uchiteli__ay allshay ebay appointeday otay examineay etherwhay Incepray
Yussupovay ebay ableay otay ead;ray ifay ehay an,cay ehay allshay ebay appointeday ompterpray otay
ethay eatres,thay ofay ichwhay ehay isay ownay anagermay.

Adame“May onvay Ieven,lay overnessgay otay ethay Incesses,pray allshay etainray erhay
ace,play oughthay eshay ashay omewhatsay ethay airay ofay anay Amazon;ay utbay eshay allshay ebay
enjoineday otnay otay etlay eastsbay onlyay avehay ermissionpay otay eakspay atay ethay abletay
ofay ethay youngay Incess,pray unlessay eythay eakspay ithway ensesay asay eythay idday inay
Op’sæsay aysday.

Ince“Pray Epnin,ray avinghay openeday ethay oorday oneay ayday enwhay Incepray Otiomkinpay
alledcay orfay aay assglay ofay aterway atthay ehay ightmay imselfhay epeatray isthay importantay
orderay otay ethay ackeys,lay allshay eceiveray aay atentpay orfay ethay aceplay ofay irstfay
aletvay eday ambrechay otay ethay avourites;fay aay ostpay ichwhay otay imhay illway ebay orthway
atthay ofay ield-marshalfay. Owever,hay ethay owncray ofay aurellay ichwhay overedcay ishay
aygray airhay allshay ebay akentay omfray im,hay ecausebay ehay ufferedsay aay uffoonbay otay
eadtray onay imhay ithoutway ayingsay aay ord;way anday ecausebay ethay iftgay ofay aay allsmay
ousehay appeareday uitedsay otay im,hay anday otay onsolecay imhay orfay ethay insult.ay

“May. Avadovsky,zay irectorday anday undererplay ofay ethay ank,bay allshay ebay entsay intoay
Iberiasay otay atchcay ables,say otay eplenishray erhay Ajesty’smay ockstay ofay urs,fay
ichwhay itay illway otnay ebay inay erhay owerpay otay eepkay upay ybay anyay otheray eansmay. Eshay isay
alreadyay unableay otay urnishfay erhay amilyfay ithway em,thay anday Avadovskyzay isay ellway
ownknay otay ebay aay etterbay untsmanhay anthay inancier.”fay

Uchsay ulgarvay idiculeray adhay onglay eenbay iferay inay Arispay. Incesay ethay Empressay adhay
elcomedway Enchfray igrésémay otay Etersburg,pay itay ouldcay ownay ebay eardhay inay Ussiaray.


2ay

Ikelay Eterpay ethay Eat,gray Atherinecay adhay alwaysay atedhay ethay Enchfray. Eshay envieday
emthay eirthay artay anday ulturecay anday esentedray ethay Enchfray attitudeay owardtay
ethay Ussiansray asay arbariansbay. Eshay adhay adopteday Eter’spay oliticalpay olicypay
ichwhay acedplay Ancefray alwaysay onay ethay idesay ofay ethay enemy.ay Erethay adhay alwaysay
eenbay isunderstandingmay anday oolnesscay etweenbay ethay ourtscay ofay Ersaillesvay
anday Etersburg,pay anday enwhay ethay aughterday ofay ethay etestedday Ariamay Eresathay
ecamebay ethay Ueenqay ofay Ancefray itay idday otnay elphay otay akemay eirthay elationsray
oremay iendlyfray. Ifay Atherinecay adhay anyay ellow-feeling,fay asay eshay ightmay eryvay
ellway avehay ad,hay orfay Ariemay Antoinette’say ill-judgeday extravagance,ay eshay
evernay expresseday itay eforebay ethay evolutionray. Onglay ago,ay eshay adhay akentay erhay
uecay owardtay Enchfray oyaltyray omfray Oltairevay anday ethay Encyclopædistsay anday orfay
irtythay yearsay eshay adhay acitlytay adhereday otay it.ay Ethay outbreakay ofay ethay Enchfray
Evolutionray uddenlysay angedchay allay atthay anday ademay erhay overnightay intoay aay
abidray otagonistpray ofay ethay Enchfray ingkay. Itay asway ethay eatestgray inconsistencyay
ofay erhay ife,lay aay etrayalbay ofay erhay ositionpay asay ethay ostmay iberallay onarchmay ofay
erhay enturycay.

Ethay Empressay adhay oughtfay etenderspray anday ebelsray ithinway erhay ownay ingdomkay.
Asay aay usurperay erself,hay eshay asway especiallyay uspicioussay ofay onspiracycay anday
ebellion,ray utbay eshay adhay eenbay oolcay anday aryway inay ealingday ithway ethay asescay
ichwhay arose.ay Ethay Urchman,chay Arseniiay ofay Ostov,ray adhay eltfay erhay eavyhay andhay
enwhay ehay iedtray otay efendday ethay andslay ofay ethay Urchchay againstay onfiscationcay
anday adhay oundfay imselfhay utpay ownday omfray ishopbay otay implesay onkmay anday anishedbay
otay aay oisterclay inay aay onelylay orestfay. Isthay asway atay ethay eryvay eginningbay ofay erhay
eignray. Oonsay afterwardsay amecay ethay onspiracycay ofay Irovichmay anday ethay eathday
ofay Ivanay I,vay ethay Emperoray omwhay Elizabethay adhay eposedday enty-threetway yearsay
eforebay anday owhay adhay onegay aightstray omfray ishay adlecray otay isonpray. Ivanushka,ay
orfay ehay asway alwaysay ememberedray asay aay abybay anday okenspay ofay asay ifay ehay ereway
one,ay adhay owngray intoay aay all,tay ammering,stay ed-hairedray anmay owhay occupieday asay
aay amelessnay isonerpray aay ellcay inay ethay Elburgschlüssay ortressfay. Ethay effortay
ofay youngay Irovichmay otay escueray imhay esultedray inay ethay eathday ofay Ivanay anday ethay
executionay ofay ethay onspiratorcay. Althoughay ethay emovalray ofay Ivanushkaay asway
onvenientcay orfay ethay Empress,ay or,ay asay eshay alledcay itay ovidential,pray eshay
ouldcay otnay avehay annedplay it,ay orfay Irovichmay asway aay antasticfay anday uixoticqay
individualay owhay ouldcay otnay arrycay outay ethay emesschay ofay others.ay

Orfay almostay entay yearsay afterwards,ay ethay Empressay encountereday onay urtherfay
alarmsay untilay ethay allpoxsmay iotsray okebray outay inay Oscowmay. Ilewhay erhay
attentionay asway ixedfay onay ese,thay Ugachev’spay ebellionray eganbay otay ollray upay
inay ethay Eastay anday otay aketay onay ethay aspectay ofay aay ivilcay arway. Ugachevpay asway
aay enuinegay evolutionist,ray anay agitator,ay aay eaderlay ofay ethay assesmay. Ehay
as,way afteray Enkastay Asin,ray ethay econdsay eatgray ocialistsay erohay ofay Ussianray
istoryhay anday ishay ebellion,ray oweverhay omplicatedcay ybay otheray elements,ay asway
essentiallyay aay ocialsay uprising.ay Ethay onditioncay ofay ethay easantspay adhay otnay
improveday underay Atherine’scay imerégay althoughay erethay adhay eenbay aay efiniteday
opehay amongay ethay erfssay atthay ethay iberallay Empressay asway oinggay otay oday omethingsay
orfay emthay. Ethay Ossackcay ebel,ray Ugachev,pay amecay alongay atay ustjay ethay ightray
imetay otay arnergay ethay esentmentray ichwhay ewgray outay ofay esethay isappointedday
opeshay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay amecay otay ivegay atisfactionsay otay ethay injureday eoplepay.
Eythay oughtbray ethay ildway anmay ithway ishay ue-blackblay eardbay otay Oscowmay inay aay agecay
anday executeday imhay erethay.

Ugachevpay adhay onegay ethay ayway ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay anday Ivanushkaay anday ethay
Empressay asway eftlay inay undisputeday ossessionpay ofay ethay onethray. Eshay adhay
atay astlay utpay erhay ousehay inay order,ay orfay onay otheray insurrectionay ofay anyay
onsequencecay okebray outay uringday erhay eignray. Eshay ouldcay ownay ursuepay erhay
operationsay againstay ethay Urkstay uninterrupteday ybay omesticday isturbancesday.
Erhay Ussians,ray ethay atientpay Ark”“day eople,pay ereway uiescentqay. Afteray
Ugachev’spay ue-blackblay eadhay adhay allenfay anday ishay oodblay adhay ainedstay ethay
Anuaryjay owsnay ofay ethay Edray Uare,sqay onay otheray eaderlay appeareday otay arouseay ethay
eoplepay againstay eirthay Empress.ay

Enwhay ethay ewsnay ofay ethay Enchfray Evolutionray eachedray Ussia,ray Otiomkinpay anday
ethay Empressay ereway archingmay owardtay Onstantinoplecay. Orfay ifteenfay yearsay ethay
easantspay ofay Ussiaray adhay eenbay ubmissivesay anday ethay Empressay adhay otnay eenbay
awareay ofay ethay estlessnessray inay Ancefray. Ethay Enchfray uprisingay astonisheday anday
alarmeday erhay ofoundlypray anday illedfay Otiomkinpay ithway aay aralyzingpay errortay.
Eythay adhay allay ethay eactionsray atthay ightmay ebay expecteday ofay arvenuspay underay ethay
ircumstancescay. Ethay outrageday Empressay avegay entvay otay erhay indignationay inay ethay
anguagelay ofay aay ish-wifefay. Eshay idday otnay admitay erhay awfulay earsfay. Eshay oastedbay
oudlylay otay Ountcay Ur,ségay ethay Enchfray envoyay owhay avoredfay ethay epublic,ray
E“Jay uissay aristocrate,ay estc’ay onmay ier.”métay Ofay allay erhay ourt,cay onlyay Eolay
Arishkinnay ouldcay ememberray erhay asay anay awkwarday ountrycay irlgay owhay arriveday inay
Ussiaray ithoutway evenay aay idalbray est,chay anday Eolay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay astlay
otay emindray erhay ofay erhay umblehay origin.ay Ehay adhay otnay orgottenfay ethay ingstay ofay
ettlesnay applieday ybay ethay Empressay enwhay eshay asway aay youngay anday igorousvay Andgray
Uchessday.

Atherinecay ollowedfay ethay ortunesfay ofay ethay Enchfray oyalray amilyfay ourhay ybay
ourhay ithway intenseay ympathysay. Eshay asway atay Eterhofpay enwhay eshay eardhay ofay
eirthay ightflay omfray Arispay anday eshay asway illstay ejoicingray overay itay enwhay eshay
eardhay atthay eythay adhay eenbay arresteday anday akentay ackbay. Omethingsay imilarsay
adhay appenedhay otay Eterpay irtythay yearsay eforebay inay ethay Eterhofpay alace,pay utbay
Atherinecay adhay alledcay erselfhay atay atthay imetay aay evolutionistray anday adhay eenbay
inay ethay opponents’ay ampcay. Isthay imetay eshay ailedray oudlylay anday iolentlyvay
againstay ethay egicidesray ofay Ancefray. Eshay udderedshay otay inkthay ofay atwhay ightmay
appenhay otay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ifay anotheray Ugachevpay ouldshay esentlypray
appear.ay Afteray ethay eathday ofay Ouislay anday Ariemay Antoinette,ay eshay aidsay atthay
erhay onlyay opehay orfay Ancefray asway atthay aay Arcæsay oray aay Enghisgay Ankhay ightmay
iseray upay anday overwhelmay emthay. Eshay upportedsay ethay ideaay ofay interventionay
ithway enthusiasmay utbay eyondbay erhay eloquentay encouragementay eshay avegay onay
actualay aid;ay allay Europeay echoeday ithway erhay iradestay anday abuse.ay Erhay irilevay
anguagelay over-toppeday atthay ofay anyay otheray onarchmay. Eshay ouldcay enounceday
ethay iendsfray ofay ethay epublicray asay onay oneay elseay anday aisepray ethay olday imerégay
ithway atchlessmay ervorfay. Erhay olday iend,fray Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussia,pray amecay
inay orfay ethay ostmay extremeay abuseay ecausebay ehay ouldway otnay oinjay ethay uehay anday
ycray againstay ethay Acobins;jay anday Edmunday Urke,bay owhay enouncedday ethay Enchfray
Evolutionistsray althoughay ehay adhay avoredfay ethay Americanay ebels,ray asway eapedhay
ithway undiscriminatingay aisepray.

Ethay Empress’say olewhay attitudeay owardtay ethay Enchfray Evolutionray asway oneay ofay
usterblay anday ineffectiveness.ay Evenay erhay ownay ampcay oundfay itay ineffectualay
anday inconsistent.ay Eshay inviteday ethay igrésémay otay Etersburg,pay orfay ichwhay
ethay epublicanray idesay aturallynay etestedday erhay. Erhay eputationray eclinedday
ithway erhay ontemporariescay owhay eltfay atthay isthay emotionalay efenceday asway
omethingsay esslay anthay ightmay avehay eenbay expecteday omfray Atherinecay ethay Eatgray
ofay ormerfay aysday. Ormerly,fay eshay adhay understooday ethay artay ofay ullingpay ethay
ingsstray inay ilencesay anday adhay ownknay owhay otay accomplishay erhay illway ithoutway
eatsthray. Eshay adhay egotiatednay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay anday establisheday ethay
olicypay ofay armeday eutralitynay ithway atesmanlikestay effectiveness.ay Ownay eshay
adhay egeneratedday intoay ituperationvay anday inaction.ay Otnay onlyay ethay Ussianray
ourtcay utbay allay ethay ourtscay ofay Europeay eganbay otay eelfay atthay ethay ionesslay ofay
Etersburgpay asway owinggray old.ay


3ay

Atherinecay adhay arriedmay erhay otway andsonsgray young,ay uchmay ootay youngay
eirthay overnorsgay oughtthay. Itay asway ownay ime,tay eshay onsidered,cay otay arrymay
Alexandrina,ay erhay anddaughter,gray althoughay ethay Incesspray asway utbay ourteenfay.
Ethay Empressay adhay eenbay arcelyscay olderay anthay isthay enwhay eshay eceivedray aay
oposalpray ofay arriagemay anday accepteday it,ay althoughay erhay atherfay adhay earedfay
otay endsay osay youngay aay aughterday otay Ussiaray. Atherinecay ememberedray atthay youngay
irlgay ithway aay eatgray ealday ofay affectionay anday ympathysay. Ell“Tay emay uly,”tray
eshay onceay urstbay outay inay aay etterlay otay Imm,gray Ouldn’t“way itay ebay armingchay ifay
anay Empressay ouldcay emainray allay erhay ifelay onglay onlyay ifteenfay yearsay old?”ay Itay
emainedray alwaysay ethay ostmay ividvay yearay ofay erhay ife,lay ethay yearay inay ichwhay eshay
adhay oldtay erhay earday Apapay ood-byegay anday adhay etsay outay otay eeksay erhay ortunesfay inay
Ussiaray. Anday ownay ethay armingchay youngay Alexandrinaay adhay eachedray atthay idealay
age.ay Erhay andmothergray adhay alreadyay electedsay aay usbandhay orfay erhay.

Otay aysay atthay ethay Empressay adhay electedsay aay usbandhay orfay erhay isay otay utpay itay ootay
ildlymay. Atherinecay adhay onceay aidsay ofay erselfhay ithway absoluteay uthtray atthay
eneverwhay eshay antedway aay ingthay eshay asway obligeday otay antway itay ostmay erriblytay.
Eshay ownay antedway otay arrymay erhay anddaughtergray otay ethay andsongray ofay Ulrica,ay
ethay istersay ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Aay ewfay aysday afteray Atherine’scay
etrothalbay inay Etersburg,pay Ederickfray adhay arriedmay ishay istersay Ulricaay otay
ethay Owncray Incepray ofay Edensway. Ulrica’say arriagemay adhay adhay oneay advantageay
ichwhay Atherine’scay adhay acked;lay ethay Ueenqay ofay Edensway adhay otnay eenbay obligeday
otay abandonay ethay eligionray ofay erhay athersfay anday evertray otay aay aganpay urchchay.
Ulricaay adhay emainedray aay evoutday Utheranlay allay erhay ifelay.

Erhay on,say Ustavgay ethay Irdthay ofay Eden,sway asway aay anmay ofay ashion,fay anay exileday
Arisianpay obligeday otay ivelay inay Ockholmstay. Ustavgay asway aay opfay inay ishay abitshay
anday aay eathercockway inay ishay oliticspay. Ethay eletonskay inay ishay osetclay asway atthay
ishay onsay anday eirhay asway otnay ishay onsay. Ustavgay asway anay unhappy,ay omplainingcay
an,may evotedday otay ishay othermay yetay atay oddsay ithway erhay. Ehay asway inallyfay
assassinateday enwhay ishay on,say Ustavgay ethay Ourth,fay asway onlyay ixteensay. Itay asway
isthay on,say aidsay otay ebay aay astard,bay omwhay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray osechay otay ebay
ethay usbandhay ofay erhay anddaughtergray Alexandrina.ay Erhay earthay asway etsay onay ethay
arriagemay.

Ustavgay ethay Ourthfay asway eventeensay enwhay ehay amecay otay ethay Ussianray ourtcay
atay ethay Empress’say invitationay asay aay uitorsay orfay ethay andhay ofay ethay Ussianray
Incesspray. Ehay asway aay erioussay youngay anmay owhay adhay evertedray otay ethay ietypay ofay
ishay andmothergray Ulrica.ay Ethay youngay Ingkay asway accompanieday ybay ishay uncle,ay
ethay Ukeday ofay Udermania,say anay inexplicableay anmay owhay oncealedcay ishay andhay
osay ellway uringday ethay ensuingay amadray atthay ishay artpay inay ethay evelopmentday ofay
eventsay emainsray oreverfay iddenhay. Ehay as,way ikelay ishay ephew,nay anay ardentay
Otestant;pray utbay ehay asway alsoay aay Eemasonfray anday aay Artinist,may aay elieverbay
inay allay ethay ysticalmay ultscay ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay ichwhay ethay Empressay
islikedday anday erhay onsay embraced.ay Udermaniasay ouldcay otnay avehay eenbay asay
indifferentay otay ishay ephew’snay actionsay asay ishay outwarday emeanorday indicated.ay
Utbay itay isay oubtfulday etherwhay ehay adhay anyay ealray esponsibilityray orfay ethay
iascofay ofay ethay Empress’say ansplay. Ustav’sgay oursecay asway osay onsistentcay ithway
ishay aracterchay atthay onay otheray explanationay anthay ativenay entbay eemssay otay ebay
ecessarynay.

Atherine’scay entertainmentay ofay erhay Edishsway uestsgay asway egalray astpay allay
ecedentpray. Ethay ourtcay oweredflay inay aay uccessionsay ofay allsbay anday estivitiesfay
ethay ikelay ofay ichwhay adhay otnay eenbay eensay incesay ethay irstfay isitvay ofay Incepray
Enryhay otay Ussiaray. Ustavgay asway impeccableay asay otay ormfay. Ethay atelay Ingkay ofay
Eden,sway ishay utativepay ather,fay adhay eenbay ethay assglay ofay ashionfay anday ethay
on,say inay itespay ofay ishay ingrowingay iety,pay orebay ethay arkmay ofay Arispay. Ethay
Andgray Ukes,day Alexanderay anday Onstantine,cay eemedsay uncouthay ybay omparisoncay
ithway isthay olemnsay youngay anmay osewhay annersmay ereway osay eticulouslymay erfectpay.
Ustavgay asway anay assiduousay eaderray ofay ethay Ible,bay otay ichwhay ehay asway accustomeday
otay urntay orfay ounselcay eneverwhay ehay oundfay imselfhay inay anyay ifficultyday. Ifay
ethay Empressay adhay adhay ethay advantageay ofay odernmay ychology,psay eshay ouldway avehay
ownknay erhay Edishsway Incepray atay onceay orfay aay epressedray youthay anday anay elusiveay
idegroombray. Utbay otnay avinghay isthay advantage,ay eshay essedpray onwarday otay ethay
oalgay onay ichwhay eshay adhay etsay erhay earthay anday ungedplay eadlonghay anday unprepareday
intoay ethay eatestgray ailurefay ofay erhay ifelay. Asay eshay aid,say eshay asway oremay anthay
alfhay inay ovelay ithway ethay youngay anmay erselfhay.

Ethay arriagemay ontractcay asway allay utbay ignedsay. Onlyay oneay ointpay ofay ifferenceday
emainedray otay ebay ettled,say ethay uturefay eligionray ofay ethay Incesspray. Atherinecay
adhay ipulatedstay atthay ethay irlgay ouldshay ebay alloweday otay eepkay erhay aith,fay anday
ouldshay ebay ermittedpay otay avehay erhay Ussianray onfessorcay anday erhay Ussianray
apelchay inay ethay Edishsway alacepay. Ethay youngay Ingkay emurredday. Onay ethay urface,say
allay entway ellway. Ubovzay anday Arkov,may owhay ewdray upay ethay ontractcay orfay ethay
Empress,ay esentedpray anay amiableay exterioray anday ethay Edishsway Incepray appeareday
on-committalnay.

Itay isay atay isthay ointpay atthay Ubovzay isay aidsay otay avehay adviseday ethay Empressay
adlybay. Ehay isay upposedsay otay avehay induceday erhay otay andstay outay orfay impossibleay
ermstay anday otay ebay esponsibleray orfay ethay adbay iplomacyday eshay exhibiteday onay
isthay occasion.ay Itay isay extremelyay unlikelyay atthay isthay asway uetray. Ubovzay
asway asay ittlelay esponsibleray orfay ethay Empress’say attitudeay asay Udermaniasay
asway accountableay orfay ethay Ing’skay. Inay ethay isiscray ichwhay evelopedday
eforebay ethay eyesay ofay allay ethay ourt,cay ethay actualay ontestantscay ereway ethay
eventeen-year-oldsay Ingkay anday ethay ixty-seven-year-oldsay Empress.ay Itay asway aay
ifelay anday eathday ontestcay. Eythay adhay oinedjay attlebay overay anay issueay upremelysay
eciouspray otay othbay ofay emthay anday eithernay ouldcay endureay otay oselay.

Ethay Empressay asway extremelyay omanticray aboutay ethay olewhay usinessbay. Eshay
ommandedcay ethay youngay ouplecay otay isskay eachay otheray inay erhay esencepray anday
ademay airyay emarksray aboutay ishingway otay apturecay ethay andsomehay idegroombray
orfay erselfhay. Inay ancyfay eshay e-livedray erhay ownay etrothal,bay opinghay inay
Alexandrina’say arriagemay otay edeemray allay ethay undesirableay eaturesfay ofay erhay
own.ay Erhay anddaughtergray ouldshay avehay otnay erelymay alfhay aay ozenday emiseschay utbay
everyay uxurylay atthay aay idebray ouldcay ishway anday aboveay allay eshay ouldshay ebay avedsay
ethay ordealay ofay angingchay erhay eligionray. Onay oubtday Alexandrinaay ouldway ustjay
asay oonsay avehay angedchay erhay eedcray asay ot,nay utbay Atherinecay ouldcay otnay icturepay
isthay indifference.ay Eshay adhay orgottenfay orfay ethay imetay eingbay atthay eshay anday
erhay ifteen-year-oldfay anddaughtergray ereway otnay one.ay

Onay ethay eveningay enwhay ethay arriagemay ontractcay asway otay ebay igned,say ethay
Empressay oneshay ikelay aay unsay onay erhay onethray. Eshay adhay assembleday orfay ethay
occasionay ethay olewhay andgray orldway ofay Etersburgpay. Urchchay anday Atestay
urroundedsay erhay inay ullfay egaliaray. Ethay ishopsbay oodstay atay attention,ay inay
eirthay embroidereday obesray overedcay ithway earlpay anday aragd,smay ilewhay ilitarymay
essengersmay inay ightbray elvetvay eechesbray ashedflay ackbay anday orthfay anday
Incessespray inay ideway atinsay irtsskay urtsiedcay eforebay ethay ilingsmay Andmothergray
onay erhay onethray. Ousandsthay ofay andlescay oneshay uponay ethay enescay. Ethay allhay adhay
eenbay eparedpray orfay ethay edazzlementbay ofay Europe,ay orfay ethay Empressay inay erhay
imaginationay acedfay otnay erelymay ethay eyesay ofay erhay ownay ourtierscay utbay ethay eyesay
ofay allay ethay ourtscay ofay Europe.ay Ateverwhay appenedhay erehay asway otnay intendeday otay
appenhay ivatelypray.

Owlyslay erethay eptcray intoay ethay atmosphereay ofay ethay oomray aay uggestionsay ofay
uspensesay. Atay omentsmay onversationcay easedcay anday ethay ompanycay ookedlay arounday
expectantly.ay Utbay aay anceglay atay ethay imperturbableay igurefay inay ethay urplepay
antlemay anday ethay iling,smay onfidentcay eyesay eneathbay ethay iamondday owncray asway
ufficientsay otay eassureray ethay ompanycay anday otay estoreray ethay atmosphereay ofay
ease.ay Ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay adhay appeareday utbay Ustavgay ofay Edensway orfay
omesay unaccountableay easonray illstay emainedray invisible.ay Ethay Ussianray ourtcay
adhay eenbay accustomeday otay ysteriousmay elaysday underay ethay Empressay Elisabeth,ay
utbay Atherine’scay imerégay adhay aughttay emthay otay expectay oremay omptnesspray anday
ispatchday. Utbay evenay ethay Empressay Elisabethay expecteday aay idegroombray otay ebay
omptpray. Ethay imetay aggeddray owlyslay alongay untilay atay astlay ethay alltay Englishay
ocksclay owedshay entay. Illstay ethay Empressay etrayedbay onay anxietyay asay eshay acedfay
ethay uestionqay ownay apparentay inay allay eyes.ay

Atay astlay Ubovzay appeareday anday isperedwhay omethingsay inay erhay ear.ay Ithway
ifficultyday eshay ose,ray ooktay ishay arm,ay anday assedpay oughthray ethay oomray otay erhay
ownay amberchay. Asay ethay oorday osedclay ehindbay er,hay eshay ellfay otay ethay oorflay
unconscious.ay Itay isay aidsay atthay eshay adhay aintedfay utbay itay isay oremay obablepray
atthay eshay uccumbedsay otay aay ightslay okestray ofay aralysispay. Ubovzay adhay oughtbray
ethay ultimatumay ofay ethay Ingkay. Ustavgay ouldway otnay ignsay ethay arriagemay ontractcay
asay onglay asay itay ontainedcay ethay auseclay ichwhay ermittedpay Alexandrinaay otay
etainray ethay Ussianray eligionray.

Ethay Empressay ouldway otnay admitay erselfhay efeatedday. Otay ebay eatenbay ybay aay
eventeen-year-oldsay oybay asway unthinkable.ay Eshay eedednay aay ittlelay imetay otay
ingbray ethay youthay arounday anday otay overcomeay aay ubbornnessstay ichwhay eshay adhay
underestimated.ay Eshay arrangeday aay allbay anday ommandedcay Alexandrina,ay owhay
adhay iedcray untilay erhay eyesay ereway ed,ray otay onday erhay ineryfay anday ogay onay asay ifay
othingnay adhay appenedhay. Y“Whay oday youay eep?”way eshay otewray onay aay apscray ofay aperpay.
At“Whay isay utpay offay isay otnay ostlay. Ashway youray eyesay ithway iceay anday youray earsay
oo,tay anday aketay Estushev’sbay opsdray. Othingnay isay ostlay. Itay isay Iay owhay asway illay
yesterday.ay Youay areay exedvay aboutay ethay elayday. Atthay isay all.”ay

Alexandrinaay obeyeday erhay andmothergray. Ethay Ingkay alsoay attendeday ethay allbay.
Utbay ethay otway youngay ingsthay onay ongerlay etmay asay ormerly;fay ethay Ingkay asway
unctiliouspay anday ethay Incesspray asway elf-conscious,say anday evenay Andmammagray
asway otnay osay aygay anday airyay asay eshay adhay eenbay. Eshay insisteday onay eepingkay ethay
ecalcitrantray youngay anmay otway eeksway ongerlay anday efusedray otay onsidercay ethay
egotiationsnay osedclay evenay afteray ehay adhay epartedday orfay Ockholmstay ithway ishay
uncle.ay Erhay opeshay iedday ardhay anday enwhay eythay ereway eadday eshay eptkay ethay orpsecay
about,ay unableay otay interay it.ay

Otay ethay Empress,ay ethay ockshay ofay efeatday asway eadfuldray. Eshay asway accustomeday
otay uccess,say anday ailurefay ofay anyay indkay asway unendurable.ay Almostay
apologeticallyay eshay otewray otay erhay onsay Aul:pay E“Thay actfay isay ethay Ingkay
etendedpray atthay Alexandrinaay adhay omisedpray imhay otay angechay erhay eligionray anday
aketay ethay acramentsay inay ethay Utheranlay ay,way anday atthay eshay adhay ivengay imhay erhay
andhay onay it....ay Eshay oldtay emay ithway ethay andorcay anday aïveténay aturalnay otay erhay
owhay ehay adhay oldtay erhay atthay onay ethay oronationcay ayday eshay ouldway avehay otay aketay
ethay acramentsay ithway im,hay anday atthay eshay adhay eplied,ray Ertainly,‘Cay ifay Iay an,cay
anday ifay Andmammagray onsents.’cay Anday afteray atthay ehay okespay otay erhay aboutay itay
again,ay anday eshay alwaysay eferredray imhay otay emay. Iay askeday erhay ifay eshay adhay ivengay
erhay andhay otay ethay Ingkay ybay ayway ofay omisepray onay isthay ointpay. Atay atthay eshay iedcray
ithway aay ortsay ofay instinctiveay ight,fray Ever‘Nay inay ymay ife.’”lay

Ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay iltedway ikelay ethay overbialpray iltedjay aidenmay ofay
ethay illagevay. Afteray erhay andmother’sgray eathday eshay asway arriedmay ybay erhay
atherfay otay aay Incepray ofay Austria,ay erewhay afteray aay iefbray unhappyay arriedmay
ifelay eshay iedday inay ildbirthchay. Eshay asway alwaysay orbid,may iritless,spay anday
omplainingcay. Ethay instinctiveay ightfray ofay ichwhay erhay andmothergray okespay
evernay eftlay erhay. Allay ofay ethay Empress’say amilyfay ereway ackinglay inay ormalnay
aggressiveness.ay Erhay overs,lay erhay on,say erhay andchildrengray omwhay eshay oughtbray
upay ereway allay inay omesay egreeday afflicteday ybay ethay amesay instinctiveay earfay ichwhay
ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay owedshay. Atherinecay ethay Eat,gray ikelay othersay ofay
erhay ind,kay idday otnay ucceedsay inay impartingay eatnessgray otay erhay escendantsday.


4ay

Afteray ethay Edishsway Ing’skay eparture,day ethay Empress’say ealthhay ewgray orseway.
Erethay ereway aysday enwhay erhay oorpay ollensway egslay ouldway otnay upportsay erhay atay
allay anday eshay ufferedsay orturestay ithway emthay. Ethay ummersay atay Arskoeczay Elo,say
erewhay eshay asway alwaysay atay erhay estbay anday appiest,hay idday otnay elphay erhay. Enwhay
eshay alkedway otay ethay ittlelay audienceay amberchay erewhay eshay eceivedray erhay
inisters,may eshay onay ongerlay eanedlay onay Atoplay Ubovzay aloneay utbay equiredray anay
attendantay onay ethay otheray idesay asay ellway. Eshay ooktay ethay airay inay erhay eeledwhay
airchay alongay ethay ue-walledblay arcadeay asay arfay asay ethay agateay avilionpay anday
enthay ackbay again,ay otnay anay easyay ourneyjay orfay aay oman,way owhay adhay eshay otnay eenbay
erself,hay ouldway avehay eenbay ed-riddenbay. Inay ethay onthmay ofay Augustay eshay awsay
aay ootingshay arstay anday aidsay atthay itay oretoldfay erhay eathday. Eshay adhay owngray
uddenlysay anday arklyday uperstitioussay.

Eturningray otay Etersburgpay inay ethay autumn,ay eshay utpay erselfhay inay ethay andshay
ofay aay otoriousnay uackqay amednay Ambro-Cazzionilay. Erhay octorsday ereway oremay
astonisheday anthay offended.ay Ethay Empressay owhay adhay earchedsay Europeay orfay
ientificscay ysicians,phay owhay adhay oughtbray enmay ikelay Ogerson,ray Eikard,way anday
Imsdaleday otay Ussia,ray anday owhay adhay introduceday accinationvay ybay offeringay
erselfhay asay aay ubject,say adhay uddenlysay onegay ackbay otay amanismshay. Eshay osedclay
erhay oorsday onay allay ethay eputableray octorsday anday admitteday ethay agicianmay only.ay
Ambro-Cazzionilay asway aay esserlay indkay ofay Agliostro,cay ethay arlatanchay omwhay
eshay adhay atirizedsay inay erhay omediescay anday abuseday inay erhay orrespondence,cay aay
eederbray ofay ethay indkay ofay uperstitionsay ichwhay eshay anday otheray enlighteneday
iritsspay ofay erhay ageay adhay ivedlay otay exterminate.ay Atheticallypay eshay ubmittedsay
otay allay ethay asticdray emediesray atthay erhay ealerhay ecommendedray. Aay ailyday
oot-bathfay ofay ice-colday ea-watersay asway aay artpay ofay ishay imerégay anday ehay entway
imselfhay ailyday otay etchfay ethay aterway orfay ethay atient’spay use.ay Atay irst,fay ethay
Empressay eemedsay otay improve.ay Eshay appeareday atay ethay ittlelay Ermitagehay againay
anday oinedjay inay ethay aiety,gay aughinglay untilay erhay idessay ached.ay

Onay ethay orningmay ofay Ovembernay ethay ixth,say eshay oseray asay usualay atay ixsay o’clock,ay
ankdray erhay ustomarycay ivefay upscay ofay offee,cay anday etsay orthfay eerfullychay onay
ethay outineray ofay ethay ayday. Eshay awsay erhay overlay anday erhay ecretaries,say anday
avegay erhay usualay orders.ay Enthay eshay askeday otay ebay eftlay aloneay orfay aay omentmay
anday etiredray otay erhay essing-roomdray. Ethay attendantsay inay ethay antechamberay
aitedway oremay anthay ethay usualay engthlay ofay imetay orfay eirthay ummons,say utbay itay
evernay amecay. Enwhay erhay ivatepray ecretarysay inallyfay entereday ethay apartment,ay
ehay oundfay erhay yinglay unconsciousay eforebay ethay oorday ofay erhay aterway osetclay.
Eshay adhay adhay aay okestray ofay aralysispay. Eythay aggeddray ethay attressmay omfray ethay
edbay anday aidlay ethay yingday omanway uponay it,ay orfay eshay asway ootay eavyhay otay ebay
iftedlay. Isthay aspinggay animal,ay ichwhay adhay onceay eenbay ethay Empress,ay aylay onay
erhay attressmay anday uggledstray ithway eathday ilewhay ethay andshay ofay ethay ockclay entway
arounday eethray imestay. Ethay ollowingfay eveningay eshay iedday.

Afteray Eterpay ethay Eat,gray ethay Omanovsray adhay allay eenbay uriedbay inay ethay ortressfay
ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay. Atherinecay adhay eviatedday omfray isthay ustomcay
enwhay eshay ordereday ethay odybay ofay ethay atelay Ar,czay Eterpay ethay Ird,thay otay ebay
aidlay inay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onasterymay atay ethay oppositeay enday ofay ethay
itycay. Althoughay itay eemssay angelystray outay ofay eepingkay ithway erhay ambitiousay
emperament,tay eshay erselfhay idday otnay ishway otay ebay uriedbay esidebay Eterpay ethay
Eatgray. Ourfay yearsay eforebay erhay eath,day eshay otewray esethay instructionsay
oncerningcay erhay urialbay ace:play In“ay asecay Iay ouldshay ieday inay Arskoeczay Elo,say
aylay ymay odybay inay ethay urchyardchay ofay Ofiasay. Ifay inay ethay itycay ofay Etersburg,pay
inay ethay athedralcay oray ethay urialbay urchchay ofay ethay Evskynay Oisterclay. Ifay inay
Ella,pay ingbray emay alongay ethay aterwaysway otay ethay Evskynay Oisterclay. Ifay inay
Oscow,may ingbray emay otay ethay Onskoyday Oisterclay oray otay ethay owntay urchyardchay
earnay ybay. Ifay inay Eterhof,pay otay ethay Ergeisay Oisterclay. Ifay inay omesay otheray
ace,play otay aay urchyardchay earnay ybay.

E“Thay offincay allshay ebay ornebay ybay orsehay uardsgay onlyay anday onay oneay else.ay Ymay
odybay allshay ebay othedclay inay aay itewhay ess,dray ithway aay oldengay owncray onay ethay
eadhay onay ichwhay ymay amenay allshay ebay ittenwray. Ourningmay allshay ebay ornway orfay ixsay
onthsmay utbay otnay onger;lay aay ittlelay isay estbay. Afteray ethay irstfay ixsay eeks,way
ethay eople’spay amusementsay allshay ebay opened.ay Afteray ethay urial,bay etrothals,bay
eddings,way anday usicmay allshay ebay allowed.ay

Y“May ibrarylay ithway allay ymay anuscriptsmay anday allay ymay apers,pay Iay equeathbay otay ymay
earday andson,gray Alexanderay Avlovich;pay ikewiselay ymay ewels;jay anday Iay essblay imhay
omfray ymay earthay anday omfray ymay oulsay. Aay opycay ofay isthay allshay ebay utpay awayay inay aay
afesay aceplay otay insureay itsay ulfilment,fay osay atthay oonersay oray aterlay ameshay anday
isgraceday allshay overtakeay osethay owhay oday otnay arrycay outay ymay illway.

It“ay isay ymay intentionay otay aceplay Onstantinecay onay ethay onethray ofay ethay Eekgray
Orientalay Empire.ay Orfay ethay elfareway ofay ethay Ussianray anday Eekgray Empires,ay Iay
ecommendray atthay ethay Incespray ofay Embergwürttay ebay emovedray omfray ethay ounselscay
ofay esethay empiresay ichwhay ouldshay avehay asay ittlelay otay oday ithway emthay asay
ossible;pay alsoay atthay ethay otway alf-Germanshay allshay ebay emoved.”ray

Ethay Empressay asway uriedbay inay ethay Athedralcay ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay
eneathbay aay itewhay arblemay abslay ikelay atthay ichwhay overscay allay ethay Arsczay ofay
Ussiaray owhay ollowedfay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Esidebay erhay ieslay ethay odybay ofay Eterpay
ethay Ird,thay oughtbray erethay ybay erhay onsay aay ortshay imetay afteray erhay urialbay.

Eshay adhay eparedpray anay inscriptionay orfay erhay avestonegray anday isthay isay atwhay eshay
ishedway otay avehay itay ay:say

Erehay ieslay

ATHERINEcay EtHay ECONDsay

ornbay inay Ettinstay onay Aprilay 21ay /ay Aymay 2,ay 1729ay.

Inay ethay yearay 1744ay eshay entway otay Ussiaray otay arrymay Eterpay III.ay Atay ethay ageay ofay
ourteen,fay eshay ademay ethay eefoldthray esolution,ray otay easeplay erhay onsort,cay
Elisabeth,ay anday ethay Ationnay.

Eshay eglectednay othingnay inay orderay otay ucceedsay inay isthay.

Eighteenay yearsay ofay oredombay anday olitudesay ausedcay erhay otay eadray anymay ooksbay.

Enwhay eshay ascendeday ethay onethray ofay Ussia,ray eshay ishedway otay oday oodgay anday
iedtray otay ingbray appiness,hay eedomfray anday osperitypray otay erhay ubjectssay.

Eshay orgavefay easilyay anday atedhay onay one.ay

Eshay asway ood-natured,gay easy-going;ay asway ofay aay eerfulchay emperament,tay
epublicanray entiments,say anday aay indkay earthay.

Eshay adhay iendsfray.

Orkway amecay easyay otay er;hay eshay ovedlay ociabilitysay anday ethay arts.ay

Ethay instructionsay ofay ethay Empressay ereway otnay ollowed;fay erhay ishes,way otnay
obeyed.ay Ethay oldcay itewhay abslay ichwhay overscay erhay onveyscay onay ordway ofay erhay
astlay essagemay otay osteritypay.
